atha saptaviṃśo dhyāyaḥśrībhagavānuvāca evaṃ kṛtvā yathāśāstraṃ divyamabjaja vai purā pitryaṃ tadanu vai kuryāt vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā  Paus pauṣkarauvācajñātum icchāmi bhagavān tvacchāsanasthitaiḥ samuddiśya pitṛśrāddhaṃ kāryam ācāryapūrvakaiḥ  Paus keṣāṃ keṣāṃ ca tat kāryaṃ kasya kasya ca kīdṛśam vidadhāti pañca pañcaiva kathaṃcaivasamyaṅnirvartitaṃ hi yat  Paus śrī bhagavānuvāca kartavyatvena vai kuryāt karmasanyāsināṃ sadā nirvāṇadīkṣitānāṃ ca bhaktānām api cābjaja  Paus anirdiṣṭakramāṇāṃ ca caturthāśramiṇāṃ tu vai bhagavad padalipsūnāṃ jñānināṃ ca tathaiva hi  Paus prītaye manyasiddhānāṃ sādhakānāṃ tu pauṣkara śubhajanmāptaye śaśvanmanyasāmukhyasiddhaye  Paus kāryaṃ tatputrakāṇāṃ tu kṛpayā deśikādikaiḥ kuryād vai samayajñānāṃ nityaṃ saddharmavṛddhaye  Paus bhūyaḥ sujanmalābhāya sadvidhādhigamāya ca bāndhavānāmāto nyeṣāṃ bhaktānām evam eva hi  Paus sadyo duṣkṛtaśāntyarthaṃ kṛpayā nityam ācaret kartānā vākarmasaṃnyāsī parivṛddho vratāśrayī  Paus na nivāṇapadaṃnīto dīkṣāyāṃ bhogalālasa tīvrabhāvaṃ vinā yastu na siddho manyasevanāt  Paus niḥ santāno pi vai mantrī na yāti siddhigocaram nūnam etat dvijaśreṣṭha sanmārgasyaiḥ kriyāparaiḥ  Paus satkartavyaprakāreṇa tvanugrāhayāḥ sadaiva hi samāsādyātra saṃyāti yathā divyaṃ paraṃ padam  Paus ātastuḥ atastudīkṣitānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ sā mayājinām avaktavyaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ etat nirvartanāya ca  Paus śrāddhakāle tu vai muktavā tair apyanyatra padmaja mantramudrākriyā dhyānamajñānādikriyāṃ vinā  Paus nābhyastavyā na yoktavyā bhaktaiḥ sāmayikādibhiḥ samāśritya nimittaṃ vai deśakālādiktaṃ dvija  Paus kriyate yat pitṝṇāṃ ca bhavatyanṛṇavān naraḥ prayāti tṛptim atulāṃ tena karmavaśād api  Paus āgate gatim āyānti śrāddhād āhlādasaṃyutām sakṛdvaikaṃ tu bahudhā kālamādehalakṣaṇam  Paus yuktaṃ tithigaṇena eva vātsarīyeṇa pauṣkāra kṣetrāptipūrveṇānnena sannimittagaṇena tu  Paus saṃsāraduḥkhaśāntyarthaṃ duṣkṛtakṣapaṇāya ca vyakte ca indriyacakrasya duḥkhajaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ hi yat save yad  dyanantakalpaṃ ca karmātmā yesaṃ yato bjajī  Paus ato bhūtamayaṃ dehaṃ samantaram asya vai duḥkhopalambhanaṃ kalpaṃ yasmāt kamalasaṃbhava  Paus duḥkhena śāmyate duḥkha sanyaskandhagate duḥkhamanyaskandhagataṃ  yathā skandhādgurutaraṃ bhāraṃ nṛṇāṃ duṣkṛtakāriṇām  Paus nidrakrāntasvapiṇḍāt vai yathā nirgatya pauṣkara vāsanādeham āśritya nānāceṣṭāṃ karoti ca  Paus bhūtapiṇḍaṃ vinā tāsāṃ na śāntim anuvindati evam annāśritaṃ pūrvaṃ prāṇam indriyasaṃgraham  Paus vyaktikṛtaṃ na vai deva haṃ dehabhāvena dehinām tāvat karmakṣayaṃ teṣāṃ kathameti mahāmate  Paus antastad upacārārthaṃ jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā saṃpādya yadvaśāt śīghram anantaṃ sukhamedhate  Paus sāmānyaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca gurvādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ sādhāraḥ saṃpradhānākhyaḥ sāṃprataṃ vidhiḥ ucyate  Paus nimantritaṃ vā saṃprāptaṃ nityam aṅgīkṛtaṃ tvatha dvijendraṃ pañjakālajñaṃ ṣaṭkarmanirataṃ tu vā  Paus snānādinā purā kṛtvā prayataḥ saṃviśet punaḥ svayam ardhyāmbunā vipra pavitrīkṛtya pāṇinā  Paus santāya kusumāstreṇa mantrāraścādhiṣṭhitena ca samuddharan netramantraṃ mantrārthādhiṣṭhitena ca  Paus samuccaran netramantram avalokya atha kadviti vāstviti  niveśya bhagavatyagre to gre praṇavādhiṣṭhitāsane  Paus pūjite vitate pūte saṃmukhaṃ vottarānanam udakdigkṣamāṇaṃ ca viniveśya tathā ca tat  Paus yathā mantreśadigraśmiprasareṇa abhividhyate mantreṇa ārādhya taṃ dhyātvā brūyāt saṃyatā ta vāgbhava  Paus samādhāya jagannāthra hṛtpadmagaganerkavat saptātrasyātha pātrāṇāṃ pātrābhyāṃ vābjasaṃbhava  Paus evaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhānaṃ prāg yatnenātra karmaṇi samuddiśya pitṝn dadyāt dānama mā ntaravedikam  Paus niveśitaṃ dvijendraṃ yad vṛttistham api mantrarāṭ antarvedī tu sā jñeyā tvābhyām abhyantaraṃ hi tat  Paus saṃpradānaṃ pitṝṇāṃ yat kuryāt satpātrapiṇḍakam tad divyam amalaṃ yasmāt caitanyam avalaṃbyate  Paus tatkālaṃ saṃvibhajyāśca tha tiṣṭhanti kamalodbhava pradātṛsaṅkalpavaśāt dattaṃ puṣkarasaṃbhava  Paus ekasya vā bahūnāṃ vā pradadyād āsanopari punarevāsanaṃ dābhamigranthi bahubhiḥ kuśaiḥ  Paus vibhoḥ yajñāṅgadehasya lomāni tu kuśāḥ smṛtāḥ tā eva nāyaḥ sarvā tasya bhūtaśarīragāḥ  Paus raśmayo bhūtadehe tu cinmūrteḥ śaktayo khilāḥ ata eva hi viprendra pitṝṇāṃ tu kuśāsanam  Paus śrāddhakāle tu vihitam āhūtānāṃ tadūrdhvataḥ yat kiṃcid dīyate bhaktayā brahmabhūtaṃ tu tadbhavet  Paus purā vai hetunānena nṛṇām aviditātmanām karmavyatra kuśājālaṃ vihitaṃ kamalodbhava  Paus yeṣāṃ sarvagataṃ brahman mantrarūpīśvaro cyutaḥ bhāvasthatatvatastābhisteṣāṃ vai na prayojanam  Paus athāścaparijaptena bhūtināvātmaśaṅkunā masṛṇenāśmacūrṇena parighāsu yathāthavā  Paus bahistadāsane kāryā tvagre dairghyācchamādhikā vaipulyācchamamānaṃ tu prāgvat pāvanatāṃ nayet  Paus nyaset tatrāpyabhagnāgrān udaṅmūlān kuśān dvija yasmād divyam udagbhāgaṃ pitryaṃ dakṣiṇasaṃjñakam  Paus svakenāmṛtavīryeṇa nityaṃ saṃvardhayanti ca darbhamārgacchatenaiva pitṝṇāṃ te marān dvija  Paus vasatyantaḥ pitṛgaṇo bhāgamāśritya dakṣiṇam citkalāṃśasvarūpeṇa nṛṇāmevaṃ hi cottare  Paus kṛtāspadāmalā nityā tvamṛtākhyākṣayā kalā ata evaṃ hi yatkiñcid ābrahmaviditaiḥ dvija  Paus pradīyate pitṝṇāṃ ca tat satyena tu pāṇinā ye dhikṛtya jagadyoniṃ mantrātmānamajaṃ harim  Paus prayacchanti pitṝṇāṃ ca toyatarpaṇapūrvakam teṣāṃ tadāśrayatvā yaduktaṃ nānakāraṇam  Paus kartavyasya ca pāramyaṃ prakṛtasya mahāmate sphuratyantargataṃ yeṣāṃ mantrārādhanapūrvakam  Paus tat svottaravaśādyeṣāṃ mantrasāṃmukhyadigvaśāt cetasā nirvikalpena kṛtaṃ bhavati cākṣayam  Paus kintu puṣkarasambhūta durlabhā bhuvi cetanāḥ iti cetasi vai yeṣāṃ niścayīkṛtya vartate  Paus satyatāmupanīye te tvevanyasye kuśācaye tilāṃstathāścajaptāśca tadūrdhve vikiret punaḥ  Paus kuruvindastu darbhāgrairyasmādetad dvayaṃ dvija sarvasya bhogajālasya janakaṃ bhuvanatraye  Paus viśeṣāt pitṛdevasya śraddhāpūtasya vastunaḥ agnīṣomasvarūpeṇa śāntyātmā bhagavāna svayam  Paus vyaktaḥ karmātmaka  ta tvānāṃ mūrtitvenātmasiddhaye sa pitryasya ca divyasya vyāpārasyātivaddhaye  Paus tattejastilabhāvena hlādo vartatyapātmanā ata evāprabuddhānāṃ prabuddhānāmapi dvija  Paus tilodakena bhāvaṃ tu gacchataḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi śrāddhasya ca parā rakṣā te dve nityamamārntraṇām  Paus tatsvarūpavidāṃ cai va viśeṣo mantravedinām nyastra strāṇyabhijaprāni tatra pātrāṇi vinyaset  Paus tatrādyaṃ cakavṛttāni hemādyutthāni  nya  saṃbhave pālāśakadalīpatratamālacchadanānyatha  Paus purānya strāmbuśaddhāni śubhaparṇamayāni ca pādayorapi pādyārthaṃ kaṃ kṣiped dakṣiṇāditaḥ  Paus āmūrdham arcayet paścād ardhyapuṣpānulepanaiḥ vastrastragdhūpadīpaiḥ tu dadhyannaṃ phalavādiṇā  Paus satāmbūlena vittena yathāśakti mahāmate samuddiśya pitṝn sarvān sanābhīyān yathākramam  Paus śabdabhāvasvarūpāstu jñavṛttisthānavigrahān bahutve sati viprāṇāṃ pitṛṇāmevamācaret  Paus yatra dvijadvayaṃ vipra pitrarthaṃ viniveśitam ekāsmin svapitṛṇāṃ tu tadā kāryaśca sannidhiḥ  Paus dvitīye jananīyānāṃ tathanyeṣāṃ tu saṃsthitim sarveṣāmekaprāptaṃ tu tṛpraye yadi yojitam  Paus omādyamasmacchabdaṃ tu pitṛbhyastadanantaram idam ardhyam idaṃ pādyaṃ tadante saṃsmaret svadhām  Paus sarvāsmin upacārānte vaṃ vā saṃsmaran naram namaḥ svadhāthavā brūyānnamontāṃ tvathavā svathavā svadhām  Paus evameva hi yaḥ kuryāt kartavyatvena pauṣkara tulyānāṃ ca svakulyānāṃ namastatra ca kevalam  Paus satyukte vyatyaye nityaṃ vihitaṃ ca svadhā dvija svayameva hi sanyāsī dadāti ca phalārthinām  Paus kāryastena namaskāraḥ svadhānte nityameva hi dadāti phalakāmastu yo nityaphalamārthinām  Paus svadhākārāvasāne tu hitaṃ tasya sadā namaḥ evam icchavaśenai va saṃvibhajya pitṝn dvija  Paus pṛṣṭvā pātramukhenaiva satṛptiṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ tato mbhaśculakaṃ pāṇau hranmantreṇāmṛtopamam  Paus dadyāt pūrṇendutulyaṃ taddhyātavyaṃ tatkalāḥ paḍhan sānusvāram akārādyairbhinnaṃ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ svaraiḥ  Paus tvaṅkārananiniṣṭaṃ ca tatra prākasthaḥ satārakam ityuktaṃ sakalasyendora vācakaṃ mantramabjaja  Paus pāṇiprakṣakanāt pūrvaṃ pātavyaṃ tena pūrvavat yenāmṛtapurāntastham annavīryam anaśvaram  Paus bhavatyāpyāyakṛd brahman pitṛdevagaṇasya ca māṣacūṇādinā pāṇiṃ prakṣālyāmaṇibandhanāt  Paus samācamyopasaṃhṛtya ūcchiṣṭaṃ tu yathāvidhi pavitrīkṛtya vasudhāṃ pāṇau kṛtvā tilodakam  Paus prīṇanaṃ bhagavatyagre samutthāyācaret tataḥ tavāstu bhagavan pūrvaḥ prītaḥ pitṛgaṇastathā  Paus śārīro devatāvyūha a  ā padā  dyo dyā vyavasthitaḥ evaṃ suvitate kuryāt karmatvārādhanālaye  Paus saṅkaṭe punaraanyatra yāyādabhyarcya mantrarāṭ sthānaṃ saṃskārasaṃśudhdaṃ kṛtvā prāktānādinā  Paus vyāptiśaktayāritaṃ bhūtastoyādhāragataṃ smaret manyamarcanapūrvaṃ tu tadagra sarvamācaret  Paus pātrāghrāṇapareṇaiva tatpātrasthena bhāvayet mādhuyuktena haviṣā darbhakāṇḍaistilaiḥ saha  Paus nirdeṣaṃ vahninā kṛtvā hṛdā darbhāgrakeṇa tu dhyātvā dhāma drumākāraṃ jñasvabhāvaṃ mahat prabham  Paus dravyadoṣagaṇa kṛtsnaṃ nirdahantaṃ samantataḥ devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ yat tṛptaye nnaṃ mahāmate  Paus tat sādhanaṃ ca vihitaṃ saṃskṛtena purānninā dvābhyāṃ deśikapūrvābhyāme tad viṣayam abjaja  Paus pradāpanamato nyeṣāṃ tatkālaṃ tasya vai hitam sadaiva vidhinānena tadarthaṃ śubhasiddhaye  Paus ekasyā śrayabījasya nānākarmavaśāt tu vai nānātvaṃ bhāvayed buddhayā pitṛkarmavyataḥ purā  Paus tenaiva tarpaṇīyaṃ tat svayaṃbhūtā tadātmanā matpravāhavadantastho bhāvayed annapātragau  Paus arhaṇāgrahagarbhau tu dvau darbhau tālasammitau hranmantramantritau kṛtvā tābhyāṃ saha samuddharet  Paus rasarūpasvabhāvaṃ tat stha  sthū latvenānnatāṃ gatam caturaṅgulamātraṃ tu grāsaṃ grāsaṃ mahāmate  Paus agnīṣomāśrayasthasya pūrvaṃ pitṛgaṇasya ca pitṝṇāṃ bījabhūtasya jñasvabhāvasya tattvataḥ  Paus daghāt piṇḍadvayaṃ cai va tvagnīṣomasamudbhavam nāḍīsvarūpau tau darbhau piṇḍena saha tatra vai  Paus layaṃ nītvā dvitīyena vyavahāradhiyāṃ  yā tataḥ pitṝṇāṃ kalpayet tena piṇḍānyanye   tne na sāṃpratam  Paus krameṇa prāgadṛṣṭānāṃ hradā saṃjñāpadena tu evaṃ dṛṣṭasvarūpaṃ ca jñātvā teṣāṃ sthitiṃ sphuram  Paus prāgvat svadhāvasānāghairmantrair oṃkārapūrvakaiḥ hranmantrālaṅkṛnairvipra tadā saṃjñāpadānvitaiḥ  Paus piṇḍaṃ prakalpayāmīti tataḥ pūrvavadācaret añjanābhyañjanādyaistu hyupacāraiḥ prapūjanam  Paus krameṇa tarpaṇaṃ kuryāt satilaiścā mbhasā tataḥ śirasā vanate  tau kṛtvā jānupādau kṣitau gatau  Paus pāṇiyugme lālārasthe ekacintaḥ paḍhed imam oṃ namo vaḥ pitaro namo vāḥ  vai puruṣottama  Paus namo viṣṇupadasthebhyaḥ svadhā vaḥ pitaro namaḥ haraye pitṛnāthāya hyagnīṣomātmane namaḥ  Paus satsomapātmane viṣṇo namo barhiṣadātmane āsaṃsārābhijanakā agniṣvāttā athācyuta  Paus pitāmahāḥ somapāstvaṃ tvamanye pratitāmahāḥ tubhyaṃ namo bhagavate pitṛmūrte nyutāya ca  Paus nārāyaṇāya haṃsāya viṣṇo tripuruṣātmane muttavā tvāmeva bhagavan na namāmi arcayāmi ca  Paus na tarpayāmi sarveśa nānyam āvāhayāmyaham stutvā evaṃ hi pitṛvyūhaṃ bhaktayā paramayā punaḥ  Paus saṃbhave sati sandhānaṃ piṇḍamūrteḥ samācaret tadagratopaviṣṭasya kramāt pitṛgaṇasya ca  Paus anusandhāya vai dvābhyām ekasmin vā dvijottama ūṣmāgrāvasthitaṃ dhyātvā pitrayaṃ pitṛgaṇaṃ kramāt  Paus praṇavena svarūpaṃ tu samutthāya tataḥ svayam madhyatiryaksthitau sthitvā hyadūraṃ nā nyadṛksthinaiḥ  Paus uttarābhimukhaiśca eva dakṣiṇasyāthavā dvija taduttarānanavaśād hranmantraṃ hradayān nyaset  Paus namo ntaṃ praṇavādyaṃ tu marudambaravigraham piṇḍāgre hyupaviṣṭasya prāṇaśakti   ktera dvijasya vā  Paus bahūnāṃ vā prayatnena svātantrān nirgato bahiḥ dhyātvā tayā saha kṣipramekībhūtatvamāgatam  Paus ātmaśaktau layaṃ nītvā yadi hyūṣmākhyalakṣaṇā kṛtvaivaṃ prāṇasaṅghaṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ vipravigrahe  Paus prāgvadāsanasaṃruddha bhojayet pūrvavat tataḥ oṃ namatvamṛtāyānnamidaṃ viṣṇupuraḥsarāḥ  Paus devā nadyastathā gāvaḥ sūryaḥ somo vanaspatiḥ oṃ mādhavo tha bhagavān mantramūrtimayo mahān  Paus madhubhāvena vo nyasmin sthitvā tṛptiṃ karotu vai anujjhitāsanaṃ kuryāt pitṝṇāṃ prīṇanāya ca  Paus tasminnevāsmi  n bhūbhāge vastvā tatpiṇḍavikṣitau   vīkṣite  sthitiḥ sarvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca sāṃprataṃ kamalāsana  Paus yāvat prāṇavimuktānāṃ piṇḍānāṃ nopasaṃhṛtiḥ socchiṣṭānāṃ kṛtā samyak tadante saṃvrajanti te  Paus svasthānāmāśiṣaṃ datvā śrāddhakarturdhiyā dvija sāmṛtaṃ sodakaṃ sthāne satilaṃ mantratejasā  Paus viviktaṃ vivṛtaṃ mārgaṃ punarāgamanāya ca nārāyaṇākhyasanmantrakarma brahmajavīkṛte  Paus sve svondriyarathe kṛtvā tṛptā yātācyutāspadam prājāpatyamidaṃ proktaṃ saṃpradāyasamanvitam  Paus saṃpradānaṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca pūrvoktaphalavardhanam samācaret sadā vyūhya mantrāṇāṃ mantrakarmaṇā  Paus nityaṃ bahutve dvitve vā prayogaṃ kamalodbhava yadyetadapyanaṅgaṃ ca tadā vai pratikarmaṇi  Paus hradādyaṅgāṅgato yojyamaṅgi pūrvavadabjaja ārādhyānāmamunetrāṇām oṃṅkāraḥ tatkriyāntare  Paus asminnarthe vikārastu ya ukto mantrapūrvakaḥ samayaḥ putrakādīnāmanyeṣāṃ bhāvitātmanām  Paus gurośca sādhakendrasya mantro mama mahāmate pradāne sa viruddhaśca tvato nyastvaviruddhakṛt  Paus samayī putrakādīnāṃ vaiṣṇavānāmapi dvija caturṇāṃ maugdalāntānāṃ tathaivāśramiṇā tu vai  Paus dīkṣayā saṃskṛtānāṃ ca dīkṣitānāṃ mahāmune sāmānyastvatha sarvatra sāṅgaḥ siddhaḥ supūjitaḥ  Paus teṣāṃ yaścopadeṣṭavyo mantravyūho hi taṃ śṛṇu sadvādaśākṣaro mantraḥ kavacaṃ brahmaṇe namaḥ  Paus evaṃ viśvātmane netramastraṃ ca paramātmane ete sapraṇavāḥ sarve śūdrāṇāṃ yogyatāvaśāt  Paus samyagvā dīkṣitānāṃ ca teṣāṃ vai praṇavojjhitāḥ vihitāca   śca yathā strīṇāṃ sadācāravaśāt tu vai  Paus asamyak pratipannānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ tu mahāmate na khaṇḍayet tu mantrāṇāṃ namaskāro bhavet punaḥ  Paus sajāterdvādaśārṇasya tadvadaṣṭākṣarasya ca ṣaḍakṣarasya vai pūrvaṃ prayojyaṃ pūraṇārthataḥ  Paus yadā tvabhihito ṣṭārṇe tvaṣṭārṇena avatāritaḥ mukhyatā dvādaśārṇasya mantrasya vihitā tadā  Paus ṣaḍakṣarasya mukhyatvaṃ bhavedubhāvavaśād api yojyasvaṣṭākṣaro mantro nityameva śikhāvadhau  Paus praṇavasya ca mukhyatvaṃ dviṣaḍaṣṭaṣaḍakṣarāḥ mantrā hṛdayapūrvāstu parijñeyāstataḥ kramāt  Paus mantrāṇāṃ varmapūrvāṇāṃ vācyatvaṃ yadi kalpyate tadātmatā ca vihitā tatsthāne praṇavasya ca  Paus devo jitaṃtāmantreṇa cittasthaḥ sannidhīkṛtaḥ yoktavyaṃ tatra ca aṅgānāṃ mantraṣaṭkaṃ yathā sthitam  Paus dvādaśākṣarapūrvaṃ tu tṛtīyaṃ yat prakīrtitam tṛtīyaṃ brahmapūrvaṃ tu dharmādīnāṃ hi vācakam  Paus praṇavaḥ sarvamantrāṇāmitaśca āsanakarmaṇi dvādaśākṣarapūrvāṇāṃ mantrasāmānyakarmaṇām  Paus darbhātilodakādīnāṃ dravyāṇāṃ pratikarmaṇi jāyate ca visṛṣṭānāmvupaśāntiśca taijasī  Paus ata evopayuktānāṃ bhogānāṃ kamalodbhava viruddhasaṃgraho bhūyastvanyāsmin hi kriyāntare  Paus gauṇī vyaktiḥ yatasteṣāmāmūlāccidādhiṣṭhitā vartate paramāśritya tat kartuḥ phalasiddhaye  Paus citsāmānyavinirmuktā hyayomyāste śarīravat mantrāṇāṃ sthāyino bhāgā yānti vai yogyatāṃ punaḥ  Paus kadācinmantrasāmarthyāt jñānabhāvanayā dvija iti nityaśrāddhavidhiḥ  atha naimittikaśrāddhavidhiḥ naimittakamataḥ śrāddhavidhānamavadhāraya gatipradaṃ pitṝṇāṃ yat karmaṇāṃ siddhibhūridam  Paus sadyaḥ satpātrasaṃprāptiṃ vinā naiva samācaret evamādyairvinirmuktaṃ śrāddhamabjasamudbhava  Paus tiṣṭhatyanugrahārthaṃ ca yadi saṃprārthitaṃ hi yat tadā niyamamātiṣṭhedagnikāṣṭhād anādikam  Paus mānamātsaryakārpavyakrodhalobhādayo khilāḥ doṣā dūratare tyājyā hyāniṣpattidināvadhi  Paus śuddhipūrveṇa vidhinā suprayatnena cetasā pradattaṃ phalamūlādyaṃ bhavet tadamṛtādhikam  Paus deśapātravaśenaiva saṃpatto sati padmaja ekāhāt saptarātraṃ tu śraddhayā tat samācaret  Paus samāśritya śubhaṃ kālamekāhaṃ kamalodbhava nirvartya parayā prītyā naiti kālaṃ yathānyathā  Paus trayamāśritya te śrāddhaṃ sānukampena cetasā satvasthena kṛtaṃ śaktyā śuddhena draviṇena ca  Paus nayatyavaśyamacirāt satyalokaṃ tadarthitam deśakālakṛtaṃ tvetat tapolokaṃ dadāti ca  Paus deśapātrāśritu śrāddhaṃ jana  no lokaṃ dadāti ca phalaṃ maharlokagati kālapātravaśāt kṛtam  Paus kevalaṃ deśamāsādya dattaṃ svargaṃ prayacchati kṛtaṃ yat kālamaśritya bhuvarlokaṃ  kā dvijayāte  Paus saumyapātrāśritaṃ śrāddhaṃ tadbhūlokagatipradam sāmānyasya ca deśādestritayasya phalaṃ tvidam  Paus tatra puṣkara puṣṭiṃ hi prasiddhaṃ dehamabjaja kālaṃ grāhyoparāgādyaṃ pātraṃ tanmayamabjaja  Paus tathā niyamavān samyak śrāddhahetorna cānyathā yaduktaṃ tritayaṃ śrāddhe saviśeṣaṃ hi tat punaḥ  Paus bhavatyutārakaṃ nṝṇāṃ savijñānena janmanā prasiddhayā vaiṣṇavaṃ deśaṃ pātrastradbhgavanmayā  yaḥ   Paus dvādaśyākhyo bṛhatkālaḥ saṅkāntyādyaiḥ pariṣkṛtaḥ trayametanmahābuddhe saviśeṣataraṃ yadi  Paus bhavatyuttārakaṃ nūnaṃ dehāntaranivāsinām svayaṃvyaktena vibhunā tvekamūrtyādinābjaja  Paus adhiṣṭhitaṃ hi sargādāvekadeśāt sahāmbunā tadviśeṣāntaraṃ deśaṃ siddhikṛt sarvakarmaṇām  Paus tasmin dvijocite kāle dvādaśyākhye bhavedyadi samuhūrtaṃ sanakṣatraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tena tadbhavet  Paus prottārakaṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca savyabāhusamanvitam samyaksiddhitrayopetaṃ pañcakālaparāyaṇam  Paus labdhalakṣaṃ pare tattve pātramekāyanaṃ dvija   jaṃ  saṃyamādyairupetaṃ ca tanmahārthāyanāttu vai  Paus pitṛṇāṃ sugatiprāptiḥ śaśvadeva hi jāyate vetaṃ  gaṃ  ca taṃ mahāvegāttulyavegaṃ hijāyate  Paus deśe śubhe śubhaṃ janma jñānasatkarmaṇā saha phalaṃ śubhatarān bhinnān pitṝṇāṃ tritayāt kramāt  Paus jñātvaivaṃ śrāddhadāne tu deśakālādayo guṇāḥ cittaśuddhisametāśca samāsannāḥ prasannataḥ  Paus etadastrādinā sarvamupakāraṃ hi karmaṇām kevalaṃ bhaktipūtānāṃ lokadharmaratātmanām  Paus jñānakarmaratānāṃ ca dvijānāmadhikāriṇām pañcakālaratānāṃ ca svakarmavyabjasaṃbhava  Paus yānti vyāghāramantreṇa parikrāmyena vai tataḥ  prabandhabrahmavarṇatvaṃ teṣāṃ tadbhagavān hariḥ  Paus ṣāḍguṇyavigraho devaḥ prabhavāpyayakṛt svayam guṇamuktasamūhena svarūpādacyutena ca  Paus kālādīnāṃ samutthānaṃ ṣāḍguvyād ata eva hi na vindanti paratvena te cānyasyācyutaṃ vinā  Paus kālādeḥ sūkṣmabhūtasya tvāśrayasyāmalasya ca ato nayadbhagavadbhaktāstanmantrajñānatatparāḥ  Paus teṣāṃ kamalasaṃbhūta kālādyamakhilaṃ hi yat sarvam antaḥsthitaṃ bhāti tatprabhāvavaśāt sphuṭam  Paus bahirantaravaścāpi yasmādetadadhīśvarāt viśvasya cāpi dehatvaṃ purā te saṃprakāśitam  Paus adhvopadeśadvāreṇa vistareṇa tadeva hi dehajñaṃ satkriyāniṣṭhaṃ jñāninaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ sthiram  Paus icchantyutārakaṃ śuddhaṃ pitaraḥ svakule pumān deśakālādayastvevamaśritya prayataḥ svayam  Paus nistuṣairujjvalaiḥ śuddhaiḥ sakṣīraid abjasaṃbhava savdyañjanasamopetaṃ saṃsādya śraddhayā purā  Paus hṛdā vā dvādaśārṇena bhāṇḍeṣvabhinaveṣu vai vinirgateṣu vā pākād bhūyaḥ snehokṣiteṣvatha  Paus evaṃ vā sādhanīyaṃ ca putraśiṣyātmanā dvija bhaginyā dharmasā pantyā  patnyā vā suhṛtsambandhavartmanā  Paus śuklāṃbaradhareṇaiva dakṣeṇa śucinātmanā śārīravyādhihīnena kṣuttṛṣṇāvigatena ca  Paus kāsaśvāsa  svabhāvātha dṛkśrutihīnakharvaṭaiḥ evaṃ vimuktādoṣeṇa bhāvabhaktipareṇa ca  Paus saṃsādhanīyaṃ śrāddhārthaṃ svajātīyena vai caruḥ anulomena vihitaṃ varṇānāṃ carusādhanam  Paus divye pitraye bjasaṃbhūta pratilomaśca doṣakṛt tadalābhāt krayakrītamaduṣṭaṃ kārukā  kaṃ śucim  ci   Paus pūrvoktādośanirmuktaṃ tenāpi kamalodbhava apikṣayavidhūnā vā  nānāṃ lausyaikaniratātmanām  Paus rajasvalānāṃ ṣaṇḍānāṃ ṛtvādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ śvānasūkaramārjāramarkaṭānāṃ tathaiva hi  Paus viḍvarāhaśivāgṛdhrapūrvāṇāṃ tu svacāriṇām tasmāt sarvaprayatnena nivātasthagitāmbare  Paus niḥśasye kuṭṭime bhūyaḥ sulipte dhavalīkṛte sthāne mantrārcanaṃ devapitṛdevasya sādhanam  Paus vihitaṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ saṃbhave sati sarvadā annavyañjanabhāṇḍānāṃ sarveṣāṃ kramaśo dvija  Paus antaścārambhakālo tu madhvājyaiḥ sakuśāstilāḥ kṣeptavyā dvādaśārṇena bhūyaḥ siddhena saṃgrahe  Paus aṣṭārṇenātha vastreṇa sthagayet tān prayatnataḥ yathā na bahiranyotthaṃ bāṣpaṃ niryāti padmaja  Paus ūrdhvapuṇḍre kṛte lipte kṣālite stha  sthā likācaye varmaṇā vāsasā cchanne maryādābhyantarīkṛte  Paus rakṣapālaṃ ca tatpaṅktau datvā snānādyamācaret agnervipramavāsānāṃ pūjāsthānasya pauṣkara  Paus bhāṇḍānāṃ bhāgapūrvāṇāṃ satsahāyagaṇasya ca viniyogaṃ purā kṛtvā pūrṇāntaṃ nityamācaret  Paus apā nāt pratiśāṭakam tasyādhaḥ śāṭikāyāṃ tu vidhūyāt tanuveṣṭanam  Paus adhūtaṃ vimalaṃ svacchaṃvisūtraṃvalkalīdikam nīlāñcitaṃ ca catkiṃcidvidyate cāmbarādikam  Paus sarvatra viṣayāṃ caivatvapāsya bhuvanādbahiḥ tato dhiyābhisandhāya mantramūrtigataṃ param  Paus yajāmyanugrahārthaṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ punareva hi niveśya prāgvadāhūya hyāsaneṣu kramād dvijān  Paus tebhyaḥ prāgānanau pūrvaṃ niveśyau dvau dvijottamau dvādaśāro dharo dhāma tritayādhiṣṭhitāsane  Paus athoktān sarvasāmānyān ṣaḍaṅgā dvijavāsvarāḥ  astramantraśikhāyuktaḥ kramādbi  ṣaḍanvitam  Paus niyojya prāṅmukhasthābhyāṃ dehatādātmyatāptaye svavācakena saddhāmno hyekamūrtyādikātmanā  Paus nyastavyaṃ devatāvyūhaṃ phaḍvauṣaṭkārasaṃyutam nṛsiṃhākhyaṃ savārāhaṃ mantramūrtidvayaṃ hi yat  Paus agnīṣomākhyadaivatyaṃ rakṣārthaṃ sarvadaiva hi avīkṣayannudagbhāga ato nye viniveśya ca  Paus tatrādau hṛdayadīnāmadhaḥpaṅktau niveśya ca dṛśā sadvarṇajānāṃ tu saṅghānāmevameva hi  Paus tasya dakṣiṇataścordhve jananīyakulasya ca kavacenāparaṃ yojyamekāntaṃ bhagavanmayam  Paus pitṛnāmnādvitīyaṃca tasya dakṣiṇatastataḥ tṛtīyamāptikārī ca caturthaṃ hṛdayena tu  Paus pitāmahābhidhānena mūrtimantreṇa pañcamam pratitāmahanāmnā vai yojyamekāyanaṃ dvija  Paus janake jīvabhāvena tadatītatrayaṃ kramāt niveśanīyaṃ tairmantrairvartate ca dvayaṃ kramāt  Paus pratitāmahapūrvaṃ tu samatītatrayaṃ nyaset sāmānyena ṣaḍaṅgena tvevamuktaṃ svakena vā  Paus mantreṇa śrāddhadāne tu viniyogaṃ dvijārcane caturmūrtādhikāreṇa dvidhāvasthamathocyate  Paus sabhogamapavargaṃ ca mantraikasmādavāpyate kaivalyaṃ kevalaṃ caiva dvitīyādamalekṣaṇa  Paus sasuhṛnmantravargasya nyasedavyaktamantrarāṭ trayāṇāṃ vāsudevāntaṃ pradyumnādyamataḥ kramāt  Paus na tadvai saviśeṣaṃ ca punarevacame śṛṇu suhṛtprapūrvamiśrāṇāmaniruddhaṃ hi vācakam  Paus pradyumnamantravargasya kāmād dvābhyāṃ dvayaṃ tataḥ praṇavena paraṃ brahmasvarūpaṃ pratitāmaham  Paus maha tā tanmu dāptamukhenaiva tarpaṇaṃ yanmahāmate navamūrtyadhikāreṇa triprakāramathocyate  Paus samitrāṇāṃ ca vātsalyād dvijānāṃ viṣṇunā nyaset tato vairājamantreṇa mātṛvargasya pauṣkara  Paus tribhirnārāyaṇadyaistu pitrādīnāṃ trayaṃ kramāt viddhi viddhā  dyā khyametaddhi śrāddhajñānaṃ phalapradam  Paus pitṝṇā yajamānasya dehalābhe  bhān  vinaiva hi vairājamantrādārabhya sāṅkarṣaṇāntamabjaja  Paus samantrapañcakaṃ viddhi  pratitāmahaniṣṭhānāṃ yatacchrāddhaṃ hi pauṣkara  Paus prayacchatyātmalābhaṃ tu śrāddhakartuḥ pitṛṣvapi ādhārāṇāṃ mantrādvai   Paus niyojanaṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ pañcānāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi mitravargāt samārabhya parametaddhi vaśvaram  Paus sāmagrībhiḥ samopetaṃ kartuḥ pitṛgaṇasya ca paraṃ yacchati nirvāṇaṃ sakṛtsnaṃ ca kiṃ punaḥ  Paus kālamājīvitaṃ vipra śraddhāpūtena cetasā kṛpayā ca samānānāṃ saṃbhave sati pauṣkara  Paus kāmye smiñśrāddhadāne tu paṅktayā nānyatra yojayet samūhamekaṃ pūrvaṃ tu viprāṇāmuttarānanam  Paus hṛnmantreṇābjasaṃbhūta sarveṣāṃ vinyaset tataḥ praṇavena svanāmnā ca jñāta hṛdādiṣu  Paus astrabhūṣaṇahetīśa pūrvamantrān sagocare evaṃ vā prāṅmukhaṃ śaktayā cakramantreṇa yojayet  Paus vipramekamudagvakraṃ  ktraṃ mukhyamantreṇa yojayet dvayaṃ codaṅmukhaṃ tatra hranmantreṇānusandhya ca  Paus suhṛmnitraṃ dvivetaṃ jetaṃ tu mātṛvaṃśamathābjaja pitṛvaṃśaṃ hi niḥśeṣaṃ smaredaparadehagam  Paus maṇḍale tvambupātrastha cakraṃ vā nṛhariṃ yajet vipramekamudagvaktraṃ mukhyamantreṇa vinyaset  Paus tṛptaye pitṛvargasya yathā mātṛkulasya ca sarvaṃ janamāto nyeṣāṃ prītaye ca svaśaktitaḥ  Paus gavā grāsaṃ samuddhṛtya dadyād ghṛtamadhuplutam darbhaistilodakairmiśraṃ na kṣāraṃ lavaṇotkaṭam  Paus ātmavaṃśādhikāreṇa karyādevamato nyathā paurohityena kṛpayā prītyā vānyasya kasya cita  Paus nirvartane tadīyaṃ hi tatpūrvaṃ vihitaṃ kulam āpādājjānuparyantamājānormadhyamasta  bāsti kam  Paus āvastimūrdhno hṛdayamāhṛdo masatakāvadhi aniruddhādayo mantrāścatvāro viniveśya ca  Paus sugatiprāptaye vipra pitṝṇāṃ nityameva hi tṛptaye vāsudevādyādāmūrdhnastvaṅ ghrigācaram  Paus catvāraścāniruddhānto yoktavyā vā mahāmate praṇavena hṛdi brahman śāntaṃ saṃvinmayaṃ tu vā  Paus samīśanalatoyakṣmābhūtānāṃ vya  vyā pakaṃ kramāt nyastavyaṃ vāsudevādyamadhyakṣāntaṃ catuṣṭayam  Paus apekṣayāniruddhādyaṃ pṛthivyādicaturṣvatha rakṣārthaṃ nṛhariṃ nyastvā navamūrteḥ paraṃ dvija  Paus mūrdhāsyakaṇṭhahṛnnābhiguhyajānudveya tvatha pādayoḥ kṣmādharāntaṃ tu nyastavyaṃ tvaṣṭakaṃ kramāt  Paus hṛdambare tu bhagavān vāsudevo pyadhokṣajaḥ kṣmāntānāṃ buddhipūrvāṇāṃ kramāt saṅkarṣaṇādikam  Paus yā  yo ktavyamathavā vipra pṛthivyādikrameṇa tu saptakaṃ bhūdharākhyaṃ tu saṅkarṣaṇāntameva hi  Paus atha ciddhṛtvadhiṣṭhāne vāsudevaṃ tu bhāvayet rasalohitamāṃsānāṃ medomajjāsthiṣu dvija  Paus krameṇa śukladhātvantaṃ nyaset saṅkarṣaṇādikam saptakaṃ ca varāhāntamāśuklād dvārasiddhaye  Paus varāhamantrādāramya saṅkarṣaṇāntamabjaja evaṃ duṣṭanirāsārthaṃ pūrvavat pātrakaṃ nyaset  Paus vyāpakatvena bhagavān bahirabhyantare svavat jīvavat sāṅkarṣaṇaṃ ca bījaṃ hṛtkamalodare  Paus sṛṣṭisaṃhārayogena saptakaṃ dhātusaptake pauṣkara uvācasāmānyena svamantreṇa sati sannihitena vai kārayorvigrahe vṛttau jvālantābhyantare yathātu vā  Paus nyāsārcanādimuktānāṃ mantrāṇāṃ yujyate katham viniyogaṃ caturṇāṃ vā navānāṃ mantrakarmaṇi  Paus śrībhagavānuvācasaṣaḍaṅgo hi sāmānyaḥ sarveṣāṃ vihitaḥ sadā sādhakasya hi mantro hi viṣamaḥ syādvirodhakṛt  Paus anujñātaḥ sasarvasya cāturātmyādikaṃ hi yat guroricchā svakīyātra svamantrādau mahāmate  Paus tatrāpi hi viśeṣāya śrāddhe dvābhyāṃ sa ucyate mantragrāme tu vinyaste viprāṇāmicchayā purā  Paus svamantramupasaṃhṛtya svadhāmnā ca dhiyā satā brahmabhāvanayā vyāpta evaṃ kṛtvāśrayādikam  Paus yadvipravigrahe vyastaṃ mantravyūhaṃ tadātmani athāniyojanīyaṃ ca kṣantu tatpāṇipūrvakam  Paus tatrāyaṃ   tredaṃ vihitaṃ vipra viśeṣaṃ tannibodhatu vyāpakatvena bhagavān prāk savyetarayostataḥ  Paus dakṣiṇe karaśākhāsu dvitīyaṃ pañcasunyaset tadandvā  dvā me tṛtīyaṃ hi tvaṅguṣṭhādikrameṇa tu  Paus taladvaye dakṣiṇādāvaniruddhamato nyaset ekaṃ vā vāsudevāntaṃ nyasedicchāvaśena tu  Paus yadā navātmā karayostadaṅguṣṭhadvaye cyutaḥ aṣṭhakaṃ ca varāhantaṃ prāgvadātarjaneḥ kramāt  Paus vāmatarjana  ni niṣṭhaṃ tu vāsudevāntameva vā svāhāmadhyoditaṃ kṛtvā pūjāsāre tathā  cene nale  Paus hutamapyanalaṃ bhūtaṃ prāgvat pāva  na katāṃ nayet evamicchāvaśenaiva mantrāṇāṃ parivartanam  Paus svārādhyā navaniṣṭhānāṃ śrāddhakāle virodhakṛt evaṃ niyojanaṃ kṛtvā śirasābhyarcya sāṃpratam  Paus sāsanaṃ puṣpapātreṇa samūhaṃ bhagavanmayam tanmadhyembhaścalaṃ cittaṃ pañcendriyasamanvitam  Paus kuryāttāṃma tanma ntrapīṭhasthaṃ madhye pāre thavā hṛdi kālamācamanāntarṃ  thaṃ tu madanugrahakāmyayā  Paus sannidhāne dvijānāṃ ca vibhoḥ sajvalanasya ca bhāvyaṃ suyantritenaiva sarvajñenāpi jantunā  Paus evaṃ bhūtaiḥ dvijendraistu  staiḥ buddhayā tu suviśaddhayā śraddheyamakhilaṃ tasya sānukampena cetasā  Paus yasmādabjasamudbhūta mānaṃ yadubhayātmakam nāsakṛt sarvabhāvānāṃ viśeṣācchrāddhakarmaṇi  Paus samayetasyayojyaṃ tat pūraṇa  ṇaṃ sarvakarmaṇām pāvanaṃ tṛptijananaṃ kiṃ punaḥ pitṛkarmaṇi  Paus ādāya manasā māntrīmājñāṃ vai śirasā saha hārdamāpādya vai śrāddhaṃ dravyotthaṃ yadvaśād dvija  Paus saphalaṃ syāt pitṝṇāṃ tu jñānamūlaṃ hi tattvataḥ anyathā hetunā kena pitṝṇāṃ tadgatipadam  Paus mūlaṃ vinā kṣmāṃ nābhyeti pādapānāṃ yathā tathā jñānamāhlādapūrveṇa phalatyāśu ca vartmanā  Paus kāraṇaṃ sarvendriyāgrāmaṃ bahirvṛttigataṃ hi yat svayamātmani saṃlīnaṃ kṛtvā hṛtkamalāmbare  Paus svabhāvaśaktyā saṃpūrya samāste sāṃprataṃ tu tat svarūpād vandanaṃ kuryādvibhoḥ sarveśvarasya ca  Paus śāntasaṃvitsvarūpasya spandānandamayātmanaḥ tāvacyutaṃ hi cit spandaṃ svayaṃ pariṇataṃ smaret  Paus sahastraśaśisūryāgniprabhayā projvalaṃ sthiram marīcicakrasaṃpūrṇacidgarbhaṃ sarvatomukham  Paus cidambarāntarāvasthaṃ suśāntaṃ bhagavatpadam tacchakti  taccitra jñānanāḍervai vilakṣaṇataraṃ hi yat  Paus smarenmarīcikoṇasthaṃ svabhāvāhlādapiṇḍakam svakaṃ pitṛsamūhaṃ tu sphurantaṃ karmaśāntaye  Paus mahataḥ pāvakādyadvacchaktirdahanalakṣaṇā aṅgārakaṇamāśritya bāhyamāyāti pauṣkara  Paus tadvadeva hi niryātaḥ kintu saṅkspaniścayāt agnīṣomau samāśritya pitaraśceśvarecchayā  Paus prakāśamantrarāḍbāhyaṃ evam ekatvam āpannāḥ saha mantreṇa tena te  tāḥ  śaśāṅkaśatasaṅkāśam atha mantreśvaraṃ harim  Paus nirastāvayavaṃ dhyātvā śaktayastatatra vaiṣṭarāḥ pitṛvyūhavad ālīnaṃ kṛtvā tadanu mantrarāṭ  Paus ātmasāt pitṛmārgeṇa tatra tenodakena ca visṛ  mṛ  jya nayane bhūyaḥ sapatnīko dṛśābjaja  Paus jalāyaiva ca nikṣipya prāgdattaṃ saha vāriṇā kṣā   śā  ntānalagataṃ devaṃ samāsādyārcanālayam  Paus mantreśam arcayitvā ca pūrvavat prīṇayed dvija tatastadupahāra  raṃ kṛtvā bhojanam ācaret  Paus bāndhavaiḥ saha mantreśaṃ dhyāyan hṛtpuṣkarodare yatavāg amṛtaprakhyairgrāsaiḥ tadanu pauṣkara  Paus nirucchiṣṭe tu bhūbhāge kṛte saṃkṣālane tataḥ so  sau danaṃ vyañjanīyaṃ yadduḥkhāyad darbhāpūtaṃ ca pāṇinā   Paus tamāhṛtyāparasmin vai pātre darbhatilānvite kṣiped dīpadvitīyaṃ tadbahirvai dakṣiṇena ca  Paus smaranmantraṃ śucau deśe datvā darbhāstaraṃ tataḥ nayed dharmakathābhistu yogya  gābhyāsena vāniśām   Paus ityevaṃ vidhināṃ śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vihitaṃ dvija saṃsāraduḥkhaśamanam acirād apavargadam  Paus kṛtam ekaprakāraṃ ca śraddhayā cobhayātmakam datvā jñānakriyānata   yāṃ yācopayujyate  Paus lokadharmasthitā sā saṃpūraṇe yāti vāsanām tasmāccitraprasādaṃ vai jāyate yena karmaṇā  Paus ācartavyaṃ prayatnena mantrajairvitatāptaye athamanasaḥsaṃskāraṃ saṃpannānāṃ samācaret  Paus aurdhvadehikasaṃjñaṃ tu vyāpāraṃ samanantaram pūrvoktaphalasiddhayarthaṃ tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu  Paus taccāpi dviguṇaṃ viddhi dvividhaṃ prathamaṃ kamalodbhava sā  ḥsu dīkṣitānāṃ sarveṣāṃ muktānāmamṛtādikai  Paus vyaktādivṛttisthāneṣu hitaṃ nityaṃ tameva hi prāgvad ārādhite mantre śraddhayā Paus jvaladavyaktabījāntaṃ niviṣṭhaṃ vartate tataḥ saumyavṛtti sasūkṣmaṃśca prāṇaśaktiparaṃśca san  Paus tad daśāṃśaṃ hi vai kālaṃ bāhyaṃ ca dinalakṣaṇam samāśritya krameṇaiva kartā tadanukalpavān  Paus tatprāṇāṃśānuviddhā  ddhaṃ ca vyaktam indriyalakṣaṇam āpādayati cāvyaktād annamūrticchalena tu  Paus śrotrendriyādikāścaiva upasthendriyapaścimāḥ yamāśritya labhetāśu samatīte daśāhike  Paus ekādaśe hni viprendra asmin śaktitvameva hi trayāstriṃśāhikenaiva brahman vyaktareṇa tu  Paus vināḍi satyapūrveṇa tatprāṇāṃśena vai punaḥ dviṣaṭkalakṣaṇenaiva śeṣaṃ tattvagaṇaṃ dvija  Paus Paus samācamya hṛdā nyasya mūlaṃ pāṇitale tataḥ āmūrdhayātha  mūrdhno tha tenaiva sakapalīkṛtya vigraham  Paus saṃkṣepeṇa niraṅgeṇa tato hṛnmantramantritāḥ sagotravihitaṃ vipra pretānugrahakāmyayā madhye madhye saṃsāramārgavat  Paus brahmanāḍīsvarūpaṃ tu dhyātavyam amalaṃ mahat kalpanālakṣaṇe bāhye vartma sadvastu vinyaset  Paus saṃśāntakarmabrahmabhyām anyonyasya tu vedane nam  gavākṣavat ādhārāsanapūrvāṇāṃ mantrāṇāṃ sarvakarmaṇām  Paus haṃsoparamaniṣṭhānāṃ siddhaye bhāvitātmanām na tatrāntaṃ sthitiṃ   nta saṃsthitaṃ kuryānmantranyāsaṃ yathāvidhi  Paus upaviśyāsane dārbhe praṇavavyāptibhāvite mūlamantreṇa niṣpādya prāṇāyāmaṃ trilakṣaṇam  Paus dhāraṇādvitayenātha dehasaṃskāram ācaret mantranyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt pūrvavat karadehayoḥ  Paus arghyaṃ pādyaṃ samāsādya prokṣayet punaḥ punaḥ madhvājyatilagokṣīrayuktaṃ mūlena nikṣipet  Paus darvyārastramantranyastāyā śrapayed hṛdayena tu siddham uttārayet paścānmūlamantreṇa mantravit  Paus prakṣālyālipya netreṇa śikhāmantreṇa  Paus nyastamantraṃ hṛdā kṛtvā tvarghyādyair arcayet tataḥ yāyād ārādhanoddeśam upaviśya yathāsukham  Paus hṛdā tam indriye dhyāyet svaśaktyā mūrtatāṃ gatam rasātmanānnaśaktau tu vibhāgena ca sthitam  Paus dhyātavyaṃ pūrvavat pretaṃ smartavyaṃ praṇavena tu annādhiṣṭhātṛbhāvena nītvā ca pratipadya ca  Paus dvijendrasya ca mantrāntaṃ saha cārghyodakena tu atha tatprāṇaśaktau tu hṛdā vaikātmatāṃ gatam  Paus naivedyaṃ ga narantastaṃ   gaganāntastaṃ pretaṃ kamalasambhava tatastad hṛdayākāśaṃ prāṇena saha vai kramāt  Paus vyaktaye śrautravṛttau tu prayātam anubhāvayet evaṃ labdhātmakaṃ kṛtvā pretaṃ Paus praṇavaṃ mūlamantreṇa pretaṃ sarvatra saṃsmaret evaṃ prāptāsmitaṃ samyagyuktam indriyaśaktibhiḥ  Paus buddhipūrvairdharāntaistu kṛtvaitam anurañjayet budhyārtham ācaret tatra śikhāmantreṇa  Paus pretam āpādya vai piṇḍaṃ prāpte māse trayodaśe yojanā pitṛmārge tu kāryāsya bhagavanmaye  Paus yathā tathābjasaṃbhūta śṛṇu me gadataḥ sphaṭam snānaṃ pūrve samākhyātaṃ paścāttadanu sādhayet  Paus Paus sammukhān mantranāthasya catvāro vāpyudaṅmukhan evaṃ pūrvānane dve tu viniveśya dvijottama  Paus tayorekasya cāstreṇa sakalīkaraṇaṃ hi yat varmaṇātha dvitīyasya nyāsakarma vidhīyate  Paus prabhṛti tasya vai  Paus pitṛtvaṃ vātsare śrāddhe kāladiṣṭeviśeṣataḥ bhrātretareṣāṃ mṛtānāṃ ca vihitā vatsare gate  Paus nānyeṣāṃ dvijaśārdūla pitṝṇāṃ śrāddhakāṅkṣiṇām pretatvamupaśānta vai jantorvāgrasthitasya ca  Paus pitṛtvaṃ labdha saṃskāraṃsaṃsthitaṃ cottarottaram evamuktaṃ hi sāṅgena mantreṇa kamalodbhava  Paus aurdhvadaihikasaṃjñaṃ tu vidhānaṃ bhāvināmatha caturbhiścāturātmīyairmantraistadvinibodha me  Paus śrotrādyupasthaparyantam indriyāṇāṃ dvipañcakam āpādya vāsudevākhyaṃ mantreṇa daśabhirdinaiḥ  Paus asmin vyaktimataḥ kuryāt sāṅkarṣaṇena pauṣkara buddhitattve tṛtīyena vā vyañjayenmanasā saha  Paus kṣmāntam ākāśatanmātrād aniruddhena pauṣkara pūrvavad vyañjanīyaṃ ca evaṃ saṃvatsare gate  Paus sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kuryād aniruddhāditaḥ kramāt caturbhirvāsudevāntairmantrairmantravidāṃ vara  Paus evam icchennavātmajñaḥ samūrtinavakena yat saṃvidhānaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha bāndhavānāṃ śubhāptaye  Paus tadidānīṃ samāsena ekāgram avadhāraya śrotrādīnām indriyāṇāṃ tṛptaye kṣmādharaṃ smṛtam  Paus bhūgā  myā  dīnāṃ nṛsiṃhaṃ tu asmin śaktau khagāsane vyaktaye brahmatattvaṃ tu buddhe samanasāṃ hitam  Paus tanmātrāṇāṃ sabhūtānāṃ mantrāṇāṃ dhāraṇātmakam evaṃ tattvakalāyuktaṃ japaṃ kṛtvā mahāmate  Paus pañcabhistu varāhādyaiḥ tataḥ saṃvatsare gate caturbhir aniruddhādyaiḥ pitṛbhāvanam ānayet  Paus pūrvoktena vidhānena jñānadhyānānvitena ca divyenānaśvareṇaiva karmaṇānekasādhanam  Paus saṃvidhānaṃ dvitīyaṃ tatproktaṃ saṃsūcitaṃ mayā tanme sphuṭataraṃ kṛsvā gadataścāvadhāraya  Paus sarvaṃ pūrvoditaṃ kṛtvā vidhānaṃ sādhane caroḥ prajvālya pāvakaṃ kuryāt prāgvatsaṃskārasaṃskṛtam  Paus dhyātvā tadantarmantreśaṃ samidbhiktarpayet kramāt tadagrato dakṣiṇāgrān kuśān āstīrya pūrvavat  Paus savāsam āsanaṃ dhyātvā tadūrdhve kamalāsanam yuktam ādyādikaiḥ prāgvad vinyased annagolakam  Paus tasmin pūrvoditaṃ sarvam āpādya tadanantaram pretanāmnā tadagre tha satilānudakāñjalīn  Paus dattvātha copasaṃhṛtya vinikṣapya jalāntare kṛtvātha saha mantreṇa ātmasādasanaṃ  dadanaṃ dvija  Paus jale khilaṃ samāhṛtya vinikṣipyānalaṃ vinā daśāhamevaṃ niṣpādya prāgvadekādaśe hani  Paus śrāddhaṃ kuryād vidhānajñaḥ piṇḍadānapurassaram saṃvatsare tha niṣpanne pitṛtvāpādanāya ca  Paus dhyānaṃ samantraṃ pūrvoktaṃtatpitṛtvādhikaṃ bhavet bhāsvajjvalanasaṃkāśaṃ samarthaikatvamāgatam  Paus tadadhyakṣatvabhūtaṃ yanmantramadhyātmalakṣaṇam adhibhūtam athāpannaṃ piṇḍaṃ nirgatya saṃsmaret  Paus tadūrdhvadeśe nabhasi vyāpāraṃ sannirīkṣayet evam annātpṛthaṅnīte viprete kamalodbhava  Paus tanmantreṇa ca tatpiṇḍād adhibhūtamayād atha samādāyannamuṣṭiṃ ca tatra tat khaṇḍitaṃ ca yat  Paus smaretpariṇataṃ samyam vyāpakatvena sāṃpratam athādibhūtaṃ cādhyātmam adhidaivam athābjaja  Paus tadannaṃ pitṛpiṇḍe tu tadūrdhve tha sthitaṃ nayet evam ekatvam āpanne prete citpratinā saha  Paus pretapiṇḍavad abjottha vācartavyaṃ hi cākhilam vyāpāramatha tasyātha tasmātpaitāmahe tataḥ  Paus tasmāt tadapi tatprāgvatparatāṃ nayet yathokte smin dvijaśreṣṭha prājāpatye tu karmaṇi  Paus āde kādaśādyāvat pitṛtvāpādane dinam tāvatpūrvoditaṃ śeṣaṃ yattatpūrvaṃ samācaret  Paus kintu bhojanabhūmau tu dvijaptairāsanasthitaiḥ vacanīyaṃ hi cākṣayyaṃ tilamiśreṇa vāriṇā  Paus etāvatāsya tātparyaṃ yathāvatsaṃprakāśitam aurdhvadaihikasaṃjñasya vyā sātvikam  Paus āsṛṣṭe sati rāgau cayathā spharati vai hṛdi pratyayāvayavau caiva pauṣkara  Paus balyarthaṃ vihitaṃ teṣām annaṃ piṇḍaṃ tu sodakam pretakriyāvidhau caiva svaṃ svaṃ kāla kulocitaṃ  Paus cāturmānaniṣedhaṃ ca vihitaṃ sūtakādike pratiṣedhaṃ gṛhīturvai ābhūtād abjasaṃbhava  Paus dvijendrāṇāṃ tu sanyeṣāṃ cāturātmyaikayājinām ārādhyānāṃ prabha bhā vācca nāstīti dvijasattama  Paus ata evādhikāraṃ tu mṛtake sūtake tu vā pratigrahe pradāne ca tatkālaṃ saṅkaraṃ vinā  Paus sahajā pratipattirvai ityeṣāmarayājinām bhagavadyājināṃ caiva nissandigdhā parasparam  Paus mārgam icchati yastvevam anusartṛṃ hi cācyutam āśaucaṃ samatītaṃ cettataḥ kuryād daśāhikam  Paus ityuktam abjasaṃbhūta sarahasyaṃyathā sthitam saṃpradānādikaṃ śaśvat śrāddhāvaraṇam uttamam  Paus atha kāmya śrāddhavidhiḥ vidhyantaram atho bhūyaḥ prasaṅgād avadhāraya svargāpavargaphaladaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām  Paus vyavahārapadasthaṃ yadvicchinnā śastra bandhubhiḥ śāstrabuddhibhiḥ  svayam icchati vaikastu dvādaśāhādvijākhilam  Paus tadidānīṃ samāsena yathāvatkathayāmyaham purā saṃbhatasaṃbhāraḥ susahāyaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ  Paus manaḥ prasādajanakam evaṃ vā bahavo dvijāḥ vibhavāddvijān puraskṛtya dine śubhre pitṛpakṣāttu vai purā  Paus prāvṛṭkāle tu vācyatra śaratkāle tu mādhave yāyād āyātanaṃ viṣṇoḥ puṣpadhūpajanākulam  Paus kūlaṃ nadanadīnāṃ vā sānvādyaṃ sodakaṃ gireḥ nirātaṅkam asaṅkīrṇaṃ śvapākaśabarādikaiḥ  Paus tamāsādya tapaḥ kuryād yāgaṃ ca vidhipūrvakam gaṇe ca nāgasthāne ca bhūtānāṃ ca vanaspateḥ  Paus kṣetravāsimukhenaiva yathāśaktyā sadakṣiṇām apare hani vai kuryāt svamantrārādhanaṃ tu vai  Paus viṣṇorāyatanasthaṃ ca mantram ajñātalakṣaṇam vyaktaṃ vāpyarcanīyaṃ ca prārthayetta  ma danantaram  Paus vibhoḥ praṇamate to  dhyakṣaṃ svacid bījānvitasya ca vyaktāvyaktādyasaṃjñasya piṇḍam indriyasaṃjñitam  Paus sthāpayāmi satattvāṃśaiḥ saṃdhayitvā yathāvidhi bhedarūpam abhinnaṃ cakāyātmāṃśucayasya ca  Paus sukṛtasya ca bhogārtham anyathā parameśvara samutkrāntasya me dehāt sthitaṃ mārutalakṣaṇam  Paus saduḥkhāyā sukhaduḥkhā bhilāṣā ca dhanena ca samāvṛtā jāyate saṃbhramopetā dīrghakālavadakṣayā  Paus niṣkriyā ca tathā jantorvaśāpyavaśāsya ca dehāntareṇa cāptena śaśvatkālāntareṇa vā  Paus sā sthitā dussahā ghora tattvato yāti saṃkṣayam tvatprasādād ato nātha śīghram annaṃ jalena tu  Paus piṇḍam indriyasaṃjñaṃ yanniṣpādyaṃ tannirāmayam niḥsantānastvasaṃdehaṃ nirāśaḥ karmajālagaḥ  Paus adhikṛtya tvamevādya karoti ṣi trāṇam ātmanā patitānāṃ nirāśānāṃ nārakāṇāṃ parā gatiḥ  Paus tvameva luptapiṇḍānāṃ śaśvad uddharaṇakṣamaḥ yatastvame va tat śaśvadnārabhya mbha sanātana  Paus niṣpattidinaparyantaṃ vighnajālaṃ savāsanam mama māyātu bhagavan karmasiddhirmamāstu vai  Paus evam abhyarthayitvājaṃ karamāpūrya vāriṇā kuryāt tat śeṣapūrṇaṃ tu āsamāpti tu saṃyamam  Paus laukikaṃ vyavahāraṃ yaddharmakāmārthalakṣaṇam nirasya pūrvavatsarvaṃ sāvadhānaṃ tato bhavet  Paus tato bhimatavṛttau tu kṛtvā devārcanaṃ tu vai tadagrato dakṣiṇe vā calayiṣye śi tarpaṇam  Paus dvijendraṃ sanniveśyātha sarvaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi nirviśaṅkena manasā tadvadeva dhiyā tataḥ  Paus svagṛhaṃcasvacaitanyaṃ dhyāyet sānnidhyam āgatam smared ekaṃ ca niṣpāpaṃ praṇavenāptakālavat  Paus gatāvasaṃ yatsaṃskāraṃ yathā śāstroditaṃ mahat kṛtabhikṣastu vihitam uktadīkṣaṃ tu vā caret  Paus asthisañcayaṃ tu evaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi samācaret tataḥ snānaṃ māntram abjaja tatra vai  Paus dvijendraiḥ kṛtadīkṣaistu ṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃgataiḥ pradhānamantrairabliṅgairupasnāto bhaved atha  Paus dvādaśākṣarapūrvebhyo madhyātprāguktalakṣaṇam japed ekatamaṃ mantraṃ dīkṣitasvekameva hi  Paus svamantrād astramantrairvā evaṃ snāne kṛte punaḥ svamantraṃ dvādaśārṇaṃ vā dhyāyan hṛtkamalāntare  Paus taptakāñcanavarṇām amuktamūrtiṃtameva vā muhūrtārdhaṃ muhūrtaṃ vā japannāste hyananyadhīḥ  Paus tena kalpāgnikaṃ vipra āśaucaṃ svakulodbhavam kṣayametyabhisandhānān narāṇām adhikāriṇām  Paus tattvaṃ mānasam anyebhyaḥ saṃbhūtānāṃ yathākramam na punaḥ sarvaśaktervai saṃbhūtānāṃ sukhānale  Paus taddhā dyāyināṃ nāṃ ca tajjñānāṃ dvijānām adhikāriṇām evaṃ saṃśuddhadehastu annaṃ saṃsādya pūrvavat  Paus sabhakṣyaṃ vyañjanopetaṃ vibhoryāgārthameva ca tarpaṇārthaṃ hi vai vahneḥ piṇḍanirvāpaṇāya ca  Paus yathāpivāhikaṃ dehaṃ dvitīyaṃ bhūtavigraham karmaṇā nāśam abhyeti dīkṣādyena ca mokṣiṇām  Paus svayaṃ saṃprati datvaivam ādaśāhādikena yat purastād upakārāya karmaṇāṃ dehameti tat  Paus dharmeṇānyaccireṇaiva bhāvināṃ kamalodbhava dīrghābhyāsena kālena saha karmacayaṃ mahat  Paus śamam āyāti vai nūnaṃ mantreśānāṃ prasādataḥ pitṛtvāpādanaṃ tena karmaṇā vimalena ca  Paus asmādgurutaraṃ caiva svayaṃ saṃpāditaṃ tu vā ādaśāhādikaṃ puṃsām upakārāya vai bhavet  Paus nityamante nivṛtte tu svārādhyaṃ saṃyajet tataḥ abhisandhāya manasā svayaṃ gurumukhena vā  Paus karmādhāraṃ hi vai bhāvi dehaṃ śrāddhacchalena tu sandhām īśvaratattvāṃgairdehabhāvāt pṛthaksthitaiḥ  Paus prāgvadiṣṭvātha mantreśaṃ bhogaiḥ saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇaiḥ satilāñjalidānāntairvidhivat kamalodbhava  Paus pūrvoktena vidhānena bhaktyā saśraddhayā tataḥ ekāhaṃ bahavo viprāḥ pañcakālaparāyaṇāḥ  Paus santarpya bhagavad yāgādyo hi vāñchati sampadam tasmād uttaraṇe heturjīvitasya mṛtasya vā  Paus na paśyāmi ṛte yāgādetasmānmantrapūrvakāt prabhavātyayatattvajñā vyāmiśrārādhanojjhitāḥ  Paus te tra pātrāstrayo nityaṃ jñānakarmaparāyaṇāḥ mantrapratiparāsaktā itikartavyācyutiḥ  Paus bhaktiśraddhāsamopetā paramuttāraṇaplavaḥ āstāṃ tāvad apāpānām upāyatvena pauṣkara  Paus yāgaṃ brahmamayaṃ śuddhaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ parairapi patitatvāttu vai teṣāṃ piṇḍadānaṃ tilodakam  Paus nāmasaṃkīrtanaṃ caite prayānti paramāṃ gatim ekamuktaṃ samutkṛṣṭam avyāpāraṃ parākramaḥ mam   Paus ā adhārādhanapūrvaṃ vā prājāpatyaṃ samācaret sapiṇḍīkaraṇāntaṃ tu ādaśāhād dvijottama  Paus agnāvagre tadantasthe mantreśe tarpite sati piṇḍanirvāpaṇaṃ kuryāt pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ  Paus viniveśyāsane vipram ekaṃ śaktyā bahūnapi tarpaṇīyāni vidhivat tattvasandhānasiddhaye  Paus bhojane phalamūlaistu bhakṣyairuccāvacaistathā pāvanairvividhaiḥ pānairlehyaiḥ peyaiśca coṣyakaiḥ  Paus dakṣiṇābhistu tāmbūlairvārikumbhasamanvitaiḥ chatropānahayānaistu dānaiḥ kāmyairyathocitaiḥ  Paus dmītim abhyeti vai yena samūhaṃ bhagavanmayam jñātvā vā vyavasāyaṃ yad deśakālabalābalam  Paus saha satpātralobhena śīghraṃ yatkartum icchati śrāddhaṃ daśāhapūrvaṃ vā pitṛtvāpādanāntikam  Paus anekadivasotthaṃ tu siddhānnena vinā dvija yathāvad arcanaṃ kṛtvā patrapuṣpādikairvibhaḥ  Paus vahnitarpaṇaniṣṭhaṃ tu svārtham uddiśya vai pitṝn pātraṃ madhvājyasiktaistu saṃpūrṇaṃ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ  Paus upariṣṭādrasairmūrteḥ phalamūlairvibhūṣitam sottarīyopavītāḍhyaṃ sarar yutam  Paus sasya ekasamopetaṃ vārikumbhasamanvitam dhūpadīpādikairyuktaṃ pūjayitvā nivedya ca  Paus pitrarthaṃ tu dvijātmārthaṃ tato dadyāt tilodakam ekamevaṃ hi caikāryaṃ vahyarthaṃbahavastu vā  Paus siddhānnaṃ sadvijendrāṇāṃ pūjita  pratipādya krameṇaiva pūjanīyaṃ hi vai vibhoḥ  Paus piṇḍaṃ madhvājyasiktairvā prāgvad āpādya taṇḍulaiḥ agnigarbhagatasyāgre vibhordarbhasu   Paus ta yathoktaṃ tu sa ti prāṇendriyāṇāṃ tu yathāvasaram atra ca  Paus gandhānāṃ pūrvavat kuryāt budhyā ca suviśuddhayā pretoddiṣṭena vidhināyathāvadātmanātmanā  Paus vidhinā mantrapūrveṇa vatsaraṃ saṃprapūrya ca pratisaṃvatsaraṃ śrāddhaṃ yāvajjīvaṃ samācaret  Paus nānādānasamopetaṃ bhāvaścāddhavibhūṣitam yathoddiṣṭena mārgeṇa kintu gotrasamanvitāḥ  Paus mantrānte viniyoktavyāḥ samaśabdapurassarāḥ svayaṃ jñānābhimānākhyaṃ mūrtiṃ dhyāyet svakaṃ dvija  Paus ataḥśuddhāṃ jvaladrūpāṃ kvacid ākṛtilakṣaṇām kvacidgolakarūpāṃ ca madhyāhnādityasannibhāt  Paus kvacinmandatarābhāṃ ca tad vyāpāravaśena tu evaṃ samāpya vidhivat bhagavadyāgapūrvakam  Paus vipratarpaṇaparyantam akhilaṃ pūrvacoditam prāgodanasyapiṇḍādyairvahnyante copasaṃhṛtaiḥ  Paus bandhubhiḥ saha cākṣīyād dattaśiṣṭaṃ dvijottama prājāpatyaṃ tu vai divye aurdhvadaihipūrvake  Paus vyāpāre smin samantre tu siddhirasti vidātmanām svayamātmani kartṝṇāṃ bhāvānmantrāṃśca sādhitān  Paus yena coparatasyāśu yathārthatvaṃ prayāti ca tatraśrāddhavidhiṃkuryānmantranyastena cākhilam  Paus āpaṅktisādhanātkāri tṛptyantam amalekṣaṇa ācared vacasā sarvaṃ mantroccāraṇapūrvakam  Paus gṛhāṇānaya saṃyaccha tvevamādyaṃ hi yaddvija manasā bhojanāntaṃ tu vyāpāram akhilaṃ smaret  Paus praṇavenārkacandrāgnisamūhadyutisannibham saṃviśantaṃ svayaṃ mantramagnau tadrūpalakṣaṇe  Paus paramātmani vā bhinne cāturātmyaṃ tu viddhi tat kadambakusumākāraṃ sarvaśaktimalepakam  Paus itīdam uktam abjākṣa jīvabhāvasthitasya ca pāratrikaṃ vidhānaṃ tu mukhakalpasamaṃ mahat  Paus atra pūrvoditaṃ vipra uktānuktaṃ tu cākhilam bhagavatprītiparyantaṃ vijñātavyaṃ samāhitaḥ  Paus vidhinānena yatkuryāt pitṛpretamayaṃ mahat prītaye paratastasya śubhāṃ yacchanti santatim  Paus bhāvamantrakriyādravyairasaṃpūrṇastu yogavat paṭhan vai śrāddhabhoktṝṇāṃ śrāddhādhyāyam idaṃ dvija  Paus samastaṃ hyagrato bhaktyā pitṝṇām anṛṇo bhavet kiṃ punarbrahmasanmantraṃ mantrakarma mahāmate  Paus pauṣkara uvāca va puvyena bhagavan brahma   me mūrtaṃ atrāsti saṃśayaḥ  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca na teṣāṃ vratacayahiḥsūryabimbaṃ yathā vinā tathā bhagavato viṣṇormūrtaṣāḍguvyavigrahān  Paus prakāśa ta pūrva ndarmāgrā  mā   Paus vyañjanti kamalodbhūta tvadanyenaiva sarvadā bheda evaṃ hi vibhoścaturmūrteḥ parasya ca  Paus yattatpiṇḍārthaṃkṛtānāṃ ca rasānāṃ bhinnarūpiṇām paraspara  dvayāpakatve sthitaṃ dvija  Paus vibhoḥ sarveśvarasyaiva sarvaḥ sarvāsu śaktiṣu vartante ca yathā   Paus atra granthapātaḥ  parupacaryate viśvātmā bhagavān vipra vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ  Paus ciddhanārutāḥ punaḥ samyagupakārāya karmaṇi syarūpu vyañjayanti ca  Paus bhāvānāṃ bhāti saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇam pūrṇātmani punaḥ sar  ver vāḥ tathātvena ca saṃsthitāḥ  Paus kintu kurvanti tāḥ kṛtyāḥ kartā pa rā prakāśaśaktyā yāṃ śakti sya ca  Paus svacitā raśmijālena yanmadhyādekam abjaja prakaṭīkṛtam ātmanam āditattvena vai saha  Paus samādhisaṃvidhānaṃ ca lābhe vā dhyānakarmaṇi paramātmā sasudbhūta  vibhuḥ  Paus svaprakāśāṃśamātreṇa ata evānumīyate evam āhlādaśaktervai lavamātraṃ hi candramāḥ  Paus jñātavyam aravindākṣa prītasya nidhi maṃ  nikhilu param kti  cicchaktiḥ parijñeyā tadvadeva hi pāvakaḥ  Paus jagatyasmin hi ye bhāvā anye tad anukāriṇaḥ jñānādayo pi labhyante tena śaktija  ca yāṃśajāḥ  Paus sarvatra bhagavānevaṃ sāmānyatvena vartate nedaṃ māyātmakaṃ rūpaṃ jaḍaśaktiguṇairyutam  Paus bhagavatyabjasaṃbhūta tvantallīnaṃ hi vidyate yato vicāryamāṇaṃ hi nityam acyutabhāvinām  Paus abhāvabhūmim āyāti svapnadṛṣṭam iveśvaram mantrāḥ śrāddhe samā ye ca ye ca dīkṣādiṣūditāḥ  Paus vyāpāreṣvapi cānyeṣu te pyevaṃ mahimānvitam budhyaivaṃ mantrapūrvaṃ ca sa  vyā pāraṃ śāstracoditam  Paus kṛtiṃ  taṃ jñānātmanābhyeti hyacirādeva karmaṇām śrotriyāṇāṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ tvadarthāśramavartinām  Paus yadvadbhuktāddha va  viḥśśūdrāt na doṣo jñānagauravāt evaṃ svabhāvadīptānāṃ nirmalānāṃ sadaiva hi  Paus navairjātaṃ na  manair malyaṃ mantrasantarpaṇāya ca  Paus vahnevo ro ṅkāravegena rasatā sūpari dvija pātayed ājyadohaṃ drāk madhye mantrātmano vibhoḥ  Paus mokṣabhogāptaye caivaṃ brahmarandhramukhe kramāt yathāgandhavanopetaṃ
