brahmapūrvam atandritaḥ  Paus niyataṃ hi ya thā śa kti prabhāte staṃ gate ravau rātriyā rātrervā madhyabhāge tu yathāśāstranibandhanam  Paus pūrvasevāvidherūrdhvaṃ prītyarthaṃ pūjitasya ca lakṣajāpādike siddhe brahmadine   Paus samāpte tatsame home vihito thavābjaja aṅgenam aṅgatulyaṃ vā dhānyairbījaistilaiḥ phalaiḥ  Paus hariṇānananārācamudrayā jalajākhyayā samatvāt juhuyāt tadanantaram  Paus ṣaṇmāsasamamānena dviguṇenātha pauṣkara caturguṇena vā śaktyā hyantarāntarayogataḥ  Paus śakta śatānte ca dvicatuṣparipūrite ve sājye tricatuṣkaikarātriṇām  Paus bhūricātma samānayet sami   Paus nakhilamantrestu saha mantrī ca saṃhitām samuccaran dhiyā samyak svaśaktyā vā pṛthak pṛthak  Paus bhinnamantragaṇaṃ sarvam ājyadohairmudaṃ nayet dhruvāccārcitayā ttu vai  Paus tallakṣaṇam atho vakṣye mānameyasamanvitam prasiddhayajñavṛkṣotthaṃ na doṣairdṛḍhamavraṇa ta m  Paus suspaṣṭaṃ kāṣṭham ādāya davāgnitrāsavarjitam nirasaṃjirakā paryuṣitaṃ śubham  Paus madhyamāṅguliparyantaṃ bāhnorāmaṇibandhataḥ tamaṅguṣṭhodarairbhūyo naguṇya ca  Paus aṣṭāvaṣṭau tyajan yāyāt śeṣāstvekādhikāhi  ācāraste vai parijñeyā dhvajādyanya ṣṭau yathākramāt  Paus tatraivam avaśeṣaṃ yacchubhaṃ ca śubhanaḥ smṛtaḥ yūyaṃ thaṃ yugmāvaśeṣācca tṛtīyācca mṛgādhipaḥ  Paus catuṣṭaya sva śva vṛddhiṃ ca pañcakā vṛṣabhaḥ smṛtaḥ karaṣmakā kareṇukā ca śeṣācca gajā vai saptakāt tu vai  Paus ekākhyaḥ saptakāḥ śuddhestatrāmī śubhadāḥ smṛtāḥ gajendrasiṃhavṛṣabhadhvajādyā ye śubhapradāḥ  Paus aśubhāyaye vighātārthaṃ svaśubhāyaye vivṛddhaye aṅgulaṃ vāṅgulayutaṃ yuktidairdhyaṃ vinikṣipet  Paus tad dīrghaṃ pañcadhā kuryāt tad virutāraṃ dalena tu siddhaye madhyadeśasya vidheyā yatra pauṣkara  Paus ādyakauśādayaśvāgoḥ tad uddeśāt krameṇa tu patrakesaracakrāṅgaṃ bhūmīnāṃ hrāsamācaret  Paus vaniparyantam unnatāstātkṣipet punaḥ nirvartyāḥ karṇacihnāstu cakrābjābhyāṃ tu sāntarāt  Paus pañcamāṃśena dairdhyaṃ tu tad vistārasamena tu dvibhāgasaṃhataṃ caiva śākhādeśāgrato bhavet  Paus cetarākāravedī kāryā vasundharā ārāpraṇālamadhyastā nānākarmavirājitā  Paus svaṃ svaṃ saṃveditaṃ kuryāt tena cāvedikaṃ śubham kṣitimaṇḍalamadhyasthabhāgenādyena vai tataḥ  Paus kamalaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ kevalaṃ ṣoḍaśacchadam sanālam abhinirvartya kesarālaṃ sakarṇikam  Paus nibījaṃ karṇikākośam īṣatparivibhūṣitam yathoktalakṣaṇāḍhyena hetīśenāvṛtaṃ tu vā  Paus cakradhārāvaniṃ kuryāt koṇeṣūbhayato ṅkitām kaustubhaiḥ svastikairvātha śaṅkhādyairmaṇḍala maṇḍitam  Paus tārāttā e gaṇāḍhyaṃ vā  kuryāccāstraṃ cograyāvadāsacet  Paus ataścāntānupātārtham aṣṭāṃśaṃ pakṣagaṃ punaḥ tyaktvā samācareddhrāsaṃ yathā syād gajapāṇivat  Paus antaraṃ vasudhābhyāṃ ṣṭāṃśasaṃmitam kāryaṃ ṣaḍaṃśatulyaṃ vā vistṛtaiḥ śubhalakṣaṇam  Paus tad vistāraṃ dvidhā kṛtvā pañcadhā vā samaiḥ padaiḥ madhyabhāgasya  Paus bhāgam abhāgaṃ ca pakṣayorvā dvayaṃ dvayam agrataścānupātārthaṃ vibhajyaiva yathecchayā  Paus skandhāntaraṃ ca  matsyavallāṃñchana yathākramam  Paus pārśvābhyām antaraṃ bāhyāt śeṣaṃ kaṇṭhātmanā nayet yathā syād gomukhe bhāsa kaṇṭhaṃ maharddhidam  Paus nirmuktavedikānāṃ tu śaṅkhādīnāṃ yadanta paṭṭena yuktaṃ padmadvayena vā  Paus vedikāvāsudhāṃśā bhyāṃ tvanupātena śātayet skandhakaṇṭhāt samārabhyatrayo grīvā yathecchayā  Paus vidhāya bhāgaṃ prāgukta tam vedikāvidhihīnasya śaṅkhasya vacanaṃ hi yat  Paus sapādabhāgasametaṃ kuryāt pañcāṅgasaṃmitam vistṛter vādhikaṃ kiñcit nyūnaṃ vā rājate yathā  Paus kumbhabhāgatrayaṃ sadmadvayaṃ saṃśātayet kramāt pṛthūdarasya śaṅkhasya pañcamāṃśena śātayet  Paus kukṣideśaṃ dvidhā caiva stragādyair arcayet tataḥ vartate mūlam āśritya dairdhyād bhāgatrayaṃ hi yat  Paus tanmadhyāt kaṇṭhadeśe prāgākṣipyāṅgaṃ yathoditam śeṣaṃ tu daśadhā kṛtvā tataḥ saptāṅgasaṃmitam  Paus daṇḍaṃ kuryād gadākāraṃ kaṇṭhavistāravistṛtam dviprakāraṃ yathoddiṣṭamatelavaṇānvitam  Paus aṃśakatritayenaiva tatra nirmāṇam ucyate vedikopagataṃ kuryād ekabhāgasamāśritam  Paus svāstikaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ madhyataḥ kamalāṅkitam karṇikā nicayaśścāntaṃ pratyaṃśaṃ racayet tataḥ  Paus aṅgaṇe petaiḥ susamair antarīkṛtaiḥ  dhārācanavidhānaivaṃ dviṣaṭkapariniṣṭhite vartulaṃ caturaśraṃ tu cayamadhyagam  Paus karagrahavatīṃ muṣṭimarodayalakṣaṇām īṣā ṣan mānādhikaṃ daṇḍaṃ bāhyam āpūrayet tathā  Paus śatapatram adhovaktraṃ pṛthulaṃ cordhvakarṇikam muṣṭiniṣṭhāyudhau vadhau kuryāt bahuparṇaṃ sakesaram  Paus athavedikṣipet pīṭhalakṣaṇaṃ cāparaṃ śṛṇu vihitaṃ cārdhakalpeyaṃ devapīṭhopamaṃ śubham  Paus uṣṇīvapadaparyantam ācāgreḥ sa vibhajya ca sa mair bhāgaiḥ purātra syudvādadiṣṭamucyate  Paus padmaṃ cakrāravindaṃ vā lakṣaṇalakṣitam kiṃtu mānaṃ vibhāgaṃ ca bhūyaḥ kṣetravaśāt śṛṇu  Paus brahmasthānāvadheḥ kṣetraṃ kṛtvā ṣaṅbhāgabhājitam dvau bhāgau bhūṣayenmadhye karṇikāpadasiddhaye  Paus paridhiścārdhabhāgena tvardhena kesarāvalim sārdhena patranicayaṃ vyoma cārdhena tad bahiḥ  Paus pārthivaṃ puram aṃśena vicitraracanānvitam sāntarāṇi samāsādya kṣetrāṇyetāni pauṣkara  Paus kiñcit kiñcit samādāya pronnateṣvavayaveṣu ca ākhyātaparito brahman dalapādānikaṃ kramāt  Paus nimnatāṃ ca nayed īṣat kṣetrāt kṣetraṃ yathoditam śeṣa eva sacakramya parimāryacānyathā  Paus khātātmakesarakṣetramānam atra yathoditam dalajālaṃ samāpādya savyoma cāṃśakena tu  Paus sacakranemivṛttaṃ tu sārdhenāṃśena tad bahiḥ bhāgakṣetraṃ kuryāt prāguktalakṣaṇam  Paus pṛṣṭhatasva kuryāt sapadmaṃ kaivalaṃ tu vā kamalaṃ dalajālaṃ ca mukha   Paus etat pramāṇanirmāṇapari  tadā prameyam asyāṃ vai jñātavyaṃ karmasiddhaye  Paus śatapatrātmanānanto muṣṭistenantavātra dhṛk antarbījātmabhāvena sthitvā cotthamukhaḥ punaḥ  Paus pataskandhaṃ yadaryātmabhūtaprāṇamarunmahat preritaṃ brahmarandhreṇa tat tad icchāvaśāt punaḥ  Paus saptapātālanālaṃ ca tvagamakṣātmanāmbujam  yadāśritya svavāhe tu hyamṛtaṃ jalavat sthitam  Paus sacakraracanājāle sthitaste satramūrtidhṛk śaṅkhavigrahadhṛgvāyurājyakośaṃ ca khaṃ tataḥ  Paus nirbījam ajam akṣobhyam ādyaṃ stragdevatasyādhidaivatam  satyabhūtam ameyaṃ ca prameyam idam acyutam  Paus saṃskārakāle tvāropya nityaṃ saṃmantrya tarpaṇe dairghyam eva tam ujjhitya vedivistārameva ca  Paus yathoktāṃśaṃ  saṃhataṃ gadādaṇḍaṃ sukhiraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ tu vā  Paus nātisthūlaṃ nātikṛśaṃ yuktam ṛjugaṇena tu evaṃ dravyamayaṃ kuryāt śubhadāramayaṃ tu vā  Paus stratukstruvānāṃ ca homārthaṃ tallakṣaṇam athocyate āyaśuddhaṃ samādāya prāguktagaṇalakṣitam  Paus trayeṃśonaṃ strucā dairdhyād aṣṭadhā cocchritaṃ bhajet tena bhāgapramāṇena tad vistāraṃ vidhīyate  Paus saṃvibhajya samāṃśaistat sūtraiḥ spaṣṭairyathākramam kalaśaṃ kḷptayenmūlād aṣṭāṃśaṃ caturaśrakam  Paus varjayitvātha bāhulyaṃ vistārārdhena kalpya vai kuryād ādhāraviśrāntaṃ kamalaṃ racitānvitam  Paus taṃ śaṃkhaṃ vitatāsyaṃ tu nandyāvartaṃ sulakṣaṇam pārśvabhāgadvayaṃ tyaktavā caturaṃśa smṛtam  Paus pāśavadgrathitaṃ madhye suvibhaktaṃ ca vartulam caturbhāgānanaṃ daṇḍaṃ nirgataṃ kalaśānanāt  Paus vitānaṃ śaṅkhavaktrād vā tritayasaṃyutam dhārānāladvayaṃ kuryāt ṣṭāṅgasaṃmitān  Paus pīṭhavat kaṇṭhapīṭhaṃ tu caturaśraṃ samāpya ca tasmin paṅkajam ullikhya cakravṛttāntarīkṛtam  Paus muktājālasamaṃ sūtraṃ śaṅkhakoṇacatuṣṭaye ekāṃśenonnatā grīvā vistāravdyaṅgasaṃmitā  Paus īṣad vaktrā na sāṣṭāṃśād ūrdhve bhāgasamujjhitām padmavaccottamāṅgaṃ ca grīvānālaṃ sakarṇikam  Paus anantakesaraprāntairāvṛtaṃ karṇikānanam tad bahiḥ patrajālaṃ tu kesarocchrāyasaṃmitam  Paus avibhāga pṛṣṭhatastiryagānanam kuryācca karrṇikāmadhye golakenaiva mudritam  Paus kaustubhenāṅkitaṃ caiva saurabhīyāśriṇāthavā sārdhahomapramāṇena dravyajājyāhuteḥ kṣamam  Paus pramāṇope lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam smṛtaṃ sadājyahomārthaṃ śeṣam anayannibodhatu  Paus sākṣād amṛtamūrtirvai varuṇaḥ kamalātmanā nālātmanā tadastraṃ ca saṃsthitaṃ vighnabhītikṛtṛ  Paus jagadāpyāyakṛt candraḥ padmatcenāgradeśa  ānandākhyaṃ hi sāmarthyaṃ jñeyaṃ tat parameśvaram  Paus deśikastu tadānyāsasādhakaḥ saṃyatastu vā daivīyam abhimānaṃ ca samāśritya te  Paus arcane sāgnikārye tu yathopakaraṇākhilāḥ sannārya svakaraṇānāṃ tu hyekasmin svāśraye sthitāḥ  Paus sarva dehenānena tvardhyapātra  śaṅkhacakrādikairyutāḥ  Paus kāryā tvam abhimatāptaye tasmād anadhikārye tha hyannadevaparastathā  Paus damaho saṃśrayet niṣiddha dehāpaharaṇaṃ śubham  Paus saṃpādya padavīṃ yāti yo dhikārapade sthitaḥ dadāti anujñājuṣṭānāṃ tvad bhaktānāṃ ca tatprati  Paus ājyasthālī bṛhad brahmalakṣaṇe  kuryāt kamalagarbhaṃ tu yāmyayātrātmato śubhāḥ  Paus gṛhītvātmāmṛtaḥ samyak saṃstutvaṃ labhate gninā dhruvaṃ pramāṇanālaṃ ca tanmūle śubhalakṣaṇam  Paus kuryād amalasāraṃ ca bjaja tatsamarthaṃ ca tannālasaṃjñitāḥ śrīniṣevitāḥ  Paus saṃpādya nalinīṃ divyāṃ praphullair ardhapuṣpitaiḥ tathā mukulitaiḥ padmaiḥ sapadmair antarīkṛtaiḥ  Paus dikpālitāścaiva dakṣiṇottarayostu vā caturvistāravaktrāṃ ca phullapadmāntarāṇi rīkṛ tām   Paus cakravyomatribhāgena nimnā vātadalena tu mūlayed galadeśa stā ḥsyād anyamanyaṃ samāpya vai  Paus uṣṇīṣaṃ cātpalopetaṃ saṃsiddhā surabhīravaiḥ sanālā nalinī teṣāṃ tatpātraṃ pārameśvaram  Paus śayanāsanasaṃjñaṃ ca satataṃ cāmṛtārṇavam dyāvāpṛthivyā   Paus straggaṃdhava teraste sapuṣpe copaladvaye praṇītādīni pātrāṇi tūpayogyāni yānyapi  Paus tāni śaṅkhābjahetīśasaṃyuktānyakhilāni ca vicitraṃ racanā dhātudārvamayāni vā  Paus yathābhimatamānāni kuryāt padmevatāni ca mantrārādhanapūrvāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ kamalodbhava  Paus sarvaṃ salāñchanaṃ kuryāpadaṃtra kalaśādi  tvāsanādīni svātmopakaraṇāni ca  Paus muktāṅgulīyakaṃ caiva bhūṣakaṃ ṇaṃ kaṭakādikam uttamāṅgodvahaṃ sarvaṃ śiroṣṇīṣādīkaṃ tu vai  Paus iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃkuṇḍalakṣaṇaṃ nāma ekonatriṃśo dhyāyaḥ atha triṃśo dhyāyaḥpauṣkara uvāca saṃjāte bhagavan lope bhaktānāṃ mantrasevinām jñānādiyoganiṣṭhasya sadvyāpārasya cācyuta  Paus pātatrāṇamupāyaṃ vai śrotumicchāmi sāṃpratam kṛtena yena bhaktānāṃ jāyate kṛtakṛtyatā  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca kathaṃ saṃvatsarādvipra karmaṇābhimataṃ phalam prāpnuyācca kriyāsaktaḥ pavitrārohaṇaṃ vinā  Paus yathāśvamedhaṃ viprāṇāṃ sarvecchāparipūrakam rājasūyaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ tathā  Paus bhūṣaṇānāṃ yathā madhye kaustubhaṃ varabhūṣaṇam jñeyaṃ pavitrakaṃ tadvadbhogajālasya cāntare  Paus yatpūrayati bhaktānāṃ vyāpāraṃ pārameśvaram bhogamokṣāptaye śaśvadbhogastasmāstu ko dhikaḥ  Paus bhaktānāṃ satataṃ bhaktyā sālokyaṃ vidadhāti vai sāmīpyaṃ sādhakānāṃ ca nānāsiddhisamanvitam  Paus sāyujyaṃ sādhakendrāṇāṃ svamantrātmani yacchati taduttarāyaṇe tīte cāturmāsasya madhyataḥ  Paus ādāvante thavā kuryād dvādaśīṣvakhilāsu ca saṃkrāntiṣu ca sarvāsu paurṇamāsiṣu cābjaja  Paus amāvāsyāsvaśeṣāsu tṛtīyāsu tathaiva ca vaiṣṇaveṣvatha ṛkṣeṣu tatkṣaṇeṣvakhileṣu ca  Paus cāturmāsyasya kālasya tūtthāna dvādaśī tu yā ṣaḍaśītimukhā divyā tasyāmāropayettu yaḥ  Paus pavitrakaṃ jagadyoneḥ sapavitrīkaroti ca atītāṃ vartamānāṃ ca eṣyāṃ svakulasantātim  Paus tatra sannihitaḥ sākṣānnānānirmāṇavigrahaḥ bhaktānāṃ bhagavān prītaḥ paramātmācyuto hariḥ  Paus yadyapyabjasamudbhūta bhaktānāṃ nityameva hi nārāyaṇastu mantrātmā sthitaḥ sannihitaḥ svayam  Paus tathāpi balavattā vai tattithestatra karmaṇi sannidhi bhajate yena mantriṇāṃ mantrarāṭ prabhuḥ  Paus grīṣmakālaṃ samāsādya yathārkastīkṣṇatā vrajet svarūpamajahanneva sannidhānataraṃ vibhoḥ  Paus saptātradeśakālānām āsṛṣṭeḥ sthitaye tu vai ataḥ pavitrakaṃ tasyāmanasyāṃ tadasaṃbhavāt  Paus kāryaṃ kriyāparairbhaktyā sākhaṇḍā yena jāyate akhaṇḍakārī puruṣo jñānakarmaparāyaṇaḥ  Paus bhaktiśraddhātathotsāhayukto yogabalairyuktaḥ brahmavyekātmatāṃ yāti acirādeva pauṣkara  Paus sarvabhāvena bhaktānāṃ yatpālayati sarvadā manovākcittajaṃ kutsnaṃ vyāpāraṃ śubhalakṣaṇam  Paus parijñerāyatastasmāt svarūpaṃ tasya yādṛśam phalameti ca vai yena bhaktānāṃ tatsamāpanāt  Paus yadacchinnaṃ jagadhoneranantaprasaraṃ sitam vicchedamakṛtajñānāmeti nānātmanā svayam  Paus jagatsūtraṃ tu tadviddhi hemasūtrādinā tu vai bāḍguvyamabhimānaṃ yaddhatte pratisarātmanā  Paus jñānarāgoparaktaṃ ca yuktaṃ kāryaistu vīryajeḥ taijasairāvṛttaṃ mantrairbalenāvalitaṃ param  Paus aiśvaryamupacāre tu saṃprāpte śaktito vyayam evaṃ pavitrakaṃ tāvatparijñātaṃ na tat prabhoḥ  Paus brahmavyadhipatau viṣṇau tadākāre pratiṣṭhite bhaktyā ca vidhivaddattaṃ dadāti bhagavatpadam  Paus sthūlasya vyatiriktasya vyavahārapadasthitaiḥ padārthaiḥ kalpanīyā ca yathā tadavadhārasya  Paus sūkṣmaṃ dṛḍhaṃ sitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ sūtraṃ brahmaprasūtayā vinirmitaṃ kumāryā vā vṛddhayā vā vinītayā  Paus viśuddhayā vidhavayā saṃpāditamathāpi vā yathālabdhaṃ tu cādāya kuryādastraviśodhitam  Paus avalokya smaranmūlaṃ viniṣpādya caturguṇam cāturātmyavyapekṣāyāmathavāṣṭagūṇaṃ dvija  Paus bhagavanmūrtibhede tu bhedabhinnopalakṣitam keśavādiṣvadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvena tricaturguṇam  Paus tantubhirviṣamaiviṣṇoḥ samasya parivarjayet pavitrikī kriyā yasmādviṣamā sā na kasyacit  Paus pavitrakāṇi kāryāṇi tantubhistaiḥ sutānitaiḥ mantrāstrakumbhayoḥ pūrvaṃ nānāmantrālayasya ca  Paus maṇḍalākhyapradhānasya tadgatastayākhilasya ca karṇikāsthasya ca vibhoḥ kesaracchadagasya ca  Paus vibhavavyūharūpasya lāñchanā stradvayasya ca mūrdhni kaṇṭhe sayoḥ puṣpapūjāyāmupari kṣitau  Paus pramāṇena jagannāthapratimāyāṃ catuṣṭayam dvayaṃ hi kuṇḍānalayoḥ śāstrapīṭhasya ca dvayam  Paus lipervāktattvabhūtasya śabdatattvasya ca prabhoḥ ghaṇṭākṣasūtrapūrvāṇāṃ kriyāṅgānāṃ mahātmānām  Paus jāyāyāṃ bhaktinamrāyāṃ raktāyāmarcane hareḥ saṃbandhināṃ ca mitrāṇāṃ bhagavaddharmasevinām  Paus taduttarasahāyānāṃ cāturātmyābhilāṣiṇām bhṛtyānāṃ svānukūlānāṃ puruṣottamayājinām  Paus vṛddhaye yoṣitā caiva pavitrīkaraṇāya ca pavitrīkaraṇaṃ ramyaṃ racanīyaṃ yathākramam  Paus ṣaḍadhvapīṭhasaṃsthasya nānāprantrāspadasya ca jñānādiguṇabhedasya catuḥsthānārcanāya ca  Paus mukhyamantrasya ca vibhoḥ śatenāṣṭādhikena ca tantunā bhūṣaṇaṃ kuryādardhenāṃśena vābjaja  Paus japahomadikā saṃkhyā pūrṇā riktā tadātmanā samīkaroti bhaktānāṃ mantrāṇāmata eva hi  Paus hemasadratnakarpūramālayakṣodakuṅkumaiḥ sarvauṣadhisamopetaistvagelādivimiśritaiḥ  Paus pāvanairvividhairdravyairnirvyājapicunā saha kuryāttadbharbharacanāṃ sūtrasaṃkhyopalakṣitām  Paus bījapūravadabjākṣa ārdrāmalakaśaṅkhavat tadantarālāni punastvavicchinnena tu tantunā  Paus vibhāgapratipatyarthaṃ granthanīyānyadūrataḥ yathecchayā tato nyeṣo yājyānāṃ parikalpya ca  Paus sūtrabhramasamopetairgabhairbhūṣaṇasaṃcayam ārādhakasya ca guroḥ sagarbhaṃ bhūṣaṇadvayam  Paus vihitaṃ bhagavanmantranyāsāttādātmyabhāvanāt ato nyeṣāmagarbhaṃca racanīyaṃ pavitrakam  Paus antarālagataṃ garbhaṃ kuryādbāhlīkarañjitam alaṃkṛtyaṃ ca sauvarṇerūpariṣṭācca rūpakaiḥ  Paus patracchedasamatthaistu jātarūpamayaistu vā śaṅkhacakragadāpadmamālāśrīvatsakaustubhaiḥ  Paus khageśatālamusalanandakajyāhalādikaiḥ mandārakusumākāraiḥ pārijātadrumopamaiḥ  Paus śrīvṛkṣācalanāgendrasvastikaiścāmarairghaṭaiḥ vedhānalārciṣāḍhyā ca vyañjanairātapatrakaiḥ  Paus saritsamudravṛṣabhabhaugajālaistu sārasaiḥ ekasyaiva bahunāṃ vā yathāsthānānurūpataḥ  Paus dhātuje pittale bhāṇḍe vastracchanne nidhāya ca dhādayedupariṣṭācca dhūpitenāhatena ca  Paus kṛtāhniko dhivāsārthaṃ daśabhyāṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ deśikendradvitīyastu kartārdhyakusumodyataḥ  Paus saha sadbrahmaghoṣeṇa stutimaṅgalapāḍhakaiḥ śaśāṅkodayavelāyāṃ kṛtvā dvāsthārcanaṃ viśan  Paus vairājabhuvanākāraṃ maṇḍapaṃ maṇḍanāṅkitam upaviśya yathānyāyamanataryāgānatamārabhet  Paus nyāsapūrvamaśeṣaṃ tu ardhyāmbuparikalpanam gaṇeśābhyarcanaṃ kṛtvā nirvighnaphalasiddhaye  Paus kalpayedbrahmakūrcaṃ tu śodhayedvasudhāṃ tataḥ sthāpanaṃ toraṇādīnāmarcanaṃ kuṇḍasaṃskṛtiḥ  Paus mantrāstrakumbharacanā tayormantrāvatāraṇam tadarcanādikaṃ sarvaṃ kuryāddīkṣāvidheḥ samam  Paus vyāpāramācareddivyaṃ kumbhakena smaran vibhum nāniśaṃ yujyate yasmāttasmādeṣā pratikriyā  Paus vibhāvyā mantriṇā kaiṃbhī āstrī rakṣārthameva hi tato vatārya bhagavānvantaṃ sthaṇḍile bhyarcya cāsanam  Paus japāntamakhilaṃ kṛtvā prayāyādbimbasannidhim aṣṭāṅgena namaskṛtya yadyādardhyaṃ tu mūrdhani  Paus anulepanasaṃyuktaṃ tataḥ puṣpāñjaliṃ śubham sāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ bhaktyā dhapūyet puruṣottamam  Paus puṣpapūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ madhyāhne yadvinirmitam apāsyādāya śirasā abhivandya samarcya ca  Paus viṣvaksenasya cāstreṇa nirmalīkṛtya vāriṇā sapīṭhaṃ bhagavadbiṃbaṃ prāsādaṃ śodhayettataḥ  Paus snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā brahmakūrcādikaiḥ snānairmantrādānaprakalpitaiḥ  Paus padārthasaṃmitaiḥ śaktyā yathāvadadhivāsitaiḥ phalai ratnādikopetaiḥ pūjayedvidhinā tataḥ  Paus bhaktyā kramopadiṣṭaistu bhogaiḥ kṛtsnairakṛtrimaiḥ sarvaṃ kṛtvā praṇāmāntaṃ yāyādhomaniketanam  Paus tatrānalaṃ ca saṃskṛsya kuryādvai mantratarpaṇam kalaśa sthārcabaimbīya saṃskṛtenātha vahninā  Paus caruṃ saṃśrapayecculyāṃ hṛdā kṣīrājyataṇḍulaiḥ samuddhṛtyājyapūtaṃ taṃ vinivedya yathākramam  Paus kalaśasthalavṛttīnāmekāṃśaṃ juhuyāttataḥ dadyātpūrṇāhutiṃ paścādbalibhiḥ sarvamantaram  Paus tarpayitvāmbusiktābhiḥ krameṇa juhuyāttataḥ tadvadājyaṃ supūrṇaṃ taṃ tad mudrābandhādikaṃ tu vai  Paus kṛtvā praṇāmaparyantaṃ sthalastasyāgrato vibhoḥ astramantreṇa saṃprokṣya kṛtsnadravyagaṇa tataḥ  Paus niveśya vāyudigbhāge sarvaṃ sūtrapuraḥsaram sitavastrānvitenaiva tvakṣetenaiva varmaṇā  Paus arcayitvāstramantreṇa sthagayet kavacena caṃ bahiḥ pakṣasamopetaṃ sarvamiṣvaṣṭakaṃ tataḥ  Paus digvidikṣvastrajaptaṃ tu dattvājyamanalālaye pañcaraṅgeṇa sūtreṇa dṛḍheṇa susitena vā  Paus prādakṣiṇacatuṣkaṃ tu smaran varma samāpayet grāsādasyāntarādbāhyādveṣṭayettadvadeva hi  Paus prāṅmukhastvāsanārūḍho gurupāṇiparicyutam brahmakarcaṃ pibet paścāccaruśeṣaṃ tu bhakṣayet  Paus pibeddhṝdayasaṃjaptaṃ hemaratnakuśodakam adyāttadanu tāmbūlaṃ dantakāṣṭhasamanvitam  Paus kutape kambalopete sthitvā ca sakuśāstare japenmantravaraṃ sāṅgaṃ paṭhan stotravarān śubhān  Paus kathāṃ sarveśvarīṃ puṇyāṃ kurvanniṣpādha maṇḍalam karmaśeṣaṃ tadāpādya bhūṣaṇānāṃ yathoditam  Paus ekādaśyāṃ prabhāte tu snānapūrvaṃ tu pūjanam sampūrṇāhutidānāntaṃ hutvā samyagyathāvidhi  Paus āsādya kalaśoddeśaṃ vinivedanamācaret tato viśeṣabhogānāṃ prabhorāmantraṇāya ca  Paus dantakāṣṭhaṃ satāmbūlaṃ mukhavāsāṃsi darpaṇam candanādīni gandhāni jātipūgaphalāni ca  Paus viniveśya nidhāyāgre dakṣiṇe tha jaga tprabhoḥ guggulaṃ mṛṣṭadhūpaṃ ca prakāśaṃ tāmrapātragatam  Paus dṛkprabhāmaṇḍanaṃ caiva hemasūtraṃ sakaṅkaṇam madhvājyapūrite pātre taijase rocanāñjanam  Paus rasaṣaṭkaṃ mahāmūrternetravastre sitāruṇe paścime tha vibhordadyāt puvyanadyudakaṃ tathā  Paus tīrthatoyānnābhogārthaṃ nagamṛt śrīphalādi yat śāḍvalaṃ nīladarbhāṃśca tāmrapātre tu vāyase  Paus uttare tha vibhordadyāddevadevasya puṣkara mālyānyoṣadhayaḥ sapta bījāni ca phalāni ca  Paus tilataṇḍulapātrāṇi kṣīraṃ dadhirasaṃ ghṛtam gandhavṛndatvagelādyaṃ dhātavo gairikādayaḥ  Paus saphalaṃ nārikelaṃ ca vikārastvaikṣavo khilaḥ sarājate kāṃsyapātre saṃbhave sati padṛmaja  Paus yajñaparṇapuṭe vāpi vinivedyamasaṃbhave sakuśodakamanyeṣāṃ tāmbūlaṃ dantadhāvanam  Paus sitāni sottarīyāṇi upavītāni candanam kuṅkumāgurukarpūraśrīkhaṇḍairadhivāsitam  Paus catuḥ sthānāvatīrṇasya dadyādtrandhapavitrakam tatordhyapuṣpadhūpaṃ ca mudrābandhaṃ samācaret  Paus ādimadhyāvasāne tu samyāgacchidraśāntaye japenmantravaraṃ sāṅgaṃ paścādvaddhāñjaliḥ paṭhet  Paus praṇavadavidyayādyaṃ dvayādyaṃ tu strotramantraṃ nivedayet sarvamantramayānanta nityasaṃnihitāvyaya  Paus guṇapradhāna yogeśa bhāvanābhogavigraha nārāyaṇaṃ paraṃ brahma prāṇeśa caturākṛte  Paus sarvagācyuta sanmūrte sarvajña puraṣottama asmātkālalavādyāvadvisarjanadināvadhi  Paus nānāmantragaṇopetaḥ sannidhiṃ bhaja me prabho devabimbe tu tanmūrtau kalaśe maṇḍalakṣitau  Paus saṃkhyāsūtre kṣasūtre ca pāvake guruvigrahe ghaṇṭāyāṃ śāstrapīṭhe ca yāgopakaraṇeṣu ca  Paus sruksruvādyeṣvaśeṣeṣu ekāntidvijamūrtiṣu viṣṇu pāṣadabhedeṣu janmakarmarateṣu ca  Paus śraddhāpūteṣu dakṣeṣu tvadekaśaraṇeṣu ca atīta vātsarīyāṇāṃ snānādīnāṃ hi karmaṇām  Paus naimittikānāṃ nityānāmapūrṇānāṃ hi śāntaye tvatprītaye yathāśāstramadya nirvartayāmyaham  Paus pāvitrakaṃ vidhānaṃ ca sarvakarmaprapūraṇam atoyaṃ mukhavāsādyamupacāraṃ hi carcitam  Paus homāntamadhivāsīyaṃ kuru sarvaṃ hi cātmasāt tvāmarcayāmyahaṃ bhaktyā suptyatīte tu jāgare  Paus yathāvadbrahmasūtrāntaibhogairbhogāpavargada vijñaptosīha bhagavan vetsi sarvaṃ hṛdi sthitam  Paus bhaktasya mama vātsalyāt prāptaḥ kāryastvanugrahaḥ evaṃ nimantrayitvājamaṣṭāṅgena namet kṣitau  Paus catuḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya hṛdi mantramanusmaran gītānṛttādikaiḥ stotrairvedapāṭhasamanvitaiḥ  Paus jayaśabdasametaistu jāgareṇa nayenniśām snātvā brāhmamūhūrte tha kṛtakautukamaṅgalaḥ  Paus mahatā vibhavena prāk dvārayāgaṃ samācaret yathāvadbhagavadyāgaṃ kuryāttadanu pauṣkara  Paus sāṃsparśikai rāsanādyairvividhairaupacārikaiḥ hṛdayaṅgamasaṃjñaistu bahubhedavinirmitaiḥ  Paus bhakṣyairbhojyaistathā lehyaiścoṣyainānāvidhairapi ṣaḍṛtuprabhavaiḥ sarvaiḥ śākairmūlaiḥ phalaiḥ śubhaiḥ  Paus pāvanaiḥ pāvakasvinnairupadaṃśādikānvitaiḥ gosaṃbhavaiḥ sthiraiḥ kāṃsyapātrairmadhvājyapūritaiḥ  Paus rasālakṣīrasaṃpūrṇairdiksthitaistu samudravat mātrāvittaiḥ satāmbūlairantarmānairyathocitaiḥ  Paus varaśayyāsametaistu pāvanairātmavallabhaiḥ svadeśaparadeśotthaiḥ krīḍābhogairakṛttimaiḥ  Paus jātarūpamayaiḥ pātrairgandhamālyādyalaṅkṛtaiḥ japamudrāvasānāntamevaṃ maṇḍalasannidhau  Paus kṛtvā tu bhagavadyāgaṃ viśeṣāddevamandire atha bhūṣaṇapātraṃ tu ādāyoddhāṭyapūjya ca  Paus pavitrakaṃ samādāya yāyātkalaśasaṃnidhim ārādhanāṅganicayamavyaktaṃ tāttvikaṃ hi yat  Paus tṛtīyamubhayātmaṃ vai adhyātmaditrayaṃ tathā anusandhāya vai tasmin saṃsmaran hṛdayāddhiyā  Paus tatrāṣṭāṣṭakasaṃkhyaṃ tu avyaktaṃ bhogasaṃgraham mantramudrāsamūhaṃ tu tāttvikaṃ parikīrtitam  Paus svādhyāyagītavādyāni vratāni niyamāni ca dānānyutsavapūrvāṇi nānānaimittikāni ca  Paus etānyubhayarūpāṇi puruṣārthapradāni ca prītidāni jagadhānau mantramūrtau janārdane  Paus bhāsvaraṃ cinmayaṃ śuddhaṃ yadeṣāṃ rūpamakṣayam tadbharbheṣvanusandheyaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tadanu pauṣkara  Paus sūryenduvahnisaṃkāśam iyattā parikalpitam tadgranthigaṇadeśeṣu bhāvanīyaṃ mahāmate  Paus susthūlaṃ vyāvahāryaṃ ca tṛtīyaṃ sārvalaukikam tattantunicayoddeśe bhāvanīyaṃ sadaiva hi  Paus evamādhyātmikī vyaptiṃ lakṣayitvā tu pauṣkara cintayeddhidevākhyāṃ vyāptiṃ māntrīmmanaśvarīm  Paus caturṇāmavinābhāvi yadrūpamamṛtopamam nānābhāsagaṇākīrṇaṃ mūrtāmūrtamanaśvaram  Paus kirīṭamālāśrīvatsakaustubhānāṃ mahāmate sannidhiṃ bhāvayennityāmmadhidevātmanā trayam  Paus pṛkhyaptejo nilākāśapañcānāṃ samudāyiyat ramaṇīyaṃ śubhaṃ rūpaṃ bhaktānāṃ paritoṣakṛt  Paus tadasya cādhibhūtatvaṃ mantavyaṃ yojanāvidhau dhyātvaivaṃ mūlamantrānte samudīryābjasaṃbhava  Paus praṇavālaṃkṛtaṃ mantraṃ tamudyatakaraḥ paṭhet tvatprāptisādhanaṃ deva jñānaṃ yadamalaṃ param  Paus bhaktiśraddhāsamopetā satkriyā svatprakāśikī akhaṇḍasiddhaye tasyā hyupāyaḥ kathitastvaya  Paus jñānakarmaprasaktānāṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām pavitrākhyaṃ yathāśaktyā tvatprasādānmayā kṛtam  Paus yathocitamidānīṃ tāṃ dhyāyasva parameśvarīm tasmācchubhataraṃ karma vijñānamamalaṃ hi yat  Paus vidhyantaraṃ mantragaṇād dravyasaṅghastvameva hi prāptiḥ pūrayitā pūrṇamapūrṇānāṃ hi karmaṇām  Paus taśyenānena bhagavan bhavabhaṅgārditasya ca aśaṭhasya kriyākāṇḍamakhaṇḍaṃ sarvamastu te  Paus vijñapto sīha bhagavan arthitā me parā tvayi vinā tvatparitoṣeṇa samyak jñānapradena ca  Paus āpatkāle tu saṃprāpte buddhipūrvaṃ mayācyuta na santyājyaṃ kriyājñānaṃ tvaṃ sarvaṃ vetsi tattvataḥ  Paus yathākālaṃ yathāvacca bhogairdeva yathocitaiḥ nārcito si yathā samyak khedaścetasi tena me  Paus pūjanaṃ bhogasaṃbhogairājyadohaistu tarpaṇam tvayyetatkṛtakṛtyānāṃ na kiñcidupayujyate  Paus sukṣetravāpitaṃ hyetadakhilārthasya maikhilam phaliṣyatyamṛtatvena jñātvaivaṃ hi purā mayā  Paus aṅgīkṛtaṃ gurumukhāt kintu sarveśvara prabho parisphurati me buddhau na nirvyūḍhaṃ yathāsthitam  Paus manovākkāyakarmaistu āprabhātāmṛniśāvadhi asvātantryādasāmarthyānmanasaścānavasthite  Paus śītoṣṇavātavarṣādyairantarāyairjvarādikaiḥ asampatteḥ kriyāṅgānāṃ deva tvadunarūpiṇām  Paus āpravṛtteḥ parānandaprāptiniṣṭhaṃ yathāhnikam yathoktamamarāṇāṃ tu yasmānna ghaṭate tvataḥ  Paus tasya saṃpūraṇārthaṃ tu pradhānataramarcanam pavitrakākhyamādiṣṭaṃ vatsaraṃ prati yattvayā  Paus tanmayā kṛtamadhyakṣamarcitaṃ yadanirmalam kriyāyogādasaṃpūrṇaṃ tanme nirmalatāṃ naya  Paus jñānato  jñānato vāpi yathoktaṃ na tu tanmayā tatsarvaṃ pūrṇamevāstu sutṛpto bhava sarvadā  Paus omacyuta jagannātha mantramūrte sanātana rakṣa māṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa kṣamasvāja prasīda om  Paus uktavaivaṃ mūlamantraṃ tu hṛdādyairlāñchanaiḥ saha samuddiśya tato dadyānmūrdhni mantrātmano vibhoḥ  Paus sarvajñānakriyābhogaśubhasaṃkalpavigraham maṇḍalāntargatasyaivaṃ prāsādāntaḥsthitasya ca  Paus vahnimadhyagatasyāpi samāropya mahāmate arcanena puṭīkṛtya pāvanaṃ ca pavitrakam  Paus yāgopakaraṇānāṃ ca dattvā śāstrātmanastataḥ deśikasya hṛdāropya pūjitasya ca devavat  Paus parituṣṭena tenātha tasya sarvārthasiddhaye sāśiṣaṃ hi sadārabhya saṃsthitasyāgnisannidhau  Paus havanāntercanānte vā hyanyeṣāṃ kramaśastu vai tataḥ prāvaraṇairdānairyathāsaṃpatti saṃbhṛtaiḥ  Paus sopavītottarīyaiśca chattropānatsamāyutaiḥ vividhairbhojanairvipra dhūpaiścālabhanādikaiḥ  Paus pūjayedbrāhmaṇān sarvān susūpāyāṃstathā yatīn trirātrādatha saptāhādupasaṃhṛtya pauṣkara  Paus mahadarcanapūrvaṃ tu kṛtvā pūrṇāvasānikam kramaśaścopasaṃhṛtya svayaṃ gurvātmanāthavā  Paus ādāya pūjite pātre arcayitvā yathāvidhi jānu nī bhūgate kṛtvā praṇipatya ca deśikam  Paus mānayitvārdhyapuṣpādyaiḥ praṇipatya svayaṃ purā vinivedya ca tatpātraṃ prasādaḥ kriyātāṃ vibho  Paus sāśiṣaṃ bhagavatprītirvācyācāryeṇa tasya tu yathāgamaṃ yathāśāstraṃ prasādāccaturātmanaḥ  Paus tvayi sāṃvatsaraṃ vipra susaṃpūrṇaṃ tadastu te samutkīrtayatastasya āsanasthasya mūrdhani  Paus kalaśadvitayaṃ mantraṃ rakṣāsaubhāgyamokṣadam visarjanaṃ vibhoḥ kuryāt pūjāpūrvaṃ yathākramam  Paus viṣvaksenaṃ yajet sāṅgaṃ tarpayettadanantaram samāhṛtyākhilaṃ paścāt kṛte vai tadvisarjane  Paus prakalpya pūrvavatsomapānamacchidrasiddhaye rukmarājatasadratnaghaṭite vā vibhūṣite  Paus cakrādhāre tu kalaśe vitate kamalodare pāñcajanyavalīgrīve śatapatraśubhānane  Paus ūdhvārdhaḥ kaumudīmālāmaṇḍalālaṃkṛte bjaja makarānanaśeṣābhiramṛtāmbupravāhake  Paus nadī samudraśrīvṛkṣamīnamālyaiḥ pariṣkṛte evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktā kte vibhorārādhanāya ca  Paus pādyārdhyācamanasnānadāne sāvatsarotsave tathā sahasrakalaśairabhiṣekavidhāvapi  Paus ityuktamaravindākṣa pavitrāropaṇaṃ param ūnātiriktādyadyati bhuvi bhaktajanaṃ sadā  Paus tasya nirvartanādmaktyā brāhmaṇo vedavidyavet śrīmānatyugraśaśaktirvai kṣattiyo cchinnasantatiḥ  Paus dhanadhānyayuto vaiśyaḥ śudrastu sukhavān bhavet gobhūsuvarṇadānānāmanantānāṃ hi yatphalam  Paus yāvajjīvaṃ pradatrānāṃ pratyahaṃ tu samāḥ śatam paramāyuṣi saṃpūrṇe tatphalaṃ prāpanuyānnaraḥ  Paus prāptakālaḥ svabudhyā tu āsādyāyatanaṃ hareḥ smaranmantreśvaraṃ samyak samyak sṛjati vigraham  Paus yānaiścandra pratīkāśairdivyastrījanasaṃyutaiḥ vījyamāno divaṃ yāti pūjyamānastathāmaraiḥ  Paus bhuktvā bhogāṃstu vipulān sarvalokāntarodbhavān kālena mahatā sādya mānuṣyaṃ punareva hi  Paus śubhe kāle śubhe deśe jāyate ca śubhe kule nivṛtte bālyabhāve tu vyakte karaṇasaṃgrahe  Paus buddhitattve prabuddhe tu janmābhyāsavaśāttu vai karmaṇā manasā vācā nārāyaṇaparo bhavet  Paus nityaṃ kriyāparo dhīmān brahmaṇyaḥ satyavikramaḥ ananyathā viśuddhātmā duṣṭasaṅgavivarjitaḥ  Paus vyādhiśokavinirmuktaḥ putradārādikairyutaḥ apamṛtyuvinirmukto jñānamāsādya nirmalam  Paus śvetadvīpaṃ samāyāti surāṇāṃ yatsudurlabham jñānināmapi cānyeṣāṃ tatra dṛṣṭvā jagatpatim  Paus paraṃ brahmatvamāyāti tatkarmaparamaḥ pumān paśyantyāropyamāṇaṃ ye brahmasūtraṃ jagatprabhoḥ  Paus tathānumodayantyanye yānti te pyamarāvatīm śruṇvanti ye vidhānaṃ tu pavitraṃ pāpanāśanam  Paus prāpnuvanti ca te puvyamiṣṭāpūrtādikaṃ hi yat nārīhyananyaśaraṇā patinā paricoditā  Paus tadbhaktā sā satī sādhvī karmaṇā manasā girā nityaṃ bhartari cādrohā prayatā sāṅgatena vai  Paus pavittakaṃ jagadyonerāropayaticābjaja sātulaṃ caiva saubhāgyaṃ prāpnuyādacireṇa tu  Paus dehānte devanārīṇāṃ devānāṃ yāti pūjyatām sātvarundhatipūrvāṇāmavā vī k samabhivīkṣate  Paus jñānamāsādayatyante yena yāntya tya ttyutaṃ padam prottārayati bandhūnāṃ duṣkṛtebhyo bjasaṃbhava  Paus pitṝṇāṃ janakādīnāṃ nāmnā snehapurastu yaḥ dadāti bhūṣaṇaṃ vipra mantrī mantrātmano vibhoḥ  Paus durgateḥ sugatiṃ yāti dyusindhorasthirā naraḥ yathā surāṇāmamṛtaṃ nṛṇāṃ gāṅgaṃ jalaṃ yathā  Paus svadhā yathā pitṝṇāṃ ca karmiṇāṃ tadvadabjaja pavitrakaṃ kriyāḍhyānāṃ pāvanaṃ bhūtivardhanam  Paus sarvadoṣabhayaghnaṃ ca sarvopadravanāśanam sarvasaukhyapradaṃ caiva sarvaguhyaprakāśakam  Paus yaḥ samyagbhagavadbhaktaḥ kṛtamantraparigrahaḥ evamave pravṛttau vā janmābhyāsātsadārcane  Paus ananyatvena vai viṣṇoḥ parasya paramātmanaḥ prayatnenārthanīyaṃ ca mahatānena deśikaḥ  Paus asannidhānāt svagurorabhāvāttasya cābjaja pravartanīyamanyena guruṇābhyarthitena ca  Paus karmaṇā manasā vācā netarasyādhamasya ca nānyadarśanasaṃsthastu madbhaktaistatparāyaṇaiḥ  Paus pavitrārohaṇādīnāmarthanīyo hi deśikaḥ māmatipratipannaṃ ca antastho vetti yadyapi  Paus kṛtārthamatibhaktatvādamuṃ manye tadā gurum prāptamuttārakaṃ śiṣyo manye bhaktivaśād gurum  Paus yatraiva cittavṛttīnāṃ sāmyamasti trayasya ca śiṣyadeśikamantrāṇāṃ tantramokṣaśca siddhayaḥ  Paus jñātvaivaṃ yastu bhaktānāmabhaktaḥ saṃpravartate mantradāne ca śiṣyāṇāṃ saṃ yāti narake dhamaḥ  Paus pratyakṣameti bhaktānāṃ bhaktiḥ prāgarjitā śanaiḥ tatsamparkasamācārān mantradaivatanindanāt  Paus tasmādviṣayasaṃbhūtaṃ yasya yadviṣayaṃ sphuṭam pareṣāmātmanaścāpi tasya tatsiddhidaṃ smṛtam  Paus yatrāsti deśikānāṃ ca bhaktiravyabhicāriṇī tatraiva yadi śiṣyāṇāmabhilāṣo sti pūjane  Paus tadā mantravaraḥ prītaḥ sannidhiṃ kurutabjaja siddhasya samabuddher vai niṣkriyasya tu yā kriyā  Paus ato nyasya kriyāṃ viddhi bhaktipūrvā tu sā smṛtā yā ca tadviṣayā bhaktiḥ pativṛttisamocitā  Paus aṣṭāṅgalakṣaṇā pūrṇā śraddhāpūtā ca mokṣadā ato nyā siddhidā siddhirvyabhicāraphalapradā  Paus sarvasyāhaṃ taṭastho hamāśayaṃ vedmi tattvataḥ bhaktirmā prati vai tābhyāṃ yadā hyavyabhicāriṇī  Paus mantrātmanānugṛhṇāmi śiṣya gurumukhena tu nābhaktena tvato bhakto dīkṣaṇīyaḥ kadācana  Paus nābhaktastvatibhaktena yojanīyastvadarcane guroraṃabhaktādbhaktānāṃ bhaktirabhyeti tāpanam  Paus śārīraṃ mānasaṃ duḥkhaṃ vardhate ca kṣaṇāt kṣaṇam bhāvamāsuratāmeti yena yātyadhamāṃ gatim  Paus guroraananyaśaraṇādbhaktānāṃ kamalodbhava dvividhaṃ trividhaṃ doṣamacirāt kṣayameti ca  Paus anugrāhyādabhaktācca sāvalepāt kriyojjhitāt gurorakīrtiṃ mahatīṃ vidveṣaṃ sahate na vai  Paus sāṃmukhyaṃ duḥsahānāṃ ca doṣāṇāṃ dikṣitasya ca tasmātsarvaprayatnena adṛṣṭaphalasiddhaye  Paus vihitaṃ yacca tatkāryaṃ śiṣyeṇa guruṇāpi ca nābhaktaḥ saṃvidāpnoti nābhakto dhyānamāpnuyāt  Paus lābhaktaḥ saṃtkriyāṃ vetti nābhaktaḥ śāstravidbhavet nābhaktamarcāṃ yāgaṃ ca vahnimarcāpayettathā  Paus bandhāpayennamudrāṃ ca śrāvayetsamayānna hi yo parādhena vā lobhādabhaktānāṃ jagadgurau  Paus viparyayārthavetṝṇāmapahārasaratātmanām abhigacchāpayenmohātsa yāti narakaṃ guruḥ  Paus prāyaścittaṃ hi pūrvoktaṃ tāpārto nācaredyadi ityuktamaravindottha yattvayā paricoditam  Paus bhaktānāmupakārātha pavitrārohaṇaṃ śubham prāvṛṭkāle pravṛtte tu trelīkyodaravartinām  Paus manuṣyāmarasiddhānāṃ vaktavyaṃ cānuvartinām pravartanti hi vegena śraddhayā vatsaraṃ prati  Paus mahatyasmin mahābuddhe vyāpāre pārameśvare vibhoḥ śayanasaṃsthasya kāle puṣphalākule  Paus gagane laṅghayamāne tu sabalākairvalāhakaiḥ kumudotpalakahlārairbhūṣite vasudhātale  Paus vanopavanaudyāne haritaiḥ śādvalādikaiḥ śālisasyādikairyukte palvalodakaśobhite  Paus pavitrakaṃ kṛtaṃ viṣṇorantaḥ sthasyātitu ṣṭidam tasya prāgvihitā vipra satataṃ śayanakriyā  Paus athoktadivase tābhyāṃ brahmannirvartite sati rakṣaṇīyamavaśyaṃ vai karmayāgaṃ kriyāparaiḥ  Paus iti śrīpāñcarātte mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃpavitrārohaṇaṃ nāma triṃśo dhyāyaḥ atha ekatriṃśo dhyāyaḥśrībhagavānuvāca pavitrārohaṇaṃ kṛtvā cāturmāsyaṃ mahāmate nirvahaṇīyaṃ niyamairvividhairlokapūjitaiḥ  Paus śayanaṃ devadevīyam arcayet tad vidhiṃ śṛṇu hemādiratnaravacite sarvāṅgapariśobhite  Paus bhagavatyanurūpe ca śayane śaśivāsite sitātapatracamarakiṅkiṇīvaramaṇḍite  Paus vaijayantīgaṇopete hemadaṇḍāṅghribhūṣite vitānakena divyena kuṅkumādyairvibhūṣite  Paus śobhite copariṣṭāttu tiryagūrdhvapaṭāvṛte jātīphalādikairlājasarvabījādipūrite  Paus vidik citrapaṭairyukte satpuṣpaprakarīkṛte ratnadīpasamāyukta ityasmin śayane smaret  Paus śrīrodārṇavamadhyasthaṃ sahastraphaṇamaulinam himakundendudhavalaṃ nāganāthaṃ mahāmate  Paus praṇavena svanāmnā ca varṇāntena sabindunā dhyātvārcayitvā stutvā ca namaskṛtya prasādya ca  Paus niveśya tasmin karmārcāṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣitam śrīkhaṇḍaśāśibāhlīkaviliptāṃ puṣpaveṣṭitām  Paus prāvṛtāṃ netravastreṇa mṛṣṭarūpaiḥ sudhūpitām svabījaṃ mantravarṇaṃ tu oṃ lakṣmīpataye namaḥ  Paus samudīrya dhiyā cārdhyam aṅgopāṅgakrameṇa tu dvādaśākṣaravarṇaistu svanāmapadasaṃyutaiḥ  Paus karmārcāyā abhāvāttu darbhamañjarijaṃ śubham yathoktena vidhānena viṣṭare viniveśya ca  Paus tasmin mantravaraṃ nyasya svapadmagaganodarāt nilīnākhila gaṇḍādiśaktipañjaramadhyagam  Paus vyaktīnāṃ mūrtidānena nītvā dhyānānvitena ca devāṅgamahitaṃ vastram abhuktam amalātmakam  Paus kṣtvopari samabhyarcya puṣpadhūpavilepanaiḥ sarvatatrvopasaṃhāraṃ citaḥ śaktiṃ tu vinyaset  Paus dakṣiṇe tvabhimānākhyāṃ mūrtiṃ tu camarodyatām evaṃ jñānaniśāṃ vāme tālavṛntakarodyatām  Paus uttamāṃ bhāvayen nidrāṃ karasaṃvāhane ratām pādāravindadeśasthāṃ lālayantīṃ karāmbujaiḥ  Paus ādāya caraṇe divye sākṣāchrīḥ sannidhisthitā ānandaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ tasyai devādhidevatā  Paus tadantaḥ smaraṇānandajātavismayalocanāḥ svanāmapadamantraistāḥ saṃpūjyāḥ praṇavādibhiḥ  Paus evaṃ hi devadevīyaṃ śayanaṃ kamalodbhava yathoktaṃ saṃpratiṣṭhāpya cāturmāsyaparairnaraiḥ  Paus kāryātra pratyahaṃ pūjā mārjanaṃ copalepanam mṛdā dhātuvikārairvā sugandhaiścandanādikaiḥ  Paus pradānaṃ dhūpadīpānāṃ vyajanenānilotthitaḥ śaśicandanasaṃyuktaśītalodaka satkriyāḥ  Paus kadalīdalakahlāraiḥ padmotpalavimiśritaiḥ svedaśāntiṃ samāpādya paunaḥpunyena pūjanam  Paus veṇuvīṇāsamopetāṃ gītiṃ ca madhurasvarām evaṃ māsadvaye yāte jāte megharave mbarāt  Paus brahman bhādrapade māsi dvādaśyāṃ hi niśāmukhe īṣat prabodham āśritya devadevo hyadhokṣajaḥ  Paus sthityartham amarāṇāṃ ca parivartanam ācaret dakṣiṇenāṅgasaṅghena tyaktvā cottānaśāyikām  Paus yoganidrāṃ samāśritya prakurvan prabhavāpyayau maruccakrākṣasaṃsthasya viśvabījasya pauṣkara  Paus mūlendumaṇḍalāccātha apāsyācchādanāmbaram āste tvāśvayuje tveṣa dvādaśyāṃ parameśvaraḥ  Paus saṃtyajecchayanaṃ divyaṃ niśāyāṃ kārtikasya tu ca utthāyāmaranāthaśca samākramya patatrirāṭ  Paus niḥśeṣabhuvanagrāmavīthīnāṃ doṣaśāntaye vicaratyaprameyātmā nandayaṃstān surādikān  Paus āvīkṣayañjagatyasmin svakṛtaṃ dharmapaddhatim evaṃ bhaktajanaiḥ kāryaṃ tasya tacceṣṭitaṃ maham  Paus vividhairutsavairdānajapajāgaraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ nṛtragītasamopetairvilāsairhāsyasaṃyutaiḥ  Paus krīḍamānaiḥ sumanasaiḥ prayataiḥ praṇataiḥ prabhoḥ ekadeśasthitairvipra ananyamānasaiḥ sadā  Paus māsaśeṣaṃ taponiṣṭhaiḥ samarthaiḥ punareva hi svāśrame vāmarakṣetre rakṣaṇīyaṃ mahājanaiḥ  Paus brahman dvādaśarātreṇa ṣaḍrātreṇa śubhena ca vā  asāmarthyaṃ trirātreṇa ahorātreṇa vābjaja  Paus nayen naktāśanenātha catvāryete śubhavratāḥ māsopavāsaniratairnaraiḥ paramavaiṣṇavaiḥ  Paus ante tridvayekarātraṃ vā kāryam acyutajāgaram puṇyākhyānakathābhistu stotrapūrvaistu gītakaiḥ  Paus savādyairmadhurairnṛttairapahāsaiḥ tu irṣadaiḥ jayaśabdairnamaskāraiḥ karatālasamanvitaiḥ  Paus samarcayecchrīnivāsaṃ juhvān dhyāyan japannapi bhogaiḥ ṣaḍrasapūrvaistu sūpūrṇaiśaipacārikaiḥ  Paus ardhyairvilepanairmālyairmṛṣṭadhūpasamanvitaiḥ brāhme muhūrte dvāśyāṃ mantramūrtiṃ yajeddharim  Paus śaṅkhadhvānasamopetairdundubhīpaṭahasvanaiḥ vandivṛndotthitoccābhirnānāvāgbhirmahāmate  Paus mahājayajayārāvaiḥ punaḥpunarudīritaiḥ prabodhalakṣaṇaistotrairutthāpya śayanāttataḥ  Paus mahatā vibhavenātha maṇḍalādau yajetkramāt mahatsnapanapūrvaistu bhogaiḥ pūṇairyathoditaiḥ  Paus mahādīpaiḥ prabhūtaistu sāṅkuraiḥ pālikāgaṇaiḥ phalaiḥ panasapūrvaistu madhvājyatilacarcitaiḥ  Paus puṣpārdhyacandanādyanatairbrahmasūtravibhūṣitaiḥ mālatīmallikāpūrvasamutthairmañjarīgaṇaiḥ  Paus kadambacūtaśrīvṛkṣaṛjuśākhāsamanvitaiḥ taraṇḍaiḥ sūtrasambadhaiḥ kuṅkumādyaiḥsupūjitaiḥ  Paus gobhūhemādikaidānaiścitraiḥ prāvaraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ evamiṣṭvā tu homāntaṃ grāmaṃ vā nagaraṃ gṛham  Paus sapavitreṇa yānena sacakreṇa śubhena vā mantrāstrakumbhayuktena tadbimbodarakeṇa vā  Paus brahmaghoṣasametena gītavādyānvitena ca gaṇikābhagavadbhaktāḥ sahanāgarikairjanaiḥ  Paus parivrāḍbrahmacārībhirjapastutiparāyaṇaiḥ mahatā ketuyuktena sitacchattrāvṛtena tu  Paus pradahan surabhiṃ dhūpaṃ pṛthak sāmyaṃ ca gugulum yānamevaṃ paribhramya draviṇaṃ cārthiṣu kṣipet  Paus tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya caturdhāṃ praṇipatya ca sarvāṅgairdaṇḍavad bhūmau bhaktyā tu puruṣotramam  Paus rathasthaṃ ālayasthaṃ tu cetasā saṃstuvan japan prakṣipan cārdhyapuṣpe tu lājān siddhārthakān phalān  Paus dṛṣṭaṃ yadeva digdevaṃ bhāvayet sarvadik tathā caṅkramedbhavanaṃ kṛtsnaṃ sthitiṃ badhnāti yena vai  Paus bhaktānāṃ bhagavān bhaktau dikkālādyair anāhataḥ etatpradakṣiṇaṃ nāma sāmānyaṃ sarvadehinām  Paus samabhyastaṃ parijñātaṃ dadāti padamācyutam jānubhyāṃ sahapāṇibhyāṃ jānubhyāṃ vā samācaret  Paus sakṛt saṃvatsarasyānte trisandhyādvādaśīṣu vā ekameva tathejyānte śirasāvanatena tu  Paus samabhyarcya tato bhāvam acirād eva karmiṇām phalaṃ yacchati dehānte kramāllokāstu vaibhavāḥ  Paus kṛtejyaḥ parayā bhaktayā praṇamyaivam adhokṣajam pradakṣiṇair arcanīyaṃ praṇipātasamanvitaiḥ  Paus sarvakṣetrābhigamanāt sarvatīrthāṭanāt tu vai phalaṃ dadāti bhagavān bhaktasya caraṇārcitam  Paus pradakṣiṇīkṛtā yena mūrtirmantrātmano hareḥ doṣaiḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya tyaktaḥ saṃbhavagairnareḥ  Paus bhagavat karmadīkṣāṇāṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām prakṛṣṭam etad vyāpāraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ śubhavartmani  Paus jñānagolakatulyatvāt cakravad bhramaṇāt tu vai pradadāti śubhaṃ nityaṃ kṣiṇoti kleśasaṃcayam  Paus bhagavat karmaniṣṭhānāṃ devāyatanavāsinām bhaktānām api vānyeṣāṃ karmavāg indriyātmakam  Paus antargarbhagṛhe viṣṇorgarbhād vā ānanamaṇḍape praṇipātagaṇaṃ kuryāt pradakṣiṇagaṇaṃ vinā  Paus vahnisthasya vibhoryasmāt pāṇipṛṣṭhasya darśanam doṣakṛnmantramūrtīnām evaṃ deham asiddhikṛt  Paus jānupradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā antaḥ sannikaṭe vibhoḥ viruddham aparaṃ vipra bhaktānāṃ caraṇabhramaḥ  Paus upānat pādukārūḍhacchatroṣṇīṣadharāstathā yānāśvaśibikāsaṃsthaḥ tāmbūlādyaṃ hi carvayan  Paus krīḍāpakṣihilādaṇḍadarpaṇaṃ vyañjanaṃ vahan prahasannathavāmodam ucchvasan pralapan bahu  Paus vilāsakelikrīḍāṃ ca kurvan kupitamānasaḥ tvarāviṣṭaḥ śubhārthī yo labhen nātra bhraman phalam  Paus ananyabuddhinā tasmāt tagdatenāntarātmanā kāryaṃ śubhepsunā nityaṃ gṛhāyatanayānage  Paus yasmād vai bhūriphaladam alpakleśaṃ mahāmate ekaberam anantaṃ ca mahāmokṣakaraṃ param  Paus evaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kṛtvā puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ avatārya rathānmāntraṃ cakrādhiṣṭhānapūrvakam  Paus pūjanīyaṃ punarapi mudrābaddhāñjaliṃ tataḥ tarpaṇīyamathājyādyairdadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ śubhām  Paus ardhyadhūpapradānādyaiḥ kṣamayet puruṣottamam yānapātraṃ tathā cchatraṃ pratipādya sadakṣiṇam  Paus śayanaṃ svagurorvipra dvijānāṃ tadasannidhau kṛtvā jānudvayaṃ bhūmau baddhāñjaliridaṃ paṭhet  Paus deva sarveśvarānāde karmaṇānena cākhilām śubhāṃ gatiṃ jano yātu prītiṃ tvaṃ paramāṃ bhaja  Paus bhojayed brāhmaṇān paścād vividhaiḥ pānabhojanaiḥ śraddhayā dakṣiṇāntaiśca tṛptyarthaṃ pitṛsantateḥ  Paus anuyāgaṃ tataḥ kuryād bandhubhṛtyasamānvitaḥ vibhave sati vābjottha kāryamevamanākulaiḥ  Paus draṣṭavyam amarairdevaṃ kṣetre brahmarathe sthitam grāmīye nāgare sthāne vimāne vā sthitaṃ prabhum  Paus ityevamuktaṃ bhaktānāṃ vidhānaṃ kaumudīyakam yasya sālokyatāpūrvaṃ phalaṃ bhāvavaśāt sthitam  Paus pavitrārohaṇādyaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām yudaktamevam akhilaṃ yathākamalasaṃbhava  Paus asvātantrād asāmarthyād vittābhāvāttu vā dvija dvādaśīṣvakhilāsvevaṃ kuryātsaṃvatsarāntare  Paus vārite pi niśāyāṃ tu cāturmāsye tu saṃyame bhaktairnirvahaṇīyaṃ ca tulābhāgāvasānikam  Paus prāk bhavetrulabho gāttu gastu dvādaśyāṃ vigataṃ yadi niśāyām ācaret kṛtsnaṃ pāramyaṃ tat titheryataḥ  Paus kuryādvratavaraṃ caiva pañcāhamubhayorapi ekādaśīpūrṇimānte tulādvai vṛścikāvadhi  Paus madhumāṃsaparityāgaṃ madirāstrīniṣevaṇam māraṇaṃ mṛgajātīnāṃ drumavicchedanaṃ tathā  Paus vanadāhaṃ ca vasudhāsvātaṃ kuddālakādinā tānaṃ gopaśūnāṃ ca vadhabandhādikaṃ nṛṇām  Paus niśāṭanam avarṇānāṃ vyavahāraṃ tu taiḥ saha mṛṣṭodanaṃ tu sābhyaṅgaṃ sarvaṃ yatnād vivarjayet  Paus upasaṃhāradivasād apare hani padmaja bhaktānām āstikānāṃ ca vihitaṃ vatsaraṃ prati  Paus kartavyam abhiṣekaṃ ca svastiśāntiśubhāptaye tasmād anugrahadhiyā kartācāryavareṇa tu  Paus jananyā janakenātha ṛtvigbhirvā vayo dhikaiḥ gurorasannidhānācca sādhakaḥ sādhakaistu vā  Paus bhadrāsane samāropya sāmbuje svastikāṅkite sūtrite navanābhe tu padme vāṣṭadale tataḥ  Paus kuṅkumādyairvilikhite kusumairvā supūrite netravastraiḥ paricchanne yathoktarajasā kṛte  Paus ghaṇṭāvidhānapūrṇaistu prāksthitairvā naṣairyute jātabījaśarāvaistu śubhapūrṇayavāṅkitaiḥ  Paus dadhidarpaṇasacchatrapuṣpaiḥ sanmāṅgalīyakaiḥ sarvabījādikaitsarvaiḥ sugandhaiḥ śrīphalādikaiḥ  Paus maṅgalyagītibhirvādyairbrahmaghoṣasamānvitaiḥ ācāryaiḥ pañcarātrajñairjapadhyānaparāyaṇaiḥ  Paus prabhavāpyayasadbrahmasadāgamamatasthitaiḥ alābuvīṇājalajairvaṃśaghaṇṭāravaiḥ saha  Paus jvālāsumanasaḥ pūrṇakumbhasadvṛkṣamañjarīḥ sākāravividhākanyālaṃkṛtaṃ yajñamandire  Paus dūrvādīnapi carvadbhirgovṛṣairbālavatsakaiḥ paritaścāvṛte gobhirvandivṛndasamākule  Paus vṛddhaye tu parāṃ lakṣmī sarvaśaktisamanvitām prāptaye tvācyutaṃ satyaṃ śāśvataṃ padamavyayam  Paus bhaktānāṃ vihitaṃ snānavidhinānena pauṣkara pūrvoddiṣṭena vidhinā adhivāsya yathākramam  Paus hemādyaṃ ratnakhacitaṃ prāguktaracanānvitam navakaṃ kalaśānāṃ tu nyastavyamudakodaram  Paus sarveṣāṃ varuṇaṃ tāvaddhayeyaṃ phaṇirathasthitam varadābhayahastaṃ ca progdirantaṃ sudhārasam  Paus svādvākhyaṃ kṣīrasaṃjñaṃ ca tu ekabhāvatvam āgatam vicitramakarārūḍhaṃ ratnapātrakarodyatam  Paus varapāṇiṃ samudraṃ ca dhyeyaṃ sarvatra cāmbuvat nārāyaṇāṅghrisaṃbhūtāṃ pūrve janaghaṭodvahām  Paus āgneye kacchapārūḍhāṃ yamunāṃ devapūjitām maṇḍūkāmbujasaṃsthāṃ ca dakṣiṇe tu sarasvatīm  Paus śanaiḥ pravāhasaṃjñāṃ ca pāśabandhavimokṣaṇīm nairṛte vṛṣabhasthāṃ ca paścime siṃhavaktrakām  Paus airāvatīṃ tu vāyavye kalaśe tu gajasthitām īśānapadmamadhye tra vitastāṃ mīnagāṃ ghaṭe  Paus narmadāṃ mahiṣārūḍhāṃ samāṅgāṃ devapūjitām vṛ dṛ ṣadvatīṃ devikāṃ ca paroṣṇīṃ baḍabāhvayām  Paus sindhuḥ kakupsu sarvāsu aṣṭāsu paritaḥ kramāt upakumbheṣu vābjasthāḥ sarvāstoyaghaṭodyatāḥ  Paus kusumaiḥstabakairyuktā jalamugdīryamānasāḥ vāsudevādimūrtiśaiḥ śatāṣṭaparimantritaiḥ  Paus pūjitairabhiṣekaṃ ca dadyāt sarvaphalāptaye dhyātvādhāre tu hemādye evaṃ cakragate mbuje  Paus nadīsamudravaruṇayathokte pūrvanirmite utkṛṣṭamuktāratnādaye svastikādyairvibhūṣite  Paus dvādaśārāsu māsekeśavādyairadhiṣṭite sarvāṅgadevatopete mantramanyaste pratiṣṭhite  Paus tadambunā tu vā kuryāt snānaṃ cāvabhṛthaṃ śubham pratyahaṃ tajjalaṃ mūrdhni dhāraṇād abhivādanāt  Paus mucyate sarvadoṣebhyo maṅgalyaṃ vṛddhimeva ca tīrthebhyastvāsamudrebhyo gaṅgādisarito gaṇāt  Paus snānotthaṃ phalamāpnoti bhāvitātmācyutāśrayī kṛte cāvabhṛthasnāne parituṣṭo tha sādhakaḥ  Paus bhagavatpadasidyarthaṃ gurupādāmbunā svayam dakṣiṇena kareṇaiva svamantraṃ manasā smaran  Paus mūrdhni saṃsicya śaṅkhākhyamudrayā cordhvavaktrayā ambusikte mbare pāsya paridhāyāpare tataḥ  Paus prāgvaduṣṇīṣapūrvaistu puṣpairgandhaistu bhūṣaṇaiḥ śarīram abhyalaṃkṛtya upaviśyāsane tataḥ  Paus yathoditaṃ purāstreṇa kuryānnirbhartsanaṃ tataḥ abhinandya kṛtanyāso maṅgalārdhyapurassarān  Paus nṛpopakaraṇān sarvān chatracāmarapaścimān deśikendrakarāt prāpya samutthāyāsanāt tataḥ  Paus namaskṛtya jagannāthaṃ parameśvaram acyutam analālayam āsādya deśikendreṇa vai saha  Paus puṣpastraggandhadhūpaiśca phalairbījaistu vā cā ñjalim pūrayitvārcanaṃ kṛtvā vibhorvahnigṛhāntare  Paus saṃsmaran hṛdi mantreśam upaviśyāgnisaṃmukham tato mantrābhijaptena sāmbunā viṣṭareṇa tu  Paus prāgvadāmastakāt sarvaṃ spṛśeddhayānadhiyā śuci kuryād vinyastadehaṃ tu dhyātvā mantraṃ karodare  Paus gandhapuṣpārdhyayuktaṃ tad dadyānmūrdhni śirohṛdi sautraṃ vā kusumaṃ dārbhā bhaṃ sve mbare mekhalāsūtre upavīte tha kūrpare kṛtvā samyam niviṣṭaṃ prāk dadyāt śiṣyakarāmbuje  Paus  evam aikyaṃ samāpādya saguṇenānalena vai āmokṣāt sarvasiddhīnāṃ tasya sāṃmukhyasiddhaye  Paus guruḥ samācareddhomaṃ pūrṇāntaṃ punareva hi miśrībhūtaiḥ samiddravyaiḥ saptabhiḥ śarkarānvitaiḥ  Paus madhyasthaṃ mantramūrtervai sāṣṭakaṃ juhuyāt śatam sahastraṃ vāyutaṃ vipra dadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ  Paus saviṣṭaram adhovaktraṃ strucām upari vinyaset strucam abhyarcya puṣpādyairājyapūrṇāṃ strucaṃ tataḥ  Paus kuryāt pūjāṃ sugandhāktaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sārdhyairnirambubhiḥ uktasaṃkhyaṃ tvatastvājyaṃ tadardham atha homayet  Paus pūjānte pātayet pūrṇāṃ punareva yathoditām śatāt sahastrād ayutāllakṣād vāmalalocana  Paus jñānātmā pūrvamūrtīnāṃ caturthāṃśa pṛthak pṛthak tatsamaṃ hṛdayādīnām athordhvam akhilāsu ca  Paus parameśvarakāntāsu tadardhena tu pauṣkara lāñchanābharaṇādīni sarvāṇi juhuyāt kramāt  Paus sādhārāsanamantrāṇāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ kālātmarūpiṇām gurvādīnāṃ ca vihitamardhaṃ lāñchanatarpaṇam  Paus sārastrāṇāṃ lokapālānāṃ dvārsthānāṃ kamalodbhava gurupūrvakramād hutvā ardham ardhaṃ yathākramam  Paus kāryā caikādhikā saṃkhyā viṣamārdhasya cāhuteḥ ājyahomasya viprendra tadvad eva ambujādiṣu  Paus brahmayajñadrumodbhūtāḥ pūjajñānadrumotthitāḥ evaṃ kṣīratarubhyo vai samidhastrimadhuplutāḥ  Paus juhuyād vidhivanmantrī nayanmantragaṇaṃ kramāt tṛptiṃ pūrṇapradānaistu aṃśāṃśahavanaiḥ kṛtaiḥ  Paus svabuddhisaṃkhyāhomena svāṅgaṃ vai viśvavighnajit tarpaṇīyaśca pūrṇāntam evam ante nalo dvija  Paus pūrṇāntena nayetrṛptiṃ mantravyūhe kṛte hṛdi iti saṃpādite home dadyāt puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ  Paus tilakaṃ cordhvapuṇḍraṃ vā kuryād vai bhūtinā śiśoḥ svasthāneṣu hṛdā varma śiromantreṇa ca kramāt  Paus hṛnmantreṇa prayoktavyaṃ sarvadā sarvakarmasu tasya sarvāṇi karmāṇi sadā tena samācaret  Paus sarvamantrākhyabhūtasya vidhimevaṃ samācaret kṛte cāstravaṇe vāribindavaḥ struṅmukhāt cyutāḥ  Paus dadyāt kareṇa śirasi praṇītābhājanāt tataḥ homametanmumukṣorvai niṣkāmasya puroditam  Paus sakāmasya mumukṣorvai kuryāt sālaṃkṛtasya ca kāṅkṣitaṃ nānujānāti sarvajño hṛdaye sthitaḥ  Paus aprārthito pi svargaṃ tu bhaktānāṃ yo dadāti ca kimadeyaṃ hi tasyāsti tasmād abhyarthanāṃ tyajet  Paus etāvadarthanīyaṃ ca parameśvaram acyutam jantunā kṛtapūjena nityameva mahāmate  Paus mama yaccha parāṃ bhaktiṃ yayā tvaṃ me prasīdasi tvayi prasanne deveśa kiṃ na prāptaṃ mayā bhuvi  Paus ityuktastvaravindākṣa ābhiṣecaniko vidhiḥ samāpya bhagavat śāstraśravaṇe dhikṛto bhavet  Paus adhikārapadaṃ divyam āsādayati vaiṣṇavam yenātibhaktaḥ saṃsārādutrārayati saṃkaṭāt  Paus kṛte kalaśadāne tha saktunā palalādinā maṇḍalādbāhyato dadyāt prādakṣiṇyena pauṣkara  Paus sarvadigbhagavanbhūta baliṃ datrvā sahāmbunā satilodakam adhvājyagandhapuṣpānvitena ca  Paus kāryā pitṛkriyā prāgvadodanenānalāgrataḥ bahirmaṇḍalavat kuṇḍād balidāne kṛte sati  Paus ācamya pūjayitvājaṃ kumbhātkuṇḍācca maṇḍalāt kṣāntyātha bhuktaṃ pūjārthaṃ mānanīyo yathāvidhi  Paus sāṅgaṃ saparivāraṃ ca dhūpayitvā yathākramam tat kṣāntiprārthanāṃ kṛtvā nirambukusumādikaiḥ  Paus vahnipūjāṃ samāpādya namaskṛtya yathāvidhi tacchaktim ātmasāt kṛtvā hṛdā saṃhāramudrayā  Paus visṛjya strukstruve kuryāt pariṣecanam ambunā yajñabhūmeḥ svaśirasi praṇītottham athodakam  Paus atha dvābhyāṃ ca saṃhṛtya hṛdi tatsthitam acyutam staropasaṃhṛtiṃ kṛtvā madhukṣīrāmbunā tataḥ  Paus saṃprāpya yarūvasudhāmānalīmapi padmaja sarvam ambhasi nikṣipya samāhṛtyārdhyapūrvakam  Paus anugrahārthaṃ śiṣyasya anuyāgaṃ samācaret bhagavadyāgavatkāryaṃ yāgaṃ tenāpi vai guroḥ  Paus dattvā śiṣyaṃ tato yāyād ātmayāge kṛte sati yathāvad adyaprabhṛti mantrārādhanam ācaret  Paus mohālasyādikairdeṣairbuddhipūrveṇa cetasā nācartavyaṃ vibhoḥ putra parityāgaṃ hi pūjane  Paus jape tathāgnibhavane snāne dāne yathodite stutipāṭhe yathā śāstracintane śravaṇe pi ca  Paus vyākhyāne bhavyabuddhīnāṃ nārāyaṇaratātmanām śirasā dadhatām ājñāṃ kṛtvā pādābhivandanam  Paus prāṇayātrāṃ tataḥ kuryāt naivedyaprāśanādikām kṛtopavāsā ye śranti prāpaṇaṃ pārameśvaram  Paus saṃpradānāvaśiṣṭaṃ ca pūtadehā narāstu te vandanīyā narāṇāṃ ca mānyā vai siddhisantateḥ  Paus anvātmatatrvaṃ vijñeyaṃ vihitaṃ tasya sarvadā ātmanaivātmasiddhyarthaṃ yāgamannena tena ca  Paus sahayajñāvaśiṣṭena sāmbunā ca phalādinā anuyāgaṃ ca taṃ viddhiṃ ātmanātmani yatkṛtam  Paus kurvanti bhojanāt pūrvaṃ pratyahaṃ prāśanaṃ tu ye tacchakrigrahaṇaṃ prāṇe prayojanavaśāt tu vā  Paus bhāvabhaktisamāyuktāḥ sanmārgasthā dṛḍhavratāḥ aprayatnena te yānti dehānte padamācyutam  Paus yeṣāṃ vratamidaṃ divyaṃ narāṇāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām te sarvavratināṃ mūrdhni tiṣṭhanti makhayājinām  Paus mantrabrahmātmanoviṣṇoḥ samyagvidhiniveditam śubhaṃ tasya parijñeyaṃ matvā vāpamidaṃ punaḥ  Paus idaṃ tadamṛtaṃ brahma idam āyuranaśvaram idaṃ jñānamidaṃ vīryamidaṃ tejastu vaiṣṇavam  Paus idamindurakhaṇḍaṃ ca sthitam annātmanā svayam parjanyadasya bhagavān vyañjanasthitasiddhaye  Paus hārdānalātmanā bhuṅkte adhyakṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ tacchaktyānugṛhītatvāt so haṃ prakṛtigaḥ pumān  Paus evamannadamannādaṃ jñeyam annaṃ puraḥ sthitam bāhyataḥ svāñyadānena saṃbodham upayāti ca  Paus yathā tathāmbunābhyeti dehastho hutabhuk prabhuḥ kāraṇaṃ rasam annasya ṣaḍguṇaṃ ṣaḍvidhasya ca  Paus ātmabrahmā tataḥ tasmād īṣat kāraṇena tu sāṃmukhyam ātmanāṃ nītvā tato nnaṃ juhuyāt śanaiḥ  Paus prāntaparvaiścaturdhā prāk cāturātmyavyapekṣayā turyāpekṣāvaśenaiva juhuyād vāhutitrayam  Paus sahṛdā mūlamantreṇa bhuñjīyāt kavalaistataḥ prayatāsyakaraścānte pibenmantrābhimāntritam  Paus toyaṃ taddhyānapādābjaparistrutamathāpi vā pratiṣṭitasya vā pūrvaṃ tadākṛtidharasya ca  Paus yataḥ tatsarvam āpannaṃ sarvadoṣakṣayaṅkaram sarvopatāpaśamanaṃ sarvasaukhyapradaṃ sadā  Paus pāvanaṃ sarvatīrthebhyo mantrebhyaḥ padmasaṃbhava atastu bhojanānte vai hārdāgnestarpaṇaṃ parā  Paus bhāvabhaktiparo nityaṃ kaṃ pibed ājyadohavat brahmatīrthe tadā pāne dviḥ paṭhedvā catuḥ kramāt  Paus datraśiṣṭasya cānnasya prāpaṇākhyasya vai tadā māhātmyam evam atulaṃ parijñeyaṃ yathoditam  Paus yāgāvasāne yogyānāṃ bhaktānāṃ parameśvare pitṝṇāṃ tarpayen nityaṃ dayādvai prītaye vibhoḥ  Paus yo vettyevaṃ mahattāṃ ca naivedyasyācyutasya ca vidhipūrvaṃ samaśrāti sayātyacyutasāmyatām  Paus vratajñena jagadyonerbhaktena ca viśeṣataḥ prāṇavad rakṣaṇīyaśca prāṇebhyo nityameva hi  Paus annadānādinā samyagvidhinānena śaktitaḥ parāṃ prītiṃ samabhyeti tasya vai parameśvaraḥ  Paus mūrtamannaṃ paraṃ brahma pūjitaṃ pradadāti yaḥ bhagavat tatrvavetṝṇāṃ dattaṃ tenākhilaṃ bhavet  Paus vrataparyantakāle tu sthāneṣvāyatanādiṣu puṇyeṣu sanmuddūrteṣu tithilagnāśriteṣu ca  Paus kṛtvākṣayaṃ bhagavato datram akṣayyam eti ca satpātrāṇāṃ tadagre tu yena tuṣyatyadhokṣajaḥ  Paus apātrāṇām abhaktānāṃ nāstikānāṃ durātmanām varjanīyaṃ prayatnena svānuṣṭhānapareṇa tu  Paus strīśūdrāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ ca bhṛktānāṃ viśeṣataḥ sakāmo vātha niṣkāmo mantrajñaḥ sadvratasthitaḥ  Paus mantrapūtaṃ hi naivedyaṃ niṣiddhānāṃ dadāti yaḥ siddho pi yāti pātivyamārurukṣustu kiṃ punaḥ  Paus pauṣkara uvāca jñātumicchāmi deveśa tattat saṃkṣepato yathā laukikaṃ yatrvayoddiṣṭaṃ bhagavaddharmasaṃgraham  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca dhanena dharmalabdhena bhūriṇālpena vā punaḥ adhikṛtyācyutaṃ devaṃ yadi vāpyaśubhaṃ śubham  Paus bhagavatprītaye tviṣṭaṃ sadasyaiḥ tanmayaiḥ saha kratuvat svalphaladā svargadā yadyapi smṛtāḥ  Paus sakāmānāṃ hi tatrāpi tena tatphaladāstu vai akāmānāṃ tu bhaktānāṃ nūnam acyutalokadāḥ  Paus kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīni tapāṃsi vividhāni ca kṛtāni bhagavatprītyai yathābhimatadāni ca  Paus yāvajjīvādhikāraṃ tu yadebhyo bhimataṃ hi yat prītyarthaṃ parameśāya aṅgīkṛtam asvedadam  Paus tatphalatyācireṇaiva divyajñānātmanā tu vai puṇyam āsādya vai kṣetraṃ tatra cāgatamavyayam  Paus sthale vā patrapuṣpādyairyorcayatyaniśaṃ vratī bhaktyā hyananyacittasatu dehānte tasya dehinaḥ  Paus prasādād devadevasya sthitiḥ syāt sārvalaukikī pūjāṃ viṣṇuvad āpnoti yāvad jīvāvadhiṃ tu saḥ  Paus dehāvasānasamaye śvetadvīpaṃ prayāti ca bhaktiśraddhāparo vidvān nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ  Paus tairvimānaiśca mārgeṇa hyacirādyān mahāmate suprasiddhaiḥ sugandhaistu hṛdyaiḥ puṣphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ  Paus arcirādyān mahāmateityantaṃ prathamo rāśiḥ ḥ paścātvibhavavyūhaityupakramyadepādāmbupūrvaṃ tu tilasatphalacarvaṇamityantā ardhanyūnā ślokaviṃśatiḥ dvitīyo rāśiḥ atha casuprasiddhaiḥityupastutyatadbhūta darśite naiva mārgeṇa mahatā muneityantā ślokadvāviṃśatiḥ tṛtīyo rāśiḥata ūrdhvaṃkṛtvā cāghrāyaityupakramya ācādhyāyasamākṣicaturtho rāśiḥ dvitīyakośavarge yathāprathama dvitīyatṛtīyarāśayaḥ yathāpūrva likhitāḥ caturthasya ārambhastu midyate yathā tṛtīyarāśeranantaraṃ punarapi dvitīyarāśim āntaṃ likhitvā tṛtīyarāśiṃ parityajyaturīyarāśiranusyūtatayā samagrā likhitā vartate kośavargadvaye pidvitīyatṛtīyarāśayoḥ vyutkrameṇa lekhanameva viparyāse hetuḥ atraivaṃsamādhiḥdvitīyaturīyarāśyoranālakṣitasandhibandhatayā sthitiḥgranthasya paripāṭī anusīvyatina viśleṣayati cayaḥ punarantarāpatitaḥ tṛtīyo rāśiḥ sa tu turīyeṇa rāśinā sākaṃ kathaṃcidapinānvetuṃ śaknoti pratyuta prathamena rāśinā samaṃ sughaṭitasundhānaḥprāptāvasaraśca saṃpadyate asmāt paraṃ dvitīyarāśiḥ sādhūpakramaḥgranthānupūrvīṃ puṣṇāti ataḥ darśitānusāreṇa granthaparipāṭī saṃniveśitā paramataḥ sudhiyaḥ pramāṇam yorcayatyacyutaṃ bhaktyā vane vā parvatāntare bahavo bhimatān kāmān prāpnotyaprārthitāṃstu vai  Paus dehānte vāsavādīnāṃ saṃpūjyo bhagavāniva vaiṣṇavāyatane divye saiddhe vā pauruṣe tu yat  Paus kuryāt karma dhiyā bhaktyā snānaṃ kṣīrādinā mahat śrīkhaṇḍāgurukarpūrabāhlikenānulepanam  Paus sitapītāruṇairdivyairduttulairveṣṭhanaṃ tu vai śubhena sottarīyeṇa upavītena tu dvija  Paus vibhave satyalaṃkāraiḥ sauvarṇai ratnarñjitaiḥ maṇḍayet ca tataḥ puṣpaiḥ snagvaraiścaraṇāvadhi  Paus dhūpayed ājyasiktena guggulena śubhena ca prabhūtaiśca mahādīpaistilatailājyapūritaiḥ  Paus abhuktāhatasuśvetarāñjitairvyativeṣṭanaiḥ garbhīkṛtatvagelādyaiḥ pūjayet tadanantaram  Paus tato madhvājyayuktena dadhnābhyarcitam īśvaram naivedyairvividhaiḥ pūtairbhakṣyaiḥ saphalamūlakaiḥ  Paus pānakaiḥ pāvanaiḥ svacchaiḥ śītalairmadhurādikaiḥ tvagelādyanviptairdhṛṣṭairdhūpakarpūravāsitaiḥ  Paus nālikerodakopetaistarpaṇīyamanantaram naivedyācamanārthaṃ tu gandhodakamanuttamam  Paus abhuktamahataṃ śuklamatha niṣpusanāmbaram atha cūrṇitakarpūraghṛṣṭaśrīkhaṇḍabhāvitam  Paus sapūgaphalamutkṛṣṭaṃ tāmbūlaṃ vinivedya ca śālayaḥ śimbadhānyāditilāḥ siddhārthakāni ca  Paus rocanā śrīphalaṃ puṣpaṃ dūrvā dhātrīphalaṃ dadhi dukūlamahataṃ śvetaṃ dakṣiṇāvartam ambujam  Paus tamālādidalacchanne dhātūtthe vaidale pi vā pātre kṛtvārdhyapuṣpāḍhaye tatra madhye niveśya ca  Paus hemamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca svaśaktyā vātinirmalam jānunī bhūgate kṛtvā śirasāvanatena tu  Paus ādāyottānapāṇibhyāṃ vinivedya jagatprabhoḥ saṃpūraṇārthaṃ sarveṣāṃ bhogānāṃ dvijasattama  Paus yenāptiḥ sarvakāmānāṃ bhāvināṃ satphalārthinām paramātmani saṃyojyam akāmānāṃ hi yena vai  Paus cāmakhyajanādīni bhogānyanyāni yāni ca śayanāsananiṣṭhāni tantrīvādyāni yāni ca  Paus bhedīmṛdaṅgasatsaṅgaparyantāni mahānti ca tat prekṣya svadhiyā samyam cittānandapradāni ca  Paus saṃbhave sati sarvāṇi manasā tadasaṃbhave śraddhābhaktivaśāccaiva yo yajavyamarājitaiḥ  Paus svargādisatyaniṣṭhānāṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathecchayā tataḥ kālāntareṇaiva devīyecchāvaśena tu  Paus tadbhūtadarśitenaiva mārgeva mahatā mune vibhavavyūhalokānāmāste kalpaśatān bahūn  Paus jñānam āsādya tatraiva hyavatīryātha bhūtale layaṃ ca sahasā yāti bhagavatyamitātmani  Paus prabhūtaiḥ pāvanairbhogairnyāyopāyasamārjitaiḥ yaṣṭavyaṃ śraddhayā bhaktyā puṇyeṣu divaseṣvatha  Paus naimittikeṣu kāleṣu nityameva nirākulaiḥ divyāntarikṣabhaumākhyaśubhalagnakṣaṇeṣvapi  Paus sadānandasukhasaubhāgyasiddhaye eṣad dinodayaṃ hyevaṃ vratajñairbhagavanmayaiḥ  Paus vratādyadivasaṃ kāryamevaṃ vratadinasya ca varjanīyaṃ prayatnena prajāsadgatikāṅkṣiṇā  Paus parapīḍadinaṃ śuddhamupādeyaṃ hi sarvadā purovartidināṃśena yuktaṃ gurutaraṃ tu tat  Paus īṣadādyadinopetam upavāsadinaṃ yadi loke labdhapratiṣṭhaṃ ca tathātvena tu sarvadā  Paus upavāsaparāṇāṃ tu na tad doṣapradaṃ bhavet niṣkāmānāṃ hi bhaktānāṃ vrataṃ vrataparāyaṇaḥ  Paus phalārthināṃ tadbhavināṃ karmatantraratātmanām pratiṣiddhaṃ ca siddhatvād upavāse śane pi ca  Paus tato ṅbhāvaṃ bhaktānāṃ natārthaṃ itikartavyatāśaktaḥ prāptādevaṃ guruṃ yajet  Paus santoṣpābhyarthyaṃ vai kṣāntiṃ vṛttyarthaṃ hi jagadguroḥ divasārdhasamānena tadūnenādhikena vā  Paus yuktāmādyadinenaivaṃ purovartica vāsaram kṛtvā naktāśanaṃ nityaṃ yadi saṃkalpamācaret  Paus phalaṃ sātiśayaṃ tasya upavāsāt tu jāyate sarvadānāvasānāntam āpādya vratavāsare  Paus tasminnevātmayāgaṃ tu vidheyamupavāsinā tadvāsarakṣayācchaśvad viśveśe pūjanādinā  Paus śiṣṭaṃ dine parasmin vai kṛtaṃ tadabhavaṃ bhavet virodhamanyathā si vi ddhi kṛtakṛtyasya dehinaḥ  Paus akṣīṇasya parityāgāt prabhāvādagrahasya ca parapīḍatithiṣvevaṃ heyopādeyatāṃ purā  Paus jñātvā tithīśanāthātmā vāsudevo cyutaḥ prabhuḥ pūjanīyo hi parvādau sopavāsaiḥ krameṇa tu  Paus pakṣayorubhayoścaiva sitapakṣe tu vecchayā pitāmahātmā bhagavān tatrādyahani Paus tataḥ saṃyamanātmāhaṃ naṃ caturthe hari ni mānayet pañcam amṛtātmānaṃ śaktiśaṃ ṣaṣṭhavāsare  Paus saptamyāṃ jñānamūrtiṃ vai viśvātmā tadanantaram navamyām atha siddhātmā dharmātmā bhagavāṃsatataḥ  Paus īśānātmātha deveśaḥ sūryātmā dikprakāśakṛt kāmātmātha trayodaśyāṃ kalātmātha mahāmate  Paus bhagavān pitṛsaṃjñātmā bhedāstvete jagatprabhoḥ kāmyakarmādhikāreṇa nityaṃ cābhimatāptaye  Paus Paus adharmaśāntaye caiva yamaṃ saṃyamatāṃ tataḥ āyurārogyavṛddhyarthaṃ pañcamyām amṛteśvaram  Paus yajecchakriprabhāvārthaṃ ṣaṣṭhyāṃ śaktīśam acyutam svasaṃvidāptaye samyak taddineśamathārcayet  Paus pañcadaśāheśo mānanīyaḥ sa sarvadā yadyapyuktaṃ tithīśānāmarcanaṃ tithiṣu dvija  Paus naikāntināṃ tadvihitaṃ dvijānāmaphalārthinām ekādaśyāṃ hi vai teṣāṃ pakṣayorubhayorapi  Paus parapīḍaṃ ca vihitaṃ vastujālaṃ hi cāparamṛ manavaścopadeṣṭāraḥ prapañcāsyāsya pauṣkara  Paus evaṃ pravartitaṃ sarvaṃ bhaktānugrahakāmyayā pūrṇabhāveśvarapadāt supūrṇamaya mida mudīritam  Paus vratārtham upavāsānāṃ yena mantrayājinām tadarcana parikhyāgād buddhipūrvāt tu kiṃ bhavet  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca mantrapūrvaṃ hi saṃkalpaṃ kṛtvā mantrasamarcane anirvedānmahābuddhe yāvadāyuṣa ṣya meva ca  Paus saṃdiṣṭadevatānāṃ ca karmaṇā manasā girā yatnāt nirvahaṇīyaṃ tat śaktyāsvavibhavena ca  Paus asvātantryād asāmarthyāt jāte vai sūtakādike vidhivat prārthanāpūrvaṃ gurum arcāpayet tadā  Paus saṃyataṃ guruputraṃ vā aihikāmuṣmikaṃ phalam anyathā parodhena na bhayena na māyayā  Paus devam arcāpayet prājño nitye pyākasmike pi vā susaṃpūrṇaphalaprāpteḥ sadvṛttyamlekṣaṇa  Paus tadarthamarcanaṃ yena nityamaṅgīkṛtaṃ purā pratyavāyaṃ hi tallopāt tasya tat phalabhāga bhavet  Paus nā vaktavyamatastasmād vṛttilopaṃ śubhepsunā kādācitketu vā nitye niyuktānāṃ hi vārcane  Paus bahiḥ pratiṣṭhitānāṃ ca sthāpitānāṃ tu vā vidhipūrvaṃ tu niḥśeṣaṃ sāmagrībhiḥ samanvitam  Paus saha vai bhogasaṃpatyā bhaktyā saśraddhayā dvija nīti mārgagatenaiva buddhyā tu suviśuddhayā  Paus mantra  mudrāsana  dhyānair devatānāṃ yadarcanam tadartha  siddhikṛt śaśvad yājakānāṃ yathāsthitaiḥ  Paus evaṃ jñātvā nāvalepaḥ kāryaḥ saṃsāra  bhīruṇā anarcane tu devānāṃ kāmye naimittike bjaja  Paus pratyahaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa tava vighnaṃ yathā bhavet viprādīnāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ viprayogā dikāt tu vai  Paus divyapitryocitaṃ snānaṃ kṛtvā tadanu pauṣkara prāṇāyāmaṃ japāntaṃ ca prādhānyenābhivartinām  Paus mantrāṇāṃ ca mahat teṣāṃ siddhāntākhyāgamasya ca prāpyate tadanuṣṭhānāt sarvotkṛṣṭhataraṃ phalam  Paus tathā ca kamalodbhūta jagatyasmin hi dṛśyate devāsura  manuṣyāṇāṃ vyavahāraṃ svabhāvajam  Paus jātyuktaiḥ svapraṇair yuktā varṇādyāśramiṇo khilāḥ purāṇa  smṛtipārajñā veda vedānta vedinaḥ  Paus svakarmadharmaniratā munayo pi mahāmate na yānti paramāṃ siddhiṃ vinā mantra piragrahāt  Paus saidhdāntikād anuṣṭhānāt tadvidhānāṃ ca sevanāt kiṃ punar lobha mohārthaṃ mānavā mandabuddhayaḥ  Paus jñātvaiva yatnamātiṣṭhen mantrārādhana karmaṇi prasādane gurūṇāṃ ca siddhāntādyavagāhane  Paus tanniṣṭhānāṃ yataḥ samyak kaivalyam amalekṣaṇa aparokṣam ato nyeṣāṃ śuṣkatarkaratātmanām  Paus jñāna  karmaratānāṃ ca siddhayo vividhāstviha sarvathā yānti kaivalyaṃ śaśvad dehaparīkṣayā  Paus pauṣkara uvācanāthar tha jñānānuviddhasya jñātumicchāmi sāṃpratam karmaṇo haṃ svarūpaṃ ca mantriṇāṃ yanmaharddhidam  Paus śrībhagavānuvācavācakāntāniviṣṭaṃ tu mantrakṛvyādikaṃ hi yat prayāti cāṅgabhāvaṃ tu bhogajāle hi mantriṇām  Paus tat tadādau parijñeyaṃ nityamārādhakena tu śuddha  saṃvit  svarūpaṃ ca prasphurantaṃ svatejasā  Paus viṣayendriyabhūtākhye nānā karaṇaśaktibhiḥ susaṃpūrṇaṃ prabuddhābhidnyagbhūtābhiḥ parasparam  Paus yaccābhimānike rūpe bhoge vyaktiṃ vrajanti ca tat punar bhogakaivalya siddhaye svayameva hi  Paus prasiddhaṃ lakṣaṇenaiva vapuṣā mantrayājinām samāyātyaṅgabhāvaṃ ca evaṃ nityaṃ sthitā sthitiḥ  Paus sāṃprataṃ ca prabuddhaistu sā padmadalalocana kṣeptavyā bhāvanāpekṣo kṣā vastu taccāsato na hi  Paus satvaṃ syād bhāva mantreṇa sadbhāvaṃ kintu sādhanam āptavākya pradhānānām āgamaika ratātmanām  Paus samyagacyuta bhaktyā vai nirmalīkṛta cetasām yathā jalatvaṃ vai vahner yuktibhir nopapadyate  Paus evaṃ jalasya vahnitvaṃ na kadācit prajāyate yatra vā mantriṇā tābhyāṃ viparyāso bhidṛśyate  Paus tadindrajālaṃ vai māntraṃ bhaktānāṃ śubhavartmani prerakaṃ kamalodbhūta nānā pratyayalakṣaṇam  Paus jñānamūrtistu bhagavān bhaktānugrahakāmyayā bhuktvā bhogātmanāṃśena bhunakti svayameva hi  Paus muktye yājakānāṃ tu dvividhaṃ vastusaṃgraham dvividhena tu bhedena tasmān nityaṃ samabhyaset  Paus jñānayuktaṃ hi vai kartṛ karmaivaṃ suvilakṣaṇam yat prāptam āptavaktrt tu āgamānniścayīkṛtam  Paus abhyarthanādinā mantraṃ yatkramāt samupāgatam mudrānvitaṃ mahābuddhe hyastitvenāpyalaṅkṛtam  Paus tat pramādād abuddhānām anyakarmaratātmanām varṇādyaiḥ vyatyayībhūtaṃ viluptaṃ vā svarādinā  Paus adhikaṃ vābjasaṃbhūta tat karotyāśubhaṃ sadā mantriṇām acirādeva tatrāpi kamalodbhava  Paus atibhaktiprabhāvena vācasyānekarūpaṇiḥ saṃmukhīkaraṇādīnāṃ karmaṇā saṃprayojitam  Paus tadanugrahasāmarthyāt vāñchitaṃ saṃprayacchati yasmāt sadbhakti bhūtānāṃ prapannānāṃ kramaṃ vinā  Paus prasādameti mantreśastvacirād bhāvitātmanām kiṃ punar vai kriyā jñānasaṃpūrṇānāṃ tu pauṣkara  Paus bhaktiśraddhāparāṇāṃ ca bodhitānāṃ ca deśikaiḥ vinā garvoktibhiḥ caiva vākyaiścittānurañjakaiḥ  Paus samudrāṇāṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ upāyaṃ prāgyato mahat paraṃparāgataṃ caiva śāśvataṃ hi gurukramam  Paus tataḥ sadāstikatvaṃ ca tat parigrāhiṇo dvija saṃyamaṃ bhaktipūrvaṃ tu sakriyaṃ tadanantaram  Paus tataścaivāgamārthaṃ tu paścāt saṃvedanaṃ svakam buddhvaiva bhaktipūrvaṃ tu hyupāyair vividhaiḥ punaḥ  Paus āptaḥ sadāgamajñaśca sevanīyaḥ sadaiva hi nityaṃ mantrapareṇaiva dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa phalārthinā  Paus saṃbhave sati samyak ca pratyahaṃ tasya pauṣkara yogakṣemādikaṃ sarvaṃ cintanīyaṃ svaśaktitaḥ  Paus yasmād asmin hi saṃsāre gurutvena pravartitam īśvarecchāvaśāt caivam acyutaṃ parameśvaram  Paus tanmukhena mahābuddhe yaḥ prasarpitum icchati svamantraṃ bhaktimatyarthaṃ tadādau tasyapauṣkara  Paus tat putrasya athavā bhaktyā anuyāgavidhau sadā nivedanīyaṃ pākāgraṃ parituṣṭhena cetasā  Paus āstāṃ tāvan mahābuddhe svaguruṃ tatsutaṃ tuvā kramaviccāgamajño nya ekāntī vā trayīmayaḥ  Paus kṛtāhnikaḥ susaṃtuṣṭaḥ śāntacinto hyanākulaḥ abhyarthito tibhakto vai cirakālaṃ mahāmate  Paus svamantrasādhanākhyaṃ vā dvi ṣaḍaṣṭaṣaḍakṣaram jitantasaṃjñaṃ praṇavam ādyaṃ cāntaṃ sabījakam  Paus evam ekatra saṃyojyam ūrdhvam aṅgārakṭavat sāṅgaṃ pāṇitale nyasya tadvijñānādināṃ tanau  Paus tad ahaṅkāram ālambya yasya sānugrahaṃ gṛhe bhunakti tad anantaṃ vai jāyete tasya tatkṣaṇāt  Paus maṇḍalādau tu mantreśo bhogair iṣṭastathākhilaiḥ tarpitaścāvnimadhye tu ājyādyairna tathābjaja  Paus samabhyeti parāṃ prītiṃ yathācāryaśarīragam tasmān nimittam āśritya pratipakṣasya cāntare  Paus tathā māsasya cābdasya māsaṣaṭkasya vā abjaja madhye bhyarcyaṃ viśeṣeṇa svamantraṃ gurusannidhau  Paus pitṝṇāṃ prītaye paścād bhūtaye pi hi cātmanaḥ prapūjya deśikendraṃtu kālaṃ rātrikṣayāvadhi  Paus pādasaṃvāhanāntaistu bhogaiḥ pādyārdhya  pūrvakaiḥ prasādya ca yathāśaktyā mātravittaṃ nivedya ca  Paus anuvrajya mahābuddhe vrajantaṃ svagṛhādikam evaṃ saṃpratipannā ye mantrārādhana  karmaṇi  Paus varṇā dvijendrapūrvāstu brahnacāri  puraḥsarā bhaikṣukāntāstu vai sarve siddhiṃ samupayānti ca  Paus pauṣkara uvāca purā yasyajagannātha mantramūrtir gṛhāntare ekā vā nekaṃ bhedotthā vidyate bimbalakṣaṇā  Paus bhaktyā parigṛhītā prāk svayaṃ vā pūrvajair dvija niveśitā mantrapūrvaṃ nikṣiptā vā pareṇa tu  Paus dhanenāptāthavānyasmād ayogyāt taskarādikāna sāṃprataṃ svaguror labdhā dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa prasiddhaye  Paus cittaprasāda janako mantraḥ saṃsāraduḥkhahṛt sa ca tadviniyuktastu sāṅgaḥ saparivārakaḥ  Paus ārādhakasya bhagavan vihitaṃ vā navādiśā śrībhagavānuvācasvayaṃ vyaktaṃ hi yad vipra tathā maragaṇair dvija sthāpitaṃ mantrasiddhestu ākāraṃ bhagavanmayaiḥ  Paus tadadhiṣṭhita  mantrāṇāṃ saha tasya ca yojanā vihitā kamalodbhūta nṛṇāṃ sannidhisiddhaye  Paus evaṃ saparivāraṃ ca na svamantraḥ sadā gṛhe mantrākṛtau tu cānyasmin yojanīyaḥ padādiṣapha  Paus pūjanīyaṃ svamantreṇa lāñchanāṅgānvitena ca bimbasaṃruddha  mantraṃ ca tadvimuktamapi dvija  Paus sarvā caiva svayaṃvyaktapūrṇānāṃ hi mahāmate niveśanaṃ hi mantrāṇām anyonyānāṃ guṇāvaham  Paus nityaṃ yo yatacittastu mantrārādhana  karmaṇi dehasthaṃ kṣapayet śeṣaṃ karmabandham aśāśvatam  Paus samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu mantreṣu ca viśeṣataḥ niṣiddhaṃ tadvinā nyeṣāṃ svamantrasya niyojanam  Paus kasyacit kutracit samyak yasmān manyākṛtau dvija prasīdati svamātmānaṃ śudhdajñānodayaṃ vinā  Paus na niṣiddhaṃ svamantreṇa kvacid anyatra pūjanam prādhānyena svamārgā cca gṛhe vā nyatra maṇḍale  Paus samāhṛtāṃ ca pūjārthaṃ mantratantrārcane sati svamantreṇa na doṣo sti tadvad āyataneṣu ca  Paus mantreṇa bhinnamārgā cca pratimā maṇḍalaṃ tu vā adhiṣṭhitaṃ yadā tatra vihitaṃ darśanaṃ tu vai  Paus puṣpadānaṃ svamantreṇa vyāpakena malātmanā cinmātratā  svarūpeṇa mantrāṇāṃ hi yato bjaja  Paus aviśeṣaṃ hi sāmānyaṃ śabdabrahmamayaṃ vapuḥ dhyāna  nyāsādikaiḥ teṣo viśeṣastu parasparam  Paus jāyate śabalaṃ bhīmam abhicāraphalapradam anugrahaparaṃ mantraṃ śabdabrahmamayaṃ svakam  Paus yājya  yājakabhāvena samabhpeti tathābjaja saṃruddham api yat tūtra vyaktiśakti  dhiyā vinā  Paus śabdabrahmātmanā tvāste tadaikyāt ca balaṃ kutaḥ paṭavyakti  dvayenaiva vinā aikyaṃ namaso yathā  Paus dvābhyāṃ śabdasvarūpābhyām evam aikyam anugrahāt sujanma caivaṃ kṣobhasya viśeṣayajanaṃ vinā  Paus svagṛhe maṇḍale yāge divyādyāyatane pi ca pauṣkara uvācaparaṃ mārgaṃ na paśyāmi jagatyasmin jaganmaya vāsudevātmakaṃ yasmāt sarvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam  Paus śrībhagavānuvācasatyam etanmahābuddhe yathā saṃyoditaṃ tvayā kintu kriyāpravṛttasya jantor bhaktiparasya ca  Paus hṛdayāvarjako go yatra viśrāmaḥ paramārthataḥ tat sanmārgo yāñakasya vaiṣṇavaḥ sa hi sātvikaḥ  Paus svayameva pravṛttasya lokānugrahakāmyayā vibhavavyūhabhāvena svacchasat ṣaṅguṇātmanā  Paus tasyopacaryate yena āgamenātha karmaṇā sanmārgaṃ viddhi taṃ vipra śaśvad brahma vibhūtidam  Paus vibhurvibhavabhāvastha icchayā vitanoti yat prākṛtaṃ kṣetramāśritya tadguṇaṃ devatātmakam  Paus tanmāyīyaṃ ca niḥśeṣajñānādyaiśchuritaṃ guṇaiḥ guṇātmakaṃ tu taṃ viddhi śabalaṃ nātinirmalam  Paus tad vyañjakaṃ hi yat śāstram itikartavyatā ca vai asanmārgaṃ tu taṃ vipra viddhi pūrvavyapekṣayā  Paus tasmāt parapadaprāpteḥ kāraṇaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam vibhavavyūhasaṃjñaṃ tu śāśvataṃ rūpam ācyutam  Paus kṣiprameva prapannānāṃ jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā dadāti satpadaprāptiṃ kartiṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām  Paus kāmyānāṃ karmaṇāṃ prāptau hi acireṇaiva padmaja upāyaṃ nāparaṃ manye nityaṃ bhogābhilāṣiṇām  Paus susūkṣma  nyūhavibhavaṃ muktvā sadbrahna  yājinām sāṃsārikaṃ phalaṃ heyaṃ svargādi  prāptilakṣaṇam  Paus prārthyamānaṃ hi yajñādyaiḥ śaśvat tasmān na cāvyate ataeva hi māyīye nārādhyo devatāgaṇaḥ  Paus samyam saṃpratipannaistu sanmārge paricodite tasmāt kamalasaṃbhūta prayatnena sadaiva hi  Paus kuryād ārādhanaṃ bhaktyā mantrāṇāṃ hi yathākṣaṇam eṣām anugrahād duḥkhaṃ trividhaṃ kṣayameti ca  Paus adhibhautikam ādhyātmam adhidevīyam abjaja pauṣkara uvāca ārādhakānāṃ bhagavan mantrāṇāṃ śaśvad arcane sarvadā patrapuṣpādyaiḥ bhogaiḥ kiṃ phalamarcanāt  Paus vistareṇārcanāt teṣāṃ bahubhiḥ kusumādikaiḥ kiṃ phalaṃ yājakānāṃ tu atra me saṃśayo mahān  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca phalasāmyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha bhāvabhaktivaśāt sthitam daridrāṇāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ phalapuṣpādinā vinā  Paus yatphalaṃ tad dvijāḍhyānāṃ nirannānāṃ tu cārcanāt sadāḍhyānāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ homādyair arcanāt phalam  Paus yat tad viddhi daridraṇāṃ bhaktānāṃ kusumādikaiḥ kṣaṇasya ca samaṃ jñeyaṃ sadā horātralakṣaṇam  Paus nṛpāṇāṃ ca daridrāṇāṃ kālaṃ yat tat kriyaśritam tatrāpi kamalodbhūta bhūtārtham avadhāraya  Paus yathālabdhena śuddhena bhogajālena vai saha kartavyā dhāraṇā dhyānaṃ mantrāṇāṃ yatra pauṣkara  Paus samudrāṇāṃ ca yogasya vistarāt nityameva hi tad yājakānāṃ yajanam acirād bhuktimuktidam  Paus saṃkṣiptaṃ dhāraṇādyair yat tat kṛtam cāpyabhogadam saṃbhogair dhāraṇādyair yat saṃkaṭaṃ tat cireṇa tu  Paus vidadhāti ca bhaktānāṃ bhogahīnaṃ paraṃ padam tasmāt śreyo rthināṃ nityaṃ bhuktimukti  phalāptaye  Paus nirvyākudhilayā bhaktyā kālāṃśam avalabmya vai vimuktamanyair vyāpārair vidhivad ghaṭate yathā  Paus susaṃpūrṇaṃ tu yajanaṃ dhāraṇādyaiḥ suvistṛtaiḥ bhogair yadyapi saṃpūrṇaiḥ saṃpattiḥ saha vai nṛṇām  Paus tathāpi karmaniṣṭhānāṃ ādhikyaṃ cāsti pauṣkara bhogāpavargahṛt śāṭhyāt tannirāsāt kṛte sphuṭe  Paus jāyete yājakānāṃ tu nāto tro tsāhaṃ parityajet dravyasaṃpadvinā nityaṃ mantrārādhana  karmaṇi  Paus paraṃ hi yasya vā bhāvo bhogavṛndasya pauṣkara bhogāpti phalaniṣṭhasya prathamaṃ cākṛtātmanaḥ  Paus na punarmokṣaniṣṭhasya karmaṇaḥ śāśvatasya ca puruṣārthapradasyāśu khaṇḍanaṃ sadvivekinām  Paus pauṣkara uvācasaṃsāriṇāṃ hi bhaktānāṃ nānākarmaratātmanām putradārādibharaṇe nityaṃ vyākulacetasām  Paus vistareṇārcane teṣāṃ kathaṃ saṃpadyate cyuta anarcanāt tvayoddiṣṭa  phalaṃ vaikalyam uttamam  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca kramayuktaṃ hi yat karma tacca śreyaskaraṃ nṛṇām tasmāt tat na parityājyaṃ saṃkṣiptamatha vistṛtam  Paus mukhyakalpaṃ hi vistāram anukalpam ataḥ param samatva ghaṭate kena hetunā kamalodbhava  Paus tatrāpi cā śaṭhānāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām vihitaṃ patrapuṣpādyaiḥ sabhogaiḥ vāgbhir arcanam  Paus karmaṇām anusaṃdhānaṃ vinā kālāntareṇa tu kṣmā  jalānalavāyvākhyaṃ nābhasīyaṃ mahāmate  Paus dhāraṇāpañcakāt caiva saṃkṣiptaṃ vihitaṃ dvayam dahanāpyāyanākhyaṃ yad ādehāt sarvaśuddhaye  Paus parāpara  svarūpāt ca dhyānāt ekaṃ paraṃ mahat hṛnmantraṃ sarvamantrayāṇām upacārakriyāvidhau  Paus karmaṇā samanaskaṃ ca praṇavādyaṃ mahāmate ekā hi ārādhyamudrā vai yogamantrasya sā smṛtā  Paus smaraṇānnetrayormadhye svoccāraṃ niṣkalasya tu nati  praṇavagarbhābhiḥ svasaṃjñābhiryadarcanam  Paus vidhivan mantramūrtīnāṃ tatparaṃ kṣiprasaṃjñitam bījair viśeṣitābhiḥ tad dvitīyaṃ sūkṣmalakṣaṇam  Paus yallakṣaṇāmṛtaiḥ piṇḍaiḥ saha saṃjñābhir abjaja japāntam akhilaṃ karma mantrāṇāṃ tad bṛhat smṛtam  Paus kṣipramādyāt ca kaivalyaṃ kiṃcit kālāntareṇa tu dvitīyād abjasaṃbhūta buddhipūrvakrameṇa tu  Paus jñānādi guṇaṣaṭkaṃ ce ihaivādyaṃ prayacchati aṇimādi aṣṭakaṃ caiva dvitīyam amalekṣaṇa  Paus samastabhuvanaiśvaryaṃ tṛtīyam acirāt tu vai sāmyaṃ niḥśreyasāvāpteḥ sarveṣāṃ kintu pauṣkara  Paus kṣipraṃ lakṣaṇapūrveṇa kālena trividhena tu mahattaiva hi mantrasya svasaṃjñākhyasya yadyapi  Paus tathāpi kamalodbhūta kṣiprapūrvādikercane bījaṃ vā piṇḍamantraṃ ca praṇavād anusaṃsmaret  Paus ārādhyaṃ mantranāthasya hṛdādīnāṃ tathaiva ca anyeṣām antaraṅgākhyaṃ mantrāṇāṃ kamalodbhava  Paus pradhānalakṣaṇānāṃ ca kamalāsanavartinām na virodhasti ataḥ anyeṣāṃ bījaiḥ piṇḍairvinā abjaja  Paus vajraḷāñchana lokeśatadastrādhārartinām tathāsanākhya vighneśa pūrvāṇāṃ dvāravāsināma  Paus brahmacāri  gṛhasthasya svatantrasya yaterapi kiṃ punastu gṛhasthasya vyāpāraniratasya cā  Paus etad vai naiṣṭhikānāṃ tu taccittaniratātmanām sādhakānāṃ savittānāṃ hitam ekāntavāsinām  Paus bhaktiśraddhāparaḥ samyaggṛhītvā yaḥ samācaret dadāti tatra manyātmā pūrvoktaṃ dvividhaṃ phalam  Paus saha sādhakasiddhībhira nirvighnena mahāmate  Paus iti śrīpāñcarātre sahopaniṣadi pauṣkara saṃhitāyām ārādhanalopavicāraḥ nāmadvātriṃśo dhyāyaḥ atha trayastriṃśo dhyāyaḥpauṣkara uvāca navamūrteḥ parijñātaṃ pūrvaṃm ārādhanaṃ mayā nānātvenāpavargārthaṃ na jñātaṃ caturātmanaḥ  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca anujjhitasvarūpasya devasya caturātmanaḥ kevalasyārcanāt mokṣaṃ bhavete tad dvidhārcanāt  Paus nānāphalāptaye brahmannānārūpadharasya ca nānātvenārcanaṃ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu samyagyathāsthitam  Pausvyāpakaṃ paramātmānam ādidevam adhokṣajam prāg arcanīyaṃ sarvatra pūjānte cāpi madhyataḥ  Paus tataḥ prabhavayogena prākpatrādi samarcayet catuṣkaṃ saṃkarṣaṇādyaṃ kramānnārāyaṇāntimaka m  Paus punarapyayayogena vandhyādhīrāpadāvadhi  nārāyaṇādyaṃ yaṣṭavyaṃ saṃkarṣaṇāntameva hi  Paus evam āgneyapadme tu pradyumnādyaṃ catuṣṭayam śabdabrahmādidevāntam arcanīyaṃ sadaiva hi  Paus dakṣiṇe tu aniruddhādyaṃ garuḍāsanapaścimam vihitaṃ caiva vinyāsaṃ prabhavāpyayalakṣaṇam  Paus nārāyaṇanṛsiṃhāntaṃ rakṣaḥpadmercayet tataḥ pratyag diksaṃsthite padme brahmādyaṃ kṣmādharāntimam  Paus saṃkarṣaṇāvasānāntaṃ viṣṇvādyaṃ mārute mbujenṛkesariṃ varāhaṃ ca jñānādyodakṛdyudak   Paus trayaṃ saṃkaṣaṇādyaṃ yat īśāne kṣmādharādikam prabhavenāpi ayenaiva mānanīyam ataḥ kramāt  Paus navasaṃkhyam idaṃ vipra prathamaṃ yatprakīrtitam tadīyaṃ jāyate tasya prabhāvaṃ tat kamārcanāt  Paus navamūrtimayaṃ mahat cāturātmyacaturvargaphaladaṃ bhāvitātmanām  Paus nānāphalāpitara ācirāt jāyate ca phalārthinām svātantryeṇārcanāt nityam eteṣāṃ caturātmanām  Paus yasya yasya caturmūrteḥ prathamaṃ yat prakīrtitam tadīyaṃ jāyate tasya prabhāvaṃ tatkramārcamāt  Paus etāvad uktaṃ hi phalaṃ sanniveśavaśāt tu vai yataḥ pratihataṃ vīryam aiśvaryaṃ prabhavāpyaye  Paus taṃ vipraṃ mantramūrtīnāṃ mantram apratimaprabham anantaṃ svaprakāśatvam anaupamyaṃ jagatprabhoḥ  Paus parameśvaramūrtīnāṃ parijñānavaśāt sati anādinidhano nantaḥ karmiṇāṃ pratipattaye  Paus taduttāraṇasidhyarthaṃ vyūhatām āgataḥ svayam prāṇecchāśabdakālakhyacaturātmatayā nava  Paus aviśeṣasvarūpasya devasyaiva mahātmanaḥ nityasannihitāśeṣaśakternityoditasya ca  Paus śabdavitsaṃbhavānandaviśeṣairgamitasya ca idaṃ uktaṃ mayā yogaṃ bhavināṃ bhavaśāntaye  Paus aheyam api abhinnaṃ ca prapañcaṃ paramātmanaḥ satyarūpasya vai samyak kṣobhaṃ niśreyasapradam  Paus yasya sāṃsārikī māyācakramicchāvaśāt punaḥ nirgatā yatra muhyanti ṛṣayaḥ sāmarā narāḥ  Paus yāvannānugṛhītā vai deśikavyaktigena ca ṣāḍguṇyamūrtinānena pareṇa caturātmanā naḥ   Paus asyārādhanakāle tu bahirvā hṛdayāmbare kadambapuṣpavad vyaktiṃ saṃsmaret ṣaḍguṇojjvalām  Paus bahvātmanā cārcakena caturvarṇamayena ca svareṇa vākṣareṇaiva kevalena sabindunā  Paus bāhyopacāranāmnā tu suprasiddhena kenacit mukhyenābhimatenaiva manasaḥ tuṣṭidena ca  Paus nyasyāṅgāni svakānyasya prāk saṃpūrṇaguṇāni ca svamantrairarcanenaiva sthānabhedaṃ vinābjaja  Paus tasmin kadambakusumasadṛśe mantragolake dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa tvabhinnena tu sāṃpratam  Paus vyaktim āpādya vai tasyāṃ punarvarṇakrameṇa tu aṅgopāṅgasthitiṃ kuryāt sthāneṣu hṛdayādiṣu  Paus hṛdi mūrdhni śikhāyāṃ ca skandhyoḥ karamadhyataḥ netrayoḥ udare pṛṣṭhe deśe bāhudvaye tataḥ  Paus urubhyāṃ jānuyugme ca pādayoḥtadanantaram tatra praṇavapūrvaṃ tu ṣaḍvarṇāstvāḍgikā matāḥ  Paus ṣaḍupāṅgābhidhāstvanye eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇu yat supratiṣṭhitaṃ śuddhaṃ sāmānyaṃ yad anāvṛtam  Paus prabuddhaṃ bhāsvaraṃ nityaṃ jñānaṃ sākṣāt tad ācyutam svasya śaktisamūhasya balādyasyākhilasya ca  Paus udayasthitisaṃhārakāraṇe ṅgātmanā punaḥ viśeṣatāṃ samāyāti svarūpam api cātyajan  Paus mantreśāmāntraśaktīnām anantānāṃ tu tadvija nānāsāmarthyavargānāṃ hṛdayaṃ ratnadīpavat  Paus ātmaprakāśakaṃ caiva balādīnāṃ tathā ca tat sarvātiśāyi caiśvaryaṃ yadguṇaṃ pārameśvaram  Paus tacchiraḥ sarvamantrāṇāṃ śrīmad bhogāpavargadam yā bhūriśaktibhiḥ pūrṇā śaktirvai pārameśvarī  Paus ūrdhvatejovahā śuddhā viddhi māntrī śikhā tu sā dhairyaṃ yannāparaṃ prāṇād ācyutaṃ dhṛtilakṣaṇāt  Paus tad eva kavacaṃ viddhi mantrāṇāṃ hi balātmakam yad apratihataṃ vīryam aiśvaryaṃ prabhavāpyayam  Paus tad vipra mantramūrtīnām astram apratimaprabham yadanantaprakāśatvam anaupamyaṃ jagatprabhoḥ  Paus tannetraṃ tatparijñānāt dhāma cālakṣyate param hṛdā saha pralīnaṃ ca tatkeṣāṃcinmahāmate  Paus svakaṃ ujjhitya vai kṣetraṃ jñānam uddīpayed sthitam mantrāṇāṃ netramantraṃ tu īśvarecchāvaśād dvija  Paus kvacid aṅgacatuṣkasya antasthā ñja janavatprabhā vartate mūrdhapūrvasya ratneṣviva upāśrayam  Paus vācakena vinā tasmāt tadīyājñāmayaprabhā bhagavatkarmakuśalaiḥ parijñeyārcanā tāḥ  Paus ityāṅgikī sthitistāvat sarvatra nyāsakarmaṇi prakāśitābjasaṃbhūta tvaupāṅgaṃ niścayaṃ śṛṇu  Paus kroḍīkaroti vai yena jñānadharmeṇa sarvadā vahirvā viṣayaṃ svalpam upāṅgam udaram ca tat  Paus saṃsiddham upacarād vai anye pyevaṃ mahāmate upāyadharmavad yastu siddhimokṣavaśāt punaḥ  Paus pṛṣṭhataḥ sarvadāne ca aiśvaryasya phalātmanaḥ pṛṣṭhasaṃjñām upāṅgaṃ tad dvitīyam amalekṣaṇa  Paus dvyātmakaṃ hi yad ullāsaṃ vibhoḥ śaktyātmano dvija sutīkṣṇam atisaumyaṃ ca tad upāṅgaṃ bhujābhidham  Paus vibhūtiśaktervyaktasya nānābījasya yanmahat rasaṃ vīryamayaṃ kṣetram ūrusaṃjñaṃ tadātmakam  Paus yatsarvajñasya śaktervai vidyāvidyātmakaṃ vapuḥ jānvākhyaṃ tad upāṅgaṃ vai pañcamaṃ parikīrtitam  Paus ācyutasthitiśaktiryat svaguṇaṃ hi vilakṣaṇam saṃdhārakatvam abjākṣa tat pādāhvam udāhṛnam  Paus sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāranyāse svātmani vā prabhoḥ dvādaśākṣarapūrvāṇāṃ pūrvāṅgopāṅgakalpanā  Paus sā punaḥ svalpavarṇānām adhikākṣaravartinām hīnātiriktarūpāpi tad aṅgāḥ parameśvara  Paus evaṃ bhajanti māṃ nityaṃ prakriyārthaṃ tu vai punaḥ svakṣetreṣu arcayen nāmnā natinā praṇavena tu  Paus varṇādhikānāṃ mantrāṇām upāṅgeṣvidamācaret saha dvādaśamānaiva varṇena samudīraṇā  Paus sāmānyaśabdabhāvena syād eva hṛnmayī sthitā akārādisvareṇaiva kādinā vā sabindunā  Paus svakhyañjanamiśreṇa piṇḍībhūtena pāṇinā yatra dvijendra vihitaṃ vyaktidānaṃ purāṇiṣu  Paus aṅgopāṅgamayī vyāptiḥ smartavyā vānyalakṣaṇā jñānāṅgopāṅganirmuktā mantrajñānaprabhātmikā  Paus yā parā prakṛtirvāṇī cidrūpā nirmalāṃ parā pūritādhyakṣabhāvena niṣkalena mahātmanā  Paus śarīram iva jīvena sthūlasūkṣmād vilakṣaṇam sthūlaṃ bhūtamatha tatra sūkṣmaṃ puryaṣṭakābhidham  Paus dehastham ātmatattvaṃ tu bhogaṃ viṣayajaṃ yathā bhunakti tadvad ādatte pūrṇavyaktigataḥ prabhuḥ  Paus sarvathā tu svamantreṇa mantreśaṃ mūrtisaṃsthitam bhogairjapaiḥ tathā stotrairvividhairvahnitarpaṇaiḥ  Paus dānairviśeṣayāgaistu pitṛtarpaṇapaścimaiḥ netavyam atulāṃ prītiṃ prayogaiḥ prativācakaiḥ  Paus mantreśasyārcanaṃ kuryāt kramāttadanu pauṣkara tanmūrtivācakādīnāṃ mantreśānāṃ hi mānanām  Paus antaraṅgāṅgayuktānāṃ lāñchanānāmapi dvija bhogabhūmau tu tanmūrtau kintu bhogāvanestu te  Paus yathoktalakṣaṇāḥ sarve dhyātavyāstu yathākramam mantramūrtau sadehe ca prasphuratkiraṇojjvalāḥ  Paus yā parā prakṛtirmāntrī vaiśvarūpyāttu sā punaḥ nānānāmākṣaratvena nānāmūrtitvam eva ca  Paus ato na vihitaṃ vitra mūrtidānaṃ pṛthak pṛthak mūlamantravad anyeṣāṃ mantrāṇāṃ pṛthag akṣaraiḥ  Paus kāraṇānirgatāḥ kecidvacaktiśaktiguṇairyutāḥ pṛthak vyaktimayāḥ cānye mantranāthāstadicchayā  Paus ekaḥ sarveśvaro nanto jīvānām anukaṃpayā nānāmantrasvarūpeṇa saṃsthitiṃ svecchayā yathā  Paus prakṛtyekā tathā bahvī hyādheyānāṃ mahātmanām lokanāthecchayā vipra bahudhā saṃvyavasthitā  Paus yā parā prakṛtirmāntrī vāsudevākhyalakṣaṇā ṣāḍguṇyavigrahā sarvaśaktitattvaguṇānvitā  Paus kośabhūtatvam āpannā svayam ānandalakṣaṇā prakāśaikasvabhāve tu sūkṣme sve mantravigrahe  Paus japāt saṃsmaraṇād yasya svavyaktisthasya pūjanāt tad abhinnaṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ param āpnoti tad vratī  Paus evam ekatvam āpannaṃ yorcayati acyutaṃ vibhum nityākṛtadhana rastasya bhogamokṣau karasthitau  Paus śuddhasaṃvitsvabhāvānāṃ jñānādiguṇināṃ tu vai svamantraśaktivyūhānāṃ vyaktaye parameśvaraḥ  Paus svecchayā śabdaśaktiṃ svām anabhivyaktalakṣaṇām prakāśya cābjasaṃbhūta yasyāṃ mantramayaṃ vapuḥ  Paus te sarvajñaguṇaiścātha mantraiḥ saṃproktalakṣaṇāḥ anugrahārthaṃ bhavināṃ nibadhnanti sthitiṃ sthirām  Paus lipivyūhe tu vividhairbījajaiḥ piṇḍavad ātmike kevale pi ca saṃmiśre bhūrisaṃkhye japātmike  Paus jñaśuddhiḥ cid adhiṣṭhātṛvaśād amarapūjitā yasyopacāramantratvam āmūlād upayānti ca  Paus śabdadehāḥ punaḥ tu ete mantrā mananadharmiṇaḥ aparicyutarūpāśca nānātvam upayānti ca  Paus nānākāravaśāccaiva nānāsattvavaśād api śraddhābhaktivaśānnānā nānāphalavaśāt punaḥ  Paus nānājātivaśāccāpi nānādeśavaśāt punaḥ nānākālavaśād brahman nānāsādhanasaṃbhramaiḥ  Paus mokṣaikaniratānāṃ ca narāṇām ātmasiddhaye viṣayākṣiptacittānāṃ bhūtaye bhavinām api  Paus pauṣkara uvāca tvayoktaṃ bhagavad yāgaṃ śuddhasattvasya karmiṇaḥ jitondriyasya bhaktasya mantrasiddhasya cācyuta  Paus yogaṃ tattvajayārthaṃ vai jñātum icchāmi ahaṃ punaḥ vidhivad yat parijñānaṃ mantrajño labhate sthitam nivātācaladīpābhe samādhau pārameśvare  Paus śrībhagavān uvāca pradhānayogam uktaṃ te karmayogād anantaram tad gārhasthasya ca munervihitaṃ nānyayājinaḥ  Paus tathā paramahaṃsasya lokabāhyasthitasya ca tattvayogaṃ ato vakṣye bhūmikābhinnalakṣaṇam  Paus śuddhaye khilatattvānāṃ
