kṛtadīkṣasya pauṣkara śaśvat sākṣtāt tu karaṇe nānāsiddhivyapekṣayā  Paus apavargāptaye caiva jñānāvaraṇaśāntaye śuddhasaṃvit svabhāvena paramātmani tiṣṭhati  Paus citprakāśasvarūpeṇa mantrātmani mahāmate vibhavavyūhayogena karmaṇācchādya saṃsthitaḥ  Paus vyāptaḥ pareṇa vibhunā sarvaśaktyātmakena tu yam ācchādya sthitaḥ samyag bodhyaṃ taṃ sarvadābjaja  Paus asaṅkīrṇam asaṃkhyaṃ ca vāsanāśatavāsitam guruṇā anugṛhītasya mantraikaniratasya ca  Paus samagraṃ tattvajālaṃ tad vinivartati nānyathā atastu labdhalakṣeṇa karmatantraratena ca  Paus nityaṃ tattvajayaṃ kāryaṃ svarūpaprāptaye tu vai vyāpakaḥ sarvaśaktyātmā samārādhya vibhāvya ca  Paus tattvādhiṣṭhātṛbhāvena āpādān mastakāvadhi jñātavyaṃ sthānabhedena dīkṣāyāṃ kathitaṃ yathā  Paus kadalīpuṭhavaccātha tato modakavad dvija tajjāyārtha samabhyasya yogam evam tridhā amalam  Paus kintu cābhyā bhyaḥsamānasya moham āyāye ti sāṃpratam nidrālasyaśramaśvāsaśūnyadṛṣṭitvam abjaja  Paus ṣaṭkośalakṣaṇaṃ viddhi savighnaṃ te tadātmanā niścayāt tad jayed etad astradhyānād japād api  Paus prāṇādīnāṃ tu vāyūnāṃ kṛtvā tu vijayaṃ purā sukhāsanopaviṣṭastu gurvaṅghriṃ vandayed dhiyā  Paus vyāpakatvena cārādhya nyastvākāraśarīragam tataḥ tādātmyam ālambya cittaṃ bāhyastham ācaret  Paus hṛtpuṇḍarīkamadhye tu tridhāma bhuvanodare praṇavenāparaṃ brahma sarvaśaktimayaṃ dvija  Paus abhyasyābhyāsayogena prathamaṃ bhāvayet tataḥ kuryāt tattvajayābhyāsaṃ vidhinānena vai dvijaḥ  Paus praṇavādyantaruddhena hṛdā saṃjñāpareṇa vā sahasraraśmiṃ dhyāyed vai tattvajālaṃ pṛthak pṛthak  Paus japād vilayam āyāti tattvajñānaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ādhāraṃ praṇavaṃ śabdaṃ hṛnmantraḥ tanmaye tataḥ  Paus tattvato bhavahṛt śabdaṃ tatsaṃjñaṃ praṇavodare svātmānaṃ praṇavaṃ śabdam ātmānandamaye harau  Paus evaṃ krameṇa kṣmādīnāṃ tanmantrāṇāṃ jayaṃ dvija kuryāt svakaraṇānāṃ ca indriyāṇāṃ parājayam  Paus iti tridaśakaṃ jitvā tattvānāṃ cāvyayena tu tato manaḥ tu ahaṃkāraṃ buddhiṃ guṇagaṇaṃ kramāt  Paus tamo rajaḥ sattvasaṃjñaṃ dhyātvā japtvā parityajet sūkṣmaṃ saṃdhātasaṃjñaṃ tu svaguṇebhyo vilakṣaṇam  Paus sākṣātkṛtvātha saṃtyajya avyaktaṃ ca jayet tataḥ kāraṇaṃ yat prapañcasya asyoktasyāparasya ca  Paus nānāmatiniviṣṭasya svavikalpotthitasya ca kālatattvam ataḥ cintyaṃ bhūtabhavyabhavātmakam  Paus suddhikṛd yad anantasya sadasadlakṣaṇasya ca prapañcasya mahābuddhe dhyātvā evaṃ tritayaṃ tyajet  Paus upāyalakṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ catuḥ saṃkhyaṃ hi lakṣaṇam jñānakriyecchātrāṇākhyaśaktisaṃjñaṃ hi śāśvatam  Paus sākṣāt kuryād japād dhyānād yogābhyāsād athordhvataḥ upādeyam ato brahman samūhaṃ vyāpakaṃ dhruvam  Paus saptasaṃjñaṃ padaṃ divyaṃ dhyātavyaṃ karmaśāntaye śabdabrahmāvasānaṃ ca jñātavyaṃ ca sadoditam  Paus śabdabrahmasvarūpasya parasya paramātmanaḥ amūrtasya ca tanmūrteḥ sthitiḥ sā ṣaḍguṇātmikā  Paus śabdabrahmana samabhyasya guṇaṣaṭkād anantaram anuccāryaṃm avarṇaṃ taṃ nirāvaraṇam asvaram  Paus sadbrahmavācakaṃ tad vai vāṅmayātītam acyutam svakhyañjanarūpāśca sarveṣāṃ mūrtivācakāḥ  Paus svaviśeṣācca bahavo daśūlakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ akṣarasvaravarṇākhyaghoṣaṣorāgasvarātmakāḥ  Paus dhvaniḥ kūṭastathā sphoṭavisargāntā mahāmate ebhyaḥ saṃkīrṇarūpābhyo yatne vākyatarātmanā  Paus āmokṣāt sarvasiddhīnāṃ pradātā siddhibhāg bhavet dhyātā tasmin hi niṣṇātaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati  Paus samyagvetti tadābhyāsāt svārādhyenānurañjanāt vilakṣaṇaṃ ca tad dhyānaṃ dhyānādhyātmakam abjaja  Paus prakāśānandarūpe ca nānābhūtaṃ hi yad bahiḥ te dve sacchabdanāthasya ūrmiḥ sūkṣmatamā amalā  Paus yathā saha samaṃ yāti tattvajñastu avyaye pade ātmalābham ataḥ prāpya parasmāt parameśvarāt  Paus jñānakarmaratānāṃ ca śraddhāsaṃyamasevinām āstikānāṃ jitākṣāṇāṃ sadbhaktānāṃ sadā bhavet  Paus na etad vācyaṃ abhaktāya nāstikāya kadācana na kutarkaṃ atiṣṭhāya karmabrahmojjhitāya ca  Paus ā prabhātāt niśāntaṃ ca vyāpāraṃ pārameśvaram lokātītāstu ye viprāḥ teṣāṃ tad hṛdayaṃgamam  Paus laukikavyavahārasthā bahavo nye ca neśvarāḥ śūnyabrahmaikaniṣṭhāya vākprapañcadhiyānvitāḥ  Paus pauṣkara uvāca tattvagrāmasya bhedaiśca heyopādeyalakṣaṇam jñātum icchāmi vidhivat tan mamā cakṣva śāśvata  Paus śrī bhagavān uvāca yathā kṣīrasya vai snehaṃ bhedena na tu vartate evaṃ hi viddhi sarveṣāṃ tattvānāṃ parameśvaraḥ  Paus ekatvena pṛthaktvena samādhau proktam abhyaset kevalaṃ hi yathāpūrvam udviṣṭaṃ ca tadāptaye  Paus ākṣiteḥ karaṇagrāmam indriyākhyagaṇānvitam uttamavyaktaparyantaṃ prapañcaṃ tad anaśvaram  Paus nānāmūrtisamākhyaṃ ca bhogakṣetraṃ hi karmiṇām sukhaduḥkhaguṇopetaṃ mohamāyāmayaṃ dṛḍham  Paus ajñānaṃ tu tadāsaktervardhane tu kṣaṇāt kṣaṇam jñānād vilayam āyāti tasmāt nityaṃ hi tad dvija  Paus heyabhāvanayā cintyam upāyaṃ yadyapi sphuṭam siddhīnām ātmalābhe tu tatrāpyasthiram eva tat  Paus sāram ādāya vai tasmātsādhanaṃ yogasiddhaye manobuddhirahaṅkāraḥ sattvaṃ sattvavatāṃ vara  Paus catuṣkam udaṃ avyaktaṃ brahmaprāptyā nivartate athopakaraṇaṃ divyaṃ pañcaśaktyopalakṣitam  Paus kālajñānakriyākhyecchāprāṇasaṃjñaṃ mahāmate aheyam aparaṃ nityaṃ karmaṇyānāṃ ca siddhikṛt  Paus tattvavṛndasya vijaye guṇaṣaṭkopalabdhaye cāturātmyaparijñāne śabdabrahmāptaye tu vai  Paus prakāśānandalābhe tu nirvikalpapadāptaye navaprakāreṇānena prākprāptena gurormukhāt  Paus prākṛtenācyutīyena sādhyasādhanavastunā tad nāsti yad na ca āpnoti sākṣātkārāttu sādhakaḥ  Paus siddhadhyāna jayāt svaṃ svaṃ phalaṃ yacchati vai sadā etasmāt kāraṇāt sādhyaṃ sādhyasyānyasya sādhanam  Paus tacca jñānādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ brahmatattvavilakṣaṇam aṇimādyaṣṭakaṃ caivam ato nyaṃ rocate hi yat  Paus prabhavaḥ pralayaśvaiva aiśvaryaṃ sarvatomukham ādhyātmam ādhidaivatyam ādhibhūtātmanā dvija  Paus tattvābhyāsasamādhau tu jñātavyaṃ tattvacintakaiḥ śabdabrahmapadād eva kṣityante tattvasaṃgrahe  Paus adhyātmaṃ paramaṃ brahma sāmānyaṃ viddhi sarvadā jñātavyam adhidaivaṃ ca seśvaraṃ praṇavaṃ tathā  Paus svaṃ svaṃ svabhāvaṃ sarvasya sthūlasūkṣmaparātmakam vijñeyam adhibhūtatvaṃ sākṣātkamalalocana  Paus sāmānyam etat sarvatra dhyeyam adhyātmapūrvakam saviśeṣam ayo vakṣye śruṇuṣvaikāgramānasaḥ  Paus nistaraṅgaṃ paraṃ brahma śabdabrahmaṇi akṛtrime adhyātmaṃ dvija boddhavyaṃ mantrakoṭyā hyanekaśaḥ  Paus adhidaivatyabhāvena tasminneva sadā sthitāḥ adhibhūtaṃ tu boddhavyaṃ tad vāktttvacayaṃ tu yat  Paus adhyātmaguṇaṣaṭkākhyaṃ śabdabrahma yathoditam cāturātmyaṃ parijñeyam adhidaivam anākṛti  Paus śaktivyūham asaṃkhyaṃ yad guṇebhyaḥ pravadanti tu tadviśeṣasvarūpaṃ ca ādhibhūtaṃ tu viddhi tat  Paus prāṇaśaktestu cādhyātmaṃ ṣāḍguṇyam akhilaṃ hi yat adhidaivatam abjākṣo vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ  Paus adhibhūtam apānādyā vāyavo viśvadhārakāḥ icchāśakteḥ paratvena sthitaṃ jñānabaladvayam  Paus jñeyaṃ tad adhidaivaṃ ca paraḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ sāmarthyam adhibhūtaṃ ca sarvatattvāśritaṃ hi yat  Paus dvayam aiśvaryavīryākhyam adhyātmaṃ viddhi pauṣkara kriyāśaktestu daivatyaṃ pradyumnaḥ parameśvaraḥ  Paus mahatprakāśaprasaram adhibhūtaṃ sadoditam tejaḥ śaktirdvijādhyātmam avyaktam amalekṣaṇa  Paus arkenduvahnitritayaṃ daivataṃ parikīrtitam guṇatrayam asaṅkīrṇam adhibhūtaṃ mahāmate  Paus guṇatrayasya cādhyātmaṃ saṅghātakaraṇaṃ svakam sattvasya daivataṃ vahnī rajasaḥ tvaṃ amṛtātpaspadam  Paus tamasastapano viṣṇuḥ satva tve jñānādhibhūtatā rajasyarāgo vijñeyam adhibhūtaṃ mahāmate  Paus mahāmohaṃ hi tamasastvadhibhūtaṃ prakīrtitam adhyātmaṃ cetano buddherdharmaṃ sadadhidevatā  Paus sa vai rāgaṃ dvijaiśvaryam adhibhūtaṃ tadātmakam ahaṅkārākhyatattvasya buddhiḥ adhyātmam abjaja  Paus adhidaivaṃ parijñeyaṃ kālavaiśvānaro mahān mahattvam adhibhūtaṃ ca manaso tha nirucyate  Paus adhyātmaṃ tu ahaṅkāro nṛvarāhaḥ prajāpatiḥ vijñeyam adhidaivaṃ ca saṃkalpaṃm adhibhūtatā  Paus pañcānām indriyāṇāṃ tu adhyātmaṃ ca manaḥ smṛtam kālātmadaivataṃ viddhi adhibhūtaṃ sukhādikam  Paus vāgādīnāṃ dvijādhyātmaṃ vyūhaṃm indriyakaṃ tu yat adhidaivaṃ tu boddhavyaṃ viśvarūpākhyam acyutam  Paus vyāpāram adhibhūtaṃ ca aṣṭayonyātmakaṃ hi yat tanmātrāṇāṃ sabhūtānāṃm adhyātmam amalekṣaṇa  Paus sūsūkṣmaṃ karaṇavyūham adhidaivaṃ nibodhatu vaibhavaṃ bhagavadvyūhaṃ vicitraṃ viddhi padmaja  Paus boddhavyaṃm adhibhūtaṃ ca tattvabhūmijayaiṣiṇām uktam adhyātmapūrvaṃ yat tritayaṃ yogasiddhaye  Paus prabhāvena krameṇaiva tatpunaḥ caturānana āpyayena krameṇaiva abhyastaiḥ sarvayoginām  Paus ā kṣiteḥsarvaśaktyātmā padaparyantaṃ ācyutam tattvabuddhanirāsārthaṃ yogābhyāsaṃm idaṃ smṛtam  Paus bhavet tattvajayād bhinnaṃ phalaṃ tattvaṃ phalarthinām iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadipauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ tattvasamākhyānaṃ nāmatrayastriṃdhyāyaḥ atha catustriṃśodhyāyaḥśrībhagavānuvāca kṣetre vāyatane divye tīrthoddeśena saṃkutne kṣudradmāṇivimukte ca vane tūpavane śubhe  Paus bhūgṛhe vā gireḥ śṛṅge gupte devagṛhāntare svāsthyaṃ matvaikadeśe vā goṣṭhe dvijaparigrahe  Paus ardharātrād atikrānte kāle kamattrasaṃbhava khamantrasyāgratastveva tattvābhyāsaṃ samācaret  Paus tatra śrramajaye ttrabdhe dattvārdhyaṃ mantramūrdhani ghaṇṭāśabdasamopetaṃ dhūpaṃ dattvā mahāmate  Paus stutvā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śucisthāne tu sāstare kṛṣṇājinapraticchanne kutape kambale tu vā  Paus nidrāṃ santyajya vai brahman pāvane śayane sthitaḥ brāhme muhūrte cotthāya pañcāṅgaṃ snānam ācaret  Paus plavane vāpsu madhye vā sandhyāṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi tasyāgrataścopaviśya nirmalaṃ darpaṇaṃ dvija  Paus darśayitvopasaṃhṛtya mantraṃ hṛtkamalodare pratiṣṭhitaṃ nitya mantraṃ vinā sthala jalātmakān  Paus mantrān kriyāṅgasaṃruddhān saṃhṛtya tadanantaram śeṣamardhyādikaṃ sarvaṃ bhuktapūrveṇa vai saha  Paus pāṇinā toyapūrṇena viṣvaksenāya cārpya ca prāgvad abhyasi nikṣipya samāhṛtya tadākhilam  Paus svadehādupasaṃhāramantrāṇāmapi cācaret manasātmani viprendra kuryād bhogārjanaṃ tataḥ  Paus bhagavadyāgasidhyarthaṃ śuddhena draviṇena ca yācayitvā ca pātrebhyo vaiṣṇavebhyo hi nānyathā  Paus pauṣkara uvāca atyarthena jagannātha bhūyobhūyaḥ praśaṃsasi bhogebhyo dhūpadānaṃ ca ghaṇṭādhvanisamanvitam  Paus mahattāṃ jñātumicchāmi pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tathā yathāvad dhūpaghaṇṭābhyāṃ dhūpāgnerdhārakasya ca  Paus svarūpaṃ dhūpadhūmasya lakṣaṇaṃ pratyudīryatām śrībhagavānuvāca śabdabrahmaikadehāyāḥ lakṣaṇaṃ kamalodbhava pramāṇamatiśuddhaṃ ca saprameyaṃ nibodhatu  Paus samamardhasamaṃ jyeṣṭham āyāmadhamam atha madhyamam tattribhāgasamaṃ viddhi caturthāśaṃ tu kanyasam  Paus tribhāgena taducchrāyād dvā daśāṃśānvitena tu pramāṇena tu vistāraṃ trividhaṃ tu vidhīyate  Paus kṛtvā sūtraparicchinnaṃ prākpratyagdakṣiṇottaram caturaśrāyataṃ kṣetram evamāpādya vai purā  Paus tiryagūrdhvagataissūtrai bhaṅktvā saṃpūryate tataḥ tatra pañcordhvasūtrāṇi dadyād ekādaśāni ca  Paus bhujākhyāni ca vai yāni vibhāgam atha me śṛṇu sārdhaistu pañcabhirbhāgaiḥ śabdakṣetraṃ vidhīyate  Paus tatra cakraṃ ca kamalaṃ sarvadaśyaṃ prakalpya ca śaṅkhaṃ kamalasaṃbhūtaṃ muktāhārādikaṃ kramāt  Paus valayatritayāntasthaṃ muktāhāraṃ suvartulam bhāgārdhenāgrataḥ kuryāt tyaktvārdhār dhaṃ tadūrdhvataḥ  Paus śiṣṭenāṃśena mahatā bhāgārdhena tadūrdhvataḥ nābhikṣetrānvitaṃ cakraṃ dvādaśāraṃ vidhīyate  Paus kevalaṃ kartarībhirvā miśraṃ kṣmāmiśritairvaśāt ṣoḍaśāraṃ tu vā vipra śataśṛṅgaṃ manoharam  Paus sāṃśenāthordhvabhāgena karṇikākesarānvitam caturviṃśaddalaṃ padmam āpādya kamalodbhava  Paus cakranābherdalāgrāṇāṃ varjayitvāntaraṃ dhiyā yathābhimatamānaṃ ca suślakṣṇaracanojjhitam  Paus dalamadhyaniviṣṭaṃ va kiñjalkanicayaṃ śubham kuryād vā karṇikālagnam ucchritaṃ ca susaṃhatam  Paus ūrdhve mārgadvayenātha bhāgena śubhalakṣaṇam karṇikāvaniviśrāntam ardhadvaśyaṃ ca śaṅkharāṭ  Paus bhuvanāvattriyogena valībhūtena bhūṣitam oṅkārāvartarūpeṇa kumbhaṃ tasyāṃśasaṃmitam  Paus kumbhoparyatha cārdhena bhāgena tu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ kalaśaṃ ku kuśatāṃ nītvā cchidradeśāvadheḥ kramāt  Paus śaṅkhakumbhāvadhervipra śātanīyaṃ ca digdvayāt matsyavallāñchanaṃ caiva ardham ardhaṃ padadvayāt  Paus caturaṃśārdhavistīrṇā prathamā bhuvanāvalī dvitīyā viratā cānyā tṛtīyā bhāgasaṃmitā  Paus ā agrāt svadhiyā tvīṣadūrdhvāntaṃ kamalodbhava anupātavaśānmadhyaṃ kṣāmaṃ kṣetraṃ vidhīyate  Paus śaṅkhopari yathā kāryaṃ tathā tadavadhāraya sārdhabhāgacatuṣkeṇa taducchrāya mahāmate  Paus vistāraṃ sārdhabhāgena gadāyāṃ vihitaṃ tu vai muṣṭisaṃjñaṃ tu yatpīṭhaṃ kuryād bhāgonnataṃ dvija  Paus caturaśraṃ tu vā ślakṣaṇaṃ citrakarmavibhūṣitam vṛttāyāṃ caturaśraṃ tu turyāśraṃ vartule smṛtam  Paus tulyarūpaṃ hi vā brahman karagrāhaṃ ca tatra yat tattvaṣṭāgraṃ śraṃtu vā vṛttaṃ sāmānyaṃ sarvataḥ smṛtam  Paus muṣṭerūrdhvagataṃ kuryād gadāstambhaṃ ca pūrvavat viddhi taṃ saptaparvaṃ tu granthikā śuktibhiryutam  Paus muktāvaligaṇopetaṃ tīkṣṇāśraṃgraṃcaturaśrakam valayākṛtirūpeṇa yuktaṃ tārāgaṇena ca  Paus śuktivṛndasametena vartulaṃ vā samāpya ca racanārahitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ kevalaṃ caturaśrakam  Paus aṣṭāśraṃ ca suvṛttaṃ vā svapramāṇena lakṣitam kuryād evaṃ gadāstambham atha tanmastakopari  Paus bhāgadvayonnataṃ kuryād dvibhujaṃ vā caturbhujam prāguktaṃ pravibhaktāṅgaṃ pakṣamaṇḍalamaṇḍitam  Paus tatpakṣavistṛtaṃ kuryāccaturbhāgasamaṃ dvija tribhāgavitataṃ cātha pucchapakṣadvayaṃ hi tat  Paus tatsamaṃ vitataṃ caiva mukhyapāṇiyugaṃ tu vai vidheyaṃ kamattrodbhūta tasya saṃpuṭavadyathā  Paus pakṣavatprasṛtaṃ svasthaṃ vedādhyayanacihnitam mantrajātarataṃ caiva vidheyaṃ vā savistaram  Paus prastāryaṃ vidhinānena svayaṃ kṣititattre tataḥ śilpinaścaiva draṣṭavyaṃ pramāṇenākṛtaiḥ teḥsaha  Paus nyūnatvam atiriktaṃ vā ato hetostadagrataḥ pūrayedghṛdayenaiva svadhiyā karmaṇā svayam  Paus calantaṃ garbhamānena tīkṣṇalohena nirmitam bhāgārdhenādhikaṃ kṣetrāt śabdavyañjakamabjaja  Paus etāvad ādyaṃ vihitaṃ nirmāṇaṃ taijasaṃ mahat vyaktaṃ yatrāśritaṃ kāttraṃ nābhisthaṃ kamalodbhava  Paus tatra cākramarāvṛndaṃ svakaṃ dvādaśakaṃ smṛtam tadeva ṣoḍaśāraṃ ca varṇaiḥ saha napuṃsakaiḥ  Paus varṇānāṃ trividhaṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣāṃ kamalodbhava saṃsthitaṃ vaikharīniṣṭhaṃ paśyantī pūrvamabjaja  Paus arāśritadviṣaṭkāre vāksvarūpaṃ paraṃ hi yat tatraiva ṣoḍaśāre ca tatrevākartarīṣu ca  Paus madhyamākhyasvarūpeṇa nityameva hi vartate ata ūrdhvaṃ caturviṃśatsaṃkhyaṃ varṇaguṇaṃ hi yat  Paus dalajālaṃ hi yatpadmaṃ parijñeyaṃ mahāmate makārasaṃjñaṃ yadvarṇaṃ viddhi sā padmakarṇikā  Paus śaṅkhaṃ yakāravarṇaṃ samuṣṭīke gadāgrahe rādayaḥsapta ye varṇā hāntāḥ parvagadātmakāḥ  Paus kṣāntaṃ patatrirāṅviddhi evaṃ kamalasaṃbhava śabdabrahmasvarūpaṃ ca ghaṇṭāvigrahalakṣaṇā  Paus vijñeyā bhagavacchaktiḥ ṣāṅguṇyāntargatā hi sā tejogaṇasamopetā tejastad dravyarūpadhṛk  Paus ghaṇṭākhyameta dvai viddhi adhyakṣīyaṃ guṇadvayam śabdabrahmatvaheyaṃ yad hṛdayākāśamadhyagam  Paus nityoditamanaupamyaṃ manasā syādagocaram upadeṣṭum ato nyeṣām abhaktānāṃ na yujyate  Paus parasvarūpamantrāṇām etallakṣaṇam abjaja daśaprakāre yacchabde visargānte  kṣarādike  Paus nānāmantrasvarūpe ca vartate varṇavigrahe bhogamokṣaprade mantre ya āptaḥ sadgurormukhāt  Paus pañcasthānagataṃ jñeyaṃ bhaktairdivyakriyāparaiḥ bahisthaṃ pratimādau tu jihvāgre hṛtkuśeśaye  Paus dhūpadhūmaśikhāyāṃ ca ghaṇṭāśabde sulakṣaṇe svarūpaṃ jyotireṣāṃ tat bhāsayatsaṃsthitaṃ hṛdi  Paus madhyamena svarūpeṇa abhyucchinnaṃ mahāmate dhūpadhūmāśritaṃ viddhi vaikharīvigrahaṃ punaḥ  Paus ghaṇṭāyāṃ cālyamānāyām acchinnam anubhūtayeyate asyām āśritya ye saṃsthā jñātavyāstu sadaiva hi  Paus nityam arcanakāle tu sādhakaiḥ siddhilālasaiḥ kālavaikhānaropetam anantaṃ śabdacodake  Paus muktāhārāśritaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ghaṇṭāyā vadane sthitam saṃsthitaṃ ca mahābuddhe tadūrdhve gaganāśritam  Paus cakraṃ yasminnaroddeśe dvādaśātmā sthito raviḥ māsātmanā punaḥ saiva kartarīṣvavatiṣṭhati te   Paus ṣoḍaśātmakalātmā vai kalādehastu candramāḥ sarveṣu vṛttakṣetreṣu varuṇaḥ svayameva hi  Paus tattvasaṃvalitāvyaktapadmapatrāśritastu vai jīvaḥ kamalakiñjalke karṇikāśrita īśvaraḥ  Paus śaṅkhāhitaśca praṇavo vidyāṃ viddhi gadāśritam prāṇādhidaivaṃ garuḍam ityevaṃ devatāgaṇam  Paus dhyātvābhyarcya purārdhyāyaiḥ dhūpayitvā yathāvidhi pīṭhapratiṣṭhitāṃ kṛtvā kāleṣu kamalodbhava  Paus saṃcālanīyā vaidheṣu tāni me gadataḥ gṛṇu gaṇeśapīṭhamadhyasthadevānām arcane tataḥ  Paus āhutīkālamantrāṇāṃ dhūpadāne viśeṣataḥ japastutyavasānābhyāṃ pravṛtte cāgnitarpaṇe  Paus pūrṇāhutipradāne ca mantrāṇāṃ ca visarjane viṣvakasenārcanākāle tatpūjāpratipādane  Paus nāto nyathā syāt vihitaṃ cālanaṃ siddhimicchatā pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇopetaṃ saprameyaṃ sadaivatam  Paus yathāvad aravindottha mukhyam ityudinaṃ sphuṭam mukhyābhāsāni cānyāni rūpāṇyasya nibodhame  Paus yathoktaṃ trividhaṃ mānaṃ vistārāyām asaṃjñitam cakrādigarūḍāntena pañcasaṃkhyoditenatu  Paus saṃcālyābhimatenaiva yogyasthānāśritena ca pādanīracanāṃ vipra sarvāsāṃ ca vidhīyate  Paus padmaṃ kuryāt tadūrdhve tu praphullaṃ cordhvakarṇikam vitataṃ dīrghapatraṃ tu kiñjalkanicayānvitam  Paus tatkarṇikāśritaṃ kuryāt śaṅkhādyaṃ tritayaṃ hi yat vaktrasūtrasamīpe tu cakraṃ vā kevalaṃ dvija  Paus kṛtvā padmānvitaṃ paścāt śakhaṃ pūrvaṃ hi tat trayam yathoditaṃ ca saṃpādya sarvaṃ garuḍapaścimam  Paus vimuktacakrapadmasya kṣetrasyopari padmaja śaṅkhaṃ gadāṃ khagendraṃ ca saṃpādya caturānana  Paus kavāṭopari padmaṃ tu dīrghacchadam adhomukham śaṅkhacihna vinirmuktaṃ gadanālakhagānvitam  Paus samānena sabhūmervai śaṅkhaṃ kṛtvā yathoditam gadā kāryā tadūrdhve tu pannāgārisamanvitā  Paus kuryād vā garuḍoddeśe ūrdhvavaktraṃ ca hetikam kamalaṃ vā khavaktraṃ tu taduddeśe vidhīyate  Paus śaṅkhaṃ ca dakṣiṇāvartaṃ valitritayabhūṣitam ekaikam evam āpādya śaṅkhacakrāmbujojjhite  Paus suślakṣṇavartule kṣetre muktātāragaṇānane nirmuktalāñchanā ghaṇṭā vighnānām āśrayā bhavet  Paus lāñchitenānvitā vipra vighnavidrāviṇī hi sā ataḥ salāñchanā kāryā nūnaṃ bhartṛphalāptaye  Paus iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ dhūpaghaṇṭālakṣaṇaṃ nāma catustriṃśodhyāyaḥ atha pañcatriṃśodhyāyaḥśrībhagavānuvāca ityuktaṃ dhūpaghaṇṭāyā lakṣaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam yasyāṃ sañcālyamānāyāṃ dhūpadānāvadhau dvija  Paus sannidhiṃ bhajate śaśvanmantra ārādhakasya ca athāṅgulaiḥ svakaiḥ kuryād adhvamānamayaistu vā  Paus caturviśatibhirbrahman dhūpaṃ dāhakam uttamam āyāmenātha śilpīyairāyaśuddhaistu pūrvavat  Paus svacaturthāṃśamānena tadvaktram analāśtreyam caturaśraṃ samāpādya vṛttaṃ vāṣṭāśram abjaja  Paus asyāṣṭāśrasya vai madhye kuryāccakraṃ tu sāmbujam kamalaṃ vā sahetīśaṃ svastikaṃ vā nalagṛham  Paus yuktamuṣṇīṣapaṭṭena niṣṭhoddeśāttu kambunā caturaśrasya vṛttasya taccakrasyātha me śṛṇu  Paus lakṣaṇaṃ hi yathāvasthaṃ saviśeṣaṃ mahāmate caturatraṃ samāpādya kṣetraṃ vā vartulaṃ samam  Paus tadantare bjam abjotthanalinīnālarājitam kevalaṃ tu sacakraṃ vā vidhivad bhogabhājitam  Paus āmadhyād aṣṭadhā taṃ vai kṛtvā vai susamaiḥ purā bhramaṃ dadyāt ṣaḍaṃśena karṇikākoṭarāt tataḥ  Paus bhramantaṃ karṇikākhātaṃ nimnatāṃ ca nayed dvija tanmānaṃ golakārdhena jānīyānmudritaṃ yathā  Paus tṛtīyāṃśena ṣaḍbhāgāt paritaḥ karṇikocchritiḥ kiñjalkaistu susaṃvītaṃ tanmānenopalakṣitaiḥ  Paus saptamāṃśāttu yacchiṣṭaṃ bahiḥ kesarasantateḥ bhāgadvayaṃ tu vai yena dalajālaṃ samāpya ca  Paus yathābhimatasaṃkhyaṃ ca evaṃ bhāgena tadbahiḥ muktājālasamopetaṃ cakramāpādya pūrvavat  Paus aṣṭamāṃśāccaturthāṃśaṃ bhāgam ādāya vai dvija kṣetrasya coktamānasya vedyartham anuyojya ca  Paus vedyāḥ koṇacatuṣke tu cakuryācchaṅkhacatuṣṭayam caturaśrasya yā proktā vedikā śaṅkhabhūṣitā  Paus sthitirnaiṣā ca vihitā vṛttakṣetrasya padmaja padmapṛṣṭhād viniṣkrāntaṃ yathābhimatavartulam  Paus vedikāvaniparyantaṃ cakranemyavadhiṃ tu vā vaktrākāraṃ suvṛttaṃ vā taduddeśāt tu taṃ punaḥ  Paus vedisaṃdhāraṇārthaṃ tu procchritaṃ paṅkajadvayam tanmadhye lakṣaṇopetaṃ sthitaṃ padmāsanādinā  Paus kuryād āgneyam ākāraṃ tatpādayugalaṃ tu vai prasāritaṃ khavaktraṃ ca procchritaṃ śrotredaśagam  Paus nālāvasāne saṃpādya karṇikākamale dvija ardhaprakullai racitaiḥ padmapatraistathāgataiḥ  Paus tanmūle sādhikā kuryāt tadvistārāṃ mahāmate kṣmākṣetraṃ svastikopetaṃ suṣiraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ tu vā  Paus pṛṣṭhadeśe tha padmasya marutkṣetraṃ sabindukam kuryād ādhārabhūtaṃ ca kṣmākṣetrasyonnateḥ samam  Paus sārdhaṃ kṣmāvyāsavistāraṃ tatsamaṃ dviguṇaṃ tu vā cakranemyāśritaṃ caiva pralīnaṃ tacca susvanam  Paus ādyaṃ vā kiṅkiṇījālaṃ vighnavidrāvaṇaṃ param ityevaṃ saviśeṣaṃ hi lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam  Paus māntrasya dhūpamātrasya sāmānyam atha me śṛṇu vṛttasyābhyantare padmaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam  Paus aṣṭapatraṃ samāpādya vyomaktṛvibhūṣitam muktāsūtrānvitaṃ vātha evameva savedikam  Paus antarā dvādaśāreṇa sāmbujenātha vāhitam vicitrapatravitataṃ kuryāt pṛṣṭhāvadhestataḥ  Paus praphullapatrasthāne tu uṣṇīṣāṃśukabhūṣitam vaktraviśrāmabhūtaṃ ca ādhāravalayānvitam  Paus śuddhaṃ suślakṣṇanālaṃ ca nalinīracanojjhitam evam abhyūhyamākāraṃ mānenābhimatena tu  Paus sarvalohaiḥ svaśaktyā tu kṛtaṃ yacchati vai sukham mantriṇāṃ sūgahasthānāṃ bhaktānāṃ kamalodbhava  Paus vakṣye samudgarākhyasya lakṣaṇaṃ taṃ nibodhatu vistāroddiṣṭamānena suṣiraṃ vṛttasaṃpuṭam  Paus susamaṃ prāksamāpādya samudgakamivābjaja sanālaṃ ca tayorekam upariṣṭācca madhyataḥ  Paus prakullakamalenaiva adhovaktreṇa padmaja dvitīyam ūrdhvavaktreṇa sthagitaṃ paṅkajena tu  Paus sacchidraṃ bījasaṅghena yuktam ūrdhvasthitaṃ hi yata nālam āpādya mūlādvai vinatena gajāṅghriṇā  Paus nāladeśagalād dvābhyāṃ sthityarthaṃ viniyojya ca evaṃ praphullarūpāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam  Paus protthitānām idānīṃ vai lakṣma śṛṇu yathāgatam prāgāyāmāccaturthāṃśaṃ vaitatyena mahāmate  Paus caturaśrāyataṃ kṣetraṃ nikṣipya vasudhātale aṣṭadhātha tamāyāmaṃ susamaṃ saṃvibhajya ca  Paus caturdhā vistṛteścaiva kuryāttadanu padmaja aṣṭabhāgonnataṃ pīṭhaṃ prāguktaracanānvitam  Paus pādādyuṣṇīṣaparyantaṃ yathāvistāravistṛtam pīṭhārdhena ucchritaṃ caiva vistārāt tryaṃśasaṃmitam  Paus kamalaṃ pīṭhamadhye tu kuryād dvitayakarṇikam aṣṭapatraṃ sakiñjalkaṃ vyomavṛttavibhūṣitam  Paus vistārāccārdhabhāgena pṛthulaṃ connateḥ punaḥ sārdhabhāgacatuṣkena aṣṭāśraṃ vā suvartulam  Paus catusśraṃ tu vā ramyaṃ tadeva racanānvitam stambham āpādyam evaṃ hi yathābhimatam abjaja  Paus yebhyo yadvartulaṃ tadvai vicitraracanānvitam stambhamarutakaviśrāntaṃ bāhulyenāṃśasaṃmitam  Paus pīṭhatulyaṃ tu vistārāddvādaśāravibhūṣitam nābhinemiprathīyuktaṃ muktāhārādyalaṃkṛtam  Paus prāgvat sakiṅkiṇīkaṃ ca cakram āpādya padmaja tadakṣamadhyasaṃrūḍhaṃ sārdhāṃśenonnataṃ tu vai  Paus agrāt pīṭhasamaṃ caiva bāhulyāccakrasaṃmitam vistārād ardhabhāgena aṣṭoddeśācca saṃkaṭam  Paus kramaśaścānupātena tadvistāraṃ vidhīyate mukham evaṃ samāpādya sadhūmasya analasya ca  Paus sadāśravaṃ sadākālaṃ vibhorarcanakarmaṇi jalajaiḥ sthalajaiścaiva prāṇibhir nākajaistataiḥ  Paus patravallīvitānaiśca saśaṅkhaiḥ svastikaiḥ kajaiḥ kusumastabakaiḥ svacchaiḥ siddhavidyādharādikaiḥ  Paus devāṅganāsametaiśca dikṣu veśo bhavedbahiḥ etat prāsādayuktasya vṛttapīṭhānanasya ca  Paus yathāvad upadekṣyāmi sanniveśamatobjaja valitritayasaṃyuktaṃ śaṅkhānanamivāsanam  Paus padmamānonnotaṃ kuryād āsanopari padmaja stambhādhāraṃ vicitraṃ ca dvivyam āmalasārakam  Paus racanāracitaṃ stambhaṃ raktapūrvam athocchritam valayāvalitulyaṃ vā stambhanālasya tūpari  Paus cakravat kamalaṃ kurcāt sakiñjalkaṃ dviṣaṭpadam vistīrṇakarṇikaṃ vipra prāgvad vaktraṃ tadūrdhvagam  Paus yathoktaracanopetaṃ paritaḥ kintu vartulam muktāsūtrānvitaṃ caiva kiṅkiṇījālalāmbitam  Paus ebhyaścoktam athaikaṃ vai savidhānaṃ tadabjaja jalajasthalajā yātmyaracanāvyomya racitā mayā  Paus samabhyūhya ca sā kāryā sarveṣāṃ sarvadābjaja sphuṭāvasya yasmin vai kṛtāṅge tyantarājate  Paus idamuktaṃ samāsena lakṣaṇaṃ ca savistṛtam dhūpadāhakriyāṅgasya nānākṛtidharasya ca  Paus saṃpādyaivaṃ ca saṃskṛtya nītvā satyantatā punaḥ svamantrādhiṣṭhitaṃ kṛtvā pūjyam ādhārasaṃsthitam  Paus mūlataḥ svastikāsthāne kṣmātattvaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam salilaṃ kamalaṃ viddhi cakram agniṃ mahatprabham  Paus kiṅkiṇījālamanilam ākāśaṃ karṇikodare ityevaṃ sādhibhūtādhidaivatānugataṃ hi vai  Paus prāk proktaṃ bhāvanīyaṃ ca siddhaye khilakarmaṇām cakrasya sakalaṃ rūpaṃ nābhyarānemisapradhi  Paus niṣkalaṃ hi suvṛttaṃ yat vyomavṛtteti gīyate evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ dhūpapātraṃ samarcayet  Paus saṃskṛtya ca yathānyāyaṃ svavaṃśasya ca kīrtayet svanāmacihnitaṃ kṛtvā pratipādya mahāmate  Paus harerāyatane divye surasiddhaniṣevite trekālyaṃ balidānena dhūpadhūmena vai saha  Paus vādayet susvanāṃ ghaṇṭāṃ bherīśabdādikairyutām stotreḥ pradakṣiṇīkuryād bahudhā divyam ālayam  Paus siddhasaṃghaṃ ca tatrasthaṃ śabdabrahmaikam āsanam śrutvā ghaṇṭāravaṃ bāhyāt paritoṣaṃ mahāmate  Paus kasyedam acirādyāti amivyaktim anāhatam bhavyānām upadeśārthaṃ yenedaṃ vyañjitaṃ bahiḥ  Paus iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadipauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ dhūpādhāralakṣaṇo nāmapañcatriṃśo dhyāyaḥ  oṃatha ṣaṭtriṃśo dhyāyaḥ pauṣkara uvāca bhagavan jñātum icchāmi tvayā yat samudīritam mahātmano nuvidhdaṃ ca lakṣaṇenopalakṣitam  Paus yad yad āyatanaṃ divyaṃ sidhdāyatanam eva ca nṛṇām upāyabhūtaṃ yad ajñānāṃ jñāninām api  Paus yatrārādhanapūrvaṃ hi māntram abhyeti mantriṇām śaśvat prasannatā deva tathā tattvajayo mahān  Paus nirvighnena bhavatyāśu snātakabrahmacāriṇām yatīnāṃ muktasaṅgānāṃ viratānāṃ gṛhāśramāt  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca ākṣiter bhedabhinnaṃ vai māyāmayam idaṃ jagat kṣetrāravyair bhagavattattvaiḥ kṣetranāthasamanvitaiḥ  Paus nānāvibhavarūpaistu vyāptavyūhātmapūrvakaiḥ nityanirmalaṣāḍguṇyavigrahaistaiḥ svayaṃ punaḥ  Paus anugrahārthaṃ bhavinām akṛtajñālpamedhasām bhaktānām apyabhaktānāṃ nāstikānāṃ tathaiva ca  Paus bhūcakrākṣaṃ gate dvīpe hyanādiprathitaṃ hi yat kṣetraṃ svakarmaphaladaṃ puṇyaṃ parimitaṃ tu vai  Paus nṛṇām anugrahārthaṃ tu sthānabhedair adhiṣṭhitam amūrtestu svasaṃjñābhiḥ kāruṇyāt kṣetrasattamaiḥ  Paus tathā kṣetrādhipaiḥ kintu mūrtair yuktā navābjaja  bījabhāvena bhūmau vā sthitiṃ kṛtvā sthitāṃrāṃtataḥ  Paus jñānādyair vāṇimādyaiḥ tu avyaktaiḥ kṣmānalādikaiḥ tattvabījakalārūpair brahmasattāsamanvitaiḥ  Paus sahāvatīrya cāsṛṣṭeḥ prāg vyaktiṃ yānti vai tataḥ svayam evātmabhāvena sarvānugrahakāmyayā  Paus kṣmāmaṇḍalopasaṃhārakālaṃ kṣetravaraiḥ saha vaśitvāvaradehāṃstu pradhānamunivigrahān  Paus svāsmin svasmin hi yugapat kṣetre kṣemagatiprade svakāmanaikabhūtāṃ ca mūrtiṃ caivābhimānikīm  Paus kṛtvā vai vyaktibhāvaṃ ca pramāṇair uttamādikaiḥ yathākālānurūpaiśca vāsudhenopalātmanā  Paus ataḥ tadrūpanāmnā vai khyātā kṣetreśvarā bhuvi prakhyātāḥ tulyanāmnānye devāḥ sāyatanāstu vai  Paus evaṃ kṣetreśvaraiḥ kṣetraiḥ karmabhūmir adhiṣṭhitā kṣetrair amūrtaiścidrūpair mūrtaiḥ kṣaitrādhipaiḥ tathā  Paus iti yuktyāvatīrṇā ye kṣetrāṇāṃ kṣaitranāyakāḥ te pi kālāntareṇaiva svayaṃ doṣaṃ śilāmayam  Paus budhvāntardhānam āyānti deśabhaṃgādikair dvija vicāraiḥ pracuraiḥ bhūyaḥ prāgvad vyaktiṃ vrajanti ca  Paus svayaṃvāvanimadhyāt tu svasāmarthyena codayet kurvannanambunidher yadvad ambudaugham acoditam  Paus iti matpratipannānāṃ svapne pratyakṣato pi vā vadanti yogakṣemādyaṃ svayaṃ vā tanmayātmanām  Paus tattattvato tibhaktanāṃ satyārthaṃ sarvadā bhavet asatyārthamato nyeṣāṃ kintu puṣkarasaṃbhava  Paus ityutkarṣaṃ bhavatyeṣām astitvena samanvitam nirāsārtham abhaktānām nāstikatvena vāsatā  Paus tuṣṭaye hyāstikānāṃ tu tīrthādīnāṃ hi siddhaye kṣetreśā vāsudevāste sthitāścopalakukṣiṣu  Paus kvacit sākṣāt tathā cakraśaṃkhapadmagadātmanā viśeṣeṇa trikūṭe tu girau raivatake tu vai  Paus sālagrāme tu sahayādrau tathā viṣṇupade dvija vyāvarte caiva kṛṣṇāśve kukṣau tu tuhinācale  Paus mahendre malaye vindhye pāriyātre thavārbude satyavratasthe hastyadrau vikaṭe parvatottame  Paus siṃhācale mama kṣetre puṇye vā sumanohare evaṃ kamalasaṃbhūta vāsudevair adhiṣṭhite  Paus anekākṛtibhedasthair anekaikena kena cit ayatnāt kalpite kṣetre svanudhyā tu vrajanti ye  Paus āśritya kṣetranāthaṃ tu vipadyante ca tatra ye avasāne tu vā cā cānye dharāṃśe madhyame tu vā  Paus ādye vā devadṛg dṛṣṭe te prayānti krameṇa tu tasya vai kṣetratāthasya satyattvakṣmāgatasya ca  Paus tat sālokyaṃ tu sāmīpyaṃ sāyujyam amalekṣaṇa parigrahavihīnaṃ ca vivekarāhitaṃ janam  Paus śaraṇāgatabhūtaṃ tu api cennāstikaṃ purā tathāntikaṃ śraddhadhānaṃ niśceṣṭaṃ cāpi pauṣkara  Paus visaṃjñaṃ bandhubhir nītaṃ kārūṇyāt kamalodbhava trāhityuktvā jagannāthaṃ kṣiptvā strībālapūrvakaiḥ  Paus jñātvā vimuktadehaṃ taṃ saha puryaṣṭakena tu mahatā tūryaghoṣeṇa kṛtvā rathavare tu vai  Paus jitvāntakabhaṭān raudrān balāt kṣetreśakiṃkaraiḥ nṛsiṃhakapilakroḍavāmanāśvaśiromukhaiḥ  Paus sasaumyavadanaiḥ padmaśaṃkhacakragadādharaiḥ sīranandakadhṛga vajrapāśāṅkuśa dhanurdharaiḥ  Paus musalāditathādaṇḍahastaiśca garūḍānanai ānīya kṣetranāthasya tvabhigacchāpayanti ca  Paus devakṣetre tvadīye sya vimuktaṃ pāñcabhautikam śarīram adyānāthasya kurūśaśvad yathocitam  Paus kṣaitranāthastu tad vākyaṃ samākarṇyāñca gaṇeritam karūṇānugatenaiva taṃ nirīkṣya tu cakṣuṣā  Paus kṛtaṃ vigatapāpaṃ tu tasminnāyatane purā saṃprāptasya svake sthāne doṣaśeṣaṃ hi vai punaḥ  Paus saṃsargeṇa layaṃ nītvā kramāt kālāntareṇa vai dvābhyām evaṃ prakāreṇa yad anyaccātmasāt kṛtam  Paus tatsthaṃ liṅgavaśātkṛṣya svaśaktyā ca svavigrahāt saṃskārayogyatāṃ jñātvā samyajjñānāptaye tu vai  Paus dadāti karmabhūmau tu janma satkarmiṇāṃ kule sava kṣetrai vā parakṣetre tatra sālokanaṃ hi yat  Paus kālāt prāptādhikāraśca kṛtvā vyāptāṃ samāsataḥ yathocitam anuṣṭhānaṃ trayodaśavidhaṃ śubham  Paus tat tena kṛtakṛtyaṃ syāt tadardhena tu cāparam tṛtīyaṃm abjasaṃbhūta samyajjñānena yujyate  Paus jñānatamātraṃ hi vai kālād indriyavyaktilakṣaṇaṃṇāt svayaṃ cīrṇavrataṃ prāgvat tat kṣetre budhdipūrvakam  Paus tīvrabhāvena vai paścāddehatyāgaṃ vratādinā kuryāt kṣetrādhipasyāgre tad vattaṃ gatakalmaṣam  Paus pṛthagdehāraṇīṃ kṛtvā jñānaṃ yada dharmamalaṃ śubham sa tasyopadaudiśatyājyaṃ  tatrai veva kamalekṣaṇa  Paus yatprāpya paramaṃ dhāma vāsudevākhyam eva ca yogināṃ tīrthapuṇyāni brahmannāpatitāni ca  Paus sadāvyādhārabhāvena hayaṃgabhāvaṃ vrajanti vai yogotkṛṣṭaprakṛṣṭaṃ ca prāpyanti jñānino pi ye  Paus śaśvajjñānasamākīrṇaṃ nirvighnenāpnuvanti ca evamāyā ya tanād brahmannupāyaṃ bhavināṃ param  Paus yato sti ca ato hetoḥ sevanīyaṃ sadaiva hi abhijātasya bījasya yathāmalamarīcayaḥ  Paus prārohajananīṃ śaktiṃ santāpān dhvaṃsayanti ca vinā svarūpahāner vai sāṃ hyevameva hi  Paus svaprabhāvena vai samyak svaśaktikiraṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ prakṣīṇakalpamaṣaṃ kṛtvā kṣetre vai kṣetravāsinām  Paus kurvantyanugrahaṃ paścāt kṣīṇapāpasya tasya ca mṛdambuhutabhug vātapātair gaganalakṣaṇaiḥ  Paus prasiddhayaṃtritaṃ hyatra asidhdaṃ tadvayaṃ śruṇu yad annāmbu parityāgādvātaṃ tad vāta saṃjñitam  Paus sarvadvāroparodhena yad annābhāsamuttamam kālaṃ vā deha pātīyaṃ sanyag jñātvātra pauṣkara  Paus kāryam ārādane yatnāt tatra bhaktyā śubhaiṣiṇā yadi na prāpnuyāt caiva janmābhyāsādavāpyate  Paus vilayaṃ yānti vai yena trāhi nāghānijanmani janmani kṛtabudhder manuṣyasya pāpenātibalīyasā  Paus na sañjātā ca tat prāptir yadyapyabjasamudbhava na śāsanasya ghorasya cāntakasya sa bhājanam  Paus mānyo yamabhaṭānāṃ ca yajñayājī yathā pumān āstāṃ hi tāvanmanujā niyamādyair alaṃkṛtāḥ  Paus bhāvabhaktiviśeṣāḍhyāḥ prāṇino nyepi tatra ye prāksaṃskāravaśājjātāḥ te pi jātyantaraṃ punaḥ  Paus nāpnuvanti mṛtā vipra sadvivekavivarjitāḥ mama bhaktāyatanānāṃ ca ityeṣāṃ yastu vindati  Paus nṛṇāṃ madhye sa dhanyo vai duṣkṛtair nātibādhyate karmaṇāṃ vai hyabhuktānāṃ na nāśosti ca yadyapi  Paus tānavaṃ kṣetramāhātmyaprabhāvāt saṃprayānti te janmābhyāsavaśenaiva nūnaṃ karmakṣayo bhavet  Paus sāmarthyāt kṣetranāthānāṃ sakṣetrāṇāṃ mahāmate kṣetreṣvevaṃ prakāreṣu dānaṃ yacchanti ye rthinām  Paus vibhorārādhanārthaṃ tu bhaktyā kurvanti vā tapaḥ sādhayanti ca mantreśaṃ tarpayanti tilādibhiḥ  Paus yajanti makhair devān labhante te khilaṃ phalam dvādaśākṣarapūrveḥ tu prasidhdaiḥ kamalodbhava  Paus mantrair jitantā matrāntaiḥ prāptairvātha guror mukhāt svakena mantremukhyena vidhivat parameśvaram  Paus ārādhyāyatanasthaṃ ca yat yatkiñcid adhikāriṇām dvijendra dvijamukhyānāṃ dīyate pāñcakālinām  Paus tad akṣayaṃ parijñeyaṃ bhavabhogābhilāṣiṇām dānānnivṛttarāgāṇāṃ tat punar mokṣasiddhaye  Paus grāma maṇḍaladeśāntarmaryādāyatanavāsinām dattam ātmasamaiḥ bhūtyai bahubhir nirūjo śnute  Paus saṃpūrṇāsu svaśaktyā ca nityaṃ janmani janmani anantabhavikaṃ vidhdi tat divyāyatanāt punaḥ  Paus ajñeyaṃ lakṣabhavikaṃ tat sidhdāyatanāt tu vai sahasrabhavikaṃ vipra viprapravarakalpitāt  Paus daśāṅgabhavikaṃ tadvai kṛtaṃ yat kṣatriyena tu tadardhabhavikaṃ viddhi sadvaiśyaparikalpitāt  Paus satśūdra kalpite vipra dattam āyatane tu vai dviṣaṭak bhavanaṃ tadvai dānaṃ jñeyaṃ dvijottama  Paus ananyaśaraṇebhyo vai varṇebhyaḥ parikalpite dvijendrāyatane dattaṃ phalaṃ tat punareva hi   Paus vyāmiśrayājibhir varṇair nirmitāyatanāstu ye pūrvoktebhyaḥ prayacchanti tadardhabhavikaṃ kramāt  Paus phalakāmaphale psūnāṃ niṣkāmānāṃ hi pauṣkara sarvāyatanago devaḥ sarvamūrtiṣvavasthitaḥ  Paus mūrtyantaragataścāpi prādurbhāvagatastvapi prādurbhāvānta rāyā  vṛttiṃ dadāti paramaṃ padam  Paus ācartavyam ataḥ tasmādyatnena mahatā dvija mantrārādhanapūrveṇa karmaṇā cidvilakṣaṇam  Paus tasmādvimuktarāgāṇāṃ nṛṇām acyutayājinām vyajyate svātmavṛttisthaṃ vāsudevam ajaṃ vibhum  Paus tadadhiṣṭhitacittastu yatra yatra yajet bahiḥ tatra tatra tadā teṣāṃ vyajyate brahma śāśvatam  Paus pauṣkara uvāca devāyatanajātānāṃ nṛṇām aśubhakāriṇām mṛtānāṃ tatra vāhya nyatra jñātum icchāmyahaṃ gatim  Paus śrībhagavān uvāca kenacit prāktanenaiva karmaṇāvimalena ca ācarantyabjasaṃbhūta matervai duṣkṛtaṃ punaḥ  Paus jñātvāpi kṣetramāhātmyaṃ vivaśāt tu balāt tu vai taṃ mriyantaṃ ca tatrāsthe ntejanmābhyāsavaśena tu  Paus kṣetre ca pāpataḥ teṣāṃ saṃkṣipatyantakasya ca śaśvadduṣkṛta śānyarthaṃ upāyair nātiśāsanaiḥ śvataiḥ  Paus tvam eva teṣāṃ kurūṣe bhuktaśeṣaṃ hi kalmaṣam śamayatyacirādeva ācaranti yathāśubham  Paus bhūyaḥ prāptena dehe bhogena asmadīye parigrahe sa cājñāṃ śirasā tāṃ vai kṛtvā caiva mahāmate  Paus karūṇānugatenaiva saṃśodhayati cetasā evaṃ vigatadoṣāḥ te yānti kālāntareṇa tu  Paus sāhacaryācca sākalyāt satsaṃparkādviśeṣataḥ prakṣīṇakalmaṣā nūnaṃ punarāyānti vaidikīm  Paus samācaranti tadvastu sāyujyaṃ yānti yena vai pauṣkara uvāca tadutpannā vipadyanti pāpiṣṭhā hyatra vai yadi kā gatir bhavate teṣāṃ narāṇām atipāpinām  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca śodhayatyantakaḥ teṣāṃ duṣkṛtiṃ nātiśāsanaiḥ gatadoṣāḥ samāyānti mānuṣyaṃ hi tadā punaḥ  Paus matir dehavipattyarthā tīvreṇa manasābjaja prayāti pūrvavacchuddhiṃ yathā duṣkṛtino narāḥ  Paus tatra jātāśca nirdeṣā ye nyatra vilayaṃ gatāḥ prayānti sāṃprataṃ te vai vimānair antakāspadam  Paus saṃpūjayatyasau teṣāṃ brūyādbaddhāñjalistataḥ sthānam āyatanaṃyeṣāṃ bhagavantaṃ vrajantu vai  Paus sālokyasaṃjñaṃ vimalaṃ bhavabandhakṣayaṃkaram madīyadarśitenaiva mārgeṇānena sādhunā  Paus bhavatāṃ saṃprayātānāṃ śubhaṃ tatra bhaviṣyati tadvāsināṃ yathānyeṣāṃ bhagavat tattvavedinām  Paus evaṃ abjasamudbhūta phalam āyatanāt bhavet narāṇāṃ nirvivekānāṃ tadanyeṣāṃ tu kiṃ punaḥ  Paus kṣitiḥ pādau ca khaṃ nābhirdyaiḥ śiraḥ śaśibhāskarau netre lokā mahatpūrvā vibhoryasya śirorūhāḥ  Paus diśaḥ śrotre bhujāścaiva vidiśaḥ sarva eva hi ādhāraśaktiparyantaṃ yasya pātālasaṃtatiḥ  Paus sthitiḥ pādataloddeśe nityākṛtidharasya ca vibhor vai rājamānyasya sarvagasya mahātmanaḥ  Paus sarvaṃ padātmakaṃ yasmād bhaktānām ata eva hi nahyanāyatanaṃ deśam āstikānāṃ dvijāsti vai  Paus carācaram idaṃ sarvaṃ nāstikānāṃ tamomayam suprasiddhaṃ tu vai sthānamāstāṃ tāvanmahāmate  Paus bhaktyāvasthāpitā yatra sthāne vipravarādikaiḥ acalā vā calā ramyā citramṛtkāṣṭhaśailajā  Paus hemādidhātulohotthā yā kācit pratimā hareḥ nṛṇāṃ tatra vipannānāṃ tanmāhātmyavaśāt tu vai  Paus sthitiḥ triviṣṭape teṣām anatyutkṛṣṭalakṣaṇā ante paricyute janma yeṣām āyataneṣu ca  Paus yathākramaṃ karmamahābuddhe parijñeyaṃ hi matparaiḥ sākṣādvṛttir dvijendrīyā kṣetrakṣetreṣu jāyate  Paus kṣatriyāyatanādvi dvṛddhi janmāmaravinirmite sadvaiśyakalitoddeśe janma puṣkarasaṃbhava  Paus munibhir nirmitasthāne acyutāyatane bjaja mā janma maudgalīyācca prāpnotyārādhanānnaraḥ  Paus kalpitaṃ mantrasiddhena nareṇāyatanam mahat bhogotkarṣaṃ hi vai nṝṇāṃ tathā kālāntareṇa ca  Paus mantrajñaiḥ kalpitāntaṃ ca yāvad āyatanam dvija śaśvat pāpakṣayaṃ cānyat kṣatriyaṃ tadanantaram  Paus krameṇa savitānaṃ ca nātidīrdheṇa pauṣkara kālāntareṇa vai teṣāṃ doṣāṇāṃ tu parikṣayam  Paus avatīrya kṣitiṃ paścād bhuktaśeṣaṃ hi padmaja kṣapayatyāśu tatraiva niyamaiḥ pūrvaduṣkṛtam  Paus prāgvat smṛtāḥ krameṇeva te yānti paramaṃ padam pātā ye vihitāścātra dehatyāgavighau śubhe  Paus vivekināṃ na vihitāḥ prāyaścittasthameva hi ājanma sañcitānāṃ ca duṣkṛtānāṃ kṣayāya vai  Paus labhante taistu nirdagdhair dehānte padam ācyutam tasmāt kṣetraṃ samāsādya prāyaścittaṃ samācaret  Paus svayaṃ pāpaphalaṃ jñātvā sattvam āśritya śāśvatam virūddhacittabuddhistu yena yāti śubhāṃ sthitim  Paus balavā nyavadyadapi kṣetraṃ nṝṇāṃ śubhagatipradam tadvivekaṃ dvitīyaṃ vai svasāmarthyaṃ tu nojjñati  Paus mano buddhīndriyagaṇaṃ karaṇagrāmasaṃyutam āmlādyasya saṃśuddhamante vā tapasā mahat  Paus kurvantyanugrahaṃ tasya śaśvadāyatanādayaḥ jīva bhāvasthito jantuḥ paralokaṃ gatastu vā  Paus bhūguṇā api cādeyāḥ sarvatra vidhigauravāt yathā mahānubhāvānām purūṣāṇāṃ tu yācakāḥ  Paus saṃhṛṣṭam annapānārthaṃ guṇajñam aguṇaṃ tu vai tyajantyaguṇatāṃścaiva saguṇaṃ vāpi cānyathā  Paus jñātvaivaṃ kṣetramāhātmyaṃ tapodhyānajapādikaiḥ karmavākcittasaṃtoṣādupaśobhāṃ nayet parām  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca caturbhir vāsudevādyair mūrtibhiḥ prāgudīritaiḥ keśavādyair dvādaśabhir matsyādyair daśabhiḥ tataḥ  Paus kṣmāntaṃ ṣaḍviṃśasaṃkhyaṃ yat tattvavṛndaṃ puroditam vyāptam īśvarapūrvaṃ vai dvādaśānām saha sthitam  Paus susthūlenānurūpeṇa daśakaṃ tena cāvṛtam tattvaṃ tattvaṃ samāsādya vāsudevādinā saha  Paus sthitir evaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ bhavaśāntaye guṇaṣaṭkasamopetaṃ vaiśvarūpyaṃ mahāmate  Paus svavyāpāravaśenaiva vyañjayanti sadaiva hi anugrahavaśenaiva vibhoricchāvaśena tu  Paus sarvaiḥ kṣititalaṃ vyāptaṃ nānākāradharaiḥ sadā ekaikā vaibhave mūrtir anantenātmatāṃ yathā  Paus yānti nānātmanām evaṃ vāhanāyudhalāñchanaiḥ ataścellokanārthāyaicchātaḥ prābhavena tu  Paus sthitir nānāprakārā vai sarveṣāṃ ca svabhūtiṣu niyataḥ sāyudhānāṃ ca lāñchanānāṃ ca yadyapi  Paus tathāpi sarvamūtīnāṃ sarve sādhāraṇāḥ smṛtāḥ yadyapyevaṃ hi vai vipra tatrāpi vinibodha me  Paus na ca anyabhrāntiśāntyarthaṃ viśeṣaṃ lāñchanair dhvajaiḥ prādurbhāvāḥ tu vijñeyāḥ svavyāpāravaśāttu vai  Paus prādurbhāvāntarāstadvadaṃśasya tu vaśādapi ādyakā rakṣakādhārāḥ kecit tu dhvajalāñchanaiḥ  Paus tulyam evaṃ trayāṇāṃ tu prādurbhāvagaṇaṃ param apare keśavādīnāṃ tulyam udvahati nti dvija  Paus ākārair lāchanaiḥ sārdhaṃ tad viśeṣeṇa vai saha pauṣkara uvāca śrotum icchāmi bhagavan sarveṣāṃ lāñchanādikam viśeṣo yaḥ layoddiṣṭo bhavināṃ bhavaśāntaye  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca śṛṇu lāñchanavinyāsam ādidevāditaḥ kramāt matto nigadataḥ samyak yathāvad amalekṣaṇa  Paus ādyaḥ pāṇiḥ caturṇā vai dakṣiṇe tvabhayapradaḥ varaprado vā bhaktānāṃ dhātavyamamalekṣaṇa  Paus vāmo śaṅkhodvahaṃ viddhi nānāsthityā caturṣvapi ādyasya paścimābhyāṃ tu vāmadakṣiṇayoḥ punaḥ  Paus kālacakraṃ gadāṃ gurvīm acyutasyāvadhāraya lāṅgalaṃ musalopetaṃ vāmahaste sadakṣiṇe  Paus paścime bhujayugme sya saṃhate ca dhanuḥ śare kheṭakaṃ nandakopetam anirūddhasya pauṣkara  Paus dvābhyāṃ paścimapāṇibhyāṃ madhyahastāditaḥ tu vai ityevaṃ hi caturmūrter etanmūrtyantareṣu ca  Paus śaṃkhacakragadāpadmalāṃchanānāṃ sthitiṃ śruṇu ādidevīyadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ tāvaducyate  Paus vāme paścimage cakraṃ viddhi śaṅkhaṃ tu dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇe mukhyahaste bjaṃ gadā tadapare tu vai  Paus evaṃ hi bhagavān dhatte keśavaḥ kamalādikam savyāpasavya hastābhyāṃ mukhyābhyāṃ tu gadāmbuje  Paus vāmādau śaṅkhacakrau tu sa dhatte paścimadvaye nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavān mādhavākhyo nibodhatu  Paus mukhye savyāpasavpaye tu śaṅkhaṃ dhatte gadāṃ prabhuḥ paścime padmacakre tu sarvapūrve bhujadvaye  Paus mūrtitrayam idaṃ divyaṃ kundendusphaṭikaprabham bhagavadvāsudevena sahāsya caturātmanā  Paus tritayasya parijñeyā mokṣadā bhavabhogadā kāmapālīyadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ kamalodbhava  Paus padmaṃ mukhyakare vāme gadānyasmin hi dakṣiṇe vibhorgovindasaṃjñasya ityevaṃ samudāhṛtam  Paus vinyāsaṃ lāñchanānāṃ ca viṣṇoratha nibodhatu vāmadakṣiṇapāṇibhyām agrataḥ śaṃkha paṅkaje  Paus evaṃ paścimahastābhyāṃ cakraṃ kaumodakīdvayam madhusūdanasaṃjñasya saṃniveśam ataḥ śṛṇu  Paus padmaṃ mukhyakare vāme pāñcajanyaṃ tu dakṣiṇe gadā paścimataḥ savye cakraṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pare  Paus trayam evaṃ hi devānāṃ saha vai jñānamūrtinām cāturātmyād dvitīyāṃ tu padmarāgojjvaladyutim  Paus atha pradyumnadevānāṃ trayāṇāṃ krama ucyate varṇabhedena saha vai lāñchanagrahaṇaṃ śṛṇu  Paus agrato vāmapāṇau ca cakram anyakare gadā vāme tu paścime śaṅkhaṃ padmaṃ tadapare smṛtam  Paus vibhoḥ trivikramākhyasya vāmanasyāvadhāraya gadāgravāmahaste tu cakraṃ mukhye tu dakṣiṇe  Paus vāme tu paścime padmaṃ śaṅkhaṃ tat dakṣiṇe kare śrīdharasya gadā vāme mukhyahaste prakīrtitā  Paus cakram agre pasavyākhye śaṅkhaṃ vāme tu paścime tadānyasmin pare padmaṃ cakraṃ koṭisamaprabham  Paus mūrtitritayam etetadvai saha ca svāminā dvija hemadhāmaprabhaṃ jñeyaṃ cāturātmyatayā sthitam  Paus ato nirūddhamūrtīnāṃ tritayaṃ cāvadhāraya lāñchanodvahanaṃ caiva varṇabhedena vai saha  Paus padmaṃ agrakare vāme tat dvitīye tu hetirāṭ savyāpasavyahastābhyāṃ paścimābhyāṃ krameṇa tu  Paus padmakośaṃ gadāṃ gurvīṃ padmanābhe nibodhatu agrage cakrarākhyapadmaṃ muḍvāmekare pare  Paus vāme gadāṃ paścimage tadanyasmiṃśca śaṅkharāṭ dhatte dāmodaro vāme gadāṃ cāgrasthite śubhām  Paus apasavye grage śaṅkhaṃ vāme cakraṃ tu paścime paścime tvapasavye tu kamalaṃ sūryavarcasam  Paus atasīpuṣpasaṅkāśam idaṃ mūrtigaṇaṃ smṛtam sahānirūddhadevena asyāpi caturātmatā  Paus viśveśvarasya vai viṣṇoḥ sthitaye smin jagattraye amūrtānāṃ ca mūrtānām āyudhānāṃ sthitiṃ śṛṇu  Paus pāṇidvayena cākrāntau pārśvadvaye pṛthak sthitau tanmukhaṃ ca nirīkṣantau gadācakrau mahāmate  Paus śaṅkhapāṇiṃ ca śaṅkheśaṃ yugmam anyena hetinā dvayādikaṃ karajālaṃ yat tannānābhisamanvitam  Paus pāṃśāṃṅkuśāsipadmādyair yuktaṃ cānyair varāyudhaiḥ mūrtyantarāṇāṃ mūrtīnāṃ ṣoḍaśānām ataḥ śṛṇu  Paus mukhyahaste caturṇāṃ tu pāñcajanyaṃ nirākṛtim sarvadehaṃ hi sañcintya gadācakre dvijottama  Paus hastadvayena cākrāntau sākāraṃ ca vibhor mukham pibantam iva mṛtpātre smartavyaṃ tatparāyaṇaiḥ  Paus amūrtamantrasaṃsthānam idānīm avadhāraya tam icchayā ca smartavyaṃ śobhālīlāvaśād api  Paus nānādeśajanasthityā āsṛṣṭeḥ saṃsthitaṃ yathā āmūrteḥ sahamūrtānāṃ saṃdhāraṇam athocyate  Paus paścimābhyāṃ bhujābhyāṃ tu yasya yadvihitaṃ dvayam mūrdhadeśāt samākrāntaṃ nirīkṣantaṃ vibhor mukham  Paus ājñāpratīkṣakaṃ caiva haste taṃtadvyajanādikam kakṣāntar gatahastaṃ vā atha vismayamudrayā  Paus yuktaṃ sampuṭasaṃjñākhyaṃ mudrayā vābjasaṃbhava caturvadanapādā vai dhānadhyānarūpaṃ tu saṃsthitiḥ  Paus sarveṣāṃ vihitā vipra prayojanavaśena tu sādhakecchāvaśāccaiva tathā kālavaśāt tu vai  Paus prārthinaścopaviṃṣṭāstu bhogaśayyāgatāstvatha cakrāmburūhapīṭhasthā hṛhi dhāmatrayānvitam  Paus dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu vācakaiḥ prāgudīritaiḥ sāmānyair dvijamantrair vā ṣaḍbhiḥṣāḍguṇyalakṣaṇaiḥ  Paus yorcayet bhaktipūrvaṃ tu svaśaktyā vibhavena vā sa muktadoṣa abhyeti tat tat padam anāmayam  Paus vyaktaṃ kṣetravaśe yasmin svayaṃ bāhaye vatāritam siddher viśeṣanāmnā ca tatra sidhyanti sādhakāḥ  Paus svamantrajapino bhaktā nityaśuddhāḥ kriyāparāḥ atha mūrtyantarāṇāṃ ca devānāṃ kamalo dbhava  Paus dhvajādyaṃ ya cca saṃketaṃ tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu trayaṃ vadāmi devīyaṃ keśavādyaṃ prakīrtitam  Paus bhūṣitaṃ prapatākena mahad garūḍaketunā mahatā tālavṛkṣeṇa lāṅgalīyena pauṣkara  Paus govindādyaṃ trayaṃ yadvai vijñeyam upaśobhitam dhvajena makarākhyena pradyumnaṃ yena ca dvija  Paus trivikramādyaṃ tritayaṃ nityam eva vibhūṣitam kuraṅgalāchanenaiva anirūddhena lāñchitam  Paus trayaṃ dāmodarāntaṃ ca hṛṣīkeśādikam hi yat viśveśvarasya ca vibhor icchārūpadharasya ca  Paus vihitāḥ sarva evaite rūpaiśvaryeṇa vai saha varāhanārasiṃhādyair devaistribhuvaneśvaraiḥ  Paus prādurbhāvāntaropetaiḥdevaiḥ sarvaguṇojvalaiḥ yathocitaiścāturātmyaiḥ keśavādyaistato bjaja  Paus haṃsamatsyahayaiḥ kūrmasiṃhasūkarasaṃjñakaiḥ yathoktalakṣaṇair brahman śaktitaḥ pratipattijaiḥ  Paus vṛttitvena jagatyasmin arcanādhyānakarmaṇi yatīnāṃ muktasaṅgānāṃ siddhānāṃ kṣetravāsinām  Paus evaṃ yathoktavadanair nṛśarīrair mahābhujaiḥ nṛvarāhanṛsiṃhākhyair nṛvājivadanābhidhaiḥ  Paus anugṛhadhiyā vyāptaṃ bhūbhāgam amalekṣaṇa tathā vāmananāthena kharvamūtidhareṇa ca  Paus snātakabrahmacārī ca lāñchanair bhūṣitena ca tasya rūpāntareṇaiva sukhānāṃ sukhadena ca  Paus trivikramākhyasaṃjñena trailokyākrāntamūrtinā rāmasaṃjñena vibhunā jvalat paraśupāṇinā  Paus bhārāvataraṇaṃ yena pṛthivyāṃ bahuśaḥ kṛtam etair anyair dvijaśreṣṭha vakṣyamāṇasamanvitaiḥ  Paus sabāhayābhyaṃtaraṃ vyāptaṃ brahmāṇḍanicayaṃ hi yat prādurmāvāntaraiḥ sārdhaṃ prādurbhāvair dvijākhilaiḥ  Paus apyayaiḥ prabhavākhyaistu gauṇamukhyaiḥ sureśvaraiḥ svabhāvam ajahacchaśvad ākārāntaram ākṛteḥ  Paus yat tattvam aṃśasaṃbhūtaṃ prādurbhāvāntaraṃ tu tat prādurbhāvāntaropetaṃ prādurbhāvagaṇaṃ param  Paus śṛṇu me gadataḥ samyak yair vyāptam akhilaṃ jagat rāmo paraḥ kṣatrajanmā bhrātrātṛbhedaiḥ stribhiḥ saha  Paus nihantā rākṣasānāṃ yo manuṣyo ham iti smaran kṛtakṛtyastu yo vettā svabhāvaṃ divyam uttamam  Paus aparaḥ sīrapāṇir vai rāmaḥ kṛṣṇātmanā saha śiśubhāvaṃ samāśritya yo mahaddivyakarmakṛt  Paus kālkiśca viṣṇur bhagavān naṣṭadharmāvatārakṛt urvyāṃ mleṃchagaṇaṃ hatvā viddhi tam yat kalau yuge  Paus dharmātmā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ prādurbhāvaṃ ca śāśvatam prādurbhūtaṃ hi vai yasmānnarādyaṃ kṛṣṇapaścimam  Paus sapañcakālaṣaṭkarmama svasvadharmaiḥ samanvitam japadhyānasamopetam evaṃ yaḥ pāti sarvadā  Paus caturmūrtimayaṃ vipra naro nārāyaṇo hariḥ kṛṣṇasaṃjñaśca bhagavān prādurbhāvottaram vibhoḥ  Paus prakāśitaṃ caturdhā te ato nyam avadhāraya viśvarūpaḥ sa bhagavāna bahuvigrahalakṣaṇam  Paus tatraikam antarākhyaṃ hi kṛṣṇanāthasya pauṣkara mānuṣyatve vatīrṇasya trayam ādyam anaśvaram  Paus sahasravadanaḥ śrīmān sahasrāṅghrikarastathā mūrtāmūrtaṃ ca yo dhatte gotreṣvamarasaṃgraham  Paus jalāravindanābhaśca prādurbhāveśvaro mahān prabhavāpyayakṛdyogair bahubhedairūpāsitaiḥ  Paus madhukaiṭabhamāthī ca prādurbhāveśvarasya ca prādurbhāvāntaraṃ viddhi padmanābhasya tadvibhoḥ  Paus mandarotpātakṛddeva vastvatvamṛtāharaṇa stathā sudhākalaśadhṛk caiva vanitākṛtivigrahaḥ  Paus bhūyo rūpāntaraṃ tasya rāhościccheda mastakam evaṃ caturdhā bhagavāneṣa eva mahāmate  Paus prādurbhāvāntaropetaṃ prādurbhāvottamottamam samastasaubhāgyanidhir lakṣmīnāthaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ  Paus na dvitīyaḥ prasannātmā nṛṇāṃ bhogāpavargadaḥ lakṣmīrūpāntarair yuktaḥ caturbhir garūḍāsanaḥ  Paus punaḥ tadāsanaṃ cānyad adaṣṭabhedaiḥśriyānvitaḥ devādīnāṃ manovṛttipūrako bhogapūrvakam  Paus bhogavān kālanemighnaḥ pakṣīndravaravāhanaḥ sahasrārakaraḥśrīmān śrīvatsāṃṅkitalakṣaṇaḥ  Paus kālavaiśvānaraḥ śālinātha ḥpāthonivāsinaḥ  ādhāraśaktijñaṃsya ā amūrtasya ca vai vibhoḥ  Paus abhimānatanuryo vai nānābhedaiśca vartate gajendragrāhamokṣī ca saṃsārādrasalakṣaṇāt  Paus jñānopadeṣṭā bhagavān kapilākṣastvadhokṣajaḥ vidyāmūrtiścaturvaktro brahmā vai lokapūjitaḥ  Paus tamaṃśabhūtaṃ vai samyak viśvavyañjanalakṣaṇam yugāvasāne saṃhāraṃ yaḥ karoti ca sarvadā  Paus śaṅkarākhyo mahārūdraḥ prādurbhāvāntaraṃ hi tat devasyānalaśāler vai sarvādhaḥ saṃsthitasya ca  Paus lokeśvaraḥ śāntatanurbaudhdaṃ yasmāparaṃ viduḥ nirya ya ntā buddhidharmāṇāṃ hiṃsādoṣasya dūṣakaḥ  Paus agnīṣomātmasaṃjñasya devasya paramātmanaḥ sūryācandramasau viddhi sākārau locaneśvarau  Paus tadvaktraṃ daivataṃ cānyaddhutabhuk parameśvaraḥ mantrapūtaṃ sadādāya hutamājyapurassaram  Paus brahmāṇḍabhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ santarpayati sarvadā viśveśaprāṇaśakter vai vāyvākhyam adhidaivatam  Paus jagatsandhārakaṃ caiva nānāskandhātmanā tu vai ete bhagavadākārāstiṣṭhantyasmijagattraye  Paus nānāveśasvarūpaiśca nānāsaṃsthānalakṣaṇaiḥ nānākāryavaśenaiva nānākāravaśena tu  Paus evaṃ kṛtakaśabdādyair bhagavāṃstatkṣaṇena ca ārādhyākṛtitulyena tajjapadhyānasevinām  Paus yathābhimatarūpeṇa guṇaṣaṭkānvitena ca jñasvabhāvena nityena svarūpeṇāmalātmanā  Paus viśvamāpūritaṃ sarvaṃ sarvānugrahakāmyayā sarvatra yāsti sarveṣāṃ yathoktānāṃ mahāmate  Paus vāsudevādimūrtīnāṃ vaiśvarūpyam anaśvaram yogaiśvaryaprabhāvena acyutecchāvaśādapi  Paus jñātvaivam abjasaṃbhūta na kāryo hṛdi vismayaḥ sphuṭeśvabhrasvarūpeṇa nānānāmānvitena vai  Paus dṛṣṭoṣṭebhagavadākāre svayaṃ vyaktādikena ca kṣitimadhye vatīrṇe ca pūrvoddiṣṭena vartmanā  Paus tīrthoddeśeṣu sarveṣu kṣetreṣu vividheṣu ca giriśṛṅgeṣu ramyeṣu tanmadhyeṣu guhāsu ca  Paus vaneṣūpavanāḍhayeṣu pātālatalabhūmiṣu lokontareṣūrdhvageṣu devair gandharvasattamaiḥ  Paus nāstikā bhinnamaryādā mohamāyāmalānvitāḥ vikalpadoṣairāviṣṭāḥ bhrāntabuddhijaḍīkṛtāḥ  Paus caraṇāmbujanālaṃ tu parāmṛśyanti ye dhamā majjanti narake ghore pitṛbhiḥsahitāścirāt  Paus sadāyatanadevānāṃ mūlaṃ ye cānviṣanti vai mūrdhnaśchedo bhavetteṣāṃ bhāvopahatacetasām  Paus dhṛtiśaktimayaṃ mūlaṃ devānāmapi durdṛśam tatkathaṃ lakṣyate mūḍhairyanmūrtadravyatāṃ gatam  Paus mānameyaiḥsvatantraṃ ca yathā tatparamadbhutama yairetanmadhyaṣaṭkaṃ tu kṣetreśāṅghrikajaissthitaiḥtam  Paus guṇairdivyayaguṇopetairūrjitaiḥ prākṛtairguṇaiḥ svayamevaṃ jayannāthair avatīrya ca yā sthitiḥ  Paus gṛhītā susthirā caiva susiddhaiścāpi kalpitā doṣaisadigvibhāgādyair anyadātvena yānti ca  Paus nityasannidhimāhātmyāt kālaṃ kalpakṣayāvadhi uttarottaratā caiva jagatyasmin hi vartate  Paus duṣṭopaśāntidā śaktyā siddhidā yā ca vai saha paurūṣāyatanānāṃ ca siddhākhyānāṃ mahāmate  Paus svayamevāvatīrṇānāṃ tattveśānāmapi kṣitau ataḥsaṃsārabhītaiśca bhaktaiḥsarveśvarasya ca  Paus gamyaiśca tercanīyāśca kālaṃ vai jīvitāvādhi nityaṃ tūpāsitavyāśca tatrasthairāśramānvitaiḥ  Paus prāptādhikārair dīkṣāntasamayajñādikairnaraiḥ yadaiva kṛtadīkṣāṇām adhikārasamanvitam  Paus acyutārādhanārthaṃ tu niḥśreyasapadāptaye tadaiva pratiṣiddhaṃ ca devatāntarapūjanam  Paus parametaddhi samayam aprameyaratātmanām sā prasiddhā tu vai vyaktād ākārāt parameśvarāt  Paus vyūhād vā vibhavākhyācca ṛte nānyat puroditāt samarcanīyam ākāraṃ na budhairvasudhāgatam  Paus kvacidbhagavadaṃśaistu prādurbhāvair adhiṣṭhitāḥ dṛśyante pārthivā liṅgāḥ śrūyante ca dvijottama  Paus yadyapyevaṃ mahābuddhe vaiṣṇavānāṃ tathāpi hi viruddhatvād anarcyāste nopādhir vaiṣṇavī hi sā  Paus svayaṃmuvāpi ye kecit surasiddhāvatāritāḥ skandarudramahendrādyāḥ pratiṣiddhāstu tercane  Paus antaryāmī ca sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ puruṣottamaḥ yadyapyavyaktarūpe ca vyaktau siddhiḥsvakā svakā  Paus bhāvabhaktivaśād vipra svakri kīyādhigamādapi jñātvaivaṃ bhaktisāṃkaryaṃ na kuryādevameva hi  Paus varjanīyaṃ prayatnena ya icched uttamāṃ gatim viprā ekāyanākhyā ye te bhaktāstattvato cyute  Paus ekāntinaḥsutattvasthā dehāntānnānyānyayājinaḥ kartavyatvena ye viṣṇuṃ saṃyajanti phalaṃ vinā  Paus prāpnuvanti ca dehānte vāsudevatvam abjaja vyāmiśrayājinaścānye bhaktābhāsāḥ tu te smṛtāḥ  Paus parijñeyāḥ tu te viprā nānāmārgagaṇārcanāt tasmāt saṃsiddhadehastu dīkṣākhyena tu karmaṇā  Paus yāvajjapādhikāraṃ tu nārāyaṇaparo bhavet japahomakriyāsaktaḥ samāste stutitatparaḥ  Paus dehānte vaiṣṇavaṃ lokaṃ prāpnuyāt punareva hi janma cāsādya cotkṛṣṭam ābālyād dvijasattama  Paus bhagavatkarmaniṣṇātaḥ tatparastanmayo bhavet nābhisandhāya ca phalam āpatkālagato pi vai  Paus tyaktvā dehaṃ punarjanma nāpnuyādiha pauṣkara pauṣkara ucāca bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa kṣetraiḥ kṣetravaraissaha pāramyena ca yairvyāptaṃ kṣityantaṃ tattvasaṃgraham  Paus vāsudevākhyasadbrahmatatvād ārabhya vai kramāt vaktumarhasi me śaśvat sarvānugrahakāmyayā  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca ṣāḍguṇyadehasaṃjñena svasthena caturātmanā svargāntaṃ svapadā vyāptam adhidevātmanā dvija  Paus yā vai sarveśvarī śaktir īśvarākhyā viśāmanī jñānādibhedabhinnena ādyena caturātmanā  Paus vyāptā cāvyaktaliṅgena bhārūpeṇa mahātmanā yā parā prakṛtirdaivī satvaikaguṇalakṣaṇā  Paus pūrṇā śaktisamūhena vaibhavīyena padmaja saha mūrtyantareṇaiva prādurbhāvāntarastathā  Paus prādurbhāvamayairbījaiḥ samūhe caturātmanā jīvakṣetrajñakātmanāmadheyam anaśvaram  Paus vartate vai samāsādya nityaṃ saiveśvarecchayā traiguṇyasāmyam ādhāram avyaktākhyaṃ ca śāśvatam  Paus tatrastham abhimānākhyarūpeṇa parameśvara m sphuṭam avyaktabhedaṃ ca cāturātmyaṃ jagatprabhum  Paus dvibhujaṃ purūṣākārayuktam ādityasannibhaiḥ bham dhvajair ābharaṇaiścihnaiḥśaṅkhacakrādisaṃjñitaiḥ  Paus avyakte buddhitattve ca sthitaṃ vyaktataraṃ vibhum caturmūrtiṃ caturvaktraṃ caturbāhuṃ caturgatim  Paus lāñchanair dhvajaparyantair vyaktairyuktamanaśvaraiḥ ahaṅkāraṃ samāśritya avyaktaṃ kamalodbhava  Paus sthitā mūrtyantarāḥsarve keśavādyāstu vai smṛtāḥ haṃsādyāḥṣaṇmayoktā ye yathāsaṃsiddhilakṣaṇāḥ  Paus manastattvaṃ samāsādya samyak jñānaguṇānvitāḥ buddhīndriyaguṇaṃ vipra ṣaḍete punaranyathā  Paus paurūṣaṃ dehamāsādya saṃsthitāḥ parameśvarāḥ kalkiniṣṭhā ṣaḍbhujāśca vāmanādyā dvijeśvarāḥ  Paus karmendriyasamūhaṃ tu tiṣṭhantyāśritya sarvadā dharmādyā viśvarūpāntā ye ca sarvaguṇairyutāḥ  Paus tanmātrāpañcakaṃ khādyaṃ samāśritya ca saṃsthitāḥ ākāśādyaṃ samūhaṃ yadbhūtānāmabjasaṃbhava  Paus saṃsthitā vai samāśritya prāguktā vibudhottamāḥ uktaśeṣair mahābuddhe prādurbhāvāntaraiḥ saha  Paus uparāgaṃ yathāsādya lokatrayasamanvitam ekadeśaṃ samāyāti tīrthasaṃṅgaṃ kurūkṣitau  Paus anugrahadhiyā caiva parayā kṛpayā dvija antakāle tu buddhānāṃ devairvyāptam anusmaran  Paus adhyakṣo daivataṃ kṣmāntaṃ vigrahaṃ tattvasaṃgraham vācyavācakayuktāstu te pi yānti parāṃ gatim  Paus yasmādvai bhagavacchaktyā tvanukampākhyayā dvija āviśya bāndhavaiḥsnigdhaṃ jantoḥ saṅgatisiddhaye  Paus tattasyānena vidhinā āpādayati vai śubham tīrthe vāyatane kṣetre visaṃjñasya mahāmate  Paus pauṣkara uvāca kṣetraiḥ kṣaitreśvaropetair bhūtānām iha yatprabho anugrahārtham ākrāntaṃ tamādiśatu sāmpratam  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca karmabhūmau manuṣyāṇāṃ bhavyāḥ kṣetrāḥ tathā hi ye agamyāḥ tvapi teṣāṃ ye surasiddhagaṇaṃ vinā  Paus sāmprataṃ me ca te śaśvadekāgram avadhāraya āryāvarte tu bhūbhāge pṛthivyāṃ puṇyasaṃjñake  Paus madhyadeśasamopete caturdikpariniṣṭhite sāmudrajalalekhāyāṃ tatparyante mahāntare  Paus āsṛṣṭeravatīrṇā yeḥ svādhiṣṭhānaiḥsahākhilāḥ ādidevādayo devā vyaktivigrahalakṣaṇāḥ  Paus yatra yatra ca bhūbhāge yo yassārveśvaraṃ vapuḥ yasmādyasmāttu vai tasmād āsṛṣṭeretya saṃsthitāḥ  Paus kṣetraśenānvitāścaiva tīrtheśena tathaiva hi yasmāddevālayodeśāt dhmātasya jalajasya ca  Paus bhavecchabdāttavedhaśca tāvat kṣetraṃ taducyate divyādyāyatanādīnām antaraṃ yadanaśvaram  Paus krośādhikasamaṃ nyūnaṃ mānenānena yena tu antarvedī ca sā jñeyā nārāyaṇaratātmanām  Paus yajane śrāddhakaraṇe dāne votkramaṇercane japadhyāne tapoyajñe agnisantarpaṇenapi ca  Paus sthitaṃ yadekadeśe tu dīpāloko dvijottama ābhāsayati bhūbhāgaṃ paratastadvadeva hi  Paus svakṣetraṃ kṣetranāthaṃ ca samāsādya ca vartate aihikāmuṣmikī caiva siddhir bhavati dehinām  Paus tatra tāvaccaturmūrter mūrtyantaragaṇasya ca sanniveśaṃ pṛthivyāṃ vai sāmprataṃ tvavadhāraya  Paus puṣkaraṃ kṣetramāśritya puṇḍarīkākṣasaṃjñayā vāsudevastu bhagavānnityasannihitaḥsthitaḥ  Paus evaṃ kṣetravaraiḥ sarvametya viśveśvaraḥsvayam caturmūrtidvijādyaṃ vai āsṛṣṭeḥsaṃsthitiṃ kratau  Paus caturṇāṃ mūrtibhedaṃ yad dviṣaṭkaparisaṃkhyayā kṣetraiḥ tīrthānvitaisteṣāṃ saṃsthānam avadhāraya  Paus keśavaḥ kleśahā loke vai dvairūpyeṇa kṣitau sthitaḥ abhivyaktena rūpeṇa govindaḥ purūṣottamaḥ  Paus bhūbhāgapadamāśritya saṃsthito nagasāhṛye  Paus sthāne vṛndāvanākhye pi dvidhaiva kamalodbhava viṣṇurlokāgha he vipra sthito viṣṇupadena ca  Paus mandarākhyagiriṃ caiva āsādya madhusūdanaḥ bhūtānām anukampārtham avatīrya ca saṃsthitaḥ  Paus yāmunaṃ jalamāśritya devadevastrivikramaḥ sthitaḥ kamalasaṃbhūta nṛṇāṃ ca sugatipradaḥ  Paus mūrtyantaraṃ vāmanākhyaṃ sahayādrau kamalodbhava svatattvādetya viśrāntaṃ bhavināṃ śokaśāntaye  Paus narmadākhyaṃ hi cākramya jalaṃ pāpakṣayaṅkaram śrīdharaḥ saṃsthito devaḥ kauṇḍale ca śriyā saha  Paus hṛṣīkeśastu bhagavān saṃsthito pyātmanā bhuvi dharādhare dhvajākhye tu kṣetre kubjāmrake bjaja  Paus padmanābhastu mādhyeśastvavatīrya ca saṃsthitaḥ dākṣiṇāṃ diśam āśritya samīpe jaladhikṣitau  Paus girau revatake vipra svatattvādetya vartate dāmodarastu bhagavān hitārthaṃ bhāvitātmanām  Paus ebhir mūrtyantaraiḥ sārdhaṃ mūrtibhiḥ viśvamandiram samāsādya dvijaśreṣṭha ato nyeṣāṃ ca saṃsthitim  Paus nibodhatu mahābuddhe sāvadhānena cetasā siddhāmarārcitaṃ viddhi śvetadvīpe tu haṃsarāṭ  Paus matsyātmā bhagavānapsu aśvātmā baḍabāmukhe rasātale tu kūrmātmā vindhyāraṇye tu pauṣkara  Paus vijñātavyo mṛgendrātmā pāpahā sarvadehinām saukarīyena rūpeṇa kṣetre tatsaṃjñake tu vai  Paus gāṅge śubhajale kūle surasiddhaniṣevite hemottamāṅgadṛgdevo hemaśailamahāntare  Paus naubandhanagirāveva mīnavaktraḥ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ kṛṣṇāśve śvaśiro devo kṣitikṣetre kṣamārcite  Paus lavaṇodadhiparyante bhūbhāge siddhasevite kūrmavaktraśca bhagavān saṃsthitaḥ śaṅkhacakradhṛk  Paus nṛhariḥ kṛtaśauce tu ujjayinyām api dvija viśākhamūlasaṃjñe tu sthāne tvevaṃ sthitastridhā  Paus kokāmukhe varāhastu vārāhe tu nagottame kandamāle vivaicetaste kulakukṣau himācale  Paus vāmanaṃ kharvamūrtiṃ ca vaiśvarūpyeṇa saṃsthitam  madhyadeśe tu gaṅgāyāḥ kurūkṣetre tu pauṣkara  Paus yāmunaṃ kulamāsādya prādurbhāvāntaraṃ mahat sthitaṃ trivikramākhyaṃ yastrailokyākrāntāvigrahaḥ  Paus nagottame mahendrākhye paraśvathakaro dvija rāmasaṃjñaśca bhagavān saṃsthitaḥ kṣatriyāntakaḥ  Paus dharādhare citrakūṭe rakṣaḥkṣayakaro mahān saṃsthitaścāparo rāmaḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇaḥ  Paus rāmo nyaḥsīrapāṇir vai yāmunaṃ bhrāmayañjalam saṃsthito mānuṣīyeṣu bhūbhāgeṣu śubheṣu ca  Paus sāmudre pi tato dvīpe dvārakākhye marārcite vartate bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ  Paus kalkī viṣṇuśca bhagavān stūyamāno dvijaiḥ sthitaḥ samāsādya vipāśāṃ ca nadīṃ niyatamānasaḥ  Paus dharmamūrtir mahātmā vai dharmāraṇye surārcite anugrahaparastvāste lokānāṃ lokapūjitaḥ  Paus narasaṃjñaṃ jagannāthaṃ siddhaiḥ saṃpūjiteṣu ca bhūbhāgeṣu ca ramyeṣu nityasannihitaḥ sthitaḥ  Paus girau govardhanākhye tu devaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ saṃsthitaḥ pūjite sthāne gavāṃ niṣkramaṇeṣu ca  Paus sāligrāme ca bhagavān rājendrākhye vane dvija tathaiva vasudhāṃśena sthito devavratābhidhe  Paus kṛṣṇo paraścaturmūrtir avatīrya dharātale sthitaḥpiṇḍārake vipra mocayanduṣkṛtājjanān  Paus śvetadvīpe kurūkṣetre himavantācale bjaja vedikāyāmapi nare viśvarūpaḥsthitaḥ prabhuḥ  Paus kṣīrodadhau padmanābhaḥśeṣāhiśayanopari sthito nābhyabjasaṃbhūto yasmāccaiva pitāmahaḥ  Paus caturdhā rūpamāśritya viśve smin saiva vartate  hitāya sarvalokānāṃ yathāvad avadhāraya  Paus āsādya śayanaṃ brahman pātālatalasaṃsthitaḥ rūpamādāya cāgneyaṃ yo nte saṃharate jagat  Paus vaṭamūlaṃ samāśritya prayāge surapūjite jagadekārṇavaṃ kṛtvā divyam āsādya pādapam  Paus santiṣṭhate sa bhagavāṃstasmiṃstīre kṣitau dvija nyagrodhaśāyinaṃ caiva dhyoyeddivyagatipradam  Paus himācalaikadeśe tu tuṅge vai bhṛgusaṃjñake madhukaiṭabhamāthī ca saṃsthitaḥ so vanītale  Paus kṣīrodakakṣitikṣetre surāsuraniṣevite mandrarādrikaro devo vartate devapūjitaḥ  Paus tatraivāmṛtajiddevaḥ saṃsthitaḥ siddhasevitaḥ kāntārūpadharaścaiva sudhākalaśadhṛk tathā  Paus siddhānāṃ ca munīnāṃ ca devānāṃ mṛtyujit sthitaḥ dvidhā kartā gaṇopetaṃ devaṃ garūḍavāhanam  Paus sālavṛkṣabhujoddeśe sāligrāme sthito vibhuḥ trikūṭagiripṛṣṭhe tu gamye gaganacāriṇām  Paus gajoddhṛticchalenaiva aprameyākhyayā sthitaḥ śvetadvīpapatir deva avatīrya ca saṃsthitaḥ  Paus gaṃgāsamudrasaṃyoge kṣityudeśe manorame yajñabhug bhagavān devo naimiśe siddhapūjite  Paus saindhavāraṇyam āśritya ananto bhagavāṃssthitaḥ śārṅgapāṇistu deveśo daṇḍakāraṇyasaṃjñake  Paus rakṣogaṇakulaṃ caiva saṃsthitaḥ tajjayaiṣiṇām utpalāvartake deśe śaurisaṃjño cyutaḥsa ca  Paus kṣitau samudrasindhvorabdheḥ saṅgame siddhasevite jñānopadeṣṭā bhagavān saṃsthito duḥkhaśāntaye  Paus āsādya sūkarakṣetraṃ devo garūḍavāhanaḥ saṃsthito garūḍārūḍhaḥ pārijātakarāṅkitaḥ  Paus siddhaiḥ suragaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ gagane cāpi pauṣkara devadeveśanāmnātha hastiparvatamastake  Paus ekadeśaṃ samāsādya sarvasya varadaḥ sthitaḥ mālyodapāṇir vaikuṣṭho magadhāyāṃ mahāmate  Paus oḍḍīnye puṇyabhūbhāge saṃsthitaḥ purūṣottamaḥ acintyātmātha bhagavān parvate gandhamādane  Paus śipiviṣṭākhyayā devaḥ śipiviṣṭavrate sthitaḥ prāksamudrāpayāne tu bhūbhāge śubhalakṣaṇe  Paus kāpilaṃ mūrtim āsādya vāsudevaḥ sthita prabhuḥ avatīrya svatattvācca brahmasaṃjñaḥ prajāpatiḥ  Paus maṇibandhaṃ samāsādya nityaṃ sannihitaḥ sthitaḥ magadhāmaṇḍale vipra mahābodhadharāśritaḥ  Paus saṃsthito lokanāthātmā devadevo janārdanaḥ devadakṣiṇagākṣṇor vai yo bhimānatanur dvijaḥ  Paus sūryasaṃjñastu bhagavān hemaśailopari sthitaḥ acyuto vāmanetre tu yo bhimānatanur vibhuḥ  Paus bhagavān somasaṃjñaḥ tu somatīrthāśrame pi ca agnisvarūpamajitaṃ saṃsthitaṃ baḍabānale  Paus vasvātmā gagane vipra bhāsate tvasurāntakṛt viṣṇunāmnā punar devaḥ tvanekāyudhamaṇḍitaḥ  Paus jayākhyayojjayinyāṃ vai sthitaḥ pāpajaye nṛṇām kāśmīramaṇḍale puṇye kṣetre cakradharābhidhe  Paus cakrapāṇistu bhagavān bhaktānāṃ mokṣadaḥ sthitaḥ surottamābhidhānaśca gadāpāṇistu pauṣkara  Paus sadā sannihitaṃ viddhi gaṅgādvāre suraiḥ saha caturbhujaścaturmūrtiścaturvaktraścaturgatiḥ  Paus sthitaḥ piṇḍārake devo viṣvaksenaḥ sanātanaḥ śubham āsādya bhūbhāgaṃ prāgjyotiṣapure tathā  Paus devaṃ viśveśvarākhyaṃ ca sthitametya svagocarāt sātatranābhidhakṣetre siddhavidyādharānvite  Paus svāmisaṃjño jagannāthaḥ sthito mandākinītaṭe bhallātake mahāyoge dhyāyinām apavargadaḥ  Paus rasātale nṛsiṃhākhye devikāyā stataṭāśrite ripukṣayākhyayā vipra devaḥ sarveśvaraḥ sthitaḥ  Paus śaṅkarākhye tu bhūbhāge sarvadevaniṣevite jñānamūrtir jagannāthaḥ saṃsthitaḥśubhakṛnnṛṇām  Paus pṛthivyāṃ tu pitṛkṣetre mocayantānṛṇatrayāt janārdanākhyayā brahman viśvātmā bhagavān sthitaḥ  Paus ete vatārāḥ kathitā leśataḥ kamalodbhava ebhiḥ kṣititalaṃ vyāptaṃ paunaḥpunyena ca svayam  Paus saṃsāriṇāṃ janānāṃ tu anugrahadhiyābjaja saṅkīrtanam agamyānāṃ trisandhyaṃ nityam ācaret  Paus matiṃ cakre kuryāccagamyānāṃ sevane darśane pi ca mlecchānāṃ teṣu deśeṣu kṣitau kṣetrādayo hi ye  Paus sāṅkaryaparihāreṇa draṣṭavyāste sadaiva hi ṛṣibhiḥ sāmaraiḥ siddhaiḥ svāśrameṣu mahatsu ca  Paus jalāśayeṣu puṇyeṣu pṛthivyāṃ vividheṣu ca sarve bhagavādākārā vibhavavyūhalakṣaṇāḥ  Paus u mu ktā gatāśca ye cānye samutprekṣya dhiyāsvayam pratiṣṭhitāśca vidhivat samantrāḥ satyavikramāḥ  Paus sthityā nānāprakārā ye bhūtabhavyādikākhyayā saumyāgneyobhayākhyena sanniveśavaśena vai  Paus līlārūcimayenaiva cittasaukhyapradena ca bhujādyāyudhasandhānaketubhedena vai saha  Paus alaṃkṛtaśca bhūbhāgo manujaistvevameva hi bhaktair anugrahītaiśca siddhādyaiśca yathoditam  Paus ādidevādayaścaite tattveśāḥ samudīritāḥ parasmin bhagavattatve tattvabhedena vyavasthitāḥ  Paus sūryasya raśmayo yadvadvahnercirgaṇaṃ yathā jaladherūrmayo yadvat tadvadevābjasaṃbhava  Paus citsāmānyāninnityaśuddhā vyāpakāḥ parameśvarāḥ tattvasattāṃ samāśritya jñānādyaiḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ  Paus aṇimādyaṣṭakopetāḥ saṃsthitāḥ svātmanā tu vai adhvāvaniṣu sarvāsu nityaṃ kurvanti sannidhim  Paus muktaye sarvabhūtānāṃ viśeṣeṇa tu vai bhuvi āviśvaprabhavāt kālādārabhya pralayāvadhi  Paus kṣetreṣu tīrthatīreṣu śabdabrahmayātmanā sāmānyenāpi mantreṇa tadvivartena bhātmanā  Paus tato vyaktetaraṃ rūpam āśrayanti ca pārthivam hitārthaṃ sarvalokānām avatīrṇam anaśvaram  Paus jagatyāyatanākhyāyām atra sidhyanti yoginaḥ kālāntareṇa vyaktīnāṃ majjanaṃ jāyate yadi  Paus sannidhiṃ śaktibhāvena nityaṃ kurvanti tatra ca yogeśvarāmarāḥ siddhāḥ smṛtvākāraṃ tadātmakam  Paus śailamuddārūdhātūtthāṃ vyaktiṃ saṃsthāpayanti ca yatrānuvedhaṃ kurūrvate mantraśaktidharā stu ye  Paus yenācyutīyanāmnā vai yadyatsvānāntaraṃ smṛtam sannidhisthasya vai rūpaṃ śabdamūrtidharasya ca  Paus bhinnātmanāṃ svayaṃvyaktirūpeṣvavyaktakeṣu ca sannirūddheṣu mantreṣu icchāvṛttigateṣu ca  Paus ākārāḥ saṃnniveśācca pārameśvaram anyathā anyathā vai jagatyasmin khyātākhyātaṃ ca śāśvatam  Paus evam āyatanānāṃ ca nityatvaṃ saṃprakāśitam anāditvam asaṃkhyaṃ ca mahattvam api pauṣkara  Paus jātā ye māṃ prasiddhir vai sati vyaktivaśād dvija vinā vyaktisvarūpeṇa śabdenāpyakṣayātmanā  Paus vdyātmanāpi hi cānyatra śabdavyāktimayātmanā anye munivarā vipra dṛṣṭvā sthānaṃ manoramam  Paus nirdeṣaṃ salilaṃ śuddhaṃ pādapauṣadhisaṃkulam sthitiṃ kṛtvā sthirāṃ tatra karmaṇā manasā tataḥ  Paus sulakṣaṇaṃ tu pāṣāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā cānyatra vāhṛtam viśvakarmakulodbhūtaṃ samājñāpya tu śilpinam  Paus upale smijjagadyonerviṣṇoḥ sarveśvarasya ca pādāravindamudrāṃ ca sampādya ca manoharām  Paus evam anye tu munayaḥ svasthāneṣu mahāmate śaṅkhacakragadāpadmapūrvā ye harilāñchanāḥ  Paus niveśaṃ tatra kṛtvā vai bhaktipūtena karmaṇā apare tu dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaktibṛṃhitamānasāḥ  Paus kurvanti sanniveśaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā pūvokteṣu ca deśeṣu siddhādyai raciteṣu ca  Paus mudriteṣu sahasrārapūrvamudrāgaṇeṣu ca pāṣāṇairvā mahābuddherāsṛṣṭeḥ pūjaneṣu ca  Paus kṛtvā saṃskārarūpaṃ tu nyāsaṃ yatrocitaṃ hi yat kurvanti vidhipūrvaṃ tu nityaṃ traikālyam arcanam  Paus ṛksāmapūrvaiḥ sanmantrairdviṣaṭkārṇasamanvitaiḥ bhagavatpadasidhyarthaṃ śiṣyādīnāṃ śubhāptaye  Paus evaṃ puṣkarasaṃbhūta grāmāśca viṣayākhilāḥ nagarāḥsapurā rājñāṃ prakhyātā ye kṣitau śubhāḥ  Paus ṛṣibhir manujaiḥśuddhaiḥ svayaṃ sarveśvareṇa tu bhaktānāṃ anukampārthaṃ nītāḥ puṇyapadātmatām  Paus vibhavavyūhabhedena sthitā cānugrahecchayā taskarādyupaghāte tu antarbhāvagate dvija  Paus pūrvamantrādayo mantrāḥ tatra ye prāṅnirodhitāḥ bimbam ujjhitya tiṣṭhanti tadbrahmavivarāmbare  Paus saṃskāraṃ na kṛtaṃ yāvat pūrvaṃ tat sthāvaroditam vardhate ca mahādoṣo dinārdhaṃ dinam anyathā  Paus taddeśajānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sādhakānāṃ nṛpasya ca dvijendrādyair atasmād vaṇigbhirvā kuṭugbibhiḥ  Paus deśikair naranāthena kāryaṃ ca bhayanārānam sarveṣāṃ pāpaśamane kṛtamantragaṇaṃ hi yat  Paus prātimaṃ vigrahaṃ śaśvatsarveṣāṃ śreyase tu vai nirjanāyatanānāṃ tu dharmārthaṃ yaḥ samācaret  Paus doṣopaśamanaṃ tasya sarvaduḥkhakṣayo bhavet bhavinām āptapūrṇānāṃ mahāmohakṣaya ca  Paus brahmaṇyadhipatitvena ākāraṃ cācyutaṃ hi yat saviśeṣaiḥ samopetaṃ vibhūtyaṃśaiḥ samanvitam  Paus prajāpatiḥ tam āsādya saṃkrāntaṃ buddhidarpaṇe tena karṇapathaṃ nītaṃ śilpinaḥ svātmajasya ca  Paus saṃpannasya ca homādyair deśikaiḥ saṃskṛtasya ca saṃkrāman hyacirāttatra gauṇam ākāramaiśvaram  Paus saha vinyāsakāle tu vācakena mahātmanā evamevam anāditvaṃ dravyajāsvākṛtīṣu ca  Paus saṃsiddhabhūtidṛṣṭir vai tulyakālaṃ tu bhūtale viśvavadvismṛtiṃ naiti śilpibuddhisamāśritam  Paus sa hi yacchati bhaktānāṃ kṛtvākāraṃ sulakṣaṇam yasya cābhimatastādṛk bhāvabhaktivaśāt tu vai  Paus dṛṣṭā svayaṃvyaktimato bhuvi bimbaṃ tu vai budhaḥ brahmarudraikasūryākhyam ācyutaṃ viddhi tanmahat  Paus yad uktaṃ vyūhabhedasthaṃ mūrtibhedaiḥ samanvitam tathaiva hi samārādhyaṃ budhyā kamalalocana  Paus ārādhane samādhau vā upaviṣṭāstu cotthitāḥ saṃsthitāḥsthānakaiścānye tamopomūrtiṣvanuṣṭhitaiḥ  Paus dhārayatyadbhūtaṃ caiva lācchanadvayam icchayā dvayaṃ karadvayenaiva lambamānacatuṣṭayāt  Paus śaṅkhacakragadāpadmapūrvādyāyudhasaṃgrahāt yathoddiṣṭakrameṇeva lokeśādiṣu vai purā  Paus jyādayaścecchayā vācānye karaistiryak prasāritaiḥ sūcayantyatibhaktānām udbhujatvena saṃpadam  Paus mandabhaktibharāṇāṃ tu tiryak saṃsthānasaṃsthitaiḥ mahadātmapadaṃ divyaṃ yad antasthaṃ hi saṃpadāt  Paus yeṣāmantaritā bhaktirnṝṇāṃ vyābhiśrayājinām prāptistriviṣṭape teṣāṃ bhujavṛndādayo mukhāt  Paus samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu brahman yadyapyahaṃ sadā upadekṣyāmi yuktyā vai madbhaktā yānti saṃpadam  Paus aparair aṣṭabhedasthair varṇair vā brāhmaṇādikaiḥ prasthāpitāśca vidhivat pratimā yā nṛpottamaiḥ  Paus pratibimbamayīṃ vyaktiṃ svayamevācyutena vā jīrṇadoṣaṃ vinā caiva cālanaṃ yad aśāntikam  Paus kṣatam utpātapūrvaistu doṣaistu nṛpanāśakṛt tadastamitamantrāṇāṃ bhūyaḥ saṃsthāpane kṛte  Paus udayaṃ jāyate śaśvacchāntaye kintu pauṣkara deśikendrair yathādhyātāḥ sūryendvanalasaṃnibhāḥ  Paus praviśanti ca mantreśāḥ praṇavadhvanisādhitāḥ karṣayanti vibhūtiṃ svāṃ kiñcitkālāntareṇa tu  Paus kṛtā vai dhvastadoṣāśca nirvidhnaṃ nirmalāḥ punaḥ niveśitāḥ susiddhādyaistīrthaiḥ kṣetravaneṣu ca  Paus nivārayanti ye mohād vibhavavyūhamūrtiṣu saṃsthānamānam ākāraṃ doṣaṃ kālāntare sthitam  Paus te cāntakāle majjanti ghore tamasi duḥsahe svalpavittair ataḥ tasmād alpabodhasamanvitaiḥ  Paus varjanīyaṃ vinānena devaṃ śreyo bhivāñchitaiḥ svayam eva jagannāthastvavatīrya yathāsthitaḥ  Paus gṛhītaḥsusthirastvevam asiddhaiścāpi kalpitaḥ doṣaiḥ sadigvibhaṅgādyair anyathātvaṃ na yāti ca  Paus nityasannidhimāhātmyāt kālaṃ kalpakṣayāvadhi uttarottaratāṃ caiva jagatyasmin hi vartate  Paus bhūtyā kāntyā ca kīrtyā ca kriyayā cāprameyayā duṣṭopaśāntidā śaktyā siddhidā yā ca vai saha  Paus pauruṣāyatanānāṃ ca siddhākhyānāṃ mahāmate svayamevāvatīrṇānāṃ tattveśānām iha kṣitau  Paus evaṃ kṣetreśvarāṇāṃ tu sakṣetrāṇāṃ mayābjaja prakāśitaṃ rahasyaṃ ca muktaye bhavināṃ mayā  Paus phalārthināṃ ca bhavināṃ kṣetre kṣetreśasevinām yathābhimatasaṃprāptim ihaivāyāntyanaśvarīm  Paus atha bhūmitale jātā pralayākhye mahānti te kṣetre kṣetreśvarāṇāṃ tu rahasyam avadhāraya  Paus jñānādyaiḥ sāṇimādyaistu avyaktaiḥ kṣmāvasānikaiḥ tattvabījair upādeyair brahmasattāsamanvitaiḥ  Paus sahāvatīrya vā sṛṣṭeḥ prāgvyaktiṃ yānti vai tataḥ svayamevārthabhāvena sarvānugrahakāmyayā  Paus kṣmāmaṇḍalopasaṃhārakālaṃ kṣetradharaiḥ saha sthitim īśvaratattve tu kurvanti ca tadicchayā  Paus saviśvavyaktisamaye prāgvyaktiṃ pravadanti ca jātijanmatathādeśaduḥkhair dehotthitaiḥ saha  Paus ādhivyādhiprapūrvaistu mānasair duḥsahaistathā ityevamādibhirdeṣair mucyate tvāpṛte katham  Paus samyagjñānaṃ vijānanto ntaṃkṣetrīyānugraheṇa vā āviṣkṛtā bhaved bhaktistīvrabhaktādyanugrahāt  Paus jāyate ca matirnṝṇām ante kṣetre dvijācyute necchanti savikalpāsu abhaktā nāstikottamāḥ  Paus vivekaḥ puruṣādīnām āyātaṃ ca taścaphalādvibhoḥ puruṣārthaparityāgaṃ na kāryaṃ bodhitena vai  Paus jīvanaṃ ca jagatyasmin viprakarmasamanvitam īśvarastannirāse tu śakto bahuvidhair makhaiḥ  Paus tadastitvaṃ gurumukhāt tatsaṃvedanasaṃyutam śraddadhānāśca bhaktāśca labhante ca narottamāḥ  Paus jñātavyam ātmanātmānaṃ tataḥ sarvajñam īśvaram abhimānam anādyaṃ yat prākṛtaṃ satvajaṃ tvatha  Paus asmitālakṣaṇaṃ ghoraṃ sarvadāvāñchitapradam vijñeyam ātmanātmānaṃ tāvad yāvannibodhitam  Paus bījānāṃ hi yathākālaṃ vyāvyuptānāṃ phalam alpadādam evaṃ vyāpānādānācca kṣetreṣvāyataneṣu ca  Paus janmābhyāsavaśāccāpi nūnaṃ karmakṣayo bhavet iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ āyatanavicāro nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo dhyāyaḥ samudita ślokasaṃkhyā atha saptatriṃśo dhyāyaḥpauṣkara uvāca pādamudrāṅkitānāṃ ca upalānāṃ jagatprabho cakrapadmāṅkitānāṃ ca nyāsaṃ saṃskārapūrvakam  Paus ādhārāṇāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ jñātum icchāmi sāṃpratam evaṃ cānādisiddhānāṃ pāṣāṇānāṃ jagatpate  Paus śaṅkhādyair aṅkitānāṃ ca lāñchanaiḥ pārameśvaraiḥ prāptaiḥ saṃpūjanārthaṃ tu gṛhasthairvā vanasthitaiḥ  Paus anyeṣāṃ caivamādīnāṃ yāganiṣpattaye tu vai calānām acalānāṃ ca saṃvidhānaṃ mamādiśa  Paus śrībhagavān uvāca āpāditaṃ purā dravyaṃ śilpinā ca yatātmanā kṛtvā saṃskārasaṃśuddhaṃ dravyaiḥ prāṅ mantraprabhāvitaiḥ  Paus yatra yatrānurūpaṃ ca tatra tannyāsam ācaret tadānugrahaśaktyantam ākṣiteḥ kamalodbhava  Paus mantrāṇāṃ sannidhiḥ kāryaścalapīṭhe tu kevale tātkālikaṃ tu vihitaṃ nirodhaṃ tatra cārcanam  Paus ādhāraśakter ārabhya mantragrāmasya pauṣkara susthire sannirodhaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ vihitaṃ sadā  Paus tatrāvāhya yajen mantram iṣṭvā cotthāpayet punaḥ na hitaṃ pūjyamantrasya pūjākālaṃ vinābjaja  Paus sādhanāt sannimittatvāt jñānenātra nirodhanam puṣpādyāharaṇe kāle pratyahaṃ parameśvaraḥ  Paus anugrahaparastvāste sa tatraiva khaśabdavat calabimbena saha vai ekībhāvagatasya vā vai  Paus pīṭhasya mantravinyāsaṃ vihitaṃ calapīṭhavat susthirasyaikayonervā viyoge susthirasya ca  Paus mantrāṇāṃ vihitaṃ nyāsaṃ sthirapīṭhoditaṃ tu vai āpādād brahmarandhrāntaṃ calabimbasya pauṣkara  Paus prākṛtānāṃ tu tattvānāṃ kuryād vai sanniveśanam kṣityādikānāṃ pādāntam avyaktād vā dharāntimam  Paus sarvatattvamayaṃ mantraṃ tasya vā kevalaṃ hṛdi prādhānikaṃ yojanīyam abhinnaṃ tattvakāraṇam  Paus athejyāvasare prāpte mantratantre niyojayet jaḍatvavinivṛtyartham tattvamantragaṇasya ca  Paus jīvabhūtaṃ tu taṃ vipra nityaṃ śuddhaṃ sadoditam sāṅgam āvāhya mantraṃ ca lāñchanādyaiḥ pariṣkṛtam  Paus upasaṃhṛtya tatrasthaṃ niṣpanne vārcane sati vinyāsam upasaṃhāraṃ māntraṃ yatsamudīritam  Paus tīrthakṣetradharāṇāṃ ca vihitaṃ tatpravāsanam nityapratiṣṭhite bimbe prāsāde svagṛhe pi vā  Paus anyatra vāṅkaṇādau tu tasya kuryāt nirodhanam ādhārapīṭhamantraistu lāñchanīyaiḥ svakaiḥ saha  Paus asthirāṇāṃ pratiṣṭhānāṃ viśeṣam idam ācaret yathodite tu saṃpanne sthāpite parameśvare  Paus kuryāt tato nuvedhaṃ ca ādhārācca śikhā vivadhi sāmarthyaśaktasūtreṇa īśvareṇākṣayena ca  Paus sati yena viluptasya vimbādyair anvitasya ca na jahāti mantraughastasya kālāntareṇa ca  Paus aprabuddhaḥ prabuddho vā tasminnāyatane pumān niveśayati yo bimbam aparaṃ dravyajaṃ tu vā  Paus tadvijñānānuviddhaṃ ca jāyate samanantaram evaṃvidhasya jñānasya trailokye smin hi padmaja  Paus pratītyāyatanatvena bhavatyācandratārakī sanniveśaṃ jagaddhātur yatra yatsiddhasevitam  Paus tad asiddhairna netavyam anyathātvaṃ malīmase ṭa yastajjñastattvavid bhaktaḥ śraddadhānaḥ sadāstikaḥ  Paus budhvāvaniviparyāsamekaṃ kālāntarodbhavam prayatnaiḥ sucikitsyaṃ yat tad aṃtardhānaśaṅkayā  Paus prasannādyaiḥ samādāya tadājñāṃ vratapūrvikām praṇavena mahāyogaṃyāgapūrvaṃ pūrṇāntam arcanam  Paus samāpādya sadānaṃ ca sanniveśyāsane pare parameśvaram anyathā jāyate tasmin sadeha  Paus vyādhitaskaradurbhikṣaṃrāṣṭrabhaṅgapuraḥsaram āgāmi vartamānaṃ ca deśaṅgādyupaplavaiḥ  Paus cālanaṃ vidhipūrvaṃ tu tu kṛtaṃ nāniṣṭadaṃ bhavet punaranyatra vā tasmin sthāne kuryācca yojanam  Paus yathāśāstroktavidhinā samyagutsavapūrvakam kintu prabodhayenmantraṃ tantraṃ yatsakriyāṃ vinā  Paus sthitaṃ śāntasamānau dhautu āśraye cākṣaye sati cālanād vidhinirmuktād doṣaḥ saṃcālakasya yat  Paus taddhomārcanadāne tu sthāpanāt prāk samaṃ nayet susthiraṃ vācalaṃ bimbaṃ tatra kṛtvā niveśya ca  Paus gobhūsuvarṇadānaṃ ca yathāśaktyā samācaret dhātumṛcchailadārūtthaṃ vastrādiṣvatāritam  Paus akasmād bhagavad bimbaṃ dhatte vai mlānatāṃ yadi vyatyayāt tatkriyālopād akālaparipūjanāt  Paus mahadbhayaṃ sarāṣṭrasya pūjakasya janasya ca tasmānmantravaraṃ sāṅgaṃ tantrasaṃśodhitaṃ ca yat  Paus kalaśe maṇḍale gnau tu saptāhaṃ tarpayet kramāt hemantaśaiśire kāle daivīm arcām tu śailajām  Paus snāpayitvārcayitvā ca vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā suvastraveṣṭitāṃ kṛtvā gavyena haviṣā tataḥ  Paus āpīṭhāt piṇḍatāṃ nītvā rañjayeccandanādinā patracchedamayaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sitādyair api picunirmitaiḥ  Paus nānādeśodbhavaiścānyaiḥ sitaiḥ pītādikaiḥ śubhaiḥ chāyāmārutasaṃśuṣkaiḥ haritairbhedasaṃyutaiḥ  Paus pūjāṃ yathoditāṃ kṛtvā bhūṣaṇairvividhaiḥ saha vāsasā sthūlaśuklena kārpāsenāvakuṇṭhya ca  Paus kuṅkumenāmaleṃnaiva kambalenāvikena vā sitena sughanenaiva abhuktenāhatena ca  Paus śītakāle hyatīte tu apanīyājyakambalam pāvanārthaṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām  Paus bhaktānāṃ nāgarādīnāṃ yacchet saṃprārthitaṃ kramāt bhūtaye śubhaśāntyarthaṃ rakṣārthaṃ prārthanaṃ kramāt  Paus vijayenāpamṛtyūnāṃ vyādhīnām upaśāntaye prāpte nidāghakāle tu pratyahaṃ śītavāriṇā  Paus yathoktena vidhānena kuryāt snānam adhikramāt masūramāṣacūrṇena rajanīśālijena ca  Paus samudvartya ca saṃkṣāṣya haviṣābhyañjanādinā vāsasā nirmalaṃ kṛtvāṃ candanena sitena ca  Paus śītakenodakenātha kṣālanīyaṃ tadālayam saṃmārjya gomayenaiva kṛtvā bāhyopalepanam  Paus vikīrya patrapuṣpāṇi kumudotpalapaṅkajān jalārdraistālavṛntaistu vījayet bimbam ācyutam  Paus stutvā ca vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ svareṇoccatareṇa tu tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya dvicatuḥsaṃkhyayābjaja  Paus naikaṃ tripañcasaṃkhyaṃ ca gaṇanāviṣamaṃ ca yat yataḥ samo hi bhagavān devaḥ sarvasya vai hariḥ  Paus saṃnyāsī daṇḍavatkuryāt praṇipātaṃ ca sarvadik pradakṣiṇasamopetaṃ bahudhotthāya cāgrataḥ  Paus vihitaṃ snātakādīnām anyeṣām evam eva hi sahāntaḥkaraṇenaiva bhaktiyuktena cetasā  Paus natapṛṣṭhaśirojānulalāṭataṭahṛtkaraḥ gṛhastha ācarennityaṃ praṇāmaṃ sapradakṣiṇam  Paus smarannaṣṭākṣaraṃ buddhyā asakṛt vitate kṣitau saṅkaṭe sati bhūbhāge bhagavatyagrataḥ sthitaḥ  Paus yathā tu bhaktitaḥ kuryāt baddhvā tu karasaṃpuṭam hṛddeśe mūrdhni kampaistu saha sarveśvaraṃ smaret  Paus kṛtenānena vidhinā svaśaktyā valitena vā yatheṣṭaṃ phalam āpnoti pumān bhaktikriyāparaḥ  Paus niṣkāmaḥ śāśvataṃ sthānaṃ prāpnuyāt surapūjitam bhaktaiḥ saṃpūjitaṃ bhaktyā ye paśyanti jagatprabhum  Paus śraddhayā cānumodante te pi tatphalabhāginaḥ saṃsārakṣayam akṣayyaṃ karmirmaṇāṃ kṣayam eti ca  Paus dvividhena hyupāyena nānyathā tu kathañcana samantrācca kriyākāṇḍāt saṃpūrṇāt pañcalakṣaṇāt  Paus samyagbodhaparijñānāt bhagavad bhaktirañjanāt karmaṇā manasā vācā yo nityaṃ bhagavanmayaḥ  Paus śāsane tvadhikārīṇām avatiṣṭhettu tattvataḥ pāramyaṃ vetti śāstrasya mokṣadasyācyutasya ca  Paus so cirācchuddhim āpnoti duṣkṛtāt pūrvasañcitām iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ āyatanavicāro nāma saptatriṃśo dhyāyaḥ samuditaślokasaṃkhyā atha aṣṭātriṃśo dhyāyaḥpauṣkara uvāca ākārāṇām anantānāṃ kṣitau kṣetreṣu vartinām kālenāntarhitānāṃ ca teṣāṃ bhūyo niveśanam  Paus kurvanti vibudhāḥ siddhāḥ smṛtvā smṛtvā tadākṛtim asatyair martyadharmasthaiḥ kathaṃ kāryaṃ niveśanam  Paus svakuloddharaṇārthaṃ ca kīrtyarthamapi cātmanaḥ śrībhagavānuvāca sāṅgenārādhya mantreṇa jñānadhyānānvitena ca bhavanārcanayuktena sajapena tu pauṣkara  Paus niveśanaṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ dravyajāsvākṛtīṣu yat vihitā sā pratiṣṭhā vai mantriṇām āptalakṣaṇā  Paus mantrasiddhipradaṃ śaśvadante mantraṃ padaṃ dvija mantrajñānām asāmarthyāt mṛtānām atha pauṣkara  Paus anugrahadhiyā cāryapreritaistatsutādibhiḥ yathoditena vidhinā tanmantreṇa mahāmate  Paus saha ṛksāmasaṃjñaistu mantraiḥ svavyāptisaṃyutaiḥ cetasā sāvadhānena vyavahārayutena ca  Paus kriyate madhyamā sā vai pratiṣṭhā svalpabhogadā padamātraṃ ca dehānte saṃyacchatyamalaṃ śubham  Paus kevalaiḥ śrutimantraistu yathāvasaralakṣaṇaiḥ dhāraṇā bhagavaddhyānamantranyāsena vai saha  Paus deśikendreṇa vai kāryā bhaktānāṃ parameśvare sāmānyā tu parijñeyā yajñavat svargabhogadā  Paus aihikāmuṣmikaṃ māntraṃ phalaṃ yatkamalodbhava vijñeyaṃ deśikādhīnaṃ loke smin lokapūjita  Paus tasmād yastattvavijñānī śāstrajñaḥ satkriyāparaḥ ṣaḍadhvavid asaṃkīrṇaḥ sarvabhāvena pauṣkara  Paus tena pratiṣṭhito devaścalo vā susthiro bṛhat tatra saṃrodhito mantraḥ samyag abjadalekṣaṇa  Paus calastharavibhāgena bhavet sannihitaḥ tadā pauṣkara uvāca deva kālāntareṇaiva dravyam eti kṣayātmatām apratyakṣo hi mantrātmā lokānāṃ lokapūjita ḥ  Paus pratīkṣyate kiṃ tattvajñair atra me saṃśayo mahān śrībhagavānuvāca karmabandhāt pṛthakkṛtya devo deśikamūrtikaḥ nānābhaktiprapannānāṃ tathā nānāphalārthinām  Paus karmiṇāṃ kīrtiśaktiryā viśvamandirapūrakī nirastadoṣā mahatī tām ākramya mahāmate  Paus divyamantrasvarūpeṇa vṛttidravyamayeṣu ca upāyeṣvanuviddhā sudhṛtyā śaktimarīcibhiḥ  Paus tiṣṭhatyanugrahārthaṃ ca sā pratiṣṭheti kīrtitā evaṃ dravyamayo yatra sanniveśo bjasaṃbhava  Paus ubhayānugrahaṃ nityaṃ karuṇābhaktilakṣaṇam pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ hi tatkarma śuktimuktiphalapradam  Paus tacca sad brahmaniṣṭhānāṃ dvijānām ātmasiddhaye kartavyatvena vai nityaṃ niṣiddham amalekṣaṇa  Paus tad doṣācca yatasteṣāṃ nistāro hi na vidyate dehāpātād ṛte nānyastatpātastvatidoṣakṛt  Paus ādāveva hi tat tasmānnācartavyaṃ kṛtātmabhiḥ tatkarmapratipannānāṃ caturṇām api taiḥ sadā  Paus kāryaṃ samyak pratiṣṭhānām anugrahadhiyā sadā noparodhasvabhāvena na lobhena na mānataḥ  Paus prāpte tvākasmike doṣe hyaṅgabhaṅgādike bjaja bhaktānām anukampārthaṃ divyairmantrairbalādikaiḥ  Paus dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu mokṣaikaphalalakṣaṇaiḥ saṃpūjitaiḥ hutaiḥ japtaiḥ kurute niṣkṛtiṃ sadā  Paus tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kartavye smin dvijottama traividyaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiḥ śūrdrairvā bhagavanmayaiḥ  Paus sakāmair atha niṣkāmaiḥ mantrārādhanatatparaiḥ snātakaiḥ bhagavadbimbasthāpanārthaṃ sadaiva hi  Paus purā prasādanīyaṃ  yaścaprārthanāpūrvakaṃ tu vai adhikārapadasthaṃ  sthaścadvijendraḥ pāñcarātrikaḥ  Paus vettā yo vyūhapūrvasya vyaktasya paramātmanaḥ so nyeṣāṃ bhagavadbimbasthāpane dhikṛtaḥ sadā  Paus anugrahapratiṣṭhā cāpyadhikāranirūpaṇā ananyair upapannānāṃ bhaktānāṃ kāryamucyate  Paus ananyāḥ pañcakālajñāḥ vyatiriktā na ye purā prāksṛṣṭestanmukhodbhūtā dviṣaṭkādhyātmacintakāḥ  Paus caturvyūhaparatvena yeṣāṃ vai prabhavāpyaye karmaṇām api saṃnyāsaṃ kurvantyadhyakṣataḥ kramāt  Paus ato nyo durlabhataraḥ pāramyaṃ yasya taṃ prati prameyaniṣṭhā śuddhā ca sphuṭā tatkarmaṇi sthitiḥ  Paus paratvam anyamārgasthā necchanti ca parasparam ya icchanti vibhosteṣāṃ sthitirnāsti tadākṛteḥ  Paus muktādhikāriṇaṃ taṃ vai labdhalakṣyam akṛtrimam pañcakālarataṃ śuddhaṃ tantrasiddhāntapāragam  Paus tena vai śrutimantrāṇāṃ trayāṇām api codanā pratikarmaṇi vai kāryā yathāvasaralakṣaṇā  Paus yasmāt abjasamudbhūta maṇḍalādiṣu vṛttiṣu svārthato vā parārthena sadārādhanakarmaṇi  Paus nityasiddhe tadākāre tatparatve pi pauṣkara yasyāsti sattā hṛdaye tasyāsau sannidhiṃ bhajet  Paus mantrarūpī jagannāthaḥ paramātmācyutaḥ prabhuḥ atyautsukyaṃ vinā vipra manasaḥ prītaye tvapi  Paus kāmāptaye tā kīrtyarthaṃ tasya tadvihitaṃ dvija sādhanena pratiṣṭhānāṃ prāsāde svagṛhe tu vā  Paus iti samyak samākhyātaṃ mukhyakalpam ataḥ param anukalpaṃ yadatrānyat tatsamāsānnibodhatu  Paus prākprāptadīkṣaiḥ vidhivat trayīdharmasthitair dvijaiḥ nityārādhanasaktaistu bhaktair bhāgavatair vibhoḥ  Paus dhāraṇādhyānapūrvaistu labdhalakṣyaistu karmaṇām mantramaṇḍalakuṇḍāstramudrādīnāṃ kṛtaśramaiḥ  Paus ṣaḍadhvavyāptiniṣṭhaistu tyāgaśīlair amatsaraiḥ anujjhitakramair dakṣaiḥ svakarmaparipālakaiḥ  Paus satkīrtiprathitaiḥ loke tathākīrtibahiṣkṛtaiḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ labhate kartā taiḥ pratiṣṭhāpane kṛte  Paus niṣidvam aravindākṣa ato nyeṣāṃ hi sarvadā mahāmahaṃ pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ tathānyaṃ miśrayājinām  Paus
