pauṣkara uvāca deva vyāmiśrayājitvaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ punaḥpunaḥ prāguktānāṃ ca yāgānāṃ draṣṭum aṅgīkṛtaṃ ca yat  Paus tanmātrasaṃśayaṃ jātaṃ chettum arhasi sāṃpratam śrībhagavānuvāca satyametanmahābuddhe yathā saṃcoditaṃ tvayā kintu kriyāntare prāpte na doṣastvadhikāriṇām  Paus yasmātsarvaparatvaṃ hi teṣām astyacyutaṃ prati tadāśritatvād devānām anyeṣāṃ pūjanāt tu vai  Paus na doṣo hi yathā loke bhrātṛbhṛtyagaṇasya ca mānanād dharmapatnīnāṃ samakṣādvā parokṣataḥ  Paus ye punarlokadharmasthāḥ samabuddhipadojjhitāḥ bhagavatyaviśeṣajñā nityaṃ kāryavaśena tu  Paus vāṅmātreṇa paratvaṃ vai sarveṣāṃ pravadanti hi adhikāraṃ vinā ye tra preritā devatārcane  Paus evaṃ mārgasthiterlobhāt parijñāya tadāśayam vyāmiśrayājinaste vai pātityapadasaṃsthitāḥ  Paus nayanti narakaṃ nūnam evam eva pravartinaḥ na tu sadbhaktipūtānāṃ vāsudevaratātmanām  Paus kadācit tatkṛtaṃ doṣaṃ vidadhāti ca khaṇḍanām āstāṃ tāvanmahābuddhe kartavyaṃ bhaktipūrvakam  Paus bhaktyā vai mantraniṣṭhānāṃ tanmantro japakarmaṇi varṇavyatyayam āpanno luptastena svareṇa vā  Paus svarādinādhikaṃ caiva mantraikārthapradaḥ sadā acirāt tatprayoktṝṇāṃ tathāpi kamalodbhava  Paus atibhaktiprabhāvācca vāñchitaṃ saṃprayacchati yasmāt sadbhaktipūtānāṃ prapannānāṃ kramaṃ vinā  Paus prasādam eti mantreśastvacirād bhāvitātmanām kiṃ punarvai kriyājñānasaṃpūrṇānāṃ tu pauṣkara  Paus śraddhābhaktiparāṇāṃ ca bodhitānāṃ ca deśikaiḥ tasmāt samyak prasannānāṃ śāsane smin mahāmate  Paus kāryaṃ dīkṣādikaṃ sarvaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhaktavatsalaiḥ mām asaṃpratipanno yo matprāptyarthaṃ karoti ca  Paus mandamadhyamabhaktānāṃ kāmabhogaratātmanām bhavināṃ māmakī dīkṣā mohād vā sthāpanādikam  Paus sa  sā nayatyacirāt tasya bhaktibījena vai saha svakarma karmatantraṃ ca siddhayaśca parāṅmukhāḥ  Paus ihaiva śīghram abjākṣa dehānte gatasadgatiḥ ghoraṃ prayāti narakaṃ bhuktvaivaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ mahat  Paus bhagavanmantramāhātmyāt tadvyāpāravaśāt tu vai saṃsargottham aghaṃ yāti prāksaṃskāravaśāt punaḥ  Paus cīrṇaduścarito bhūyaḥ prāpnuyānmānuṣīṃ tanum prayatnam ācarecchubhraṃ yena śāntim avāpnuyāt  Paus sāhaṅkāraṃ tam ācāryam abhaktaṃ nādhikāriṇam prāpnoti nūnaṃ sa labhet sakāmaṃ nārakīṃ sthitim  Paus sarvagastvapi mantrātmā sarvānugrahakṛ dṭa dvija yadyapyevaṃ hi tatrāpi na bhajet tatra sannidhim  Paus pratimām arcya dehāntaṃ nūnaṃ māṃ na viśatyuta tatkṣaṇād bhūtavetālāḥ kurvantyarthādikakṣayam  Paus anyadarśanasaṃsthā ye nānugrāhyā ato bjaja nāpāsyo hi tathācāryaḥ saṃsārabhayabhīruṇā  Paus samyagbhaktipareṇaiva ḍambharāgojjhitena ca ata eva mahābuddhe pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ makhottamam  Paus nirvartanīyam āmūlāt vaiṣṇavānāṃ hi vaiṣṇavaiḥ pauṣkara uvāca caturṇāṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ bhagavadbhāvināṃ vibho hitārthaṃ jñātum icchāmi bimbāpādanameva ca  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca devārthaṃ vanayātrārthaṃ kuryād rakṣādike śubhe prāpte vanabhuvo deśe kṛte tad devatārcane  Paus śāśvataṃ vanaparyante pāṣāṇaṃ vā hareddrumam cetasā suviśuddhena bhagavadyāgapūrvakam  Paus saha tatpañcarātrajñaistathā ṛksāmapūrvakaiḥ bhaktaiḥ kriyāparaiḥ svacchairvinītaiḥ śilpibhiḥ saha  Paus saṃyatair dīkṣitaiścāpi vṛkṣādyaṃ prāk samāharet pāṣāṇaṃ dhātavo mṛdvā mṛdudgarbhāṃstu secayet  Paus vanabhūmivanotthānāṃ dhātūnāṃ mṛtsvarūpiṇām saṃgrahaṃ vihitaṃ svalpaṃ melanīyaṃ ca tad dvije  Paus pratimāpādanārthaṃ ca mahāmṛtsaṃcaye śubhe dhātudravyamayānāṃ ca mṛdgarbhāṇāṃ hṛdā saha  Paus tārahāṭakatāmrotthareṇūnāṃ kamalodbhava vihitā yojanā nityaṃ mantramṛddāhaśāntaye  Paus aṅgārakāṣṭhaparyantaṃ vanāntād upayujyate tatsarvaṃ vidhipūrvaṃ tu siddhikṛt syāt samāhṛtam  Paus evam ādāya tu purā vṛkṣapūrvaṃ vanāvaneḥ tatra vā svagṛhoddeśe bimbāpādanam ācaret  Paus vidhivat karmaśālāyām ājñaptaṃ guruṇā yajet śilpisvāmisvakaṃ paścāt svotthitena krameṇa tu  Paus buddhimān yajamāno vā ārambhādeva santyajet sarvottame smin vyāpāre bhāvaṃ rājasatāmasam  Paus nūnaṃ kaluṣabuddhīnāṃ na tatsaṃpadyate bjaja yadyeva paripūrṇaṃ vā vighnadoṣaśatākulam  Paus karmaṇā prāktanenaiva sāttvikasyāpi padmaja ghaṭamāne ṅgavaikalyaṃ jāyate daurmanasyakṛt  Paus atha tatra vidhānaṃ yad vihitaṃ tannibodha me varṇakaiścitrabimbasya gālitenāmbhasādinā  Paus vihitāvayavānāṃ ca yojanā gandhabhāvitaiḥ sitaraktādikai rāgaiḥ pāvanair astramantritaiḥ  Paus mṛdā mṛnmayabimbānāṃ madhvājyakṣīramiśrayā kauśayacūrṇayutayā suvarṇodakasiktayā  Paus dārujasya tu saṃjāte bhede bhaṅge tu vābjaja yojanā vastrāśastrabhyāṃ vihitā śāntipūrvikā  Paus sarvadā vihitaṃ tyāgam aśmajānāṃ bṛhatkṣate kṣate hīṣatkṣate jāte sati ratnaśalākayā  Paus sahemayā ca vihitaṃ ghṛṣṭaśāṇasya gharṣaṇam kṣatasāmye kṛte caiva pratimā syād guṇāvahā  Paus sthāpanaṃ sakṣatānāṃ ca karoti maraṇaṃ dhruvam gurośca ssayajamānasya śilpiśreṣṭhasya deśinām  Paus kṣatam indriyacakrasthaṃ karturbhavati doṣadam ākarṇān nābhiparyantam agrasthaṃ putramṛtyakṛt  Paus paścāddvaye tu jāyāyāḥ praṣṭhāṅgaṃ bhrātṛhānidam ākaṭeḥ pāyuparyantaṃ bhaginīnāṃ kṣayo bhavet  Paus ūrumūlācca jānvantaṃ yatra yatra bhavet kṣatam dhanadhānyapaśūnāṃ ca kṣayakṛccācireṇa tu  Paus jānoḥ pādatalāntaṃ ca bhṛtyavargasya doṣadam sarveṣām anukampārtham ātmanaścāpi kīrtayet  Paus kartā kamalasaṃbhūta kṣatam akṣatatāṃ nayet kriyamāṇasya bimbasya madhūcchiṣṭojjhitasya ca  Paus jāte vayavavaikalye hyanukalpam idaṃ śṛṇu vigrahārambhe kṣatadoṣaḥ bhagavatpratipattau tu jātāyāṃ sati tatra ca tattyāgaṃ ca vināśaṃ ca viruddhaṃ hyuttarottaram  Paus bṛhad bimbādyapekṣāyāṃ dravyatyāgaṃ hi nocitam hemādīnāṃ tu dhātūnām utkṛṣṭānāṃ viśeṣataḥ  Paus jāte vayavavaikalye śāntyarthaṃ yāgam ācaret bhūyaḥ saṃpūrya tasyāṅgaṃ viśeṣavidhinābjaja  Paus kevalaṃ hema haimasya yathālābhaṃ kṣate kṣipet sarvaṃ ratnamayaṃ cūrṇaṃ dvādaśākṣaramantritam  Paus etatpūrvaṃ tathā cānyadhātūtthānāṃ mahāmate īṣatsuvarṇamiśreṇa pūrayetsvena dhātunā  Paus yadi vai vidhinānena kriyamāṇena pauṣkara na bhaveccittanairmalyam ācartavyaṃ kriyāntaram  Paus saṃmatena guruṇāṃ ca prāgvad arcanapūrvakam āvīkṣayanti vai sākṣāt nayeccāmūrtatāṃ punaḥ  Paus āpādyam aparaṃ tena bimbadravyeṇa cākṣatam sarvāvayavasaṃpūrṇaṃ manohāri vilakṣaṇam  Paus saṃbhave sati tacchaśvad vinā kālāntareṇa tu yasmāt kamalasaṃbhūta saṃkalpād eva śāśvatam  Paus sthānam āsādayantyāhustasya pūrvapitāmahāḥ prapitāmahapūrvāstu vivadanti parasparam  Paus prāyaśo muktadoṣāstu santānena kṛtā vayam yāsyāmo vāsudevatvaṃ yadi cecchati tatpunaḥ  Paus tataḥ śīghrataraṃ kāryaṃ pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ makhaṃ mahat prītaye cāturātmyānām anūnāṃ mīṣāṃtattvavedinām  Paus ṛṣīṇāṃ vibudhānāṃ ca pitṛṇāṃ padmasaṃbhava mānavānāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ trailokyodaravartinām  Paus bhinnāgamotthitād bhagnabimbād dhātumayād dvija kṛtabimbāntaraṃ kuryād evam āmuṣmikādikam  Paus atastadeva vihitaṃ tad bhedaṃ vā tad anvayāt lokadvayodbhavaṃ yena kartāpnoti śubhaṃ mahat  Paus saṃsthitānāṃ svadeśe ca vihitānāṃ dhanādinā dravyapramāṇaṃ kartavyaṃ pūrvair bhedair vibhājitam  Paus yorthe vai bāndhavādīnāṃ kuryādvai pratimāṃ vibhoḥ sarvadoṣavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati  Paus svayaṃvyaktaṃ tathā saiddhaṃ vibudhaiśca pratiṣṭhitam ṛte viprādikairvipra devabimbaṃ niveśitam  Paus vinyastaṃ tatra yanmantram aṅgamantraiḥ salāñchanaiḥ saha prayāti svaṃ sthānaṃ bimbaṃ tyaktvā kriyāṃ vinā  Paus śaptvācāryaṃ tathā kartrā yadarthaṃ ca pratiṣṭhitam piśācabhūtavetālāḥ sayakṣāścaiva rākṣasāḥ  Paus sthānaṃ ca pīṭhaṃ bimbaṃ ca dhvajāntaṃ saṃśrayanti ca evaṃ jñātvā mahābuddhe tathā kāryaṃ śubhepsunā  Paus pratiṣṭhitasya bimbasya yathā saṃpadyate śubham pūjāhomapradānaiśca vāditraiḥ saha gītakaiḥ  Paus svagṛhe calabimbasya puṣpadhūpādikīṃ sthitim sarvakālaṃ yathāśaktyā bhaktaiḥ kāryā śubhāptaye  Paus yāvajjīvāvadhiḥ kālaṃ tattvamantrair adhiṣṭhite traikālyaṃ calabimbe tu mantraṃ mantrī svakaṃ yajet  Paus dvādaśākṣarapūrvaṃ vā sāmānyaṃ guruṇāṃ purā nyastaṃ saṃpratipannānāṃ bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā  Paus saṃhṛtyaivaṃ yathāśāstraṃ bhaktyā bhogaphalāptaye nivedya mātrāsahitaṃ svagurorbhavaśāntaye  Paus tadaṅghrigau karau kṛtvā vijñāpya natamastakaḥ tvayā dehaparityāgakāle yogyasya vā mama  Paus nyastavyaṃ vaiṣṇavaiḥ pūrṇaṃ madanugrahakāmyayā dehasaṃnyāsakāle tu svaśiṣyasyānukampayā  Paus evaṃ hi guruṇā kāryā yogyasyānyasya codanā tenāpyanyasya dehānte saṃyatasya mahāmate  Paus satkriyasya ca bhaktasya tad abhāvānmahāmate sthitirvāyatane vipra vidheyā gṛhamedhinā  Paus asaṃpattestu bhogānām annādyaṃ saṃparityajet vibhorārādhanārthāya śuciḥ snātaḥ prasannadhīḥ  Paus mūrdhni dattvāmbunārghyaṃ prāk sapuṣpaṃ kevalaṃ tu vā ambupūjeyamādyā vai bhogānāṃ mūlameva hi  Paus yato rasamayāḥ sarve tadrasaḥ parameśvaraḥ nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavāṃstadarghyaṃ cottamaṃ smṛtam  Paus pādayostatpunardadyāt bhogajālaṃ yato khilam svakāraṇapuṭāntastham ānantyam upayāti ca  Paus acirād eva bhaktānāṃ mantriṇāṃ mantrayājinām kṣmānalāmbaravāyavyavibhavenāpi yadyapi  Paus puṣpadhūpādayo bhogā mantrāntāḥ parikīrtitāḥ tatrāpi rasamūlā vai vyaktisteṣāṃ tadātmikā  Paus sthitamānandabhāvena khādīnāṃ caiva tadrasam sarvaḥ sarvatra vai yena rasiko dṛśyate bjaja  Paus ityevaṃ mānavīyānām arcanāṃ kamalodbhava calānām acalānāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ samudāhṛtam  Paus muktvā dvijendrakarmārcām anyāṃ vai vaiṣṇavīṃ calām nārkarudrendrasaṃsthānāṃ saṃsthānaṃ bhagavadgṛhe  Paus vihitaṃ pratimānāṃ ca pramādajanakaṃ ca tat na mūrtyantaradevānāṃ mūrtayo vyūhalakṣaṇāḥ  Paus bhuvanāntargatāḥ kāryā vidhinā susthireṇa tu prādurbhāvāntarāṇāṃ ca prādurbhāvāstathaiva ca  Paus niṣiddhaṃ bhittigeheṣu uccastheṣu niveśanam devānāṃ bhavanādvāme ucchrāyāyāmasamaṃ vinā  Paus yathoktaṃ mukhyakalpād vai hetvapekṣāvaśād bhuvaḥ vyatyayaṃ kartumicchedyaḥ śraddhābhaktipuraḥsaram  Paus pūjāhavanapūrvaṃ ca ājñām ādāya daiśikīm tathaiva ca samūhotthāṃ bhuvanāntaravartinām  Paus surāṇām arcitānāṃ ca kadācinna virodhakṛt anyathā kṣmāmarāṇāṃ ca bhaktibhāgānuvartinām  Paus ādṛṣṭavigrahāṇāṃ ca pīṭhānām aśubhaṃ bhavet evam āyatanasthānāṃ gṛhītāntaravartinām  Paus vibhavavyūhamūrtīnāṃ mantramūrtercane sati vihitaṃ vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca viprādīnām upārjanam  Paus ārādhanārtham ādau tu mantrāntam akhilaṃ tu vai mukhyatvenānukalpe hi yadanyasthaṇḍilādikaiḥ  Paus ūnam aṣṭāṣṭakāccāpi bhogajālād asaṃbhave sarveṣām eva bhogānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kamalo dbhava  Paus ūnādhikaviśālārthā bhagavadyāgalakṣaṇā vidheyā paramā śāntiḥ satataṃ ca śubhārthinā  Paus pauṣkara uvāca sarvadoṣapraśamanī yathā kāryātha deśikaiḥ śāntirmāntrī parā devī tām ādiśa jagatpate  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca sarvadoṣapraśamanaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām hitaṃ pūrvoditaṃ cakraṃ paṅkajaṃ veśmavarjitam  Paus yasmādvā sthāpya pīṭhaṃ ca viṣvaksenāntam arcanam nopuyajyati vai tatra ṛte sarveśvarārcanāt  Paus vyatiriktā nirāśānām ambarasthāmbareṣu ca vidhijñena sthitiḥ kāryā ṛgvidarcāpayet tataḥ  Paus pīṭham aśrānvitaṃ kṛtvā puraṃ tvācaraṇānvitam tatra pūrvoditanyāsaṃ kuryād ādhārapūrvakam  Paus svadehavat tamālakṣya smṛtvādhyakṣaprakāśitam tad vācakena mūrtestu citsāmānyena sāṃpratam  Paus yatheha ca savedyādi smṛtvā yuktasvavigrahe na hi sāṃkaryadoṣo sti adhyakṣādhiṣṭhite sati  Paus tathaivādhāraśaktyādi viṣvaksenāntam arcanam nirdeṣaṃ maṇḍale kintu bhagavacchabdapūrvakam  Paus sarvasya nāma coccārya tadante tvātmane namaḥ evam āsanadevānāṃ dharmādīnāṃ samarcanam  Paus sthānabhedasthitānāṃ ca kṛtvā tadanu pauṣkara maṇḍale mantramūrtīnām āhūtānāṃ samarcanam  Paus saṃpūrṇaṃ śāntaye tatsyād asaṃpūrṇam aśāntaye ataḥ svaśaktyā śāntyarthe sadānaṃ vahnitarpaṇam  Paus bhagavadyāgapūrvaṃ tu sarvatra vihitaṃ sadā tacca jñānānuviddhena karmaṇārghyādikaiḥ saha  Paus samyaktato da rayīṃ jñātvā sadravyaṃ saṃsthitaṃ śubham yathā bījāṅkurābhyāṃ tu ananyatvamanādimat  Paus phalāptaye phalepsūnāṃ jagatyasmiṃstathābjaja anyonyānugatatvaṃ hi saṃsthitaṃ jñānakarmaṇoḥ  Paus jñātavyam avivekācca budhyā tu suviśuddhayā bhagavadvāsudevākhyaparasya paramātmanaḥ  Paus anugrahārtham ullāsaṃ jñānakarmasamanvitam mantramudrāsametaṃ ca karmiṇām anukampayā  Paus tattvaśaktisamopetaṃ jñānādyairanvitaṃ guṇaiḥ aṇimādyaṣṭakenāpi siddhibījena vai saha  Paus śāntaye sarvadoṣāṇāṃ śaśvat parapadāptaye parameśvarollāsaḥ pārameśvaram ullāsam ityabhinnaṃ dvijottama parijñeyaṃ yathā vahnernirdhūmasyārciṣaḥ śubhāḥ  Paus samudrasyormayo yadvad raśmayo bhāskarasya ca saṃkalpād bhaktipūrvāt tu sūryavaddhṛdayāmbuje  Paus karoti nityam udayaṃ bhavyabuddheḥ mahāmahe saṃkalpalakṣaṇair bhogair makhairiṣṭvā tu pūrvavat  Paus bahiḥ śubhataraiḥ paścāt bhogair ājyādikaistataḥ tarpitaścānalādhāre yathoktavidhinābjaja  Paus deśikadvijamūrtiśca sānnapānadhanādinā paritoṣaṃ paraṃ nītaṃ śāntiṃ yacchati vai pararām  Paus pauṣkara uvāca karmaṇāṃ śāntikādīnām ādhāre maṇḍalādike dhyātam asya jagaddhātur jñātum icchāmyahaṃ prabho  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca vyaktiḥ saṃpūjyate yā yā jñānādyaiḥ sā guṇair yutā jñātavyā kamalodbhūta nityā sarvātmanā vibhoḥ  Paus saṃsāraduḥkhaśāntyarthaṃ tajjā vā sā suśāntaye saṃyajed gocarīkṛtya bhaktyā suśraddhayā tu vai  Paus vācakair dvādaśārṇādyaiḥ śaśvaccābhimatāptaye vicitrākṛtir astrāṅgavastrasragbhūṣaṇādikaiḥ  Paus śaktipūtaiḥ susaṃpūrṇā tathānyaiḥ sādhanaiḥ svakaiḥ śuddhasaṃvinmayaṃ tvevaṃ vyaktavigraham ācyutam  Paus pauruṣeṇa tu rūpeṇa smartavyaṃ satpadāptaye vapuṣā sundareṇaiva divyenāvikṛtena ca  Paus muñcantam aniśaṃ dehād ālokaṃ jñānalakṣaṇam prayatnena vinā jñānaṃ nyāsakṛd dhyāyināṃ mahat  Paus sragvastrābharaṇair yuktaṃ svānurūpair anūpamaiḥ cinmayaiḥ svaprakāśaistu anyonyarucirañjitaiḥ  Paus pūrvakarmānalārtānāṃdhyāyināṃ svedaśāntaye svadattenducayotthena hlādeyad gogaṇena tu  Paus vidyākalābhidhe śaktī saṃdhatte śaṅkhacakravat jñānakriyātmake viddhi icchāsaṃvalite bjaja  Paus anantaśaktir bhagavāṃstam anantaguṇaṃ smṛtam dṛśyadṛṣṭāntasūryenduvahnitattvair vilakṣaṇam  Paus svabodhapratyayenaiva iyattāsya vidhīyate sarvam evaiṣa bhagavān kimu sarvam ataḥ param  Paus dhyeyam asya yadā bhāti sā vidyā svātmani sthitā bhaktyā yathocitadhyānād etasmād eva śāntaye  Paus evam asya paraṃ rūpaṃ paramaṃ vinibodhatu dhyāyināṃ bhavyabuddhīnāṃ paramānandadaṃ hi yat  Paus dhanukuñcitanīlāliga dalitāñjanasannibhaiḥ karpūradhūsarairdivyaiḥ puṣpasaṃvalitāntaraiḥ  Paus kirīṭamakuṭākrāntaiḥ śobhitaṃ suśiroruhaiḥ sthalābjakāśasaṃkāśapadmarāgaruciprabhaiḥ  Paus pāṇipādatalai raktairvadanair adharādikaiḥ nāsāśravaṇarandhrāntair muktābhāsādikair dvijaiḥ  Paus īṣadāraktagokṣīraśuddhanīlābjalocanaiḥ evaṃ hṛtpuṇḍarīke prāk puṇḍarīkākṣam acyutam  Paus nānāmantraprabhākāntidhyānam icchāpradaṃ bhavet bahirvai maṇḍale dhyānaṃ bhavaduḥkhaṃ nayet kṣayam  Paus parasmād bhagavattattvād ananyatvena vartate atra sthitaṃ bahirjñeyaṃ mantravyūhaṃ sadoditam  Paus nānāvyaktisvarūpeṇa bhavināṃ mokṣadaṃ hi yat tatra tāvat parijñeyā kramaśo vai puroditāḥ  Paus nirdiṣṭalakṣaṇā brahman varāhādyāstu śaktayaḥ tāsāṃ vyaktaṃ kramād dhyānaṃ yathāvat prāk prakāśitam  Paus parasya brahmaṇastvevaṃ nityā vā vyāpakāmalā mūrtirvai vāsudevākhyā tvabhedena sthitābjaja  Paus jvālā jyotstnā prabhā yadvat vahner indor vivasvataḥ svecchayā yo bhimānākhyarūpaṃ dhatte yathoditam  Paus anugrahārtham evaṃ vai bhagavanmantraśaktayaḥ vyayañjayanti svakaṃ rūpam ābhimānikam uttamam  Paus yamālambyācireṇaiva japād dhyānāt samarcanāt sarvam āpnoti mantrajñaḥ tava bhaktipradaḥ sthitaḥ  Paus sāhajaṃ prākṛtaṃ karmabandhaṃ karmātmajaṃ hi yat saṃsthitaṃ hi yathā tāmraṃ dhātorabjaja kālikam  Paus bhūtvā sarvajñaśaktiḥ sā svayaṃ mantratarātmanā kramāt karmātmatattvānām anuvedhaṃ karoti ca  Paus bhaktiyuktam asaṃbādhaṃ śaśvad ye cāpnuvanti te pibanti paramaṃ brahma īśaṃ mantrātmanāptaye  Paus labdhādhikārāḥ kramaśaḥ saṃprāpya sveśvare pade prayānti mantrasāmarthyād yasmānnāyānti te punaḥ  Paus jñātvaivaṃ kamalodbhūta dhyeyāḥ pūjyāstathaiva hi ye pradhānatarā mantrā mūrtayo pi jagatprabhoḥ  Paus ārādhanājjapād dhyānāt parijñānācca te śubham yacchanti padam ātmīyaṃ tat tad akṣayam ācyutam  Paus dahanti vahnivat karmajālaṃ karmātmanāṃ mahat evaṃ jñātvābjasaṃbhūta suprasiddhaistu vācakaiḥ  Paus dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu ṣaḍaṣṭākṣarapaścimaiḥ svasaṃjñākhyaiḥ svabījairvā saṃprāptair deśikānanāt  Paus smartavyā vāsudevākhyā dvibhedāḥ parameśvarāḥ catvāraścāniruddhāntāścaturvyūhavyavasthayā  Paus evam anye varāhādyāścaturvyūhena vai saha tathaiva keśavādyā ye dvādaśāḥ śasaṃprakīrtitāḥ  Paus anujjhitasvarūpasya nānāmūrtiyutasya ca nānāvyatyayasaṃsthasya yajanaṃ caturātmanaḥ  Paus yat tu nānārthasiddhyarthaṃ tathā ruciguṇāptaye samyag jñātvā tu ṣāḍguṇyaṃ mahimā śāntatā parā  Paus prāptum icchati yacchīghraṃ dhīmatā tena pauṣkara pūjanīyaṃ yathāvastham adhyakṣāntaṃ hi kevalam  Paus prāgvadvibhavamūrtīnāṃ pañca vyūhādyapekṣayā aiśvaryapūrvaṣāḍguṇyaṃ cāturātmyādyam icchati  Paus sapradyumnācyutādhyakṣavāsudevādyam arcayet yaḥ punarmūrtipūrvaṃ tu icched guṇagaṇaṃ mahat  Paus saṃkalpasiddhayaḥ sarvā vividhāścāṇimādayaḥ sarveśvaro nugantavya adhyakṣāntaṃ tu sācyutam  Paus pradyumnāntaṃ tu satataṃ samādhāvarcane hitam mukhyatvena tu vai yasya calādyaṃ guṇasaṃgraham  Paus pratibhāti gurorvaktraṃ dhīraṃ tasyārcane punaḥ vāsudevācyutādhyakṣakramaṃ pradyumnapaścimam  Paus ṣaṭkaṃ tu vīryapūrvaṃ vai icchatyārādhanāttu yaḥ apradyumnaṃ tam adhyakṣamacyutaṃ saṃyajettadā  Paus tejaḥpūrvaṃ tu ṣāḍguṇyaṃ yorcanād abhivāñchati tasyārcane tu vihitaṃ bhūyo dhyakṣādikaṃ trayam  Paus prāgarcanāttu mūrtīnāṃ kevalād arcanāt tu vā kaivalyaṃ bhagavattattvaṃ mantrajñaḥ samavāpnuyāt  Paus mūrtitrayaṃ tadante yat sarvagaṃ yadyapi sthitam tathāpi viśvavibhavaṃ yatsatyaṃ tvātmanā prabhuḥ  Paus jñātvaivam arcanīyaṃ tu tameva samanantaram jāgrad īśvaram adhyakṣaṃ tvayā nāthātmanā saha  Paus trayāṇām acyutādīnāṃ prāthamyena tu pūjanāt tatpadeṣvādidevasya kramād ārādhayet trayam  Paus cāturātmīyayogena guṇānām evam arcanam kuryād vai vidhivanmantrī yathā tadavadhāraya  Paus jñānaṃ balamathaiśvaryaṃ vīryaṃ ca tadanantaram catuṣṭayam idaṃ bhinnaṃ yajanāt siddhikṛt sakṛt  Paus balam aiśvaryavīrye ca tejoniṣṭhaṃ catuṣṭayam yaṃ ya icchatyabhimataṃ parijñānād avāpnuyāt  Paus tejaḥ śaktistathā jñānaṃ balaṃ vīryāntam eva hi iṣṭaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ dadyāt mantriṇām idam abjaja  Paus jñānātmane samuccārya praṇavādyaṃ padaṃ śubham yathā jñānaguṇasyoktaṃ sarveṣām evameva hi  Paus anujjhitakrameṇaiva vyatyayenoditena ca mokṣabhogāptaye tvevam arcanaṃ vividhaṃ smṛtam  Paus bhedabhinnaṃ jagadyoner abhedena yajet punaḥ dvādaśāre mahācakre tathāsaṃkhyacchadodare  Paus guṇātītastu bhagavān pūrvavat kaṇikāntare dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa patragaṃ hi tadakṣaraiḥ  Paus namaḥ praṇavasaṃruddhaiḥ prādakṣiṇyena prāk padāt prāptaye guṇabhūtānāṃ ṣaṭkayuktaṃ hi yacca te  Paus divyānāṃ cāturātmyānāṃ trayaṃ saṃcaritaṃ hi yat trayaṃ guṇamayaṃ cānyat cākārāṇāṃ kramād yajet  Paus upāyaistaiḥ phalaprāptyai tasmād yaṣṭavyam icchayā bhaktiśraddhāsametena jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā  Paus svavarṇāśramadharmeṇa saha samyak samādhinā ā anugrahakālācca yāvajjīvāvadhi dvija  Paus tīvraprabhāvaśāntācca jñānam ārādhanena ca dehenānena tenaiva hyanenānyatareṇa vā  Paus mandamandavaśād bhāvavaśād amarapūjitaḥ evaṃ yad adhikāreṇa kuryād ārādhanaṃ hi yaḥ  Paus bhogairyathoditaiḥ śuddhaiḥ kriyābhirvividhaistataḥ niṣpattau tu kriyāṅgānāṃ hṛdāstrārghyaṃ svamantrarāṭ  Paus nānarcitaṃ vibhorbhogaṃ kalpitaṃ vinivedya ca praṇavādyantakenaiva sanamaskapadena tu  Paus kalpayāmīti nāmnā tad bhogānāṃ vidhyupārjanam dhiyā nivedanaṃ teṣāṃ śirasāvanatena yat  Paus samarpaṇe yad vijñeyaṃ vācakena hṛdeśvarāt pūrakeṇa hṛtānāṃ prāk bahiḥsthānāṃ krameṇa tu  Paus hṛdayaṅgamasaṃjñaṃ yat pañcakaṃ tvarhaṇādikam kṛtam añjalimudrāyāṃ śraddhāpūtena cetasā  Paus nivedanīyaṃ bahudhā yathāsaṃbhavameva vā paramāśritya vai yattu indriyaiḥ saṃyataiḥ saha  Paus vadanaṃ nāsikārandhre sthagayitvāmbareṇa tu svaśvāsopahataṃ caiva na bhavet tad yathābjaja  Paus subharjitānāṃ bījānāṃ prasavaṃ na punaryathā kriyāphalānāṃ ca tathā prathamaṃ cācyutārcanāt  Paus āstāṃ tāvanmahābuddhe karmasaṃjñaṃ hitāccayutam phalahīnaṃ hi cāmūlād bhavakṣayakaraṃ param  Paus aśvamedhādayo yajñā nūnaṃ karmaphalapradāḥ te pi sanmantrabhaktānāṃ na yacchanti phalaṃ svakam  Paus jñasvabhāvāstu vai yajñāḥ samyagbudhvā parāśayam yachanti paramāṃ śāntiṃ bhagavattattvavedinām  Paus svargādyaṃ phalamanyeṣāṃ martyabhogaṃ tu vepsitam phalam āmuṣmikaṃ caiva aihikaṃ vābjasaṃbhava  Paus kṛtvā buddhiniviṣṭaṃ tu japādīn śraddhayā caret bhaktipūtena viprendra tātparyeṇa tu vai saha  Paus sāṅgaṃ saparivāraṃ ca iṣṭvaivam ajam avyayam śaktivyaktivibhedena ādimūrtikramāttu vai  Paus ṛṅmayenātha yajuṣā pūjanīyaṃ tameva hi acirākhye pade mantre tantrair abhimatāptaye  Paus paraṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma pavitraṃ paramaiśvaram sāmarthyād acyutaṃ netrā nāmnā yatsamudāhṛtam  Paus vyaktam asya parabrahma kvacinnayanalakṣaṇam antarnigūḍhamantrāṇāṃ vartate nyatra vai bahiḥ  Paus ata eva ṣaḍaṅgāni pañcāṅgāni mahāmate vācakāni tu vācyāni yuktānyārādhanāttu vai  Paus netrākhyaṃ bhagavattattvaṃ yadaṅgebhyo tiricyate śiro mbare tu mantrāṇāṃ pradhānetaravartinām  Paus svabījaṃ viniyoktavyaṃ sthityarthaṃ prāk prabhātmakam parāvarasvarūpeṇa smaret tatsthaṃ digīśvaram  Paus audayena tu yogena mantrāṇi ca parāt padāt yathākramasthānyāhūya arcanāvasaraṃ prati  Paus niveśya ca yathāśāstram astrāvaraṇapaścimam saṃpanne vidhivad yāge punaḥ sarveśvare harau  Paus kramāt pravilayaṃ kuryāt sādhakaḥ siddhim icchatām evaṃ niyantṛśaktir vai netrākhyā pārameśvarī  Paus prabhā bha vatvena mantrāṇām apyayatvena vartate bahirvā kamale hārde smartavyā sāmalāntare  Paus niṣedhākhyena bījena sānusvāreṇa svenaṃ ca sahasrānalasūryenduvarāhāyutabhāsvarā  Paus vācyavācakayogena mānanīyaṃ sadaiva hi sahasṛṣṭisvareṇaiva sṛṣṭau sarvaṃ yad īpsitam  Paus bhogabījam akhaṇḍaṃ ca pratīpaṃ mantriṇāṃ punaḥ śaśvad ajñānānusiddhaṃ ca saṃprayacchati pūjanāt  Paus nityamantropasaṃhāravelāyām udaye pi ca yathāvad ādau boddhavyaṃ kramān mantraṃ yathāsthitam  Paus bījaṃ piṇḍaṃ padākhyaṃ ca tathā mantraṃ salakṣaṇam bhedam etaddhi mantrāṇāṃ phalaṃ bhedena cānvitam  Paus nānāvācyasvarūpeṇa yataḥ sarveśvaraḥ sthitaḥ catuṣprakārair amalairvācakair upacaryate  Paus vācakānāṃ hi vācyānām evamasti parasparam āpekṣikaṃ vaiśvarūpyaṃ saṃsiddhe niyame sati  Paus vinā piṇḍākṣarairbrahman saṃjñākhyaiḥ padalakṣaṇaiḥ svakairbījākṣaraiḥ kuryād vācyasya parikalpanam  Paus sopāṅgānāṃ tu cāṅgānāṃ dvādaśānāṃ svasaṃjñayā kevalānāṃ tu ṣaṇṇāṃ vai pañcānām api cecchayā  Paus te nusvārayutāḥ sarve kāryāḥ praṇavamadhyagāḥ nyāsātmavān manomūrteḥ sāmānyārādhane param  Paus karmānurūpamante tu namaskārādikaṃ nyaset tathā phalābhisandhāne namaskāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Paus saṃprāptau tvaṇimādīnāṃ svāhākāram udīrayet āpyāyane tu vai vauṣaṭ sarvatra kamalodbhava  Paus vaśyārthe cāpi vidveṣe duṣṭoccāṭanakarmaṇi huṃphaṭkāraṃ ca vihitam anyonyaprītaye vaṣaṭ  Paus tṛptyarthe balidāne ca tejaso hyabhivṛddhaye ṛte sapraṇavād vipra namaskārapadāt tu vai  Paus mantrāṇāṃ karmasaṃnyāsakartṝṇāṃ jātayo parāḥ niṣiddhāstatphalopetāstathā siddhāntināṃ nṛṇām  Paus mantrasiddhāntavetṝṇāṃ mantrajñānāṃ viśeṣataḥ tathā tantrāntarajñānāṃ mantriṇāṃ kamalodbhava  Paus saha jātigaṇenaiva vidhinā mantrasiddhayaḥ phalārthinām anujñātāḥ kāmabhogaratātmanām  Paus prakṛtipratyayādhīnā mālāmantrādikāstu ye śrutimantraiḥ samopetāstutimantrāśca ye smṛtāḥ  Paus āvarjayanti tajjñānāṃ satataṃ cittam abjaja natinaḥ praṇavādyā ye tyāgapiṇḍaṃ tathābjaja  Paus mantrāṇāṃ vividhārthānāṃ teṣāṃ vai pārameśvarī śaktirnityoditā sūkṣmā sattākhyā jñānalakṣaṇā  Paus āviśvasādhanaṃ kāryā teṣām icchā kriyābjaja vikāsayati sad vipra pradāne muktaye pi ca  Paus bhaktikriyāparāṇāṃ ca hitārthaṃ nityasevinām vidvān yathoktanītyā tu oṣadhyo mūlam ūrdhvagāḥ  Paus dagdhāgnināpi kurvanti samyagjñātakriye bhuvi kiṃ punastvāgamajñaistu bhaktyā tu vidhipūrvakam  Paus upadeṣṭā prabuddhānāṃ kurvanti ca manohitam teṣāṃ gantā rahaḥ sarvaṃ baddhādyaṃ śabdaḍambaram  Paus hitaṃ yat padamantrāṇāṃ samāśrityānupūrvakam pauṣkara uvāca jñātum icchāmi bhagavan kālabhedena vai saha svarūpaṃ mantrasiddhānām āgamānāṃ yathāsthitam  Paus kālabhedaḥ śrībhagavānuvāca kālam ekaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha tad vyāpāravaśāt punaḥ bhinnamābhāti kartṝṇāṃ bhagavadbhāvināṃ tu vai  Paus nāḍikākalitaṃ yad vai ahorātraṃ tu ṣaḍṛtu pañcadhā viṣamāṃśaistad āprabhātād vibhajya ca  Paus brāhmaṃ muhūrtam āsādya mantrajñaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ śodhayitvā svakaṃ deham āyāmādyair yathoditaiḥ  Paus mantravinyastadehotthaṃ kuryān mantrārcanaṃ tataḥ japastotrāvasānaṃ ca yāvad ādityadarśanam  Paus kuryād bhogārcanaṃ paścāt puṣpamūlaphalādikam gate dināṣṭame bhāge snānapūrvaṃ samācaret  Paus prāgvadārādhanaṃ mantraṃ tṛtīyapraharāvadhi tataścaturthaprahare śāstrādhyayanam ācaret  Paus cintanaṃ śravaṇopetaṃ vyākhyānaṃ svadhiyecchayā astaṃgate dinakare āsādyārādhanālayam  Paus kuryānmantrārcanaṃ samyagjapadhyānasamanvitam āsādya śayanaṃ paścāt smarenmantreśvaraṃ hṛdi  Paus kṣapayitvā niśāṃśaṃ tu utthāya śayanāt tataḥ yogaṃ yuñjīta vai māntraṃ prāgvaddhṛtkamalodare  Paus talpam āsādya vai bhūyaḥ prabuddhaḥ kamalodbhava utthāya śayanaṃ tyaktvā tataḥ pūrvoktam ācaret  Paus kālabhedam imaṃ viddhi śāstrabhedam athocyate kartavyatvena vai yatra cāturātmyam upāsyate  Paus kramāgataiḥ svasaṃjñābhibrāhmaṇair āgamaṃ tu tat viddhi siddhāntasaṃjñaṃ ca tatpūrvam atha pauṣkara  Paus nānāvyūhasametaṃ ca mūrtidvādaśakaṃ hi yat tathā mūrtyantarayutaṃ prādurbhāvagaṇaṃ tu vai  Paus prādurbhāvāntarayutaṃ dhṛ vṛtaṃ hṛtpadmapūrvakam lakṣmyādiśaṅkhacakrākhyagārutmyasadigīśvaraiḥ  Paus sagaṇair astraniṣṭhaistu taṃ viddhi kamalodbhava mantrasiddhāntasaṃjñaṃ ca śāstraṃ sarvaphalapradam  Paus vinā mūrticatuṣkeṇa yatrānyad upacaryate mantreṇa bhagavad rūpaṃ kevalaṃ yāgasaṃyutam  Paus yuktaṃ śriyādikenaiva kāntāvyūhena pauṣkara bhinnair ābharaṇair astrair āvṛtaṃ ca savigrahaiḥ  Paus tantrasiddhāntasaṃjñaṃ tacchāstraṃ bhogāpavargadam mukhyānuvṛttibhedena yatra siṃhādayastu vai  Paus catustridvayādikenaiva yogenābhyarcite tu vai na tu saṃvṛtāḥ parivāreṇa svena svenānvitāstu vā  Paus yacchaktyārādhitaṃ sarvaṃ viddhi tantrāntaraṃ tu tat evaṃ nānāgamānāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ viddhi sarvadā  Paus nāmadvayaṃ ca siddhāntaṃ pañcarātreti pauṣkara ekaikaṃ bahubhirbhedair āmūlādeva saṃsthitam  Paus nānāśayavaśenaiva siddhādyaiḥ prakaṭīkṛtam saṃkṣiptaṃ saprapañcaṃ ca tṛtīyam ubhayātmakam  Paus setihāsapurāṇaistu vedair vedāntasaṃyutaiḥ ye janmakoṭibhiḥ siddhāsteṣām anto tra vai smṛtaḥ  Paus ya tasmāt samyak paraṃ brahma vāsudevākhyam avyayam etasmāt prāpyate śāstrād jñānapūrveṇa karmaṇā  Paus siddhāntasaṃjñā viprāsya sārthakā ata eva hi purāṇaṃ vedavedāntaṃ tathānyatsāṅkhyayogajam  Paus pañcaprakāraṃ vijñeyaṃ yatra rātryāyate bjaja phalotkarṣavaśenaiva pañcarātramiti smṛtam  Paus sadāgamākhyaṃ mūlaṃ tu parabrahmaprakāśakam divyasiddhipradaṃ caiva śāntikṛd vighnakarmaṇām  Paus iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ adhikāranirūpaṇaṃ nāma aṣṭātriṃśo dhyāyaḥ samuditaślokasaṃkhyā atha ekonacatvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥpauṣkara uvāca pramāṇam āgamānāṃ ca sasaṃjñaṃ parameśvara jñātumicchāmyahaṃ śaśvat saṃbandhaṃ vibudhādikam  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca saṃkṣiptaṃ triprakāraṃ ca kanīyomadhyamottamam anuṣṭup chandobandhena baddhaṃ ślokaśatāt tu yat  Paus pādasaṃjñaṃ hi tacchāstraṃ mūlākhyaṃ dviguṇaṃ ca tat yat sārdhaṃ śatasaṃkhyaṃ tu taduddhāram iti smṛtam  Paus nyūnabhedāstrayastvete ūnādhikyena vai saha bahudhā cāpi sarveṣāṃ na saṃjñā calate punaḥ  Paus sārdhaṃ śatadvayaṃ yad vai parijñeyaṃ taduttaram bṛhaduttarasaṃjñaṃ ca yad etad dviguṇaṃ bhavet  Paus sārdhaṃ sahasrasaṃkhyaṃ tu kalpaṃ tat samudāhṛtam trayasyāsya parijñeyam ūnādhikyaṃ punaḥ śataiḥ  Paus evaṃ saṃjñāntarāstvanye āgamāḥ santyanekaśaḥ kalpaikadeśāste sarve parijñeyāstathābjaja  Paus ā sahasratrayāt sārdhāt ṣaṭsahastraṃ hi sottaram dviṣaṭsahasraparyantaṃ saṃhitākhyaṃ tadāgamam  Paus ye cānye cāntarālaṃ vai śāstrārthenādhikaiḥ śataiḥ sarveṣāṃ saṃhitāsaṃjñā boddhavyā kamalodbhava  Paus sapādalakṣaparyantā ye ca śāstrāṇyatordhvataḥ sahasraśatamānena ādhikyena prakāśitāḥ  Paus kalpaskandhāt tu te sarve parijñeyāḥ krameṇa tu lakṣādhikaistu bahubhiḥ sahasraistu śatānvitaiḥ  Paus sārdhakoṭitrayāntaṃ ca tacca tantrākhyam āgamam navaprakāramityetad bhedamuktaṃ trayasya ca  Paus yatrāntarālasaṃkhyānām asaṃkhyeyaṃ pravartate yugānusārabodhena traiguṇyavalitena ca  Paus divyādyavāntarāntena saṃbandhena ca bhūriṇā aprameyābhidhānaṃ ca ata ūrdhvaṃ samāgamaḥ  Paus kālena saha niryāntam asaṃkhyaṃ parameśvarāt tad vai viditavedyānāṃ siddhānāṃ saṃsthitaṃ hṛdi  Paus yaiḥ svabodhapramāṇena koṭisaṃkhyaṃ prakāśitam pādāntā yasya vai bhedāḥ kramaśaḥ samudāhṛtāḥ  Paus yatra yatrecchayā jātaṃ matabhedena vai saha kriyāntarāśca bahavaḥ śuddhā rājasatāmasāḥ  Paus ādyaṃ sarvāgamānāṃ ca pārameśvaram āgamam pramāṇapariśuddhaṃ ca hitam abjaja sātvatam  Paus siddhānte bhagavat tattvavedinaḥ paramārthataḥ kramāgataśca taiḥ prāptaṃ muktaye bhavināṃ tu vai  Paus pauṣkara uvāca vibhoḥ sarveśvarādyena svīkṛtaṃ pārameśvaram aprameyaṃ mahat śāstram anantaṃ gaganopamam  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca sarveśvarasya ca vibhor avyayasyācyutasya ca vācyasya vāsudevasya aprameyākhyam āgamam  Paus apṛthaglakṣaṇaṃ viddhi svasya śabdaṃ yathā dvija jñānātmasaṃjñam ātmānaṃ nītaṃ vai svecchayā dvija  Paus svabhāvamāptakāmasya tasyaitat svavaśasya ca jñānāṃśenābhimānākhyaṃ guṇaśaktimayaṃ mahat  Paus gṛhītasvayam ātmānam atīndriyam anaśvaram śabdamūrtiḥ sa bhagavān svecchayā svayametya ca  Paus viśrāntaṃ jñānamūrtau tu sa ca saṃkarṣaṇo vibhuḥ svayaṃ vīryam anantaṃ ca mūrchitaṃ jñānamūrtinā  Paus guṇaṃ śaktimayaṃ yasya prakāśākhyaṃ tu vigraham ābhimānikam akṣobhyaṃ pradyumnākhyaṃ tu śāśvatam  Paus mahatā tena bhūtena śāstraṃ vidyutprabhojvalam śvasitaṃ vīryamūrtistu praviṣṭaḥ svayameva hi  Paus atha vīryātmanā vipra prasaraṃ taijasaṃ mahat janitaṃ cāniruddheti dhatte yo naśvaraṃ vapuḥ  Paus guṇaśaktiguṇopetam aparājitam akṣayam tyaktam udgāravat śāstraṃ pradyumnena mahātmanā  Paus ādāya vidhṛtaṃ tad vai aniruddhātmanā hṛdi guṇavyaktimayaṃ devaṃ vāgīśam asṛjat prabhuḥ  Paus aniruddho vyayātmā ca arthayugmaṃ tadāgamam anuddhṛtam asandigdhaṃ gataṃ cāvyayatāṃ tataḥ  Paus yadaṃśād viditaṃ tad vai jñānamūrte svavigrahe avyayīkṛtamādye tu svarūpaṃ jñānamūrtinā  Paus nītaṃ samarasatvaṃ ca pratiśāstre prakāśite vāgīśvarācca siddhānāṃ tairuddhṛtya yathoditam  Paus samyak samuccayīkṛtya navanītaṃ yathothādadheḥ vibhorvidyādhidevasya brahmaṇo sya prakāśitam  Paus rudrādityendrapūrvāṇāṃ devānāṃ coditairdvija svāṃśotthānāṃ ca rudrādyaiḥ svāṃśotthairarthināmapi  Paus brahmaṇā nāradādīnāṃ svasutānāṃ prakāśitam tebhyo lokatrayāntasthaṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām  Paus svābhiprāyavaśenaiva nānākālavaśād api nānādeśavaśāccaiva nānājātivaśād api  Paus ityetat śāstrasaṃbandhaṃ kathitaṃ te yathāsthitam sarahasyaṃ mahābuddhe boddhavyaṃ hi yathārthataḥ  Paus iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ āgamanirṇayo nāma ekonacatvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥ samudita ślokasaṃkhyā atha catvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥpauṣkara uvāca parijñātaṃ mayā deva doṣopaśamanaṃ mahat śāntikaṃ paramaṃ yad vai vyatyayāt saumanasyakṛt  Paus śāstrasaṃbandhaparyantaṃ prasaṅgāt tvadanugrahāt nānādharmapratiṣṭhā ca bhavināṃ svargadā ca yā  Paus idānīṃ jñātum icchāmi tvattaḥ saṃkṣepatastataḥ sarahasyaṃ jagadyoneḥ pratimālakṣaṇādikam  Paus saṃvidhānaṃ pratiṣṭhākhyam aśeṣaṃ pūrvacoditam kṣatadoṣāstu yercānāṃ madhūcchiṣṭoditāḥ kriyāḥ  Paus tāstvayoktāḥ purā deva mānonmānādikairvinā āmūrdhadeśakeśīyaṃ caraṇāntaṃ hi lakṣaṇam  Paus mayā yathāvanna jñātaṃ naipuṇyena jagatpate śrībhagavānuvāca nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ purā kṛtvā tu pauṣkara mokṣārtham ācarecchuddhāṃ pratiṣṭhām ācyutīṃ parām  Paus sulakṣaṇe tu bhūbhāge gavyair bhaktena vai purā prāgdiksiddhisametaṃ tu vasudhālakṣaṇaṃ ca te  Paus sphuṭam uktaṃ pratiṣṭhārthaṃ vijñātavyaṃ tad eva hi jalāśrayādikā yā bhūrvividhaiśca vibhūṣitā  Paus vanaughavanasaṃyuktair grāmaiḥ saha purādikaiḥ pratigrahaṃ pratiṣṭhārthaṃ pūrvavad vidhipūrvakam  Paus saṃpādya kusumārāmaparyantaṃ ca suvistaram uttamaṃ vanayātrāntaṃ tataḥ kuryāt sadeśikaḥ  Paus horādyena ca lagnena muhūrtenārcitena ca śakune gāgane bhaume cittasaukhyaprade śubhe  Paus kiñcid adhvāvaśiṣṭe tu vastavyaṃ ca vanād bahiḥ śubhe grahe nukūle ca nakṣatre vāsare pi ca  Paus kuryād vanapraveśaṃ ca tatreṣṭā vanadevatāḥ ādāya lakṣaṇopetam upalaṃ vai sitādikam  Paus susnigdhaṃ susvanaṃ śuddhaṃ doṣairhīnaṃ sphuṭādikaiḥ vṛkṣaṃ vā lakṣaṇopetam akṣataṃ saralaṃ dṛḍham  Paus phalaṃ la puṣpapradaṃ sthūlaṃ sakṣīraṃ vā tadujjhitam nānājāti ca karmaṇyaṃ yajñāṅgānāṃ guṇāvaham  Paus sattvādyaṃ tad adhiṣṭhātṛbalidānapuraḥsaram kṛtvā visarjanaṃ caiva madhvājyāktena deśikaḥ  Paus śastreṇa praharaṃ dadyācchetavyaṃ śilpinā tataḥ candanaṃ syandanaṃ tatra tathā surabhicandanam  Paus agaru karṇikāraṃ ca kāśmaryaṃ raktacandanam bilvāmalakacūtāśca tālavarṇakasiṃhakāḥ  Paus śrīparṇī nālikeraṃ ca nāgamātṛkapīnakam gavyaṃ kapitthaṃ ca tathā himatālatamālakam  Paus badaraṃ khadiraṃ phalgu madhūkaṃ kiṃśukadrumam phālavetaṃ ca kharjūraṃ nīpanāraṅgaśiśupam  Paus pippalaṃ vṛkṣam aśvatthaṃ pippalīviṭapaṃ mahat suradāru harītakyaṃ bakulaṃ cāpyudumbaram  Paus kālākhyaṃ puṣpakūlaṃ ca vairaṃ cānyat phaladrumam phālāsyaṃ bhūrjavṛkṣaṃ ca palāśaṃ kṛtamardakam  Paus tindukaṃ bījasāraṃ ca mātuluṅgadrumaṃ mahat rājavṛkṣaṃ kohitakaṃ sunābhikuṭakārjunam  Paus saralaṃ kuṭajaḥ śākaḥ śamīśrīveṣṭaketakāḥ asanaspandanākhyaṃ ca stabachastabaketi ca  Paus sāravanto makhīyā ye susiddhā lokapūjitāḥ grāhyāstarūttamāḥ sarve karmaṇi sthāpanādike  Paus ekaikatālavṛddhyā tu dvādaśāntakarāvadhi dviraṣṭakaṃ tu bimbānām evaṃ syād aparaṃ tu vai  Paus prayojanavaśenaiva taravo bimbakarmaṇi vihitāḥ kramaśastvete svalpānām ādināṃ mahat  Paus kecit phalavaśenaiva vihitāśca phalārthinām niṣkāmānāṃ ca vihitāḥ sarve sarvaphalapradāḥ  Paus etaiḥ pūrvoditāḥ kāryāḥ saptāṅgaistoraṇāḥ śubhāḥ agnikāryopayogyāni sruvādīnyuditāni vai  Paus agnāvindhanakāṣṭhāni samitparidhayastathā ārādhanārthaṃ mantrāṇāṃ bhadrapīṭhāni puṣkara  Paus mantrabimbānyaśeṣāṇi tatpīṭhāni tathaiva ca prāsādādīni citrāṇi prākārasahitāni ca  Paus śayanānyāsanādīni devopakaraṇāni ca rathādirathayātrārthaṃ vaiṣṇaveṣūtsaveṣu ca  Paus ketudaṇḍāni dīrghāṇi śikharāṇāṃ śiropari āhareta yathāśāstraṃ chāyāśuṣkakṛtāni ca  Paus bhaṅgabhedakrimicchidrasiṃhaṛkṣanakhakṣataiḥ doṣair aśanipātādyair nāhared dūṣitāni vai  Paus pauṣkara uvāca bhagavan bhadrapīṭhānāṃ pratimānāṃ ca lakṣaṇam devīyapiṇḍikānāṃ ca prāsādānāṃ tathaiva ca  Paus yathāvad jñātum icchāmi rathādīnāṃ ca saṃsthitim pramāṇaṃ dhvajadaṇḍānāṃ maṇḍapān maṇḍayanti ye  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca svānukūladine śuddhe gurūṇāṃ saṃmatena ca mānam ādau tu sarvatra cintayet saha śilpinā  Paus suniveśena saha vai sarvam āpādayet tataḥ yānyuktāni purā brahman vyaktisthānāni vai vibhoḥ  Paus dvayaṃ tebhyaḥ śubhataraṃ bhadrapīṭham akṛtrimam mānonmānapramāṇāḍhyaṃ divyam ākāram abjaja  Paus tatra tāvat suvarṇādyair lohaiḥ śubhataraiḥ smṛtaḥ śubhā bhagavadākārāḥ śailajāḥ samanantaram  Paus kāṣṭhaṃ lepaṃ tathālekhyam iṣṭaṃ bhūtivyapekṣayā tatrāptānāṃ dvijārcāsu sthitirmokṣāptaye smṛtā  Paus sevāparāṇāṃ āptānāṃ bhūtaye marayājinām makhahomaparāṇāṃ tu divi devāsanāptaye  Paus yatīnāṃ muktasaṅgānāṃ hṛdi sarveśvare harau ehi  hīti śreṣṭhataraṃ vipra arcādeśaṃ sulakṣaṇam  Paus cittaprasādam atulaṃ yatrābhyeti samarcanāt yatnena ca samāpādya mantraiḥ saṃskṛtya vaidikaiḥ  Paus mṛdbhūtitīrthatoyādyair mūladravyaiḥ supāvanaiḥ saṃsmarecca maṇisvarṇatāratāmramayairvinā  Paus svadehavad upādeyair nāḍīvyūhaiḥ savāyavaiḥ dhātubhiḥ somasūryāgnisahajñānādikairguṇaiḥ  Paus guṇakāraṇataḥ kṣmāntaṃ yad anyattattvasaṃgraham dravyam āśritya vai baimbaṃ vartate yad idaṃ mahat  Paus tatra hṛtkamalākāśe mantraratnaprabhojjvalam brahmabhāvanayā nyastaṃ yacchati prātimaṃ phalam  Paus śraddhāparāṇāṃ kartṝṇāṃ phalatābhyeti ca sthiram pratipattiṃ parāṃ brāhmīm ākāraṃ prati sarvadā  Paus prāpnoti sadvaśād ante jñānam ātmaprakāśakam pratimānām ato mānaṃ sāṃprataṃ cāvadhāraya  Paus tālapramāṇād ekaikaṃ hrāsayet aṅgulaṃ kramāt caturaṅgulaparyantaṃ yāvanmānaṃ punastataḥ  Paus ekaikaṃ vardhayed vipra śamaparyantam aṅgulam tāladvayonnatiṃ yāvaccalārcānām atordhvataḥ  Paus acalānāṃ dvijārcānāṃ vdyaṅgulaṃ vdyaṅgulaṃ kramāt catuḥśamāvadhiṃ yāvad atordhvaṃ tu samācaret  Paus ekaikaṃ tālavṛddhayā tu dvādaśāntakarāvadhi vardhayed ata ūrdhvaṃ tu sapādaṃ tālameva ca  Paus ādhikyena dvijārcānāṃ jāyate nyaccatuṣṭayam dadyāt tadunnater bhūyo vṛddhyarthaṃ dvādaśāṅgulāt  Paus tṛtīyāṃśaṃ tṛtīyāṃśāt pratimātritayasya ca bhūyastadunnater dadyāt tālārdhaṃ tālam eva vā  Paus dvitīyapratimānāṃ tu ucchrāyeṇa varaṃ bhavet śamam ekaṃ tatordhvaṃ tu unmānārthaṃ tu vardhayet  Paus ekaivārcā bhaved anyā vardhayed ata ūrdhvataḥ kramācchatāvadhiṃ yāvat sāṃśāt tālādvijottama  Paus yathābhimata ucchrāyasiddhaye bhimatāptaye bhūyo bhūyonnatiṃ kuryāt prādurbhāvākṛtervaśāt  Paus prayojanavaśāccāpi mahattvaṃ bimbakarmaṇi vihitaṃ kramaśaścaiva svasvamānādinā saha  Paus tathā phalavaśāccaiva vijñeyaṃ hi phalārthinā niṣkāmānāṃ ca kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sarvaphalāptaye  Paus mānato bahudhā proktam ityevaṃ pratimāgaṇam dhātumṛcchailadārūtthaṃ yathāsaṃpattito dvija  Paus adhirudhya svavṛkṣotthabhinnair avayavasthitiḥ varṇakaiḥ samavetātaiśca baddhaiḥ śastrāmbarādikaiḥ  Paus bhinnaiḥ snāyvasthimāṃsādyairjīvānāṃ vigrahaṃ yathā mantrāṇām evam abjottha vyaktirdhātvādikī smṛtā  Paus aprabuddhaiḥ prabuddhairyā caturvargaphalāptaye pūjyate vividhairbhogair antaḥ saṃpūjanād bahiḥ  Paus citraśailamayīṃ muktvā pratimāṃ mahatīṃ ca yām mṛddhātudārujaṃ vipra ghaṭate katham anyathā  Paus pramāṇapariśuddhaistu bhinnair avayavair vinā etāvat pratimāṃ vipra mānamātram udāhṛtam  Paus bhaktiśraddhāparāṇāṃ ca pūjārthaṃ hi calācalam tatrāyatanatīrthānāṃ yātrāyāṃ gamane calā  Paus pratimāprayatānāṃ ca dadyād doṣadikaṃ vinā pūjitāmuṣmikīṃ siddhim aihikīṃ ca prayacchati  Paus ato bhinnāsanārūḍhā svāśrame svāśramāntare tasmāccalānām arcānāṃ bhinnaṃ pīṭhaṃ śubhapradam  Paus calasthiravibhāgena vihitaṃ sarvam eva hi mṛṇmayā leśataḥ proktāḥ prāntapīṭhāstu kevalāḥ  Paus idānīṃ saviśeṣeṇa vakṣye bhaṅgāsanāttu vai sāṃprataṃ bhadrapīṭhānāṃ dārujānāṃ ca lakṣaṇam  Paus vyāpakaṃ hi yad anyeṣāṃ śailahemādikātmanām dviṣaṭkāṅgulamānācca dvihastāntaṃ mahāmate  Paus kuryād aṅgulavṛddhyā tu bhadrapīṭhagaṇaṃ śubham trividhair aṅgulaiḥ prāgvad yathābhimatalakṣaṇaiḥ  Paus dvidaśāṅgulaparyantāḥ sarve saṃkṣiptalakṣaṇāḥ sarvaikahastaniṣṭhāstu madhyamānāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  Paus ata ūrdhvaṃ dvihastāntā mānato vitatāḥ smṛtāḥ ādyārcā kramaśo viddhi prādhānyaṃ cottarottaram  Paus phalādhikyena saha vai arghyapuṣpādinārcanāt sapraṇālāścatuṣpādāḥ sarve sadracanānvitāḥ  Paus ekapādāmbarasthā ye boddhavyāḥ pārthivairvinā pranālarahitāste vai pādagātravibhūṣitāḥ  Paus darpaṇodaravat kāryāḥ pariśiṣṭā mahāmate muktāmālāsamopetair ardhacandraiḥ sadarpaṇaiḥ  Paus karṇikāvitatopetaiḥ karṇikākamalacchadaiḥ haṃsairvidyādharaiścāpi saṃyuktair antarāntarā  Paus yathā śobhānurūpeṇa evaṃ saṃpādya sāṃpratam bāhulyaṃ bhadrapīṭhīyaṃ praṇālenopaśobhitam  Paus tadārādhyasya vai kuryād uttareṇa tu sarvadā svātmano dakṣiṇe bhāge tallakṣaṇam athocyate  Paus vistṛte bhadrapīṭhasya tṛtīyāṃśena madhyataḥ pūrvoddiṣṭena dairghyeṇa ślakṣṇaṃ vā racanānvitam  Paus prollasantaṃ yathā bhāti snānābhaṃ mbhaḥnikhanet tataḥ samāṃśenāgrato bhāgairvibhajya susamaistribhiḥ  Paus mūlataḥ kaṇṭhadeśād dvau bhāgau bāhyād viśodhya ca tridhāgraṃ mūlataḥ kṛtvā madhyamaṃ vrajanirgatam  Paus jalopabhogakānto pi viddhi bhāgadvayopari racanoparyududdiṣṭā kāryā karmāṇinī  ca sā  Paus makarānanarūpā sā tyājyā kāpilalakṣaṇā tṛtīyāṃśena vistārād bhūgataḥ sāṅghrisantatiḥ  Paus samudgatā na vai kuryād bāhulyaracanānvitā sarvato bhadrabimbaiva madhyato gātrakānvitā  Paus bhūṣayed gātradeśebhyaḥ puṣpaiḥ patraistu sāṅkuraiḥ bhavecchaśikalākāralāñchanaiḥ svadhiyāthavā  Paus kuryāt taduttare padmaṃ sacakraṃ kevalaṃ tu vā ānataṃ taṃ bahiḥ kuryād ābhogaṃ vānanaṃ mahat  Paus tadānanaṃ tatheśānye bhāgāntena susaṃyutam vidheyaṃ ca tathābhogaṃ dakṣiṇāvartalakṣaṇam  Paus saṃniveśama nataḥsvāṅgaṃ gātramadhyāntaṭagaiḥ saha na ca prāsādabhadraṃ ca ekāgram avadhāraya  Paus ardhenārdhyācca pīṭhāt tu vistīrṇaṃ pṛṣṭhadeśataḥ vidheyaṃ caturaśraṃ tu suvṛttaṃ vāmabhāgataḥ  Paus bāhulyavantaṃ bāhulyāt tasmiṃścaiva śiro nyaset stambhaṃ suvṛttaṃ vihitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ vā caturaśrakam  Paus aṣṭāśram athavā ramyaracanāracitaṃ tu vā bāhulyāt triguṇād dīrghaṃ vihitaṃ stambhaveṣṭanam  Paus latāvitānapatrāḍhyair vanair upavanaiḥ saha dhyānāsaktairmunīndraistu vedādhyayanatatparaiḥ  Paus śaṅkhacakragadāpadmamūrtāmūrtairmahāmate sākṣasūtrakarairvāpi siddhestu bhagavanmayaiḥ  Paus ityeṣāṃ racanāṃ kuryād aparāṃ vābjasaṃbhava praphullapadmairāpūrāt karṇikākesarānvitaiḥ  Paus uparyupari saṃmūḍhaiḥ karmabhistvevameva vā sragdaṇḍavad vidheyaṃ vā nālaṃ bhadrāsanīyakam  Paus pṛṣṭhadeśe tu yad bhaktaṃ vṛttādyaṃ parikalpitam cakrādhārasvabhāvena ūrdhvavaktrāmbujātmanā  Paus nītvā tad bāhyataḥ kuryāccakraṃ sarvāṅgacihnitam caturbhiḥ kūrmavat kuryāt staṃmbham ādhāram uttamam  Paus samatvenāsanīyasya vistārasya mahāmate vistāraṃ tasya tenaiva sārdhena vihitastu vai  Paus māhendramaṇḍalākāraṃ vṛttaṃ vā vasudhāvane samaṃ vā mastakoddeśād anupātena saṃkaṭam  Paus tribhāgaṃ samatulyaṃ vā budhnadeśācca vistṛteḥ samāpādyaiva saṃskṛtya prāgvad vai bhavanānvitam  Paus saṃnidhīkṛtya mantreśaṃ mantraṃ mokṣāptaye tu vai yaṣṭavyaṃ parayā bhaktyā svaśaktyā vā phalāptaye  Paus mahatā vibhavenaiva sādhakaiḥ svagṛhasthitaiḥ ete bhedāsya vihitā aṣṭāśrāḥ kamalodbhava  Paus ṣaḍaśrā vartulāścāpi caturasrā athāpi vā svadalena samopetaṃ caturaśrasya kalpayet  Paus tadāsya sattvasiddhyarthaṃ sarvadaivaṃ mahāmate vibhavānuguṇenaiva proktamānāt tu sādhitam  Paus racanāsaṃniveśena samabhyūhya samāpya vai iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ bhadrapīṭhalakṣaṇaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥ samuditaślokasaṃkhyā atha ekacatvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥpauṣkara uvāca uktamārgeṇa coddiṣṭaṃ māntraṃ saṃsthāpanaṃ tu vai yathāvad uktaṃ tad ahaṃ jñātum icchāmi sāṃpratam  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca nṛṇām ārādhakānāṃ tu mantraikaniratātmanām mantrākṛteḥ prabuddhasya guptaṃ kṛtvārcanaṃ hitam  Paus atha dārvādikānāṃ tu dhātūtthānāṃ samāhitaḥ racanāsaṃniveśaṃ ca sastaṃbhānāṃ nibodhatu  Paus tathā staṃbhavimuktānāṃ bhūbhāgāṅghriniveśinām bāhulyaṃ ca svavistārāt tṛtīyāṃśasamaṃ smṛtam  Paus praṇālaṃ tatsamaṃ dairghyād vistṛtervārdhasaṃmitam vibhajya susamair bhāgair adhamaṃ balavatpurā  Paus svalpā dvādaśasaṃkhyaistu madhyamāstu dvisaptakaiḥ dvir aṣṭasaṃkhyair vitatāstatrādyānāṃ tu madhyataḥ  Paus vidheyaṃ ṣaḍbhir aṃśaistu pīṭhaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ samaṃ śubham suvṛttaṃ caturaśraṃ vā svapadmaṃ kevalaṃ tvatha  Paus cakrāmburuhayuktaṃ vā taducchrāyaṃ vidhīyate ardhabhāgena bāhulyāt tatsārdhaṃ sakajasya ca  Paus samaṃ sacakrapadmasya tayoḥ pūrvoktalakṣaṇam vihitaṃ kintu viprendra caturaśrasya kalpayet  Paus koṇeṣu śaṅkhanirmāṇaṃ śaṅkhādyaṃ vā catuṣṭayam vartulasya na te kāryāstathaiva kamalodbhava  Paus cakrapadmaviyuktasya caturāśrāśrayasya ca yaduktaṃ cakrapadmābhyām ardhe tuṅgatvam abjaja  Paus na kevalasya vihitaṃ mantrāspadasya ca tad abjaṃ nikhanenmadhyād dvyaṃśaṃ dvyaṃśaṃ samantataḥ  Paus khātaṃ bhāgaṃ samaṃ caiva sārdhaṃ dairghyād vidhīyate jalāśrayaṃ tu paritaḥ khātād bhaṅgasamaṃ bahiḥ  Paus sopavītaṃ ca vihitam antarekhāśrayasthite dvādaśāṃśakṛtānāṃ ca ityeṣām aṃśakalpanā  Paus vihitā kāṣṭhavargāṇāṃ śailajānām api dvija bhaṅgād vibhaktibhirbhāgairmātraṃ yatkalpitaṃ purā  Paus tanmadhye munibhirbhāgaiḥ sarvaṃ pūrvoktam ācaret bhāgadvayaṃ dvayaṃ caiva parito nikhanet kramāt  Paus janmāśrayaṃ tu bhāgena sārdhena paritaḥ smṛtam tatordhvam uktamānaṃ yat tatra tad vihitaṃ tu vai  Paus vibhajya tat ṣoḍaśadhā madhye bhāgāṣṭakena vai vidheyam akhilaṃ prāgvad bhāgāt pādena vai saha  Paus parito nikhaned droṇīṃ brahman bhāgadvayena tu jalāśrayaṃ tu vihitaṃ pādonena dvayena vā  Paus āpādya cakraṃ prāguktaṃ kamalādyaṃ yathoditam navapadmamayīṃ kuryāt saṃsthitiṃ cārcane vibhoḥ  Paus yathāyathā ca vistāraṃ samabhyūhya tathātathā ādāya khātapūrvebhyo madhyadeśe tu yojayet  Paus vibhaktaṃ bhavate yena kṣetraṃ ced ambujasya ca navānām api padmānām atha mantravarāśritam  Paus padmaṃ sādhāraṇājjālaṃ yujyate bhyarcitaṃ yathā iti vistīrṇabhāgānāṃ vibhāgaṃ hi yathoditam  Paus kṛtvātha racayed yatnād bāhulyaṃ mekhalādikaiḥ jalāśrayasamenādau tad uddeśāt krameṇa tu  Paus śodhayitvānupādena bāhulyaṃ dikcatuṣṭayāt tricatuḥ pañca vā ṣaḍ vā tataḥ pucchāśriter bhajet  Paus tridhā vibhaktaṃ soṣṇīṣaṃ sapadmaṃ mekhalātrayam catur vibhaktenoṣṇīṣaṃ mekhalāṣaṭkamadhyagam  Paus kuryād vai kiṅkiṇījāladvayena nalinīṃ śubhām munibhakte tu bāhulye ṣoḍhā kamalasaṃbhava  Paus bhāgenoṣṇīṣavargaṃ tu ślathagātrāgravad bhavet tadadhaḥ śuktikākāraṃ sūtraṃ chinnaṃ vidhīyate  Paus adhastācchuktibhāgasya vṛttaṃ kuryāt sakarṇikam vṛttāsanaṃ ca vihitaṃ caturaśraṃ samantataḥ  Paus tadadhastritayaṃ kuryānmekhalānāṃ sulakṣaṇam sapādāścoktapādebhyaḥ kiñcitkiñcid yathākramam  Paus sthitirantarasūtrīyā vibhāgajananī hitā santyajyoṣṇīṣapīṭhāṃśaṃ garuḍaṃ ca kṛtāñjalim  Paus svavaktreṇāpareṇaiva yuktaṃ pāṇidvayena tu kuryāt pūrvāparābhyāṃ vā manye bhadrāsanasya ca  Paus gaṃgāyamunayor madhye varuṇaṃ yādasāṃ patim madhyatastad udagbhāge bhadrapīṭhasya kalpayet  Paus pārśvadvaye pramāṇasya samudraṃ ratnapātradhṛt vidheyaṃ saumyamūrtiṃ ca divyair jalacaraiḥ saha  Paus dikcatuṣkam ataḥ śeṣam āpūryaṃ kiṅkiṇīgaṇaiḥ dravyaje calabimbe vā aṅgulaiḥ parinirmite  Paus athordhvaṃ tu nṛpādīnāṃ hitaṃ nānāniveśanam mahādhanānāṃ cānyeṣāṃ śubhepsūnāṃ ca kīrtaye  Paus nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ tatra tāvat samācaret rājā vā sādhakaścānyo lokadaṃ svargadaṃ hi yat  Paus vṛṣotsargaphalenāśu nivṛttiṃ tasya karmaṇaḥ kṛtvā tadanu vai kuryād hareḥ saṃsthāpanaṃ punaḥ  Paus viśeṣakarmanicayaṃ pratyastama  meti yatra vai saṃkalpād eva nādharmamājīvam abhivindati  Paus samyak samāpto yenaiva tenānyasmin hi janmani vivekajaṃ paraṃ jñānam āpnuyānmokṣasiddhidam  Paus nānyena karmaṇā yasmād viṣakīrṇena karmaṇā jāyate parayā śāntirdharmavaśyo kṣayapradaḥ  Paus pauṣkara uvāca nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā jñātum icchāmi bhagavan tvattaḥ saṃdehaśāntaye  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca pañcāyatanūparvaṃ prāk kṛtvā devālayaṃ śubham kāmanārahitenaiva cetasā vimalena tu  Paus dharmārtham āśritaṃ tasmin puraṃ kuryād dvijāspadam sarvalokeṣu sāmānyaṃ sarvadoṣakṣayaṅkaram  Paus sarvadharmottamaṃ caiva sarvadā sarvakāmadam pravaraṃ pañcakālajñasamūhaṃ bhagavanmayam  Paus ṣaṭkarmanirataṃ cāpi trayīdharmaparāyaṇam jñātiśuddhaṃ parijñāya nirdvandvaṃ ca parasparam  Paus dāśāgnihotrasaṃyuktaṃ vedādhyayanatatparam nadīśailavanopete duṣṭaprāṇivivarjite  Paus sasyaśāliphalāḍhye tu snigdhaśaṣpasamākule svādutoyaprade deśe suprākāravibhūṣite  Paus tam āsādya śubhaṃ tatra pūjayitvā jagatprabhum tataḥ snātvānuliptaṃ ca vastrālaṃkārabhūṣitam  Paus tāmraśāsanapūrvaṃ tu brāhmaṇaṃ viniveśya ca āsaneṣu samūhantaṃ pādyārdhyakusumair yajet  Paus taṃ ca dhūpaiḥ sugandhaiśca tāmbūlena mahāmate yathākramopadiṣṭeṣu dadyāt pāṇau kuśodakam  Paus dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa pramādyam iti pāṭhayet pratiṣṭhāsīti vai sāma kuryād vai prārthanāṃ tataḥ  Paus yathāvad arcanīyaśca madanugrahakāmyayā svagṛhe puṇḍarīkākṣa svakulotthena karmaṇā  Paus sahasaddharmacāriṇyā vyaktavedyāṃ yathāgamam samidādīni cāgnīnām agnervā śaktyapekṣayā  Paus traikālyamā ca kartavyaṃ svadharmaḥ paripālyatām praveśaṃ na samāpannā dā  d dātavyaṃ pāpakarmaṇām  Paus saṃskāryā svasutāḥ kanyā bhṛtyāmātyāḥ svavaṃśajāḥ vaiṣṇavena vidhānena kāryāste bhagavanmayāḥ  Paus ā muhūrtāt tu vai brāhmād yāvadādityadarśanam snānapūjājapastotrapāṭhaiḥ saṃdhyāṃ samācaret  Paus yāgasādhanabhogānām upārjanam anantaram tataḥ snānaṃ tu vidhivad yathoktaṃ vidhinā hitam  Paus sāyam ābhūtaśuddhiṃ ca antaryāgam anantaram yathoktavidhinā cātha kuryād ārādhanaṃ bahiḥ  Paus tato gnihavanaṃ caiva kriyāṃ paitrīm anantaram balidānaṃ ca bhūtānām atithīnām athārcanam  Paus bandhubhṛtyasamopetam ātmayāgam anantaram ṛksāmapūrvaṃ svādhyāyam itihāsādicintanam  Paus ācartavyaṃ samādhānaṃ svahṛtpadmāntare tataḥ trayodaśāṅgam ityuktam āhnikaṃ bhagavanmayam  Paus kāryaṃ vai pratyahaṃ bhaktyā kṣīyamāṇe kṣapāgame saṃnyāsam ācared bhūyaḥ kuryādgrahaṇam asya vai  Paus deśikendramukhenaivam ājñātuṃ gṛhamedhinām dattvā nirgatya vai tatra kartā kuryāt pradakṣiṇam  Paus iti brahmapratiṣṭhānaṃ vidhānaṃ kathitaṃ ca te vaiṣṇavīyaiḥ pālanīyaṃ nṛpendraiśca svasiddhaye  Paus svasiddhāntapratiṣṭhānam athedānīṃ nibodhatu maṭham āyatane kṛtvā vṛttipūrvam akṛtrimam  Paus vaṇikkuṭumbabhṛtakairyuktaṃ dāsagaṇena tu vāpyo gharaṭṭajāliṭanyaḥ saha vātāyanaiḥ sthitāḥ  Paus tatrānnaṃ vyañjanopetaṃ bhakṣyakānnādikaṃ bahu vividhaṃ sādhayitvāṃ prāk snātvā tu guruṇā saha  Paus dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu mantrair nyastatanuḥ sudhīḥ arcayitvā jagannāthaṃ parameśvaram acyutam  Paus abhyāgatān samāhūya brāhyaṇān vedapāragān idaṃ tad amṛtaṃ cānnam idamāyuḥ prajāpatiḥ  Paus idaṃ viṣṇuridaṃ prāṇam idaṃ jīvam idaṃ param sarvasattvahitārthaṃ ca anuyāgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  Paus pañcabhūtajagadyoner annamūrte janārdana ā bhūtasaṃplavaṃ kālaṃ bhava sannihitastviha  Paus codayed ṛṅmayān prāgvat sāmajñād dve pare śrutī gurur abhyarthanīyaśca sakuṭumbena vai purā  Paus abhyāgatagaṇenāpi saha cānyaiḥ pareṇa tu yoktavyaṃ pālanīyaṃ ca madanugrāhyayā dhiyā  Paus tarpayeta tato nnena annād arcārcitena tu samūham upaviṣṭaṃ tu ucchiṣṭaṃ śodhayet tataḥ  Paus yāyāt pradakṣiṇīkṛtya abhyāgatagaṇaṃ tatam idam annapratiṣṭhānam uktam acyutabhāvinām  Paus jñānapratiṣṭhānam param uddharaṇopāyaṃ tathākhilasukhapradam atha jñānapratiṣṭhānam idānīm avadhāraya yatkṛtvā jāyate jñānaṃ vivekasahitaṃ hi yat  Paus pariśuddhān samuccitya pañcarātrīyasañcayān sadāgamādikān kṛtsnān vedevadāṅgasaṃyutān  Paus smṛtismṛtyantaropetān itihāsasamanvitān ānvīkṣakībhir vidyābhiḥ saśabdākhyābhisaṃvṛtān  Paus nadī  ndi nāgarakairvarṇaivividhān varṇasaṃcayān pūrayitvā vinikṣipya saṃpuṭeṣvakṣayeṣu ca  Paus grathayitvāsitādyena sūtreṇa sudṛḍhena tu susthire suprasiddhe ca nṛpanāgarasevite  Paus dvijoṣitebhyaḥ saṃkīrṇe satsamūhena pālite samīpe śmamayaṃ veśma lohayantrasamanvitam  Paus sakavāṭārgalopetaṃ sudhādhavalitaṃ śubham kañjasthayā vāgīśvaryā bhūṣitaṃ citrabhūṣayā  Paus śaṅkhacakragadāpadmakaraprodyatayā tayā prodvahantyākṣamālāṃ tu śāstrasañcayahastayā  Paus varadābhayadāyinyā siddhādyairvāntayā paraiḥ tataḥ prāgvat kṛtanyāsaḥ śuklāmbaradharaḥ śuciḥ  Paus lohayantrāyane tasmin praṇavādhiṣṭhite rcite yathākramaṃ samāropya śāstrasaṃgrahapustakān  Paus pūjitāṃstu samālabdhānnetravastraistu veṣṭitān dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa pūjayitvā paṭhed idam  Paus viśuddhajñānadehāya viṣṇave paramātmane supratiṣṭhitam akṣayyaṃ tiṣṭha śāstrātmaneha vai  Paus ajñānām upakārārthaṃ prabodhajananāya ca muktvā tvāmevam akṣayyaṃ kṣayavanto marādayaḥ  Paus uktvaivam arcayed bhūyo vedavedāntavigraham sadāgamādyairbhagavatpurāṇādyair alaṃkṛtam  Paus pratyahaṃ parayā bhaktyā vidyāpīṭhasya cāgrataḥ śabdabrahmamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ bhadrapīṭhe purodite  Paus niyuktaṃ cārcane kuryād apramattaṃ dvijottama tataḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya dhūpaṃ dattvā kṣamāpeyat  Paus sañcāradāne rthināṃ ca saṃcayaṃ tatra saṃcayet śāsanāvanibandhāṃ ca tasya vṛttiṃ supuṣkalām  Paus kṛtvā tacchāsanaṃ dadyād jñānakośānupālane tasmin devagṛhe paścād brahmacārīṃstu pāṭhayet  Paus mantradvayaṃ puroddiṣṭaṃ svayaṃ baddhāñjaliḥ paṭhet ajñānatimirāndhānāṃ janānām avivekinām  Paus śāstrapīṭhapratiṣṭhānāt jñānam eti ca nirmalam etasmād utthitenaiva phalena mahatā hariḥ  Paus prītim āyātu paramāṃ phalaṃ me nopayujyate vidyāpīṭhapratiṣṭhānam idaṃ samyak prakāśitam  Paus phalārthināṃ jñānaniṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ yacchati cepsitam vāpīkūpataṭākānām ārāmāṇāṃ ca mokṣaṇam  Paus pratiṣṭhāpanapūrvaṃ ca svargadaṃ hi phalārthinām karmasanyāsināṃ viṣṇostatpunastatpadapradam  Paus kāraṇaṃ jagatām īśo bhūtaḥ sarveśvaro cyutaḥ śabdātmikām amūrtāṃ ca jñānakarmātmalakṣaṇām  Paus samāsādya svarūpeṇa jagatyām avatiṣṭhate tanmayaṃ deham āśritya yatsatyāhlādam uttamam  Paus sāmarāṇām ṛṣīṇāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ mahāmate evaṃ nānārasamayīṃ śaktiṃ viṭapavigrahām  Paus dāvānalasthasa prakarīṃ nānāvyaktamayaiḥ svaraiḥ pravālapatrakusumamārutāmbuvimiśritaiḥ  Paus ajaṅgamāṃ pādapākhyāṃ patrapuṣphalapradām mūrtiṃ devopavaraṇīṃ bhūmiṃ vai prathamāṃśakām  Paus aparāṃ jaṅgamāṃ mūrtiṃ saurabhaṃ saṃśritāspadām tatastad utthitaistāvat pañcaupaniṣadātmakaiḥ  Paus mantritaiḥ pañcabhirmantrairgomayādyair yathākramam saha ṛksāmapūrvaistu kuśodakasamanvitaiḥ  Paus śuddhaye pi ca tatkhātaṃ paryukṣya paritaḥ purā nayet pāvanatāṃ paścād ambunā paripūritām  Paus kṣmāgatenāthavādyepyena ko  kaupenālpena vā dvija akṣāreṇa sutoyena sāṃprataṃ śītalena ca  Paus saṃbhave sati hehaimena deśakālavaśād api krītena tāṭakīyena pallaveṣvanenoddhṛtena vā  Paus gobrāhmaṇānāṃ sāṃmūlyaṃ  mukhyaṃgatvā śatapadādikam khātamadhye vinikṣipya sa khāto vitato mahān  Paus bahukāle jalasthāyī yathābhimatavistṛtaḥ kāryo vai sarvadiksevyo navasthā jāyate yathā  Paus kulastrījanavṛddhānāṃ sneham āharatāṃ bhṛśam dhanurdvayasamaṃ kuryānnimnatvena tu sarvadā  Paus sārdhakārmukatulyaṃ vā ekajyāniṣṭhameva vā dhanurdvayāt samārabhya yāvad dhanuḥśataṃ tu vai  Paus vihite khātavistāre hyata ūrdhvaṃ yathā ca te tatpārthivaṃ ca vāyavyaṃ saumyam āgneyameva ca  Paus caturaśrāyataṃ caiva āpādya śubhalakṣaṇam samūbhāgavaśāccaiva padavīgaṇabhūṣitam  Paus vṛkṣavallīgaṇopetaṃ śāḍvalasthalabhūṣitam pāthikāvāsakairyuktaṃ tathā viśrāmatoraṇaiḥ  Paus evaṃ kṛtvā yathoddiṣṭaṃ yatra govigrahakṣitau avadhārya ca sandhārya khātahrāsaṃ ca kurvatī  Paus kālaṃ pravṛttiparyantaṃ tarpayantī ca tajjalam evaṃ saṃskṛtya ca tataḥ prāgbhāgam api vīkṣayan  Paus pratyagbhāgasthitaḥ kartā guruṇā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha taduddhṛtenāmbhasātha athavānyena sāṃpratam  Paus mṛdā gomayayutayā tatkālaṃ lepayet sthalam dvādaśārṇena gāyatryā sāmnā vai vāsudhena tu  Paus pūrvadakṣiṇasaumyānāṃ digbhāgānāṃ yathākramam homārtham ṛgyajuḥsāmapāṭhakān viniveśya ca  Paus sthaleṣu vālakīyeṣu kuṇḍeṣu suśubheṣu vā dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa kṛtanyāsasvakena vā  Paus mṛtpiṇḍam ekam ādāya svātamadhyāt tu pātrakam kauśeyakusumopete āsane viniveśya ca  Paus toyapūrṇaṃ tadūrdhve tu kalaśaṃ kāñcanodaram vastreṇa veṣṭitaṃ samyak kuṅkumādyair vilepitam  Paus puṣpasraṅmañjarīdūrvādarbhabījaphalodakam sitopavītam āśubhraṃ netram uṣṇīṣabhṛnnyaset  Paus pārthivena ca śūnyena jīvayuktena bhāvayet sabindunāmayelenātha sāmṛtenācyutaṃ vibhum  Paus nārāyaṇaṃ parāṃ mūrtim utthitāṃ madhuradhvaneḥ padmamante niyoktavyam asya bījatrayasya ca  Paus nārāyaṇāya bhagavaṃstato bhūtātmane namaḥ snānapūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhānam ācartavyaṃ yathāvidhi  Paus dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa athavāṣṭākṣareṇa tu ṣaḍakṣareṇa saṃpādya pūrṇāntā havanakriyā  Paus arcayitvā yathāśakti gurupūrvān dvijottamān samādāyātha kalaśaṃ pūrṇaṃ palvalajaṃ hi yat  Paus kartā vinikṣipet pūrvaṃ mṛtpiṇḍaṃ puṣkarodare kalaśodakam utkīrya imaṃ mantram udīrayet  Paus āmūrte bhagavan nātha vāsudevāmṛtātmane ācandratārakaṃ kālaṃ tiṣṭha tvaṃ supratiṣṭhitam  Paus māmakasyāñjasā trāṇaṃ nātha sānugasaṃyutān devān pitṝn sasādhyāṃśca bhūtānyāpyāyitā sadā  Paus phalena tu ihotthena yātu prītiṃ parāṃ bhavān tṛptirbhavatu bhūtānāṃ trailokyodaravartinām  Paus ityuktvā pāṭhayet sāma dhruvādyau ṛṅmayāṃstataḥ pratiṣṭhāsīti vai sāma sāmajñān brāhmaṇottamān  Paus pūjanair vividhaiḥ paścāt tadutthena tu sāmbhasam tarpayed brāhmaṇān sarvān khātakartṝna tathākhilān  Paus prasādya dānapūrveṇa deśikān vibhave sati dīnānāthāṃstathā bhṛtyānanantaphalasiddhaye  Paus suvarṇavasudhādānaṃ yathāśaktyā samācaret kanyādānaṃ vṛṣotsargaṃ pitṛśrāddhapuraḥsaram  Paus vadhabandhotthitaṃ doṣaṃ dhanadaṇḍotthitaṃ ca yat vicāraṇīyaṃ lokānām arthayitvā nareśvaram  Paus kintu vī vi dhyantaram idaṃ vihitaṃ sati saṃbhave pradhānaphalavṛkṣaṃ tu aśvatthaviṭapaṃ tu vā  Paus ārāmasaṃpratiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃskṛtya snānakarmaṇām samālabhya svalaṃkṛtya upavetya yathāvidhi  Paus vāsasā veṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā puṣpasrakparibhūṣitam homāntam akhilaṃ prāgvat samantraṃ tatsamācaret  Paus tena yāti paraṃ kartā pāraṃ saṃsāravāridheḥ phalamūlānnādipratiṣṭhā phalamūlānnapratiṣṭhāṃ śṛṇu vakṣye phalārthinām nānnadānāt paraṃ dānaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vidyate  Paus sadyaḥprītikaraṃ hṛdyaṃ prāṇadaṃ prāṇināmapi utpattāvapi saṃskāre rasam annasya kīrtitam  Paus annād bhavanti bhūtāni tasmāt sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam tacca pratiṣṭhitaṃ yena tena sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam  Paus ātmanā saha loke smin svarloke brahmasaṃjñite yāvajjīvaṃ ca nīrogo vased duḥkhavivarjitaḥ  Paus putradāradhanair annair vṛddhiṃ yāti kṣaṇāt kṣaṇam prāpnoti paramāṃ pūjām utkṛṣṭebhyo mahattarām  Paus devatā ṛṣayaḥ siddhāstasya saṃcintayanti ca nityam eva parāṃ vṛddhimāyuṣaḥ saha connatām  Paus hṛṣṭaḥ puṣṭastato bhūtvā tṛpto bhavati sarvadā bhuktvā bhogān suvipulānante nārāyaṇālayam  Paus yāti candrapratīkāśairvimānairdevanirmitaiḥ svargādau sarvaloke tu sthitvā kalpaśatān bahūn  Paus kālāt punar ihāyāti deśe sarvottame śubhe satāṃ kule samāsādya janma jātyuttamaṃ mahat  Paus jāyate rūpavān vāgmī vidyājñānaparāyaṇaḥ dviṣatām api sarveṣāṃ pūjyaḥ priyataraḥ sadā  Paus śīlavāñ śauryasaṃpanno dhṛtyutsāhasamanvitaḥ dvijadevaparo nityaṃ dātā bhūtahite rataḥ  Paus ekāntī dharmavettā vai nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ trivargam akhilaṃ bhuktvā yathābhimatalakṣaṇaḥ  Paus janmābhyastaṃ śubhaṃ karma kṛtvānantaguṇaṃ punaḥ jñānam āsādyate yena prayāti paramaṃ padam  Paus na hi vai kūpavāpīnāṃ surabhīṇāṃ ca pūjanam dadyācchuddhaṃ hi tādātmyaṃ vidhānaṃ sarvam ācaret  Paus nītvāṅgabhāvam asmiṃśca gogaṇaṃ bhagavadgṛhe snānopabhogapūrvāṇāṃ vibhor analatarpaṇāt  Paus prītyarthaṃ surabhīṇāṃ tu pratipādyaṃ tu śāsanam tam agniṃ govrajopetaṃ dhṛtadīpasamanvitam  Paus devavat pālanīyaṃ ca yāvad ācandratārakam aniśaṃ jvalamānaṃ ca vaset karmakaraiḥ saha  Paus ṣaḍaśītimukhādyaṃ vai kālam āsādya puṇyadam kuṇḍaṃ sulakṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā divyādyairveṣṇavairgṛhe  Paus svayaṃ pratiṣṭhite vāpi dharmaskandheṣu vai purā dvādaśākṣaramantrādyaiḥ śubhaiḥ sūktaistu vaiṣṇavaiḥ  Paus ṛgyajuḥsahasāmaistu devadevapraśaṃsakaiḥ evaṃ hotā śanaiścāpi saṃpaṭhecchāntike kṛte  Paus ghṛtādyair akṣataiḥ pītaiḥ sitakṛṣṇānvitaistilaiḥ saṃskṛtya cānalaṃ kuṇḍaṃ prājāpatyena karmaṇā  Paus āhutīnāṃ tu juhuyāt sahasrād ayutāvadhi śatādyaṃ ca sahasrāntaṃ tāmrajena sruveṇa tu  Paus pālīyenāṣṭamāṃśena dhṛtaṃ tu juhuyāt tataḥ akāmo vā sakāmo vā dadyāt pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ  Paus nārāyaṇastu vedātmā sahavedamukhena tu dadātyabhimatān kāmān upāyaṃ naiṣṭhikaṃ tu vai  Paus evaṃ kṛte tu saṃpādyād badhnīyād dhiṣaṇopari saptāhaṃ vasudhārāṃ ca trirātram athavā śubham  Paus ekāhaṃ vā svaśaktyā tu tad vidhānam athocyate nirdhūme vitate kuṇḍe dṛḍhaiḥ kāṣṭhaistu yājñikaiḥ  Paus kṛtvāgniṃ mekhalābhūmer adhikaṃ śibikopamam dhanurdvayocchrite vātha tadūrdhve tāmrajaṃ tatam  Paus kaṭāhakaṃ yojanīyaṃ kāṣṭhaje valaye dṛḍhe sthiravaṃśacatuṣpāde padavīsahanakṣame  Paus aṅgulair atha mānīyaiścatuḥsaṃkhyaistu connatam haimīṃ suvarṇamānotthāṃ śalākāṃ sarvataḥ samām  Paus tatpramāṇasamopetaṃ madhyame tu kaṭāhake vedhaṃ kuryācca lohena vastrāpūtam athāharet  Paus vyājahīnaṃ ghṛtaṃ havyaṃ sugandhi śubhalakṣaṇam kaṭāhake samutkīrya yatna pūrvaparikṣayaṣkṛtam  Paus pravahaṃ dinarātrīyaṃ kālaṃ yat trividhaṃ smṛtam  etāvad uktam ārabhya devam ātmānaṃ akṣamam  Paus āprabhātāntamathavādyaṃ vāharayet praharaṃ ghṛtam praharadvitayaṃ vātha praharatrayam eva vā  Paus praharāṇāṃ catuṣkaṃ vā svasāmarthyādyapekṣayā ādau ṣaṭprasthamānāt tu catuḥprasthāntameva hi  Paus pravāham āharecchaktyā pālikaṃ tu ghṛtasya vā adhibhūtādhidevāḍhyaṃ stṛtvādhyātmatayā ghṛtam  Paus pavitram amṛtaṃ brahma ājyam adhyātmameva hi adhidevaṃ paraṃ vahnir adhibhūtaṃ ca gogaṇam  Paus smṛtam uktaṃ mamaivaṃ hi vasu matvā svarūpadhṛk tadvāraparimāṇena vidhitvena ca vartate  Paus svadaridram imaṃ lokaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vai yatprabhāvataḥ vitatena tu pātreṇa sthagayitvā kaṭāhakam  Paus daivatvenārcanīyaṃ ca bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ sāṃprataṃ cārghyapuṣpādyair vasugarbhakaṭāhake  Paus anugrahakarastvāste svayaṃ śraddhāvatāṃ nṛṇām ārambhād eva niṣpattiparyantaṃ śubhakarmaṇām  Paus arcayitvā namaskṛtya dvādaśārṇena cācyutam tato nulepanaṃ dadyāt puṣpasragdhūpam eva hi  Paus naivedyaṃ madhuparkādyaṃ sabhakṣyaṃ saphalaṃ mahat atha sarveśvaraṃ bhaktyā vibhum āyatanasthitam  Paus mahatā vibhavenaiva snānapūrveṇa karmaṇā pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ satsūktaiḥ samyaguttamaiḥ  Paus rahasyamantrapūvaistu sāṣṭārṇadvādaśākṣaraiḥ jānubhyām avaniṃ kṛtvā natamūrdhāgrato bhavet  Paus tadekakṣema pūrvaṃ tu viniveśya idaṃ paṭhet paraṃ vasu ghṛtā ṛktvaṃ sarvaṃ saṃpūritaṃ tvayā  Paus tāreyaṃ paramā śaktisvamiyāsvāmitvādeva pūjitaḥtā vāsādyānanam āgneyatulyaṃ yajñasya vai phalam  Paus sumahadgokulopetaṃ grāmaṃ yad viṣayoditam tatpālakānāṃ viprāṇāṃ śāsanena samāpya ca  Paus yathā nocchidyate caiva kīrtidharmaparaṃ mahat nṛpeṇaitat tathā kāryaṃ yaśodharmavivṛddhaye  Paus ṣaṭkād yad adhikaṃ caiva saśubhaṃ kīrtitaṃ trayam goṣṭham agniṃ ca dīpaṃ ca aṅgam āyataneṣu tat  Paus dharmajñaiḥ pālanīyaṃ ca vicchedo na bhaved yathā yasmād vahnimukhenaiva trayastriṃśattu koṭayaḥ  Paus pratyahaṃ tṛptim atulāṃ vibudhānāṃ prayānti ca dadhikṣīrājyapūrvaistu vividhairgosamutthitaiḥ  Paus prītim abhyeti bhagavān upahāraistu sāttvikaiḥ paramādityavat sarvam ābhāsayati tejasā  Paus prabhāvāccaiva dīpasya nityaṃ sannihitasya ca yo dhikṛtya jagannāthaṃ ṣaḍaśītimukhāsu ca  Paus tithiṣvarcyastu bhagavān kalaśe maṇḍane nale sopavāsaḥ śuciḥ snātaḥ kṛtakautukamaṅgalaḥ  Paus praṇavādinamontena mantreṇānena bhaktitaḥ prīyatāṃ mama deveśo dharmādhyakṣo vṛṣākapiḥ  Paus gohito gopatirgoptā sarvamāvṛtya ca sthitaḥ tato nulipte bhūbhāge kutapaḥ kevalaṃ tu vā  Paus abhuktamahataṃ śuddhaṃ prastīryaṃ satilākṣatam samastabījaṃ sakuśaṃ siddhārthakasamanvitam  Paus tad bahistejasaṃ dadyāt pūrṇaṃ prāgāditaḥ kramāt pātrāṣṭakaṃ payaḥ śālidadhyakṣatarasaistilaiḥ  Paus ghṛtena sarvabījaistu vastrairyavanikā bahiḥ iṣubhiḥ saha sūtraistu barhipakṣaiḥ suviṣṭaraiḥ  Paus jātabījaśarāvāśca pūrṇakumbhamukhasthitāḥ pūrṇaśākhāsametāśca taruśākhābhyalaṃkṛtāḥ  Paus dikṣu prajvalitair dīpaiḥ saha nyasya ṛgādikaiḥ tato vatārya tanmadhye surabhiṃ kṛtamaṇḍanām  Paus sālaṃkṛtāṃ savastrāṃ ca ghaṇṭācāmarabhūṣitām saratnahemakumudāṃ tacchṛṅgaparibhūṣitām  Paus muktāpravālalāṅgūlāṃ rajatāṅghrim abhipriyām lalāṭadarpaṇāṃ śrīmatsraguṣṇīṣabalāṃ mahat  Paus evam evātha vīryadhvaṃ surabhiṃ kṛtamaṇḍanām yauvanasthāmadhṛṣṭāṃ ca vāmabhāge vṛṣasya ca  Paus kāṃsyopadohasaṃyuktāṃ pūrvedyur adhivāsitām nandāsunandāsurabhiśītalākhyapadānvitām  Paus catvāro dhenavaḥ sthāpyāḥ prāgādau tatra saṃmukham suśaktivibhavopetā dugdhadohapradakṣamāḥ  Paus sagarbhāśca savatsāśca prasūtāśca sakṛt sakṛt iṣṭadevam athoddiśya digbhāgān sāṃprataṃ tu vai  Paus hetinā ca tadīyena candanenātvacotsṛjet vṛṣṇikṣetrasametaṃ ca tasya cāsaṃbhavāt tu vai  Paus ānuguṇyaṃ yathāśaktyā tanmūlyaṃ tu na kalpya ca caturṇām agnihotrāṇāṃ bahiḥsthāḥ pratipādya ca  Paus vastrālaṃkaraṇopetaṃ mūlyaṃ ca surabhīyakam vasudhāṃ vasudhārthaṃ vā vṛṣopakaraṇaṃ hi yat  Paus praṇipādya gurorbhaktyā vṛṣabhaṃ surabhiṃ tyajet dakṣiṇe skandhadeśe ca hetinābhimatena ca  Paus lohenānalataptena mudraṇīyaṃ kṣaṇena ca evaṃ kṛtvā vṛṣatyāgaṃ taduddeśena vai punaḥ  Paus prabhūtam annadānaṃ ca dadyāccaiva sadakṣiṇam samantranātham uddiśya hyātmanorthe parasya vā  Paus vṛṣotsargaṃ hi yaḥ kuryād brahmalokaṃ vrajatyasau vṛṣo hi bhagavān dharmo loke kāmārthabandhataḥ  Paus tena tyaktena saṃtyaktaṃ janmaduḥkhaṃ hi śāśvatam prakṛtyā saha vai śaśvat surabhī savinaśvarā  Paus tad viśeṣācca tisro yāḥ śaktayo madanātmikāḥ buddhir asmīti pūrvā ca pañcendriyam athāparā  Paus vinivartanti sarvāstā gotvamāśritya ye sthitāḥ nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ vṛṣotsargeṇa vai saha  Paus uktam abjasamudbhūta idānīm avadhāraya apavargapradaṃ divyaṃ sūcitaṃ yat punaḥ punaḥ  Paus pratiṣṭhāpanam abjākṣa ācyutaṃ bhuktimuktidam iti śrī pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ nānādharmapratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma ekacatvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥatha dvicatvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥśrībhagavānuvāca dvādaśākṣarapūrvaistu mantraiḥ sarveśvaraḥ purā  Paus ārādhyo bhagavān bhaktyā vedyāṃ vā kalaśe sthale santarpyājyādikair bhaktyā mantraiḥ śrutimayaistataḥ  Paus bhagavān viśvakarmātmā sagaṇeśaṃ tu yājayet vividhair upacāraistu puṣpadhūpānulepanaiḥ  Paus visarjane kṛte viṣṇau sānale kamalodbhava śilpino yatra ye dakṣā mānyāsti tadanantaram  Paus yathāprasannabuddhyā tu śaśvannirvartayanti ca tair api prayataiḥ snātaiḥ tarpaṇīyaḥ svakaḥ patiḥ  Paus tataḥ parigṛhītavyaṃ kṣetraṃ tvabhimataṃ dvija abhuktam athavā bhuktaṃ vasudhāguṇalakṣitam  Paus niḥśalyam anukūlaṃ ca sthapatīnāṃ ca saṃmatam samādāya pratiṣṭhārthaṃ yathābhimatavistṛtam  Paus mahendro pāṃpatirvāyurvirttapeśānadikṣu ca padam āsādya vai kuryād divyād āyatanāśritam  Paus pañcāyatanapūrvaṃ tu śubhaṃ devagṛhaṃ mahat siddhaye tatsvamārgāt tu vimārgāt tadasiddhaye  Paus etāvad arthanānmuktaṃ ato nyeṣāṃ tu doṣakṛt svamārgaṃ paramārgaṃ vā yeṣāṃ sarvagato hariḥ  Paus sphuratyavirataṃ buddhau guruṃ taṃ śāstrataḥ svayam śubhe nukūle nakṣatre namaskṛtyācyutaṃ vibhum  Paus nirvartya nityaṃ vighnena pūrvam arcāpayed dvija saha ekāyanaiścānyai ṛgyajuḥ sāmapāṭhakaiḥ  Paus sāṃlaṃkāraiśva soṣṇīṣaiḥ sitāṃbaradharaistathā samālabhanamālyaiśca bhūṣitaiḥ sāṅgulīyakaiḥ  Paus śaṅkhavāditranirghoṣair gītibhir māṅgalīyakaiḥ phalapuṣpākṣatakaro jālasiddhārthakādikam  Paus samādāya śuciḥ kartā deśikena saha dvija sthānam āsādya sarveṣāṃ vāsudevaṃ hṛdi smaran  Paus puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā ca gāyatrītritayādikam uddhoṣya śākunaṃ sūktaṃ śivasaṃkalpameva ca  Paus śrīsūktena samopetaṃ bhadraśrīsāmam uttamam karmārambheṇa saha vai svasti bho ityayaṃ paṭhet  Paus camaṣaṭkāṃstatodīrya śāntādyāstadanantaram japannaṣṭākṣaraṃ tiṣṭhan kartāste deśikastataḥ  Paus bahiḥ kṣetrasya caiśānyāṃ prācyāṃ vā kamalodbhava tatāṃ parṇakuṭīṃ kṛtvā vātavṛṣṭikṣamāṃ śubhām  Paus tatra puṣpārghyadhūpādyaṃ kṛtvā vai bhadrapīṭhagam pañcagavyaṃ samāpādya sārdhaṃ mantrairvilakṣaṇaiḥ  Paus nārāyaṇam apāṃ mūrtiṃ hemādye kutape śubhe sannidhīkṛtya saṃpūjya sarit tīrthāmbupūjite  Paus hemasarvauṣadhīratra darbhavargasraganvite mantrāstrakalaśābhyāṃ tu saṃpādya racanāṃ tataḥ  Paus sādhāram āsanaṃ tābhyāṃ jñātvā kuryāt tadarcanam hṛdi mantreśvaraṃ sāstraṃ pūjayitvā yathāvidhi  Paus nyastavyam āsane kaumbhe prāṇavanmanasā saha saumyanāḍīpathā caiva tato hyastraṃ samantrarāṭ  Paus dakṣiṇena tu mārgeṇa tvapasavyaghaṭe vibhoḥ avatārya jvaladrūpaṃ dahantaṃ vighnasaṃcayam  Paus mantratrayaṃ tu sāmānyaṃ sarvatra vihitaṃ dvija ṣaḍaṣṭākṣaramantraṃ yat tathā vai dvādaśākṣaram  Paus hetīśaṃ yat sahasrāraṃ parijñeyaṃ tadāyudham kṛtadīkṣeṇa yallabdhaṃ suprasannācca vai guroḥ  Paus astraṃ tadaṅgam āpādyaṃ saviśeṣam idaṃ śubham sāṅgaṃ samarcayitvā tu bhogair mātrāvasānikaiḥ  Paus satsūktair yajubhiḥ sāmair yathāvasaralakṣaṇaiḥ vyañjakair atha sarveśam atha homaṃ samācaret  Paus sahasraśatasaṃkhyaṃ yat pūrṇāntaiḥ sākṣataistilaiḥ kuṇḍamantrāstradṛkpūtairevaṃ kuryāt tu deśikaḥ  Paus sthaleṣu vālukādyeṣu prāgādau viniveśya ca catvāraścāturātmīyā mantrajñāḥ kṛtamaṇḍanāḥ  Paus ṛgvedādyāścatasro ye īśād vāyupathāvadhi bhaktyā kriyāparā yājyā homārthaṃ kṣetrasaṃgrahe  Paus hotavyaṃ bhramiliṅgaistair mantrair ājyādikaṃ bahu caturbhiścāturātmīyair dviṣaṭkārṇapurassaraiḥ  Paus hotavyam aparair vipraiḥ smaran sarveśvaraṃ harim upadraṣṭā catuṣkoṇe ekaikaṃ viniyojya ca  Paus homārthaṃ sarvakuṇḍeṣu mantravinyastavigraham śucayaḥ saṃyatā dakṣā vāstuśāstrakṛtaśramān  Paus viśvakarmakulodbhūtān āhūyāgre niveśya ca pañcagavyādinābhyukṣya sitāmbaradharāṃstu vai  Paus mālyacandanasoṣṇīṣair bhūṣitāṅgulikādikān saṃvīkṣya pāvanīkṛtya hyādāya ghaṭikānvitam  Paus kārpāsaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ sūtraṃ sahasrārābhimāntritam sthapatīnāṃ kare dadyāt saha caikaśalākayā  Paus prokṣitān pañcagavyena sahasrārābhimantritān vikīrya lājasaṃmiśrān bījān siddhārthakānvitān  Paus japannastraṃ sacakraṃ ca tridhā kuryāt pradakṣiṇam prākpadāt tatpadaṃ yāvat saha ghaṇṭāravaiḥ śubhaiḥ  Paus kṣetramānam athādāya karair abhimataistataḥ śiṣyadeśikakartṛsthair viśvakarmāṃśakaistu vā  Paus īśakoṇādi tatsūtraṃ caturdikṣu prasārya ca śaṅkubhiryajñadārūtthair mudrayecca diśāṣṭakam  Paus tato bhūtabaliṃ dadyāt prādakṣiṇyena buddhimān tilapiṣṭaṃ niśācūrṇaṃ salājadadhisaktukam  Paus bhūtakrūram iti proktaṃ tena bhūtabaliṃ haret bhūtāni rākṣasā vāpi ye traṃ tiṣṭhanti kecana  Paus te sarve dyāpagacchantu sthānaṃ kuryāmimaṃ hareḥ śaravetralatācarmapuñjādyair grathitān drumān  Paus mṛdaṅgordhvasamākārān pāṇḍumṛdgrahaṇakṣamān nacāṅgahomāsyustīkṣṇān kuddālākhyakhanitrakān  Paus sudṛḍhān yajñakāṣṭhotthān hastipādāṃśca pūjayet kṣetrabrahmapade sthitvā yathābhimatadiṅmukhaḥ  Paus saṃsmṛtya dvādaśārṇena bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ adhibhūtādhidevākhyaṃ smared adhyātmalakṣaṇam  Paus saptadvīpavatīṃ tatra samudrādisamanvitām saptapātālasahitāṃ bhūtairyuktaṃ carādikaiḥ  Paus śaktibhiḥ śabdaniṣṭhābhiḥ sarvabhābhiḥ samāvṛtām brahmabījasametena lakāreṇa sabindunā  Paus svasaṃjñānātiyuktena mānayitvā purā tataḥ bhāvayitvādhibhūtatvam ādhidaivamataḥ smaret  Paus sāmarthyaṃ yad bhagavato viṣṇoḥ sarveśvarasya ca param adhyātmarūpaṃ ca vārāhaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ mahat  Paus etāvad uktaṃ sāmānyaṃ dhyānaṃ kṣitiparigrahe devālayavaśād anyad viśeṣaṃ cātra saṃsmaret  Paus caturaśre caturmūrtivyaktivyūhaṃ vicintya ca caturaśrāyate dhyāyed divyaṃ vidyāgamaṃnvidam  Paus vṛttaśāntoditaṃ cakraṃ saṃvṛtāvayavaṃ smaret anantaśayanaṃ devaṃ dhyāyed vṛttāyate gṛhe  Paus puryaṣṭakaṃ yad amalaṃ kālapuṣkaradehabhṛt nābhirandhrodbhavaṃ viṣṇoḥ sthitam aṣṭadigātmanām  Paus devālaye dvijāṣṭāśre smartavyaṃ vasudhāgṛham dhyātvaivaṃ dvādaśārṇena mantreṇa ca punaḥ punaḥ  Paus ṣaḍakṣareṇa saṃrodhya mudrāṃ baddhā dvijācyutam adhidhyānasamādhānād yāvat kalaśasannidhim  Paus prāgvad vilakṣaṇair bhogair athāṣṭārṇena pūjayet saha vipraiḥ svayaṃ dadyād agnau pūrṇāhutiṃ punaḥ  Paus sarvakarmasamādhyarthaṃ kṣetre kṣetrīkṛte sati kuryāt pādapratiṣṭhāṃ vai suśubhe divase pare  Paus atha karmakarā dakṣā niyoktavyāḥ krameṇa tu saṃtoṣya cānnapānādyaistoṣam āyānti vai yathā  Paus śrībhagavānuvāca evaṃ parigṛhīte tu kṣmāṃśe śalyojjhite sati ādhṛṣṭe sopalā bālā vasudhā vasubhūmidā  Paus śuddhiṃ sopekṣate kiñcit kṛtrimām udapāsara  yāvannopavanastāṃtu cirarūḍhair mahādrumaiḥ  Paus saṃkīrṇā tat prasūtaiśca mūlairvyāptā nirantaraiḥ jñātaṃ tasyāpi bālatvaṃ śuddhirvai bhāvinī smṛtā  Paus tyaktā saritpravāhair na nagaragrāmadeśikāḥ mahāntaṃ prekṣate śuddhiṃ bhaṅktvāśā bahuśo yataḥ  Paus svātvā vai bhāvam uddhṛtya dādyād abhyeti mṛcchubhām sitāmaśarkarāṃ snigdhāṃ jalāntarnikhaneta vā   Paus dṛṣṭvā jalaṃ samabhyarcya tarpayedyādasāṃpatim nāganāthasamopetaṃ surasaṅghamatasthitam  Paus sthityartham upalaiḥ sarvaiḥ saha saṃpūryate mṛdā mṛdopalaiśca saṃpūrya jātiṣu snigdhayā tayā  Paus ākoṭaya paunaḥ punyena bālād vai vāparisecanā t samīkṛtyopalipyātha gogaṇāṃstatra vāsayet  Paus bālavatsasametaṃ ca vṛṣendragaṇasaṃyutam satoyāḥ śālayaścaiva prabhūtatṛṇasaṃcayam  Paus vikīrya satilaṃ tatra santyakte gomayādikaiḥ apāsya gogaṇaṃ paścād upalipya punarmahīm  Paus samarcayitvā sūryātmā prāgvad diksiddhim ācaret prāsādaṃ bhagavad rūpasametaṃ kamalodbhava  Paus yathābhimatadigvaktraṃ niścayīkṛtya vai purā bhūbhāge sati vai kuryāt tadagre yāgamaṇḍapam  Paus diktraye tadalābhe tu saumyayāmyadigāyatam ānuguṇyāya śuddhiṃ ca sukhaṃ nirbādhamiśritam  Paus śaraiḥ kāśaiḥ śaraiḥ kūrcair acchinnaṃ vā paraistu vā sāntaraṃ vihitaṃ tatra pārthivaṃ pīṭhapañcakam  Paus saptaṣaṭpañcahastaṃ ca vibhavānuguṇaṃ tataḥ caturhastaṃ tu vai sārdhaṃ caturhastam athāpi vā  Paus suvistṛtai teṣṣaḍaṃśena sarveṣāṃ parivarjya ca antarālāni viprendra tad ucchrāyam athācaret  Paus caturviṃśatimāṃśena svena svena mahāmate tad vistārocchrite sarve koṇastambheṣu bhūṣayet  Paus tanmānena samāropya stambhānāṃ śirasopari racanāracitāścānye daṇḍāstiryakprasāritāḥ  Paus sarve sthūlābjasaṃbhūtāścaturdiktoraṇānvitāḥ tṛtīyāṃśena vai pīṭhāt toraṇāvistṛtirbhavet  Paus suvistṛtaistribhāgena sarveṣāṃ unnatiḥ smṛtā sacakragaruḍāḥ sarve tricatuḥpañcasaṃkhyayā  Paus sāntarālapramāṇena sastaṃbhāstoraṇākhilāḥ viniveśyāḥ kṣitau kṛtvā sarve caiva sulakṣaṇāḥ  Paus caturaśrāstvatho deśā hyaṣṭāśrā madhyato dvija vartulācordhvabhāgāśca samāṃśena vibhājitāḥ  Paus vīthī prākpaścimā bhāgā ubhayoḥ pīṭhasaṃmitā sottaraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bhāgam ekaikaṃ pīṭhavartakam  Paus kṛtvaivaṃ bhagavad yāgamaṇḍapaṃ sarvakarmaṇā udagdikpīṭhataścordhve dhiṣṇyaṃ kuryāt kajaṅkitam  Paus vartulaṃ caturaśraṃ vā prakāśākhyaṃ sulakṣaṇam śaṅkhacakragadāpadmaiścihnite mekhalāvanau  Paus dravyāṇām adhivāsārthaṃ tatsamīpasthitāṃ mahīm madhyame maṇḍalaṃ pīṭhe mantrāstrakalaśārcanam  Paus catuṣkaṃ snānakuṃbhānāṃ soṣadhīnāṃ niveśane anyatra śayanaṃ tasmin snānapīṭhe tu vinyaset  Paus snānakuṃbhasamīpaṃ tu snānadravyasamanvitam pīṭhaṃ tatpañcamaṃ viddhi vālukābhiḥ supūjitam  Paus sadvāraṃ sagavākṣaṃ ca sakavāṭaṃ hi sārgalam kṛtvaivaṃ adhivāsārthaṃ prākāravalayaṃ mahat  Paus prāsādakṣetramānaṃ ca santyajya paritaḥ sthitam samekhalaṃ sapīṭhaṃ tat dikṣu kuṇḍāṣṭakaṃ likhet  Paus anukalpe tu vai kuryāt prācyāṃ diṅmaṇḍalādbahiḥ tatpāścātye tu vā bhāge ekapīṭhāḥ satoraṇāḥ  Paus stambhā vā pṛthakpīṭhā viviktāśca parasparam prāgbhāge cakrapadmākhyaṃ dakṣiṇe kevaleśvarī  Paus caturaśraṃ tu vā kalpyaṃ gadāmekhalam abjaja padmād uttaradigbhāge śaṅkhaṃ koṇacatuṣṭaye  Paus eṣa pādapratiṣṭhāyāṃ kuṇḍānāṃ saṃsthitiḥ smṛtā cāturātmyādidevānāṃ brahman sthāpanakarmaṇi  Paus saṃsthitiṃ śṛṇu kuṇḍānāṃ vividhā digvidikṣu ca mahavibhavasaubhāgyaāyurārogyavṛddhaye  Paus  siddhaye sarvakarmāṇāṃ vighnānāṃ vinivṛttaye vyatyayācca phalaṃ viddhi muktaye samatānasau  Paus gadādvandvadvayopetaṃ prāgdikturyāśrameva ca cakradakṣiṇadigvipra śaṅkhaṃ pratyaggate tataḥ  Paus padmam uttaradigbhāge yathābhimatapallavam āgneyaṃ tu samāpādya kuṇḍam aśvatthapatravat  Paus vimuktakamalaṃ kuryāt trikoṇaṃ pūrvavartulam homārthaṃ yātudikkuṇḍam aṣṭāśraṃ vāyave pade  Paus dhiṣṇyaṃ śrīvatsasaṃjñaṃ yat prāgvad ardhendulakṣaṇam aiśānyāṃ tu samālikhya lakṣaṇenopalakṣitam  Paus ato paraṃ saṃniveśam ekāgram avadhāraya dhiṣṇyaṃ pūrvapade vṛttam āgneyyāṃ kaustubhākṛtim  Paus cakraṃ dakṣiṇadigbhāge śārṅgākāraṃ tu yātudik āpyaṃ gadākṛtiṃ prāgvanamālākhyā vāyave pade  Paus udagdikkamalākāraṃ śrīvatsākāranīśagam vistārasamamānaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vihitaṃ tu vai  Paus prāgvad dvādaśamāṃśaṃ tu oṣṭhārdhaṃ parimṛjya ca susamaṃ mekhalābandhaṃ kuryāt tadvistṛteḥ samam  Paus samekhalā vai viṣamāḥ sarveṣāṃ pūrvavad dvija yathoktalakṣaṇā kāryā yoniḥ pippalapatravat  Paus madhyadeśe suvṛttaṃ ca turyaṃ śrīvatsalakṣaṇam prāsādakṣetrabhūmer vā tamevaiśapade bahiḥ  Paus saṃpādya mānayuktaṃ vā tarpaṇe sarvakarmaṇām vāstvaṅgavibudhānāṃ ca lokeśānāṃ mahāmate  Paus vighneśadvārapālānāṃ kṣetreśasya tathā kṣiteḥ saṃpādyam evam abjottha sakuṇḍaṃ yāgamandiram  Paus tato ntarāt sabāhyaṃ ca ūrjanaṃ paribhūṣayet suvicitrair dhvajai ramyairvaijayantīgaṇaiśca taiḥ  Paus procchritaiḥ kadalīrūpair drumāṅgaiḥ pāvanair dṛḍhaiḥ savastraiḥ pūrṇasughaṭaiḥ puṣpairvai mañjarīgaṇaiḥ  Paus vitānaivividhākārair vinānalagṛhaṃ tu vai saśarairbarhipakṣaistu sūtrairbhūtādhidaivataiḥ  Paus prāk prāptair lokanāthādyair dvāḥsthaiḥ kṣetralatāgṛhaiḥ darpaṇaiścāmaraiścitrair ghaṇṭāvṛndaiḥ svarānvitaiḥ  Paus madhvājyadadhisakṣīrasupūrṇaiḥ kāṃsyabhājānaiḥ upakuṃbhānanasthaiśca haritaiḥ pālikāgaṇaiḥ  Paus śālitaṇḍulapātraistu sahiraṇyaiḥ phalodvahaiḥ lājasiddhārthakair bījabhājanaiḥ ṣaḍrasānvitaiḥ  Paus satsugandhaistvagelādyaiḥ pātraiḥ pūgaphalaistataḥ madhūkabadarīlākṣāsubhistriphalaiḥ phalaiḥ  Paus yathā tatprabhavaiḥ puṣpaiḥ bahubhiḥ prakarīyakaiḥ ityevamādyair vividhair bhogapūgaistu pāvanaiḥ  Paus bhūmayaḥ pīṭhabāhyāstu sarvadikparivārya ca saṃpraveśyākhilaṃ tatra saṃbhāraṃ bhūrisaṃbhṛtam  Paus śubhe grahe nukūle ca nakṣatre susthire tataḥ lagne sthire sthirāṃśe ca pariśuddhe guṇānvite  Paus prāsādāṅghripratiṣṭhārthaṃ kartā vai bhagavanmayaḥ kṛtāhniko dvijendrādyair deśikena samanvitaḥ  Paus bherīpaṭahavāditraśaṅkhaśabdādikaiḥ saha ṛgyajuḥ sāmapūrvāṃśca praśastāḥ saṃpaṭhan śrutīḥ  Paus dvārapālārcanaṃ kṛtvā yāgāgāraṃ praviśya ca saṃsmṛtya svāsane vyāptim arcayitvopaviśya ca  Paus madhyapīṭhasamīpe tu prāṅmukhaṃ paścime pade prāgdikpratyaṅmukhaṃ yojyamṛṅmayāścāsaneṣu ca  Paus udagdakṣiṇadigyantraṃ yajurvedāṃstu yojayet prāṅmukhaṃ paścime bhāge sāmajñānviniyojya ca  Paus saha caikāyanair viprair mūrtisaṃjñopalakṣitaiḥ diguttarasyāṃ ca tato nityakarmaparāyaṇān  Paus niveśyātharvavedāṃśca sarve dvidvikasaṃkhyayā pṛṣṭhataḥ susahāyādyaiḥ samyagjñānapratīkṣakaḥ  Paus upadeṣṭā ca mantrāṇāṃ dvijādīnāṃ samarcane dakṣiṇe svātmanaḥ kuryād ekacitraṃ samāhitam  Paus tataḥ samācaret nyāsaṃ dvādaśākṣaramūrtinā mantrābhimānaśaktiṃ vai samālambya dhiyā tataḥ  Paus athāṣṭākṣarapūrvaistu mantraiḥ śrutimayaistataḥ prākproktavidhinā pādyaṃ bhṛṅgārakamalaṃ purā  Paus pādyārghyaiḥ pañcagavyaṃ ca kṛtvābhyarcya dvijātaye samālaṃbhanapuṣpādyaiḥ savastrair aṅgulīyakaiḥ  Paus sapavitrakaistu hemāḍhyair dhūpayitvā yathākramam prayataḥ sasahāyaśca sthapatiścopaveśayet  Paus dattvājñāṃyarjamānasya karmabhūmau sthitāni ca suvarṇarājatotthāni navatāmramayāni vā  Paus śailajānyanukalpe tu mṛtkumbhānyathavābjaja tatra madhyamakumbhaṃ yat caturviṃśāṅgulena ca  Paus vistṛte madhyatastacca dvyaṅguladvyaṅgulonnatam vaktram aṅgulaṣaṭkena tatrāsyaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ smṛtam  Paus mekhaloparito jñeyā tryaṅgulā kamalodbhava ye tu dikkamalānyevaitad ardhenonnataiḥ samāḥ  Paus phalaiśca vividhaiścaiva saha saṃpūrya vai mṛdā ākoṭya khādiraiḥ kāṣṭhaiḥ prabalair ambusañcitāḥ  Paus pūraṇārtham aśeṣāt tu kṛtvā khātaṃ tu sādhakam samīkṛtyopalipyātha prāgvad diksiddhim ācaret  Paus bhūṣayecca dhvajair anyair vaijayantīḥ samutkṣipet śobhayet kadalīpūrvair drumāṅgaiḥ pāvanair dṛḍhaiḥ  Paus vastraiḥ pūrṇaghaṭaiḥ puṣpaiḥ kauśeyair mañjarīgaṇaiḥ śubhe grahe nukūle tu nakṣatre śubhadarśane  Paus lagne sthire sthirāṃśe ca pariśuddhe guṇānvite prāsādāṅghripratiṣṭhārthaṃ kartā vai bhagavanmayaḥ  Paus kṛtāhniko dvijendrādyair deśikena samanvitaḥ bherīpaṭahavāditrasarvaśabdādikaiḥ śubhaiḥ  Paus vandivṛndasamopetair gīyamānaiśca maṅgalaiḥ sāmaṛgyajupūrvāstu praśastāḥ pāṭhayecchrutīḥ  Paus sahasaṃbhṛtasaṃbhārakṣmākṛtaṃ kṣmāmalaṃ viśet samācamya kṛtanyāso dvādaśākṣaramūrtinā  Paus athāṣṭākṣarapūrvaistu mantraiḥ śrutimayaiḥ saha pādārghyapañcagavyaṃ tu kṛtvābhyarcya dvijottamam  Paus sthapatiścārghyapuṣpādyaiḥ pravarteta sukarmaṇi oṃkārapūrvāṃ gāyatrīm ekaikaṃ pāṭhayed dvija  Paus gāyatrīsāmapūrvaṃ ca kanikrandam udīrya ca evam oṅkārapūrvaṃ ca karmākarambham anantaram  Paus paṭhed ekāyanaṃ paścāt śivasaṃkalpam eva ca ṛgvedajño yajurjño tha bhadronaṃ samudīryaṃ ca  Paus bhadraśrīsāma sāmajñaḥ śatādyau kṛtyadharmavit vibhajya pūrvavat kṣetraṃ pavitrīkṛtya sāṃpratam  Paus pavitramantrair akhilair vaidikaiḥ pāñcarātrikaiḥ kanyāṃ ca saumyadigbhāge aiśānyāṃ vālayāvane  Paus maṇḍalaṃ pārthive pīṭhe vinivartya catuḥ same aśubhaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ vaśyāgāradvayānvitam  Paus bhadrapīṭhāsanasthaṃ ca sodakaṃ ca ghaṭadvayam stragādyair bhūṣitaṃ kṛtvā ekasmin sādhanaṃ yajet  Paus dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ śrutyuktair mantramukhyaistu tadastraparake ghaṭe  Paus mantrair hetīśaliṅgaistu caturvedasamutthitaiḥ maṇḍapāgramathāsādya hārdam āpādyam arcanam  Paus avatārya bahiḥ kuryāt pūjanaṃ prāgyathoditam pūrṇāhutiṃ vināgnau tu tarpayitvā yathāvidhi  Paus yajed vāstu narādyaṃ vai surasaṅghaṃ tadaṅgakam śataṃ śatārdhaṃ pādaṃ vā āhutīnāṃ samāpayet  Paus tilānām ājyasiktānām ājyasya tadanantaram sāmarair vāstuliṅgaistu mantrair devavratādikaiḥ  Paus susamaṃ kalaśānāṃ tu navakaṃ tvatha dhātujam yathāśaktipramāṇaṃ tu nālpaṃ vai dvādaśāṅgulam  Paus śailajaṃ mṛnmayotthaṃ vā supakvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ śumam bhṛṅgāratulyam aṣṭāśraṃ śaṅkhākāraṃ tu vocchritam  Paus valihīnaṃ viraktāsyaṃ dravyāṇāṃ grahalakṣaṇam śuddhyartham atha sarveṣāṃ snānakarma samācaret  Paus adhivāsyāmbaracchannān sadyo vānye hani dvija kramaśaḥ pūrayed dravyaistalliṅgaiḥ śrutisaṃpaṭhaiḥ  Paus gāyatryāṣṭākṣareṇaiva dvādaśākṣaravidyayā suvarṇasikatābhistu ratnair muktāphalādikaiḥ  Paus dhātubhiścākhilair dhānyair athānyaiḥ pāratādikaiḥ siddhārthakānvitair bījair dhānyair nīvārapūrvakaiḥ  Paus karpūramalayakṣodakuṅkumāgarumiśritaiḥ paṭṭastrakcandanādyaistu bāhyataścopaśobhayet  Paus evaṃ saṃpūjya saṃskṛtya caturṇāṃ madhyato nyaset padmāsanagatāṃ lakṣmīṃ nidhibhiḥ parivāritām  Paus caturṇām atha cānyeṣāṃ ratnarāṭ kaustubhābhidhaḥ samantreṇa svanāmnā ca nidhināthaiḥ samanvitām  Paus bhagavān sarvaśaktyātmā ekasmin paricintayet ṣaḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa niṣkalaṃ śabdavigraham  Paus brāhmaṃ catuṣpadaṃ kṣetraṃ nayed aṣṭacchadātmanā nyasya sārveśvaraṃ kumbhaṃ madhyataḥ karṇikodare  Paus ratnakuṃbhacatuṣkaṃ tu dikcakreṣvaṣṭadikṣu ca prādakṣivyena prāgbhāgān mantrān vā laukikān dvija  Paus lakṣyaṃ kumbhacatuṣkaṃ yad īśād vāyupadāvadhi evaṃ nyastvā tataḥ kuryād arcanaṃ madhyagasya ca  Paus catuṣkaṃ hṛdayādyaṃ vai ratnakuṃbhagataṃ yajet caturṇāṃ mantram ekaṃ tu śrīkumbhānāṃ tu pūjayet  Paus purato netramantraistu madhyakumbhe ca tasya ca kṛtvaivaṃ niṣkalaṃ nyāsaṃ sarveṣāṃ sāṃprataṃ tataḥ  Paus vidhānanavakaṃ dadyāt tāmraṃ vā śailajaṃ samam suvṛttaṃ caturaśraṃ vā sudhanaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam  Paus catuśśaktiniruddhaṃ ca tatra madhyagate dhaṭe śaktirvā yā parā devī viśvasandhāraṇakṣamā  Paus prabhāsā vaiśvarī dikṣu jñānaśaktyāmṛtā ca sā vidigghaṭasamūhe tu smared ānandalakṣaṇā  Paus kriyākhyā yācyutī śaktiḥ śuddhā śaktasya janmadā nyastvaivam arcanaṃ kuryāt śriyādīnāṃ svasaṃjñayā  Paus nidhīnāṃ nidhināthānāṃ mantraṃ sāṅgaṃ yajet tataḥ mudrāṃ pradarśayet māntrīṃ sarvasāmarthyalakṣaṇām  Paus dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa japtavyaṃ ca samācaret sannirodhaṃ dviṣaṭkārṇe na sannidhim  Paus yajurjñaṃ tvatha sañcodya yujyateti ca yadyajuḥ ṛcaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ sāmajño viṣṇusaṃhitām  Paus atharvāyeti ṣaṭpādya dvijam ekāyanaṃ tataḥ ātmavyūhādikaṃ kuryāt saṃjñāmantracatuṣṭayam  Paus
