namaskārasamopetaṃ tataḥ sāma rathantaram āhutvā hā harṣapūrvaṃ vai ṛnvedaṃ samudīrayet  Paus pratiṣṭhāsīti vai sāma sāmajño tha udīrayet ato ntaraṃ tu kumbhānāṃ  Paus āpādyam atha sarveṣāṃ sudhālepena caiva hi digaṣṭakaṃ mudraṇīyaṃ kṣetraṃ śaktyaṣṭakena tu  Paus śilāntaḥ sannirodhena śilānāmasamāstu vā kāryā ūrdhvasamāḥ sarvāḥ sarvatobhadralakṣaṇāḥ  Paus snānādyaiḥ saṃskṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ vāsastragvarṇabhūṣitā ratnāṣṭakāsanasthā ca aṣṭānāṃ ca suvinyaset  Paus mantram akṣarabhedena praṇavādyantaṇaṃ tu vai prāgādāvīśadiṅniṣṭham aṣṭakaṃ vyaktigaṃ nyaset  Paus praṇavena svanāmnā ca namo ntena mahāmate balavīryavatī nityā anantākhyā sthirā dhruvā  Paus sandhyākhyā dhṛtisaṃjñā ca sthitirnāmnā dvijāṣṭamī vedādyantaṃ samuddhoṣya yajurvedavrataiḥ saha  Paus haye ca vidyā ṛksūktā brūyād ekāyanaṃ tataḥ yadivāyo savetyādiva hutvaivaṃ kamalodbhava  Paus dattvā pūrṇāhutiṃ brūyāt mantram āśrāvikaṃ hi yat kartā ca deśikendro tha saṃsmaran mantrasaṃhitām  Paus nyastaśriyādikair nāmamantraiḥ sarvaiḥ samanvitam eṣāṃ buddhiḥ saptadheti mantram ekāyanaṃ paṭhan  Paus dadyād āhutikaṃ sarvaṃ karmaṇāṃ pūraṇāya ca etāvad uktam abjākṣa mukhyakalpaṃ mayā ca te  Paus anukalpamato vakṣye sarveṣāṃ ca hitāvaham etasmin kalaśe sarvam anyakṣetragaṇārcitam  Paus mantravyūhaṃ yathoktaṃ ca sthalagopalagaṃ nyaset sarvaśaktimayīm ekāṃ śaktiṃ vai pārameśvarīm  Paus niveśya madhyatastasmin dadyāt kośaṃ sudhādikam varṇakaiḥ kuṃkumādyaistu tatrordhve bjaṃ likhet tataḥ  Paus bhūbhāgaṃ khātaśeṣaṃ yat samantāt samatāṃ nayet prāgvadākoṭṭanādyena sarvāṅgairipubhistataḥ  Paus pañcaraṅgeṇa sūtreṇa śaṅkubhir yājñikair dṛḍhaiḥ astramantreṇa mantrajño jīmūtam atha saṃpaṭhet  Paus catuḥ strakcandanopetāṃ baliṃ vai sācca kāmikīm dadyāt pūrvoditāṃ dikṣu samācamya praṇamya ca  Paus dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa tristhānasthaṃ ca mantrarāṭ kṣāntvā tadopasaṃhṛtya prāgvadarcanapūrvakam  Paus sāṃsārīnāṃ bahiryāvad ācaret sthapatiṃ punaḥ viśvakarmā puraskṛtya anyeṣāṃ piśitāśinām  Paus dadyād dvijendrapūrvāṇām aśanaṃ dakṣiṇādikam anyeṣām arthinām annaṃ dhanadānaṃ svaśaktitaḥ  Paus nānādeśavaśāccaiva kuryād evaṃ gṛhāsanam vibhāgena samāyuktam ālayaṃ vividhaṃ tathā  Paus dhvajāsanāvasānaṃ ca vibhajya svadhiyā tataḥ iti śrīpāñcarātre mahopaniṣadi pauṣkarasaṃhitāyāṃ prāsādasya pādapratiṣṭhā nāma dvicatvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥ samudita ślokasaṃkhyā atha tricatvāriṃśo dhyāyaḥśrībhagavānuvāca prāsādāvāsataḥ koṇe samārabhya yathāruci prāṅkaṇaṃ sarvadikkṛtvā prākāraṃ parikalpayet  Paus grahikāsapratolīkaṃ kevalaṃ vāmarānvitam prāsāde tu catudvāre caturmūrtir alaṃkṛte  Paus dvidvikaṃ tu pratolīnāṃ dikṣu prākāragaṃ hitam catuṣkaṃ  prāṣṭakaṃ kuryāt prāsādānāṃ mahāmate  Paus ekarūpaṃ hi vā nānālakṣaṇaṃ bhagavadvaśāt yathābhimatamānaṃ ca prāsādābhāsamātrakam  Paus pakveṣṭhakāśmadārutthaṃ tatra koṇacatuṣṭaye catuṣkaṃ vihitaṃ vipra aṣṭakaṃ kalpayed yadi  Paus parasparamukhaṃ kuryād dvāroddeśadvaye tataḥ sāntaraṃ diktraye kuryāt prāsādānāṃ dvikaṃ dvikam  Paus sapīṭhād devamānācca dvārocchrāyam udāhṛtam pramāṇenonnatānāṃ ca devānāṃ ca mahāmate  Paus nānāhṛsvapramāṇānāṃ pīṭhenonnatimānayet vaitatyenonnatattvena lakṣaṇāniyamojjhitam  Paus dvāraṃ sukhapraveśaṃ ca saṃkaṭānāṃ guṇāvaham kṛtāyāṃ śuddhavihitaṃ ṛkṣeṇānugataṃ tu vai  Paus vistārāyāmayoścaiva ādāyāṅgulasantatim śubhāya ṛkṣalābhārthaṃ guṇayecca parasparam  Paus śodhayed vātha lābhārthaṃ muṣṭibhiścāṅgulisthitiḥ ekatripañca vai sapta śeṣāḥ sarve śubhāḥ smṛtāḥ  Paus dhvajaśārdūlavṛṣabhagajendrāḥ kramaśo hi te evaṃ nakṣatralābhārthaṃ śobhayet tāṃ sthitiṃ punaḥ  Paus ādekāt saptaviṃśāntaṃ śeṣāntaṃ hṛṣṭam ācaret varayed aṅgulaṃ caikaṃ pādayorvā prayatnataḥ  Paus nūnam aṅgularāśair vai śubhaṛkṣāya siddhaye vicāryaivaṃ purā samyak kuryād bhūmisurālayam  Paus śayanāsana āsīnaḥ suparṇasthasya vā vibhoḥ diktraye bhimate caiva evaṃ vā diktraye trayaḥ  Paus upaviṣṭaṃ tu yāmyāyāṃ paścime yā digutthitam udagdigdakṣiṇadvāre prāsāde garuḍāsanam  Paus catuṣṭayaṃ caturṇāṃ tu koṇānāṃ yat prakīrtitam tatrānale dignyastham udagdvāre tu prākcaram  Paus svabodhaparimāṇena sattvenābhimatena ca kalāsaktā iyattākhyāḥ paricchedavaśāt smṛtam  Paus tam āsthāpanasaṃjñaṃ ca viśeṣaṃ kamalodbhava saṃpanne brahmapāṣāṇasaṃskāre paiṭhike pi ca  Paus udvartanābhyañjanena mṛdbhūtigomayādinā śilpidoṣopaśamane snānamātre kṛte sati  Paus niṣpanne netradāne tu snāne saṃpādite pare utthāpya mūrtipālaistu gurvādīn bahubhirbalāt  Paus niveśanena mantraṃ yad vividhaṃ sāṃprataṃ kṛtam tritaye caikatāṃ prāpte vajralepena pauṣkara  Paus prokte lagnodaye mantranyāsam ācaraṇāt tu vai yacchakter anusandhānāt tat sthitisthāpane tathā  Paus prāsādāntarabhittīnāṃ likhitaṃ vāmbarādike sidhyarthaṃ sādhakendraistu siddhikālāvadhiṃ tu vai  Paus calabimbasya yanmantraṃ nyāsaṃ vai sāsanasya ca nityam ārādhanārthaṃ tu karmārcāyām api dvija  Paus taṃ vipra calanākhyaṃ tu sthitisthāpanam eva ca kṣmābhaṅgair jalapūrvaistu doṣairyā cātidūṣitā  Paus uddhṛtya yojanānyatra sthāne tu śubhalakṣaṇe samyak saṃsthāpanād bhūyaḥ saṃsthāpanam udāhṛtam  Paus vidyutprapātapūrvaistu doṣairyā cābhidūṣitā tadutthānakṛte śaśvannirdeṣe cāsane sthitim  Paus tatsamā lakṣaṇāḍhyā ca pratimānyā mahāmate he anyasmin vā neva pīṭhe bimba vatpariyojitā  Paus boddhavyaṃ tad viśeṣaṃ ca sthāpanotthāpanaṃ tu vai jñānasaṅghojjhitatvācca ekadiksamamīkṣaṇāt  Paus prādhānyenātha dikcakraṃ svagātrair iha vāsanāt śayanāsanasaṃsthānacalācalavaśād api  Paus pratiṣṭhākhyaviśeṣāśca bahavaḥ sarvasiddhidāḥ sāmānyasanniveśācca tad viśeṣaguṇāt tu vai  Paus sthitaṃ cākṣarayā śuddhyā sāmānyārccā phalārthinām phalasāmyaṃ parijñeyaṃ kiṃ tvanyasmin hi janmani  Paus cāturātmyapratiṣṭhā ca jñānaṃ yacchati śāśvatam yatprāpya na punarjanma punarevāpnuyānnaraḥ  Paus phalakāmastu yaḥ kuryāccaturmūrtiniveśanam śraddhayā parayā bhaktyā saṃkalpād eva padmaja  Paus paitṛkaṃ mātṛkaṃ caiva jāyākhyaṃ saptasaṃkhyakam kulam uddharate tasmin janmaprāptau kṣitau punaḥ  Paus dharmopetāṃ harer bhaktim āśraya tyantyabjasaṃbhava jātajanmā tṛtīyā tu prāpnuyāt sadvivekavat  Paus samuttarati vai yena ghorāt saṃsārasaṃkaṭāt rūpam ādyapratiṣṭhāyā ityuktaṃ dvijasattama  Paus viśeṣasanniveśebhyastvidānīm avadhāraya manīṣitaṃ phalaṃ bhuktvā divyeṣu bhuvaneṣu ca  Paus janmāsādya samutkṛṣṭam ācaret punareva hi daivī brahmapratiṣṭhādyā yā parasmin hi janmani  Paus prāgvad yacchati vijñānaṃ parameśapadāptigam etāvad uktaṃ vaiṣamyaṃ sati sāmyaṃ mahāmate  Paus yajñottamasya divyasya saphalasyābjasaṃbhava acyutasyāvināśasya bhavakṣayakarasya ca  Paus bhedaṃ yad vastumātreṇa sthitaṃ tad avadhāraya varṇā nāṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ gṛhāśramaratātmanām  Paus ādīkṣitānāṃ prāgvipra bhītānāṃ maraṇādike vyavahārasthitānāṃ ca pratiṣṭhādyā mahāmate  Paus nirvarjitāḥ prayacchanti phalamuktaṃ hi yanmayā nirvāṇadīkṣitānāṃ ca guruṇācyutavedinām  Paus bhaktyā prāptādhikārāṇāṃ nityaṃ ārādhanaṃ prati samyaksamādhiniṣṭhānām iha janmaikaśeṣiṇām  Paus vikalpakṣīṇacittānāṃ pratiṣṭhā vihitābjaja trāṇārthaṃ svakulādīnām anantānāṃ ca saṃbhavāt  Paus yāvajjīvāvadhiṃ kālaṃ teṣām āsthāpanaṃ tu vai vihitaṃ paritoṣārthaṃ buddher buddhimatāṃ vara  Paus jñātvaivaṃ dharmalabdhena dhanena ca balena ca ākṣipan grahaṇāt sarvaṃ dhvajāntaṃ vai samāpyaya ca  Paus viśvāvāsapadāvāsaṃ dakṣiṇānanam āsthitam pīṭhastham upaviṣṭaṃ ca prāgdvāre nirṛte gṛhe  Paus evaṃ khageśapṛṣṭhasthaṃ vāyudiṅmandire hitam divyabhogaphalāvāptiṃ saha diktalpagāt tu vai  Paus prajāpatitvam āpannā uktadigviniveśanāt sthitiṃ triviṣṭapādīnām upariṣṭāt tu śāśvatīm  Paus vihāyasagatiṃ divyāṃ yānagāt prāpyate pumān bhaktānāṃ phalalipsūnāṃ sthānasthalaphalādikam  Paus phaladiksaṃsthitāḥ sarve nagarāṇāṃ phalārthinām utkṛṣṭajanmūparvaṃ tu janma cātmaprakāśakam  Paus tad viddhi bhavaśāntyartham acirād eva padmaja yathoddiṣṭakrameṇaiva diktraye viniveśya ca  Paus nṛsiṃhakapilakroḍamūrtayo vā mahāmate prāgvadvidikcatuṣkeṣu caturṇāṃ vihitaṃ kramāt  Paus vājivaktraṃ tu muktānāṃ siṃhādīnāṃ niveśanam diktraye kacchapādīnāṃ kuryāt saṃsthāpanaṃ tu vā  Paus mīnavāmananāthānāṃ devānāṃ prākphalāptaye vidikṣu viniyoktavyaṃ yathoddiṣṭakrameṇa tu  Paus trivitramakuṭhārāstrakaraṃ kāntāvapurdharam sarvadevamayaṃ viśvarūpaṃ tu parameśvaram  Paus etāvad uktaniyamam ato nye ye khilāstu vai prādurbhāvāntarāścaiva prādurbhāvābjasaṃbhava  Paus gurūṇāṃ saṃmatenaiṣa yoktavyaṃ nānyayājakaiḥ sadevāṃ hi kuṭīṃ ramyām āpādyābhimatāṃ tataḥ  Paus dvārāgre maṇḍapābhāsaṃ sopānapadavīyutam vedīvibhūṣitaṃ kuryāt sthitam ārādhanāśrayam  Paus bhogānāṃ sthitaye nyeṣāṃ vātavṛṣṭikṣamaṃ śubham prāsādāṅghripratiṣṭhārtham āpādyābjaja vai tataḥ  Paus pañcānāṃ vā navānāṃ ca ekasmin vā ghaṭodake sarvaratnamayopete nyastaṃ yatparameśvaram  Paus āṅgaṃ salāñchanaṃ māntraṃ parivārasamanvitam svaśaktikhacitaṃ caiva pratyahaṃ pūjayecca tam  Paus mantrabimbapratiṣṭhārthaṃ kālavighnopaśāntaye anyathā jāyate vighnam anivāryaṃ mahāmate  Paus gacchanti sannidhiṃ mantrā nityaṃ traikālyam arcanāt yacchantyanarcanācchokaṃ rodhitaṃ yatra yatra ca  Paus padāni prāṅkaṇe caiva devānāṃ viniveśane uktāni padmasaṃbhūta idānīm avadhāraya  Paus madhyadeśe tu tadbhūmeḥ prāsāde bhimate tate sanniveśavaśenaiva nānāsaṃjñāvasaṃsthitaḥ  Paus pīṭhabrahmavaśāsthānasta mbhamba  sya  caturātmanaḥ caturdigvīkṣamāṇasya yānusandhānalakṣaṇā  Paus boddhavyaṃ sā pratiṣṭhā ca digvyūhaparipūrakī dhṛtiśaktisvarūpeṇa amūrtenātyayātmanā  Paus sthitaye prakriyārthaṃ ca brahmapāṣāṇatāmratā sarvaṃ brahmaśilāniṣṭham ākṣiteḥ kamalodbhava  Paus vyāptamāmūlataścaiva tenāmūrtena vai punaḥ dravyamūrtim amūrtāṃ ca gṛhītastamba lakṣaṇam  Paus ekasyācyutabījasya bhinneṣu prativastuṣu saṃsthitā sthitir acchinnā sā pratiṣṭhita eva hi  Paus bhinnānāṃ vyūhamūrtīnāṃ kevalā dyakhilasya ca prādurbhāvasamūhasya vdyādikasya tu yad dvija  Paus ekasmin viśvapīṭhe tu sthitirekasya cecchayā pratiṣṭhākhyaṃ viśeṣaṃ tat sthāpanaṃ samudāhṛtam  Paus cicchaktim anuviddhaṃ ca avyaktaṃ tattvasaṃgraham dravyamūrtau calākhye ca nītam ekātmanā dhiyā  Paus bimbasaṃskārakāle tu adhivāsābhidhe dvija acalatvena sanmantraṃ calabhāvanayā punaḥ  Paus sāṅgaṃ salāñchanaṃ caiva kṛtvā abhimataṃ tu vai ārādhanārthaṃ hṛdayanyastaṃ taddhṛdaye punaḥ  Paus samāharet kṛtārthatvānnityaṃ kālāntareṇa vā sadākhyam aparaṃ tattva   Paus nānāsaṃjñaṃ tathā nānāpramāṇaṃ tadvadeva hi racanābhistathā nānāvividhābhistu rañjitam  Paus bahvībhirbhūmikābhistu citritābhir alaṃkṛtam āpādabhūmeraṇḍāntam anurūpaṃ ca yattrayam  Paus uttarottarataḥ kuryād bhūrbhuvasvādikotthitaiḥ sthāvarair jaṃgamaiḥ siddhair vividhair mañjarīgaṇaiḥ  Paus nagaindrair nāgarājaistu suśubhair nalinīvanaiḥ murajaśṛṅkhalābaddhair divyair nānālatāgṛhaiḥ  Paus purujādyair jalodbhūtaiḥ prāṇijālaistathaiva hi vanajair nagajaiścānyair mṛgarāṅgaṇapūrvakaiḥ  Paus vāraṇāḥ śabarāścaiva haṃsapadmasamāśritaiḥ śaṅkhasvastikakahlārapūrvair anyaistu vārijaiḥ  Paus nandikaiḥ kesarai ramyaiḥ śatapatravad utthitaiḥ sakiṅkiṇīkaiścamarairātapatrair dhvajādikaiḥ  Paus bhūmigābhūmigaiḥ sarvaiḥ samudraiḥ saritānvitaiḥ navopakaraṇair devaiścandrārkajvalanādikaiḥ  Paus prādurbhāvāntarair dvivyaiḥ prādurbhāvasamanvitaiḥ dvīpair dvīpāntaropetaiḥ pātālaistajja nānvitaiḥ  Paus maharjanastapaḥsatyalokanāthair mahāprabhaiḥ dhyānamaunaparair brahman vahnidevayutair dvijaiḥ  Paus ityevam ādikaiścānyair jaṅghāstambhavatīḥ śubhāḥ bhūṣayet kamalodbhūta sarvadiṅnāsikaiḥ saha  Paus garbhagṛhāmbaramadhyāt kuryāccakrāmbujāṅkitam pitāmahādyair vibudhaiḥ siddhavidyādharaiḥ saha  Paus puṣpajapamālādharaiḥ prahvaiścāmarair vyajanoddhataiḥ vanamālāgadāśaṅkhacakrapadmaśriyādikaiḥ  Paus khageśavedavedāṅgair akṣasūtrakarāṅkitaiḥ āvāryāvarakatvena cakrapadmādbahiḥ sthitaiḥ  Paus antarbhittigaṇaṃ sarvadevadaityādikairgaṇaiḥ nṛttagī ta paraiścānyair nāradādyairvibhūṣayet  Paus praṇavena svanāmnā ca natiniṣṭhena tatra vai sannirodhya ca tanmantraṃ bhūlokaṃ pādamākṣiti  Paus evaṃ prāsādapīṭhe tu bhuvarlokaṃ yathāsthitam jaṅghāyāṃ svargalokaṃ ca mahacchikharabhūmigam  Paus stambhaṃ ca talapaṃ caiva caraṇaṃ jaṅghameva ca sthānaṃ sthūṇaṃ ca pādaṃ ca paryāyavacanāstvime  Paus janarlokaṃ ca tad vedyāṃtastapaḥsaṃjñaṃ ca daṇḍakam satyasaṃjñaśca tallokaṃ tacchikhāyāṃ surālaye  Paus bhāvayecca parāṃ vyāptimeva vai sāptalaukikīm bhuvanordhvamayīṃ vipra prāsāde bhimate tu vai  Paus anuviddhaṃ pādapādyair anyaisvattāsvarūpakaiḥ parasparaṃ hi sarvatra vyāpakaiḥ paralakṣaṇaiḥ  Paus bhūrlokāṃśaṃ vinā brahmaṃstathānyair ujjhitaṃ hi tat rajastamomahattvācca īṣat sattvaguṇāt tu vai  Paus sattvaikaguṇarūpāṇām anyeṣām ata eva hi bhūrlokaṃ ca pṛthaksaṃsthaṃ padādyadhvagaṇasya ca  Paus kūrmabrahmātmasaṃjñāyāṃ śikhāyāṃ ca padatrayam nyastavyaṃ jāgradādyaṃ yad ratnanyāse kṛte sati  Paus turyabrahmapadopetaṃ mantrādhvapratimāsane tābhyāṃ taṃ pādato nyasya tattveyaṃ kamalodbhava  Paus ānābhemūrdhaparyantaṃ kalādhvaṃ bhāvayet tataḥ tad brahmarandhrakamale mantrabrahmatalakṣitau  Paus karṇikāyāṃ paraṃ brahma sāmānyaṃ śāśvataṃ vibhum dīkṣākāle yathoddiṣṭā mayā te dhvamayī sthitiḥ  Paus prāsādānāṃ tu sā siddhiḥ śikhāntānāṃ mahāmate pratimānāṃ sapīṭhānāṃ sādhibhūtādilakṣaṇam  Paus tatrādhyātmaṃ hi bhagavān mūrtaṃ śāntaṃ mama ācyutam sa eva hi virāḍātmā hyadhidaivatamavyayam  Paus adhibhūtaṃ dvijāvyaktaṃ sarvatattvamayaṃ hi tat vidyākalādikaiścānyaiḥ parārthaira khilaiḥ saha  Paus sabīje vilaye yadvat susūkṣmādyair vyavasthitaḥ tattvāḥ śabdādayaścaiva buddhiniṣṭhā mahāmate  Paus tadvatprāsādadehe tu te devādhiṣṭhite smṛtāḥ sarvaśaktimaye vipra śuddhaṃ satsattvalakṣaṇaiḥ  Paus yathopacād vihitaṃ mantraṃ sarveśvarād vibhoḥ sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ caiva sarvakartāram īśvaram  Paus mantramūrtestathā viddhi upacārāt tu tadgṛham saṃskṛtasya tvato yatnāt sapīṭhasya yathāvidhi  Paus devavat sthāpanaṃ tasya vihitaṃ sattvajasya ca sopānapadavī yuktā jagatī yā sulakṣaṇā  Paus prāsādasya ca pīṭhaṃ tat parijñeyaṃ yadātmakam ekībhūtatvam āpannaṃ sudhālepaistu sāyasaiḥ  Paus pakveṣṭakāsametaiśca sthiramṛccopalaistathā pramāṇalakṣaṇopetaṃ viśvavid racanānvitam  Paus rañjitaṃ rāgajālena phalaṃ yacchati śāśvatam jīrṇatvācca kṛtaṃ bhūyaḥ svayaṃvyaktādibhirdvija  Paus ākāreṣvācyutīyeṣu vividheṣvarciteṣu ca phalaṃ sahastraguṇitaṃ kartāpnoti mahāmate  Paus toyāśayeśayā vṛkṣā kṣetraṃ puṣkaramādiyat paunaḥpunyena sadbhaktaiḥ kṛtaduṣkṛtaśāntaye  Paus anādyajñānasaṃsargāt kālahrāsavaśād api naṣṭaṃ narendranāthā ye pālayantyarcanādikaiḥ  Paus dehānte yānti te svargaṃ rājyadoṣair anāvṛtāḥ kālenetya punaḥ svargāt jñānam āsādya nirmalam  Paus yena sāṃsārikaṃ duḥkhaṃ duḥsahaṃ nāśameti ca phalam etāvad uktaṃ hi devālayasamāpanāt  Paus savittānāṃ ca bhaktānāṃ nṛpāṇām api padmaja sarvādhvabhāvanopetam āstāṃ tāvat surālayam  Paus bhuvanādhvamayīṃ vyāptim āpādayati kevalāt anugrahecchayācāryo bhaktānāṃ saṃpradarśayet  Paus lakṣmyā lakṣaṇayuktasya sthapateraśaṭhasya ca prāguktaṃ labhate kartā susaṃpūrṇaphalaṃ dvija  Paus prāsādānāmamantraṃ tu svayaṃ śilpikarāt tu vai yatphalaṃ labhate kartā hemakṣmānnādikaṃ hi tat  Paus phalaṃ sarvasvadānād vā labhate vidhipūrvakāt mṛdā dārviṣṭakādyaistu svalpaṃ vā madhyamaṃ mahat  Paus pramāṇalakṣaṇopetaṃ surākīrṇaṃ surālayam yathoditair guṇair yuktaṃ grāmyaṃ vā kuṭisaṃjñitam  Paus digvidiksāntarād bāhyād yuktaṃ prasthāpitaiḥ paraiḥ vibhavavyūhasaṃjñaistu prādurbhāvāntarāstu vā  Paus avanīcalanādyaistu doṣaiḥ saṃcālitaṃ yadi dīrghakālavaśenāpi snātānāṃ dhanakarmaṇām  Paus kuryād yathāvad uddhāraṃ gurūṇāṃ saṃmatena tu rājā vā tad amātyo nyaḥ sadbhaktaśca nṛpājñanayā  Paus vratārcanādikāryāṇāṃ labdhvānujñāṃ parāṃ vibhoḥ anantaśayane dārbhe uttānasthaṃ smared vibhum  Paus dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa svargeśaṃ bhagavān hariḥ ayutaṃ tvayutārdhaṃ ca śatam ardhādhikaṃ tu vā  Paus athānukūle nakṣatre nṛpasya nagarasya ca śāntyarthaṃ jīvabhūtaṃ yanmantreśaguṇamūrtibhṛt  Paus traiguṇyaṃ yacchate hastam arcayitvā yathāvidhi tarpayitvā ca dehānte samidbhirbahubhiḥ kramāt  Paus bhuvanādhvamayaṃ śaktirvyaktisaṅghaṃ yathoditam tathā varṇādhvapadasaṅghaṃ sattābhūtaṃ hi pañcakam  Paus tarpayitvārcayitvā ca sādhibhūtādhikaṃ tu vai bhūtaśaktigaṇaṃ tadvat susūkṣmam aparaṃ hi yat  Paus devapīṭhālayaṃ vipra ruddhaṃ kuryād yathākramam udayārkasamaṃ jñātvā saṃjñāmantrapadaiḥ svakaiḥ  Paus praṇavādyair namo ntaiśca vyaktisthaṃ punareva hi prātimaṃ rakṣa bhagavan mantravṛndaṃ hi cādhvajam  Paus udumbarārdhamānasthaṃ digvidigbhūmikaṃ hi yat buddhidharmasthitair darbhair vyāptāmā baimbalakṣaṇe  Paus samyak tadaparijñānād anusandhānam ācaret tad utthāpanakāle tu kṛtanyāsastu sāṃpratam  Paus upoddharaṇaliṅgaiśca sāṣṭāṅgair vedikaistathā ekaikam ātmasākṛtvā pūrakeṇārkabimbavat  Paus susaṃmate rcite kuṃbhe hemādyair mūrtike tu vā nirodhyodakasaṃpūrṇe pūjayet pratyahaṃ tataḥ  Paus saṃpannotpattaye samyagavatārya yathoddhṛtāt saṃskṛtasya pratiṣṭhānam ācartavyaṃ hi vai punaḥ  Paus nṛpendrarāṣṭrasthānānāṃ godvijānāṃ ca vṛddhaye yatpadaprāptaye śaśvat sakhilasyākhilasya ca  Paus prāsādapratimānāṃ ca evam utthāpanaṃ dvija gobhūhemādikānāṃ ca rāṣṭrasya sanṛpasya ca  Paus jāyate śubhaśāntyartham ihaloke paratra ca ato nyathā mahān doṣo bhaved vai padmasaṃbhava  Paus prāsādagrāhikānāṃ ca bahiścābhyantare tu vā bimbānāṃ cālyamānānāṃ mantrair aṣṭākṣarādikaiḥ  Paus prāgvannyastasvamantrāṇāṃ samāharaṇam ācaret maṇinā sūryakāntena ādityād analaṃ yathā  Paus samāhṛteṣu mantreṣu cālyamāneṣu pauṣkara bhaṅge karmavaśājjāte pratimāsu pramādataḥ  Paus prāktanenaiva pāpena prāyaścittaṃ caret tadā cittaprasādajanakaṃ kīrtiśarmakaraṃ tu vai  Paus tatraikarātrapūrvaṃ tu trirātraṃ ṣaḍahantu vai vrataṃ dvādaśarātraṃ ca svaśaktyā tu samācaret  Paus snānādihavanāntena karmaṇāvahitena tu ca tilāni sahiraṇyāni dānaṃ sarajatāni ca  Paus śāntipūrvaṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ sājyakṣīrodanādikam bhojanaṃ tu yathāśakti bahūnāṃ vai mahāmate  Paus sadānamevaṃ nirvartya vrataṃ vai deśikādijam vased āśritya vai kṣetraṃ prasiddhaṃ siddhasevitam  Paus suprasiddhaṃ tu vā tīrtham ekāhaṃ vā dinatrayam āvartayan mahāmantramasakṛd dvādaśākṣaram  Paus kālaṃ muhūrtasaṃjñaṃ yat pratisandhyātrayaṃ tu vai pūrṇam āyatane kuryād divye vā siddhasaṃjñake  Paus sati vai bhaktisāmye tu prāyaścittam idaṃ smṛtam sāmānyaṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ manasaḥ prakaṭe tu vai  Paus uttarottaram ādhikyaṃ japakarmaṇi vai smṛtam śūdraviṭkṣatraviprāṇāṃ bhaktānāṃ nānyayājinām  Paus uktaṃ hyetat prakāśe tu atha yāvatprasannatām tāvatkālaṃ japenmantraṃ bhakṣayet pāvanaṃ matam  Paus yāvatprasādam āyāti svabuddhir manasā saha aprakāśe dviṣaṭkārṇaṃ mantram aṣṭākṣaraṃ hi yat  Paus ṣaḍakṣaraṃ dvijaśreṣṭha kramāt sandhyātrayaṃ tu vai snānaṃ yathoditaṃ kuryājjaped antarjale sthitaḥ  Paus trimantrasahitāṃ śaktyā snānakāle tvananyadhīḥ aṣṭārṇamuktasaṃkhyaṃ tu prātarmadhye dinakṣaye  Paus deśakālaṃ tu vai kuryāt pratisnānaṃ tu vai sakṛt pañcāṅgam abhiṣekaṃ ca śeṣaṃ sandhyādvaye hitam  Paus jaghanāntamadhaḥkāyaṃ saṃprakṣālyāmṛtāmbhasā adhovāsaḥ parityajya śubham ādāya cāmbaram  Paus dinatrayaṃ ca ṣaḍahamaṣṭāho dvādaśāhvikam śūdrādīnāṃ dvijāntānāṃ hitaṃ cottaratottaram  Paus kramam etanmahābuddhe manasaḥ śuddhikāraṇam phalenānugataṃ bhūyo vidhyantaram athocyate  Paus saṃkṣiptaṃ sarvasāmānyaṃ yathābhimatabhūmikam caturhastadviṣaṭkāntaṃ kṣetraṃ kṣetra kam  Paus uttarottarapūrvābhyāṃ nyūnaṃ nyūnatarāvadhi bhāgaistridaśaparyantair bhaktaiḥ pañcaśatādikaiḥ  Paus bhittayoṃśadvayenaiva pañcāṅgād antaraṃ tu hi garbhaṃ sārdhatrayenāto bhittayordhadvayena ca  Paus viddhi ṣaṭkaramānasya bhūbhāgasya ca kalpanā aṣṭamāṃśojjhitair bhāgair garbhaṃ saptapadaṃ tu vai  Paus parijñeyaṃ caturbhirvai tacchiṣṭair bhittayoṃśakaiḥ caturbhir aṣṭabhāgaistu sārdhair aṣṭakarāgraham  Paus bhāgatrayena sārdhena bhittivyūhaṃ samāpayet sāṅgaṃ pañcakaraṃ garbhakṣetraṃ navapadāt tu vai  Paus śeṣeṇa karasaṅghena bhittayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ṣaṭkaraṃ daśahastasya garbhakṣetrasya vistṛtam  Paus karadvidvitayenaiva bhittisaṅghaṃ vidhīyate ekādaśakarakṣetrāt garbhaṃ sārdhaṃ ca ṣaṭkaram  Paus sārdhaṃ catuḥkaraṃ caiva bhittimānam udāhṛtam kṣetradvādaśabhāgāt tu pādonaṃ samasaptakam  Paus devālayaṃ parijñeyaṃ pādonaikaṃ catuṣkaraiḥ vidheyā bhittayaścaiva vibhajyaivaṃ tameva hi  Paus kṛtvā trayodaśāṃśaistu phaladībhittayoṃśakaiḥ navāṃśe vabhabhiḥ pūrṇe vidheyaṃ bhagavad gṛham  Paus śubhāpacaya siddhim āpādya vdyaṅgulenāṅgulena vā eṣāṃ prasādagarbhāṃśabhittibhyāṃ pātayenmanaḥ  Paus mānādhikaṃ vinikṣepya kṣetrāṇāṃ ca nipātayet paramāṇusamaṃ mānaṃ kiṃ punaścāṅgulādikam  Paus matā vṛddhikarī nṝṇāṃ vṛddhipātam aśobhanam samānīyaṃ hi yatnena mahatā tacca pauṣkara  Paus racanābhirūpetaṃ ca vihitaṃ ca caturmukham cāturātmyavyapekṣāyāmekadvārathā  Paus yathābhimatadigvaktraṃ nānāsiddhiphalāptaye cirāyuṣārthī prāgvaktraṃ yaśorthī dakṣiṇāmukham  Paus kuryāt pratyaṅmukhaṃ caiva vṛttyarthaṃ ca svatantrake udaṅmukhaṃ ca prāsādaṃ dhanadhānyaṃ prayacchati  Paus etāvat uktaṃ hi phalamaihalaukikam uttamam nānābhogasamopetaṃ sarvāsāṃ viddhi pauṣkara  Paus svakṣetre vitate ramye svatantraṃ svāṅkanakṣitau saha pūrvapratiṣṭhāyām athavāyatane hareḥ  Paus svāyambhuve vā siddhākhye mukhyakalpam idaṃ smṛtam anukalpamato nyatra boddhavyaṃ vibudhāṅkaṇe  Paus prākprāsādadhvajacchāyāviniyukte tate pade iṣṭakāṃ ca sudhācūrṇaṃ doṣaiśca pariśodhite  Paus tadantare pratiṣṭhāpya homādyuktaṃ hi sonnatam prāsādadvāramānaistu sapīṭhaṃ viśvam ācyutam  Paus saṃpūrṇaṃ lakṣaṇaiḥ sarvairārṇavāntarakīrtaye ṣyātītasya vaṃśasya svakasyoddharaṇāya ca  Paus yadaivaitatkṛtā buddhiḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ pādayāmyaham tatkṣaṇād eva tatkīrtiḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ labhate cyutām  Paus bhūlokādyakhilānāṃ ca sthānānām api kiṃ punaḥ vibhavena jagadyoneḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ yaḥ samācaret  Paus pitrāsū dī nāṃ gatāsūnām anyeṣāṃ vā karoti yaḥ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca pratiṣṭhānaṃ svaśaktyā vibhavena vā  Paus acirādeva te yānti śaśvadevāntakāspadam vaiṣṇavaṃ ca paraṃ sthānaṃ tataḥ kālāntareṇa tu  Paus kṣityaṃśaṃ śubham āsādya kulaśīlādikaiḥ saha ācaranti śubhaṃ yena prāpnuvanti punarbhavam  Paus kṛpayānantu pratiṣṭhāṃ yaḥ samācaret jātīnāmathavānyeṣāṃ tadutthaṃ ca phalaṃ  Paus praviśanti ca mantreśāḥ praṇavadhvanisādhitāḥ karṣayanti vibhūtiṃ svāṃ kiñcitkālāntareṇa tu  Paus kṛtā vai dhvastadoṣāśca nirvighnam amalāṃ punaḥ niveśitāḥ susiddhādyaistīrthaiḥ kṣetrāvaneṣu ca  Paus nivārayanti ye mohād vibhavavyūhamūrtiṣu saṃsthānamānam ākāraṃ na doṣaṃ kālāntarotthitam  Paus smartavyā vāsudevādyā dvibhedāḥ pārameśvarāḥ catvāraścāniruddhāntāścaturvyūhavyavasthayā  Paus evamanye va rāhādyāścaturvyūhena vai saha tathaiva keśavādyā ye anyenānyatareṇa vā  Paus mandamandatarād bhāvavaśād amarapūjita evaṃ yad adhikāreṇa kuryād ārādhanaṃ hi yaḥ  Paus bhogair yathoditaiḥ śuddhaiḥ kriyābhirvividhaistataḥ niṣpattau tu kriyāṅgānāṃ hṛdāstrārghyaṃ samantrarāṭ  Paus nānarcitaṃ vibhorbhogaṃ kalpitaṃ vinivedya ca praṇavādyantagenaiva   Paus
